 &T;u leofusta bro&d;ur  sui&d;e freondlice &amp; sui&d;e fremsumlice &d;u me t&ae;ldes&d;  &amp; mid ea&d;mode inge&d;once &d;u me ciddes&d;  for&d;on ic min ma&d;  &amp; wolde fleon &d;a byr&d;enne &d;&ae;re hirdelecan giemenne. 
 &D;ara byr&d;enna hefignesse  eall &d;&ae;t ic his geman  ic awrite on &d;isse andweardan bec  &d;yl&ae;s hi hw&ae;m leohte &d;yncen to underfonne; 
 &amp; ic eac l&ae;re &d;&ae;t hira nan &d;ara ne wilnie &d;e hine unw&ae;rlice bega; 
 &amp; se &d;e hi unw&ae;rlice &amp; unryhtlice gewilnige  ondr&ae;de he &d;&ae;t he hi &ae;fre underfenge. 
 Nu ic wilnige &d;&ae;tte &d;eos spr&ae;c stigge on &d;&ae;t inge&d;onc &d;&ae;s leorneres  su&ae; su&ae; on sume hl&ae;dre  st&ae;pm&ae;lum near &amp; near  o&d;&d;&ae;t hio f&ae;stlice gestonde on &d;&ae;m solore &d;&ae;s modes &d;e hi leornige; 
 &amp; for&d;y ic hi tod&ae;le on feower: an is &d;ara d&ae;la hu he on &d;one folgo&d; becume; 
 O&d;er hu he &d;&ae;ron libbe; 
 &D;ridda is hu he &d;&ae;ron l&ae;re; 
 Feor&d;e is hu he his agene un&d;eawas ongietan wille &amp; hira ge&d;&ae;f bion  &t;yl&ae;s he for &d;y underfenge his ea&d;modnesse forl&ae;te  o&d;&d;e eft his lif sie ungelic his &d;enunga  o&d;&d;e he to &d;riste &amp; to sti&d; sie for &d;y underfenge his lareowdomes; 
 Ac gemetgige hit se ege his agenra un&d;eawa  &amp; bef&ae;ste he mid his lifes bisenum &d;a lare &d;&ae;m &d;e his wordum ne geliefen; 
 &amp; &d;onne he god weorc wyrce  gemyne he &d;&ae;s yfeles &d;e he worhte  &d;ette sio unrotnes  &d;e he for &d;&ae;m yflan weorcum h&ae;bbe  gemetgige &d;one gefean &d;e he for &d;&ae;m godan weorcum h&ae;fde; 
 &D;yl&ae;s he beforan &d;&ae;s dieglan deman eagum sie ahafen on his mode &amp; on his ofermettum a&d;unden  &amp; &d;onne &d;urh &d;&ae;t selflice his godan weorc forleose. 
 Ac monige sindon me sui&d;e onlice on ungel&ae;rednesse  &d;eah &d;e hi n&ae;fre leorningcnihtas n&ae;ren  wilnia&d; &d;eah lareowas to beonne  &amp; &d;yncet him sui&d;e leoht sio byr&d;en &d;&ae;s lareowdomes  for&d;on&d;e hi ne cunnon &d;&ae;t m&ae;gen his micelnesse. 
 From &d;&ae;re dura selfre &d;isse bec  &d;&ae;t is from onginne &d;isse spr&ae;ce  sint adrifene &amp; get&ae;lde &d;a unwaran  &d;e him agniat &d;one cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;s lareowdomes &d;e hi na ne geleornodon. 
 &D;&ae;tte unl&ae;rde ne dyrren underfon lareowdom. 
 For&d;on&d;e nan cr&ae;ft nis to l&ae;ranne &d;&ae;m &d;e hine &ae;r geornlice ne leornode  forhwon beo&d; &ae;fre su&ae; &d;riste &d;a ungel&ae;redan &d;&ae;t hi underfon &d;a heorde &d;&ae;s lariowdomes  &d;onne se cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;s lareowdomes bi&d; cr&ae;ft ealra cr&ae;fta? 
 Hua nat &d;&ae;t &d;a wunda &d;&ae;s modes bio&d; digelran &d;onne &d;a wunda &d;&ae;s lichaman? 
 &amp; &d;eah &d;a woroldlecan l&ae;cas scoma&t; &d;&ae;t hi onginnen &d;a wunda lacnian &d;e hi gesion ne magon  &amp; huru gif hi nou&d;er gecnawan ne cunnan ne &d;a medtrymnesse ne eac &d;a wyrta &d;e &d;&ae;rwi&d; sculon. 
 &amp; hwilon ne scoma&d; &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;s modes l&ae;ceas beon scoldon  &d;eah &d;e hi nana wuht ongitan ne cunnon &d;ara g&ae;stlecena beboda  &d;&ae;t hie him onteo&d; &d;&ae;t hie sien heortan l&ae;cas. 
 Ac for&d;on&d;e nu eall se weor&d;scipe &d;isse worolde is gecierred  Gode &d;onc  to weor&d;scipe &d;&ae;m &ae;wf&ae;stam  &d;&ae;t &d;a sindon nu weor&d;oste &d;e &ae;wf&ae;stoste sindon  for&d;on licet sui&d;e monig &d;&ae;t he &ae;wf&ae;s&d; lareow sie  &d;e he wilnia&d; micle woroldare habban. 
 Be &d;am Cris&d; selfa cleopode  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Hi seca&d; &d;&ae;t hi mon &ae;rest grete &amp; weor&d;ige on ceapstowum &amp; on gebeorscipum  &amp; &d;&ae;t hie fyrmest hlynigen &ae;t &ae;fengieflum  &amp; &d;&ae;t ieldes&d;e setl on gemetengum hi seca&d;. 
 For&d;on hie sua on ofermettum &amp; mid upahafenesse becuma&d; to &d;&ae;re are &d;&ae;re hirdelecan giemenne  hi ne magon medomlice &d;enian &d;a &d;enunga  &amp; &d;&ae;re ea&d;modnesse lareowas bion; 
 Ac sio tunge bi&d; gescinded on &d;am lariowdome &d;onne hio o&d;er l&ae;r&d;  o&d;er hio liornode. 
 Suelcum monnum Dryhten cidde &d;urh &d;one witgan  &amp; him suelc o&d;wat  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Hie ricsedon  n&ae;s &d;eah mines &d;onces; 
 Ealdormen hi w&ae;ron  &amp; ic hie ne cu&d;e. 
 &D;a &d;e sua ricsiea&d;  hi ricsia&d; of hira agnum dome  n&ae;s of &d;&ae;s hiehstan deman  &d;onne hi ne beo&d; mid nanre sylle underscotene &d;&ae;s godcundlican m&ae;genes  ne for nanum cr&ae;fte gecorene  ac mid hira agenre gewilnunge hie bio&d; onb&ae;rnede  &d;&ae;t hie gereafia&d; sua heane lariowdom sui&d;or &d;onne hi hine geearnien. 
 Hie &d;onne se eca &amp; se diegla dema upahefe&d; suelce he hi nyte  &amp; ge&d;afiende he hit forbire&d; for &d;am dome his ge&d;ylde. 
 Ac &d;eah hi on &d;am hade fela wundra wyrcen  eft &d;onne hi to him cuma&d;  he cui&d;: Gewita&d; from me ge unryhtwyrhtan; 
 Nat ic hw&ae;t ge sint. 
 Eft he hie &d;reade &d;urh &d;one witgan for hira ungel&ae;rednesse  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;a hierdas n&ae;fdon andgit: hie h&ae;fdon mine &ae;  &amp; hi me ne gecniowon. 
 Se &d;e Godes bebodu ne gecn&ae;w&d;  ne bi&d; he oncnawen from Gode. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce cu&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Se &d;e God ne ongit  ne ongit God hine. 
 Unwise lareowas cuma&d; for &d;&ae;s folces synnum. 
 For&d;on oft for &d;&ae;s lareowes unwisdome misfara&d; &d;a hieremenn  &amp; oft for &d;&ae;s lareowes wisdome unwisum hieremonnum bi&d; geborgen. 
 Gif &d;onne &ae;g&d;er bi&d; unwis  &d;onne is to ge&d;encanne hw&ae;t Cris&d; self cu&ae;&d; on his godspelle  he cw&ae;&d;: Gif se blinda &d;one blindan l&ae;t  hi fealla&d; begen on &ae;nne pytt. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan se sealmscop cu&ae;&d;: Sien hira eagan a&d;istrode &d;&ae;t hi ne geseon  &amp; hiora hrygc simle gebieged. 
 Ne cu&ae;&d; he &d;&ae;t for&d;y&d;e he &ae;negum men &d;&ae;s wyscte o&d;&d;e wilnode  ac he witgode sua sua hit geweor&d;an sceolde. 
 So&d;lice &d;a eagan &d;&ae;t beo&d; &d;a lareowas  &amp; se hrygc &d;&ae;t sint &d;a hieremenn; 
 For&d;an &d;a eagan bio&d; on &d;am lichoman foreweardum &amp; ufeweardum  &amp; se hrycg f&ae;r&d; &ae;fter &ae;lcre wuhte; 
 Sua ga&d; &d;a lareowas beforan &d;&ae;m folce  &amp; &d;&ae;t folc &ae;fter. 
 &D;onne &d;am lareowum a&d;istria&d; &d;&ae;s modes eagan  &d;e beforan gan scoldon mid godum bisenum  &d;onne gebig&d; &d;&ae;t folc hira hrycg to hefegum byr&d;enum manegum. 
 Ne eft &d;a gel&ae;redan &d;e swa nylla&d; libban swa hie on bocum leornedon  &d;&ae;t hi scoldon ne underfon &d;a are &d;&ae;s lareowdomes. 
 Monige eac wise lareowas winna&d; mid hira &d;eawum wi&d; &d;a g&ae;s&d;lecan bebodu &d;e hi mid wordum l&ae;ra&d;  &d;onne hie on o&d;re wisan libba&d; on o&d;re hi l&ae;ra&d;. 
 Oft &d;onne se hirde g&ae;&d; on frecne wegas  sio hiord &d;e unw&ae;rre bi&d;  gehrist. 
 Be suelcum hirdum cw&ae;&d; se witga: Ge fortr&ae;don Godes sceapa g&ae;rs &amp; ge gedrefdon hiora w&ae;ter mid iowrum fotum  &d;eah ge hit &ae;r undrefed druncen. 
 Sua &d;a lareowas hi drinca&d; sui&d;e hluter w&ae;ter  &d;onne hi &d;one godcundan wisdom leornia&d;  &amp; eac &d;onne hie hiene l&ae;ra&d;; 
 Ac hie hit gedrefa&d; mid hira agnum un&d;eawum  &d;onne &d;&ae;t folc bisena&d; on hira un&d;eawum  nals on hira lare. 
 &D;eah &d;&ae;t folc &d;yrste &d;&ae;re lare  hie hie ne magon drincan  ac hio bi&d; gedrefed mid&d;am&d;e &d;a lareowas o&d;er do&d; o&d;er hie l&ae;ra&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m Dryhten cw&ae;&d; eft &d;urh &d;one witgan: Yfle preostas bio&t; folces hryre. 
 Ne dere&d; nan mon sui&d;or &d;&ae;re halgan gesomnunge &d;onne &d;a &d;e &d;onne noman underfo&d; &amp; &d;a endebyrdnesse &d;&ae;s halgan hades &amp; &d;one on woh do&d;; 
 For&d;on hie nan monn ne dearr &d;reagean &d;eah hie agyltan  ac mid &d;am beo&d; synna sui&d;e gebr&ae;dda &d;e hie beo&d; sua geweor&d;ade. 
 Ac hie woldon selfe fleon &d;a byr&d;enne sua micelre scylde  &d;a &d;e his unwier&d;e w&ae;ron  gif hie mid hiora heortan earum woldon gehieran &amp; geornlice ge&d;encan &d;one Cristes cuide  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Se &d;e &ae;nigne &d;issa ierminga besuic&d;  him w&ae;re betere &d;&ae;t him w&ae;re sumu esulcweorn to &d;&ae;m suiran getiged  &amp; sua aworpen to s&ae;s grunde. 
 &D;urh &d;a cweorne is getacnod se ymbhwyrft &d;isse worolde &amp; eac monna lifes &amp; hira gesuinces  &amp; &d;urh &d;one s&ae;grund hira ende &amp; se si&d;emes&d;a demm. 
 &D;onne bi&d; sio cweorn becierred &d;onne se monn bi&d; geendod; 
 &D;onne bi&d; sio micle cweorn becierred &d;onne &d;eos weorld bi&d; geendod. 
 Se &d;onne to halgum hade becym&d;  &amp; &d;onne mid yflum bisnum o&d;&d;e worda o&d;&d;e weorca o&d;re on won gebring&d;  betre him w&ae;re &d;&ae;t he on l&ae;ssan hade &amp; on eor&d;licum weorcum his lif geendode; 
 For&d;&ae;m gif he on &d;&ae;m wel de&d;  he h&ae;f&d; &d;&ae;s god lean  gif he yfle de&d;  l&ae;sse wite he &d;rowa&d; on helle  gif he ana &d;ider cym&d;  &d;onne he do  gif he o&d;erne mid him &d;ider bring&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;re byr&d;enne &d;&ae;s reccenddomes  &amp; hu he scyle eall earfo&d;u forsion  &amp; hu forht he sceal beon for &ae;lcre orsorgnesse. 
 For&d;on we &d;iss feawum wordum s&ae;don  &d;y we woldon gecy&d;an hu micel sio byr&d;en bi&d; &d;&ae;s lareowdomes  &d;yl&ae;s &ae;nig hine underfon durre &d;ara &d;e his unwier&d;e sie  &d;yl&ae;s hie &d;urh &d;a wilnunga &d;&ae;re woroldare underfo &d;one latteowdom &d;&ae;s forlores. 
 Sui&d;e medomlice Iacobus se apostol his stirde  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Bro&d;or ne beo eower to fela lareowa. 
 For&d;&ae;m se wealhstod self Godes &amp; monna  &d;&ae;t is Crist  fleah eor&d;rice to underfonne. 
 Se se &d;e ealne &d;one wisdom &d;ara uferrenna g&ae;sta oferstig&d; &amp; &ae;r worolde ricsode on hefenum  hit is awriten on &d;&ae;m godspelle  Iudeas comon &amp; woldon hine don niedenga to cyninge. 
 &D;a se H&ae;lend &d;&ae;t ongeat  &d;a becierde he hie &amp; gehydde hiene. 
 Hwa meahte ie&d; monnum r&ae;dan butan scylde  &d;onne se &d;e hi gescop? 
 Ne fleah he &d;y rice &d;y his &ae;nig monn bet wyr&d;e w&ae;re  ac he wolde us &d;a bisene astellan  &d;&ae;t we his to sui&d;e ne gitseden; 
 &amp; eac wolde for us &d;rowian. 
 He nolde beon cyning  &amp; his agnum willan he com to rode gealgan. 
 &D;a weor&d;mynde cynehades he fleah  &amp; &d;&ae;t wite &d;&ae;s frace&d;lecestan dea&d;es he geceas  for&d;am &d;&ae;tte we  &d;e his liomu sindon  leornedon &ae;t him &d;&ae;t we flugen &d;a oliccunga &d;isses middangeardes; 
 &amp; eac &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t we his ege &amp; his brogan us ne ondreden  &amp; for so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse &d;&ae;t we lufigen gesuinc  &amp; orsorgnesse we us ondr&ae;den  &amp; hi for&d;y forbugen. 
 For&d;am for &d;&ae;re orsorgnesse monn oft a&d;int on ofermettum  &amp; &d;a earfe&d;u &d;urh sar &amp; &d;urh sorge hiene gecl&ae;nsia&d; &amp; geea&d;meda&d;. 
 On &d;&ae;m gesundfulnessum &d;&ae;t mod wier&d; upahafen; 
 &amp; on &d;&ae;m earfe&d;um  &d;eah hit &ae;r upahafen w&ae;re  hit bi&d; geea&d;medd. 
 On &d;&ae;re gesundfulnesse mon forgiett his selfes; 
 On &d;&ae;m gesuincum he sceal hine selfne ge&d;encean  &d;eah he nylle. 
 On &d;&ae;re orsorgnesse oft &d;&ae;t he to gode gedyde he forlies&d;  on &d;&ae;m earfo&d;um oft &d;&ae;t he longe &ae;r to yfle gedyde  he gebett. 
 Sui&d;e oft monn bi&d; &d;&ae;re earfo&d;nesse lareowdome under&d;ieded  &d;eah he &ae;r nolde his lareowes &d;eawum &amp; larum bion. 
 Ac &d;eah hine &d;onne &d;a brocu getyn &amp; gel&ae;ren  sona  gif he on rice becym&d;  for &d;&ae;re weor&d;unge &d;&ae;s folces  he bi&d; on ofermettu awended  &amp; gewuna&d; to &d;&ae;m gielpe. 
 Sua sua Saul se cyning  &ae;res&d; he fleah &d;&ae;t rice  &amp; tealde hine selfne his sui&d;e unwier&d;ne. 
 Ac sona sua he &d;one anwald onfeng &d;&ae;s rices  he astag on ofermetto  &amp; hine bealg wi&d; &d;one ilcan Samuel &d;e hine &ae;r on &d;&ae;m rice gebrohte  &amp; hine to gehalgode  for&d;am&d;e he him s&ae;de beforan &d;am folce his un&d;eawas  &d;a he him &ae;r hiera &d;onces gestieran ne meahte; 
 &amp; &d;a he him from wolde  &d;a gefeng he hine  &amp; toslat his hr&ae;gl  &amp; hine geunarode. 
 Sua eac Dauit  &d;e folneah on eallum &d;ingum Gode licode  sona sua he &d;a byr&d;enne n&ae;fde sua monegra earfe&d;a  he w&ae;s mid ofermettum gewundad  &amp; &d;&ae;t sui&d;e w&ae;lhreowlice gecy&d;de on Urias sl&ae;ge his agenes holdes &d;egnes  for &d;&ae;re scamleaslecan gewilnunge his wifes. 
 Se ilca se monegum yfelum wi&d; hine selfne forworhtum &ae;r gearode  he wear&d; eft sua ungemetlice gr&ae;dig &d;&ae;s godan dea&t;es  butan &ae;lcre scylde &amp; &ae;lcre wi&d;erweardnesse wi&d; hine. 
 Se ilcan Dauid &d;e forb&ae;r &d;&ae;t he &d;one kyning ne yfelode  &d;e hine on sua heardum wr&ae;ce gebrohte  &amp; of his earde adr&ae;fde  &d;a he his wel geweald ahte on &d;&ae;m scr&ae;fe  he genom his lo&d;an &ae;nne l&ae;ppan to tacne &d;&ae;t he his geweald ahte  &amp; hine &d;eah for &d;am ealdan treowum forlet. 
 Se ilca Dauid miclum his agenes herges pleah  &amp; monigne forsende  &d;&ae;r he ymb his getreowne &d;egn unsynnigne sierede. 
 Sio scyld hine sui&d;e feorr of ealra haligra rime atuge  &d;&ae;r him eft &d;a gesuinc &amp; &d;a earfe&d;u ne gehulpen. 
 Ond hu oft sio bisgung &d;&ae;s rices &amp; &d;&ae;s recedomes toslit &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s recceres. 
 Sui&d;e oft gedrefe&d; &d;a heortan sio manigfealde giemen &d;&ae;s underfangenan lareowdomes  &amp; &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; on monig tod&ae;led  hit bi&d; on anes hw&ae;m &d;e unf&ae;stre  &amp; eac &d;e unyttre. 
 Bi &d;am cu&ae;&d; Salomonn se snottra: Sunu min  ne tod&ae;l &d;u on to fela &d;in mod  &amp; &d;in weorc endemes. 
 For&d;an oft &d;onne mon forl&ae;t &d;one ege &amp; &d;a f&ae;s&d;r&ae;dnesse &d;e he mid ryhte on him innan habban scolde  hine sp&ae;n&d; his mod to sui&d;e manegum unnyttum weorce. 
 He sorga&d; ymb &d;a  &amp; bi&d; &d;ara sui&d;e gemyndig  &amp; forgiett his selfes  &d;onne he sui&d;or his mod gebint to &d;am unnyttran weorcum &d;onne he &d;yrfe. 
 Him bi&d; sua sua &d;am menn &d;e bi&d; abisgod on f&ae;relde mid o&d;rum cierrum  o&d;&d;&ae;t he nat hwider he &ae;r wolde  ne ge&d;encan ne con hw&ae;t him losa&d; on &d;&ae;re g&ae;linge &d;e he &d;a hwile amierre&d;  &amp; hu sui&d;e he on &d;am gesynga&d;. 
 Ne wende na Ezechias Israhela kyning &d;&ae;t he gesyngade  &d;a he l&ae;dde &d;a &ae;ll&d;eodgan &ae;renddracan on his ma&d;mhus  &amp; him geiewde his goldhord. 
 Ac he onfunde &d;eah Godes ierre on &d;am hearme &d;e his bearne &ae;fter his dagum becom. 
 &amp; &d;eah he wende &d;&ae;t hit nan syn n&ae;re. 
 Oft &d;onne hw&ae;m gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t he hw&ae;t m&ae;rlices &amp; wundorlices gede&d;  &amp; his &d;onne wundria&d; &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde bio&d;  &amp; hine heriegea&d;  &d;onne ahef&d; he hine on his mode  &amp; his Deman ierre fullice to him gecig&d;  &d;eah &d;e he hit on yfelum weorcum ne geopenige. 
 Sua&d;eah mid &d;y selflice se Dema bi&d; genieded to &d;&ae;m ierre  &amp; se Dema se &d;e &d;&ae;t innge&d;onc eall wat  he eac &d;&ae;m innge&d;once dem&d;. 
 We magon monnum bemi&d;an urne ge&d;onc &amp; urne willan  ac we ne magon Gode. 
 Hw&ae;t se Babylonia cyning w&ae;s sui&d;e upahafen on his mode for his anwalde &amp; for his gelimpe  &d;a he f&ae;gnode &d;&ae;s miclan weorces &amp; f&ae;gernesse &d;&ae;rre ceastre  &amp; hine o&d;hof innan his ge&d;ohte eallum o&d;rum monnum  &amp; suigende he cw&ae;&d; on his mode: Hu ne is &d;is sio micle Babilon &d;e ic self atimbrede to kynestole &amp; to &d;rymme  me selfum to wlite &amp; wuldre  mid mine agne m&ae;gene &amp; strengo? 
 &D;a suigendan stefne sui&d;e hra&d;e se diegla Dema gehirde  &amp; him sui&d;e undeogollice gondwyrde mid &d;am witum &d;e he hit sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice wr&ae;c. 
 &D;a upahafenesse he arasode &amp; hie get&ae;lde  &d;a he hine ascead of &d;am woroldrice  &amp; hine gehwyrfde to ungesceadwisum neatum  &amp; sua awende mode he hine ge&d;iedde to feldgogendum deorum; 
 &amp; sua &d;y &d;earlan dome he forleas his mennisce. 
 Se ilca se &d;e wende &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re ofer ealle o&d;ere menn  him gebyrede &d;&ae;t he nyste self hw&ae;&d;er he monn w&ae;s. 
 Sua&d;eah  &d;eah ic nu &d;is recce  n&ae; t&ae;le ic na micel weorc ne ryhtne anwald  ac ic t&ae;le &d;&ae;t hine mon for&d;y upahebbe on his mode; 
 &amp; &d;a untrymnesse hiera heortan ic wolde getrymman &amp; gestiran &d;&ae;re wilnunge &d;&ae;m unmedemum  &d;&ae;t hiera nan ne durre gripan sua orsorglice on &d;&ae;t rice &amp; on &d;one lareowdom  &d;yl&ae;s &d;a gongen on suafrecne stige  &d;a &d;e ne magon uncwaciende gestondan on emnum felda. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m &d;e magon on ealdordome nytte beon on bisnum &amp; on cr&ae;ftum  &amp; &d;onne for hira agenre ie&d;nesse &d;&ae;t fleo&d;. 
 Ac monige siendun mid miclum giefum monegra cr&ae;fta &amp; m&ae;gene geweor&d;ode  for&d;on&d;e hie hie scoldon monegum t&ae;can  &amp; for o&d;erra monna &d;earfe onfo&d; &d;ylicca giefa. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hie gehealda&d; hira lichoman firenlusta cl&ae;nne; 
 O&d;er is &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; on f&ae;rh&ae;f&d;nesse strenge strange; 
 &D;ridde is &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; mid lara suetmettum gefylde; 
 Feor&d;e is &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; on &ae;lengum &d;ingum &amp; &ae;lcre longunge ge&d;yldige  &amp; on forebyrde ea&d;mode; 
 Fifte is &d;&ae;t hie habba&d; &d;a arodnesse &amp; &d;a bieldo &d;&ae;t hie magon anweald habban; 
 Siexte is &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; fremsume; 
 Siofo&d;e is &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; re&d;e &amp; str&ae;ce for ryhtwisnesse. 
 &D;a &d;e &d;onne &d;yllice beo&d;  &amp; him mon suelcne folga&d; beode&d;  &amp; hie him wi&d;saca&d;  oft him gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t hie weor&d;a&d; bereafod &d;ara giefa &d;e him God for monigra monna &d;ingum geaf  n&ae;s for hiera anra. 
 &D;onne hie synderlice &d;encea&d; hu hie selfe scylen fullfremodeste weor&d;an  &amp; ne giema&d; to hwon o&d;erra monna wise weor&d;e  mid &d;y hi bereafia&d; hie selfe &d;ara goda &d;e hie wilnia&d; synderlice habban. 
 Be suelcum monnum Crist on his godspelle cu&ae;&d;: Ne scyle nan mon bl&ae;cern &ae;lan under mittan. 
 &amp; eft he cu&ae;&d; to Petre &d;&ae;m apostole: Petrus lufastu me? 
 He cu&ae;&d;: &d;u wast &d;&ae;t ic &d;e lufige. 
 &amp; &d;a cu&ae;&d; Dryhten: Fed &d;onne min sceap  gif &d;u me lufige. 
 Gif &d;onne seo feding &d;ara sceapa bi&d; &d;&ae;re lufan tacen  hwi forcwi&d; &d;onne se &d;e him God suelce cr&ae;ftas gief&d; &d;&ae;t he ne fede his heorde  buton he cue&d;an wielle &d;&ae;t he ne lufige &d;one Hlaford &amp; &d;one hean Hierde eallra gesceafta? 
 Be &d;am Paulus se apostol cu&ae;&d;: Gif Crist for us eallum dead w&ae;s  &d;onne weor&d;a&d; ealle menn deade. 
 Hw&ae;t is &d;onne betere &d;a hwile &d;e we libben  &d;onne we ures fl&ae;sces lustum ne libben  ac &d;&ae;s bebodum &d;e for us dead w&ae;s &amp; eft aras? 
 Be &d;am cu&ae;&d; Moyses: Gif hwa gefare &amp; nan bearn ne gestriene  gif he bro&d;or l&ae;fe  fo se to his wife. 
 Gif he &d;onne bearn &d;&ae;rbig gestriene  &d;onne cenne he &d;&ae;t &d;am gefarenan bre&d;er &d;e hie &ae;r ahte. 
 Gif he &d;onne &d;&ae;t wif wille forsacan  &d;onne hr&ae;ce hio him on &d;&ae;t nebb foran  &amp; his m&ae;gas hine anscogen o&d;re fet  &d;&ae;t mon m&ae;ge si&d;&d;an hatan his tun &d;&ae;s anscodan tun. 
 &D;is w&ae;s ryht dom on &d;&ae;re ealdan &ae;  &amp; is nu us to bispelle. 
 Se &ae;r gefarena bro&d;or getacna&d; Crist. 
 He hine &ae;tiede &ae;fter &d;&ae;re &ae;riste  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Fara&d; &amp; cy&d;a&d; minum bro&d;rum &d;&ae;t hie cumen to Galileum; 
 &D;&ae;r hie me geseo&d;. 
 He gefor suelce he butan bearnum gefore  for&d;on he n&ae;fde gefylled &d;agiet &d;one rim his gecorenra. 
 Sua sua &d;&ae;s gefarenan bro&d;or wif on &d;&ae;re ealdan &ae; w&ae;s geboden &d;&ae;m lifiendan bre&d;er to onfonne  sua is cynn &d;&ae;t sio giemen &d;&ae;re halgan ciricean  &d;&ae;t is Cristes folces gesomnung  sie &d;am beboden &d;e hie wel ofer m&ae;ge  &amp; hiere wel r&ae;dan cunne. 
 Gif hire &d;onne se wi&d;sace  &d;onne is cynn &d;&ae;t him spiwe &d;&ae;t wif on &d;&ae;t nebb  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hine t&ae;le &d;&ae;s folces gesomnung  emne suelce hie him on &d;&ae;t nebb sp&ae;ten  for&d;on&d;e he nyle giefan &d;&ae;t him God geaf  &amp; helpan &d;&ae;s folces mid &d;am &d;e he his healp. 
 Sua is cynn &d;&ae;t sio halige gesomnung t&ae;le &ae;lces &d;ara god &d;e hit him anum wile to gode habban  &amp; nyle o&d;era mid helpan. 
 Se bi&d; eac mid ryhte o&d;re fet anscod  &amp; hine mon scyle on bismer hatan se anscoda. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Crist on his gospelle: Sceawia&d; iowre fet  &d;&ae;t ge sien gearwe to ganganne on sibbe weg &ae;fter minra boca bebodum. 
 Gief we &d;onne habba&d; sua micle sorge &amp; sua micle gieman urra niehstena sua sua ure selfra  &d;onne h&ae;bbe we begen fet gescode sui&d;e unt&ae;llice; 
 Gif we &d;onne agiemeleasia&d; urra niehstena &d;earfa  &amp; &d;encea&d; ymbe ure synderlice  &d;onne bi&d; us sui&d;e fraco&d;lice o&d;er fot unscod. 
 Monige menn siendon  sua sua we &ae;r cu&ae;don  &d;e beo&d; geweor&d;ode mid miclum &amp; mid monegum Godes giefum  &amp; &d;onne beo&d; on&ae;lede mid &d;&ae;re gierninge &d;ara smeaunga Godes wisdomes anes  &amp; fleo&d; &d;onne &d;a nyttwyr&d;an hiersumnesse &d;&ae;re lare  &amp; nylla&d; &d;&ae;s &d;encean hu hie m&ae;gen nyttweor&d;uste bion hiera niehstum  ac lufia&d; diegla stowa  &amp; fleo&d; monna onsiena. 
 Gif him &d;onne God ryhtlice &amp; str&ae;clice deman wile  &amp; he him for his mildheortnesse ne ara&d;  &d;onne beo&d; hie sua monegum scyldum scyldige sua hie manegra un&d;eawa gestiran meahton mid hiora larum &amp; bisenum  gif hi ongemong monnum beon wolden. 
 Hw&ae;t &d;encea&d; &d;a &d;e on suelcum weorcum scina&d;  &amp; magon hiera niehstum sua nytte beon  hwy hie &d;ara geearnunga &amp; diegelnesse &amp; anette bet truwigen &d;onne &d;&ae;re hu hie o&d;erra monna m&ae;st gehelpen? 
 Hw&ae;t se ancenneda Godes sunu of his f&ae;der bosme w&ae;s ferende to urre andweardnesse &d;&ae;t he ure gehulpe. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m &d;e for ea&d;modnesse fleo&d; &d;a byr&d;enne &d;&ae;s lareowdomes  &d;onne hie beo&d; ryhtlice ea&d;mode &d;onne hie ne winna&d; wi&d; &d;one godcundan dom. 
 &D;onne siendon monige &d;e fleo&d; for ea&d;modnesse anre  for&d;on hie noldon &d;&ae;t hie mon ahofe ofer &d;a &d;e him beteran &d;yncea&d; &d;onne hie selfe. 
 Nis &d;&ae;s &d;onne nan tweo  gif suelc ea&d;modnes bi&d; mid o&d;rum godum &d;eawum begyrded  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t bi&d; beforan Godes eagum so&d; ea&d;modness  &d;onne he for nanre anwielnesse ne wi&d;cui&d; &d;am nyttan weorcum &d;e him mon beode&d; to underfonne. 
 Ne bi&d; &d;&ae;t na so&d; ea&d;modnes  gif mon ongiett &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t Godes willa sie &d;&ae;t he ofer o&d;re beon scyle  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne wi&d;sace  ac beo under&d;ieded Godes willan &amp; his dome  &amp; forl&ae;te &d;a uncyste &d;&ae;re anwielnesse. 
 &D;onne he oferst&ae;led bi&d;  &amp; him gereaht bi&d; &d;&ae;t he o&d;rum m&ae;g nytt bion on &d;am &d;e him mon &d;onne bebeode&d;  mid his mode he hit sceal fleon &amp; &d;eah for hiersumnesse he hit sceal underfon. 
 &D;&ae;tte oft &d;&ae;s lareowdomes &d;enung bi&d; swi&d;e unt&ae;lwyr&d;lice gewilnad  &amp; eac swi&d;e unt&ae;lwier&d;lice monige beo&d; to geniedde. 
 &T;eahhw&ae;&d;re monige wilnia&d; folgo&d;es &amp; ealdordomes sui&d;e unt&ae;lwier&d;lice  &amp; monige beo&d; togeniedde eac sui&d;e unt&ae;lwier&d;lice. 
 &D;&ae;t we magon sueotole ongietan  gif we ge&d;encea&d; &d;a twegen witgan &d;e God wolde sendan to l&ae;ranne. 
 O&d;er hiene his selfes willum gebead to &d;&ae;re lare &amp; to &d;&ae;m f&ae;relte. 
 O&d;er for &d;&ae;m ege  &d;e he ondred &d;&ae;t he hit sua medomlice don ne meahte  him wi&d;soc. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;s Heremias. 
 &D;a he hine sendan wolde  &d;a b&ae;d he ea&d;modlice &d;&ae;t he hiene ne sende &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Eala eala eala Dryhten  ic eom cnioht; 
 Hw&ae;t conn ic sprecan? 
 Ac Essaias  &d;a Dryhten acsode hwone he sendan meahte  &d;a cu&ae;&d; Essaias: Ic eom gearo; 
 Send me. 
 Loca nu hu ungelic spr&ae;c eode of &d;issa tuega monna mu&d;e. 
 Ac hio w&ae;s of sui&d;e gelicum willan  for&d;on hio aweoll of anum wille; 
 &D;eah heo an tu tefleowe  &d;eah w&ae;s sio &ae;spryng sio so&d;e lufu. 
 Ymb &d;a we habba&d; tua bebodu: an is &d;&ae;t we lufigen God  o&d;er &d;&ae;t we lufien ure niehstan. 
 For &d;&ae;re lufan Essaias wilnode hu he nyttos&d; meahte beon his nihstum on &d;ys eor&d;lican life  &amp; for&d;on he wilnode &d;&ae;re &d;egnunga &d;&ae;s lariowdomes. 
 Hieremias &d;onne wilnode singallice hine ge&d;iedan to &d;&ae;re lufan his Scippendes  &amp; for&d;am he forcw&ae;&d;  &amp; nolde &d;&ae;t hine mon sende to l&ae;ranne. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t he unt&ae;lwyr&d;lice ondred to underfonne  &d;&ae;t ilce se o&d;er swi&d;e hergeondlice gewilnode. 
 O&d;er ondred &d;&ae;t he forlure sprecende &d;a gestrion &d;e he on &d;&ae;re swigean ge&d;encan meahte; 
 O&d;er ondred &d;&ae;t he ongeate on his swygean &d;&ae;t he sumne hearm geswigode &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r he freme gecleopian meahte  gif he ymb &d;&ae;t geornlice swunce. 
 Ac we sculon swi&d;e smealice &d;issa &ae;g&d;er under&d;encean  for&d;on&d;e se &d;e &d;&ae;r wi&d;cw&ae;&d;  na fullice ne wi&d;cw&ae;&d;  &amp; se se &d;e wolde &d;&ae;t hine mon sende  he geseah &ae;r hine cl&ae;nsian &d;urh &d;a colu &d;&ae;s alteres  &d;yl&ae;s &ae;nig uncl&ae;nsod dorste on swa micelne haligdom fon &d;&ae;re cl&ae;nan &d;egnenga &d;&ae;s sacerdhades  o&d;&d;e eft &ae;nig durre on ea&d;modnesse hiwe hit ofermodlice forcwe&d;an  swelce he licette ea&d;metto  &amp; doo &d;eah for gilpe  gif hine gecist sio uplice gifu. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hit swa earfo&d;e is &ae;negum menn to witanne hwonne he gecl&ae;nsod sie  he m&ae;g &d;y orsorglicor forbugan &d;a &d;egnunga; 
 Ond n&ae;s swa&d;eah to anwillice ne forbuge he  swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don  &d;onne he ongiete &d;one ufancundan willan &d;&ae;t he hit don scyle. 
 &AE;g&d;er &d;issa gefylde Moyses &d;a he wi&d;soc swa miclum ealdordome. 
 &AE;g&d;er ge he wolde ge he nolde  &amp; &d;eah for ea&d;modnesse ge&d;afode. 
 We witon &d;&ae;t he n&ae;re ea&d;mod  gif he underfenge &d;one ealdordom swelces unrimfolces buton ege; 
 &amp; eft he w&ae;re ofermod  gif he wi&d;cw&ae;de &d;&ae;t he n&ae;re under&d;idd his Scippende. 
 Ac &ae;g&d;er &d;issa he dyde for ea&d;modnesse &amp; for under&d;idednesse. 
 He sceawode hine selfne  &amp; pinsode  &d;a &d;a him &d;uhte &d;&ae;t he hit doon ne meahte  &amp; swa&d;eah ge&d;afode  for&d;am&d;e he getruwode &d;&ae;s m&ae;gene &d;e hit him bebead. 
 Hw&ae;t se haliga wer ongeat &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde Godes fultom  &amp; swa&d;eah ondred &d;&ae;t he underfenge &d;one lattiowdom &d;&ae;s folces  &amp; nu him ne ondr&ae;da&d; &d;a dolan for hiera agnum scyldum &d;&ae;t hie sien ofer o&d;re  &amp; ne magon him gegaderian on &d;yllicum biwene hu micel synn &amp; hu micel frecennes hit bi&d;. 
 God selfa tyhte Moyses on &d;one folgo&d;  swa&d;eah he him ondred; 
 Ond nu fandia&d; swelce wr&ae;ccan &amp; teo&d; to  woldon underfon &d;one weor&d;scipe &amp; eac &d;a byr&d;enne; 
 &amp; &d;a &d;e beo&d; mid hira agnum byr&d;ennum of&d;rycte &d;&ae;t hie ne magon gestondan  hie willa&d; lustlice underfon o&d;erra monna  ond unniedige hie underluta&d; mid hira sculdrum o&d;erra byr&d;enna toeacan hiera agnum; 
 He ne m&ae;g his agne aberan  &amp; wolde &d;eah maran habban. 
 Be &d;&ae;m &d;e wilna&d; biscephad to underfonne  hu hie gegripa&d; &d;one cwide &d;&ae;s apostoles Paules hiora gitsunge to fultome. 
 Ac &d;a &d;e willa&d; gripan on swelcne folga&d; for hiera gitsunge hie do&d; him to leafe &d;one cwide &d;e sanctus Paulus cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e biscephade gewilna&d;  god weorc he gewilna&d;. 
 Gif he hit &d;a herede &amp; on tyhte  eft he stierde &d;&ae;re gewilnunge &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Biscepe gedafna&d; &d;&ae;t he sie t&ae;lleas. 
 &D;&ae;rbufan is geteald hwelc he beon sceal  gif he unt&ae;lwier&d;e bi&d;. 
 Mid o&d;rum worde he hierte  mid o&d;rum he bregde  swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Ic herige &d;&ae;t ge seca&d;  ac leornia&d; &d;&ae;t ge witen hw&ae;t hit sie  ac gif ge agiemeleasia&d; &d;&ae;t ge ameten eow selfe hwelce ge sien  sua eow on hierran folgo&d;e ahebba&d;  swa ge sweotolran &amp; widm&ae;rran gedo&d; eowre t&ae;lweor&d;licnesse. 
 Sua se micla cr&ae;ftiga hiertende toscyf&d;  &amp; egesiende stier&d; ofermetta mid &d;&ae;re t&ae;linge his hieremonnum  &d;&ae;t he hie gebringe on life. 
 Eac is to ge&d;encanne &d;&ae;t on &d;a tiid &d;e se biscephad swa gehiered w&ae;s  sua hwelc swa hine underfeng  he underfeng martyrdom. 
 On &d;a tiid w&ae;s to herigeanne &d;&ae;t mon wilnode biscephades  &d;a &d;e nan twio n&ae;s &d;&ae;t he &d;urh &d;one sceolde cuman to hefegum martyrdome. 
 &D;&ae;t is to tacne &d;&ae;t mon endebyr&d;lice &d;one biscepdom healde  &d;&ae;t he hine on godum weorcum geendige. 
 For&d;on hit is gecweden: Se &d;e biscephad gewilna&d;  god weorc he gewilna&d;. 
 Se &d;onne for &d;&ae;re gewilnunge swelcra weorca biscopdom ne sec&d;  he bi&d; &d;onne him self gewita &d;&ae;t he wilna&d; him selfum gielpes; 
 Ne de&d; he &d;onne &d;&ae;t an yfel &d;&ae;t he ne lufa&d; &d;a halgan &d;egnunga  ac eallinga he hie forsieh&d;; 
 Ond &d;onne he funda&d; to &d;&ae;m weor&d;scipe &d;&ae;s folgo&d;es  his mod bi&d; afedd mid &d;&ae;re smeaunga &d;&ae;re wilnunga o&d;erra monna hiernesse &amp; his selfes upah&ae;fenesse  &amp; f&ae;gena&d; &d;&ae;s hu hie ne mon scyle herigean. 
 Ahef&d; &d;onne his heortan for&d;y  &amp; for &d;&ae;re genyhte &d;&ae;s flowendan welan he blissa&d;. 
 He licet ea&d;modnesse  &amp; sec&d; mid &d;am &d;isses middangeardes gestreon. 
 On &d;&ae;m hiewe &d;e he sceolde his gielpes stieran on &d;&ae;m he his strien&d;. 
 Mid &d;y &d;e he sceolde his gestreon toweorpan  mid &d;y he hie gadra&d;. 
 &D;onne &d;&ae;t mod &d;ence&d; gegripan him to upahefenesse &d;a ea&d;modnesse  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he utan eowa&d; innan he hit anwent. 
 Hu &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte wilna&d; for o&d;re beon lih&d; him selfum  &d;onne hit &d;enc&d; fela godra weorca to wyrcanne  &amp; &d;&ae;t licett o&d;rum monnum  gif he worldare h&ae;bbe  &amp; wile hit &d;onne oferhebban  si&d;&d;an he hie h&ae;f&d;.

 Ac on uteweardum his mode he lieh&d; him selfum ymbe hine selfne bie &d;&ae;m godum weorcum; 
 Licet &d;&ae;t he lufige &d;&ae;t he ne lufa&d;: &d;isses middangeardes gilp he lufa&d;  &amp; he licett swelce he &d;one onscunige  &amp; hine him ondr&ae;de. 
 &D;onne he wilna&d; on his mode &d;&ae;t he sciele ricsian he bi&d; swi&d;e forht &amp; swi&d;e behealden; 
 &D;onne he h&ae;f&d; &d;&ae;t he habban wolde  he bi&d; swi&d;e &d;riste. 
 &D;onne he to funda&d;  he ondr&ae;t &d;&ae;t he ne mote to cuman  ond sona swa he to &d;&ae;re are cym&d;  swa &d;ync&d; him &d;&ae;t se hie him niedscylde sceolde se se hie him sealde  &amp; bryc&d; &d;&ae;re godcundan are woruldcundlice   &amp; forgitt swi&d;e hr&ae;&d;e &d;&ae;t he &ae;r &ae;f&ae;stlices ge&d;ohte.

 Ac sona beo&d; &d;&ae;s modes eagan eft gewende to &d;&ae;m weorcum &d;e hit &ae;r worhte. 
 Ac &d;ence &ae;lc mon &ae;r hu nytwyr&d;e he sie &amp; hu gehiersum &d;&ae;m &d;e he &d;onne mid ryhte hieran scyle on &d;am &d;e he &d;onne de&d;.
