 He sceal bion str&ae;c wi&d; &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;r agylta&d;  ond for ryhtwisnesse he sceal habban andan to hira yfele; 
 Ond &d;eah for &d;ara bisgunge ne sie his giemen na &d;y l&ae;sse ymb &d;a gehirsuman; 
 Ne eac for hira lufan geornfulnesse ne forl&ae;te he &d;a ungehirsuman. 
 Ac &d;is &d;&ae;t we nu feam wordum arimdon we willa&d; hwene rumedlicor her&ae;fter areccean. 
 Hu se lareow sceal bion cl&ae;ne on his mode. 
 Se reccere sceal bion simle cl&ae;ne on his ge&d;ohte  &d;&ae;tte nan uncl&ae;nnes hine ne besmite &d;onne he &d;a &d;egnunga underfeh&d;  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge adrygean of o&d;ra monna heortan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;ron fules sie. 
 Hit is &d;earf &d;&ae;t sio hond sie &ae;r gecl&ae;nsad &d;e wille &d;&ae;t fenn of o&d;erre a&d;ierran; 
 Gif sio &d;onne bi&d; eac fennegu  &d;onne is wen &d;&ae;t hio &d;a o&d;re wiers besmite gif hio hire anhrin&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s &d;urh &d;one witgan gecueden: Doo&d; eow cl&ae;ne  ge &d;e bera&d; Godes fatu. 
 &D;a &d;onne bera&d; Godes fatu  &d;a &d;e o&d;erra monna saula underfoo&d; to l&ae;danne on &d;a treowa hira agenra gearnunga to &d;&ae;m innemestan halignessum. 
 Ge&d;encen hie &d;onne betwuh him selfum hu sui&d;e hie sculon beon gecl&ae;nsode &d;a &d;e bera&d; on hira greadum &d;a a libbendan fatu to &d;&ae;m ecean temple on hira agenne borg. 
 For&d;y w&ae;s &d;urh &d;a halgan stemne beboden &d;&ae;tte on Arones breostum sceolde beon awriten sio racu &d;&ae;s domes on &d;&ae;m hr&ae;gle &d;e mon h&ae;t rationale  &amp; mid noslum gebunden  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte sio oferflownes &d;ara ge&d;ohta ne meahte ofsittan &d;&ae;s sacerdes heortan  ac hio sciolde beon gebunden mid &d;&ae;re ilcan race  &d;&ae;tte he ne &d;ohte nawuht ungesceadwislices ne ungenetlices. 
 For&d;&ae;m he bi&d; gesett to bisene o&d;rum monnum  simle he sceal &ae;tiewan on his lifes gest&ae;&d;&d;ignesse hu micle gesceadwisnesse he bere on his breostum. 
 On &d;&ae;m selfan hr&ae;gle  &d;e he on his breostum w&ae;g  w&ae;s eac awriten &d;a naman &d;ara twelf heahf&ae;dera. 
 &D;onne bir&d; se sacerd sui&d;e unt&ae;llice awriten &d;ara f&ae;dra naman on his breostum  &d;onne he singallice ge&d;enc&d; hiera lifes bisene. 
 &D;onne st&ae;p&d; se sacerd sui&d;e t&ae;lleaslice on &d;one weg  &d;onne he &d;a bisene &d;ara for&d;gefarenra federa geornlice &amp; unablinnendlice sceawa&d;  &amp; on &d;&ae;t su&ae;&d; &d;ara haligra singallice winna&d; to spyriganne  &amp; unaliefde ge&d;ohtas of&d;ryc&d;  &d;yl&ae;s he ofer &d;one &d;erscold his endebyrdnesse st&ae;ppe. 
 Sui&d;e ryhte &d;&ae;t hr&ae;gl is gehaten  &d;&ae;t se sacerd beran sceolde &d;&ae;s domes racu  for&d;am se sacerd scolde &amp; git sceal simle smealice ge&d;encean &d;&ae;t he cunne god &amp; yfel tosceadan  ond si&d;&d;an geornlice ge&d;ence hu he gehwelcne l&ae;ran scyle &amp; hwonne  &amp; hw&ae;t him gecopust sie  &amp; nowuht him selfum synderlice wilnige  ac his niehstena god he sceal tellan him selfum. 
 Be &d;am is awriten &d;&ae;t mon sceolde writan on &d;&ae;m hr&ae;gle &d;e Aron b&ae;r on his breostum  &d;onne he inneode beforan Gode  &d;a lare &amp; &d;a domas &amp; &d;a so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse. 
 &D;a domas he b&ae;r on his breostum beforan Gode Israhela bearna simle. 
 Sua sceal se sacerd giet simle beran &d;a domas awritene on his breostum Israhela bearna  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hie &d;ara &d;ing &d;e him under&d;iodde bio&d; for &d;&ae;m ege anum &d;&ae;s innecundan deman inweardlice undersece  &d;&ae;tte sio mennisce oliccung for nanum freondscipe &d;&ae;rto ne gemencge  for&d;on he bi&d; to Cristes bisene &amp; to his anlicnesse &d;&ae;r aset. 
 &amp; &d;eah for &d;&ae;re geornfulnesse &d;&ae;re ryhtinge ne sie he to hr&ae;d ne to sti&d; to &d;&ae;re wrace  ac &d;onne he bi&d; ongieten &ae;fstig wi&d; o&d;ra monna yfelu  anscunige he eac his agenu  &d;yl&ae;s &d;a smyltnesse &d;&ae;s domes gewemme o&d;&d;e se dierna &ae;fst o&d;&d;e to hr&ae;d ierre. 
 Ac gif he ge&d;enc&d; &d;one ege &d;&ae;s deman &d;e ofer eall sitt  &d;onne ne stier&d; he no his hieremonnum butan miclum ege. 
 Ac se ege &d;onne he geea&d;med &d;&ae;t mod he hit gecl&ae;nsa&d;  &d;yl&ae;s sio gedyrstignes his modes hine to uppahebbe  o&d;&d;e &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sces lus&d;fulnes hiene besmite  o&d;&d;e &d;urh &d;a wilnunga &d;issa eor&d;cundlicra &d;inga &d;&ae;t mod a&d;istrige se forhwierfeda gewuna gemalicnesse  sio oft &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s recceres astyre&d;. 
 Ac hit is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t mon hire sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice wi&d;bregde  &d;yl&ae;s sio scyld &d;e hiene &d;urh scienesse costa&d; for his luste &amp; for his wacmodnesse hine ofersui&d;e; 
 For&d;on gif hio ne bi&d; hr&ae;dlice aweg adrifen  he bi&d; ofsl&ae;gen mid &d;&ae;m sueorde &d;&ae;re ge&d;afunge. 
 Hu se lareow sceal beon on his weorcum fyrmest. 
 Se lareow sceal bion on his weorcum healic  &d;&ae;t he on his life gecy&d;e lifes weg his hieremonnum  &d;&ae;tte sio hiord se &d;e folga&d; &d;&ae;m wordum &amp; &d;&ae;m &d;eawum &d;&ae;s hierdes  &d;&ae;tte sio heord m&ae;ge bet gan &ae;fter his &d;eawum &d;onne &ae;fter his wordum. 
 He bi&d; genied mid &d;&ae;m folgo&d;e &d;&ae;t he sceal healice sprecan; 
 Ge&d;ence he &d;onne &d;&ae;t him is efnmicel nied  si&d;&d;an he hit gesprecen h&ae;f&d;  &d;&ae;t he eac sua doo sua sua he l&ae;r&d;  for&d;on sio stefn &d;&ae;s lariowes micle &d;e ie&d;elicor &d;urhf&ae;r&d; &d;a heortan &d;&ae;s gehirendes  gif he mid his &d;eawum hi &d;&ae;ron gef&ae;s&d;na&d;; 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he sprecende bebiet &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t wyrcende o&d;iewe  &d;&ae;t hit &d;urh &d;one fultum sie for&d;genge. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh &d;one witgan: &d;u &d;e wilt godspellian Sion  astig ofer heane munt. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte se sceal  se &d;e wile brucan &d;ara godcundra &d;inga &amp; &d;ara hefonlicra lara  forl&ae;tan &d;as ni&d;erlican &amp; &d;as eor&d;lecan weorc  for&d;am he bi&d; gesewen standende on &d;am hrofe godcundra &d;inga. 
 Sua micle he m&ae;g ie&d; his hieremenn geteon to beteran  &amp; he bi&d; sua micle sel gehiered sua he ufor gestent on his lifes geearnungum. 
 For&d;am bebiet sio halige &ae; &d;&ae;t se sacerd scyle onfon &d;one sui&d;ran bogh &ae;t &d;&ae;re offrunge  &amp; se sceolde bion asyndred from &d;&ae;m odrum fl&ae;sce. 
 &D;&ae;t &d;onne tacna&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;s sacerdes weorc sculon beon asyndred from o&d;erra monna weorcum. 
 Nalles na &d;&ae;t an &d;&ae;t he god doo gemang o&d;rum monnum  ac eac synderlice sua su&ae; he on &d;ync&d;um bi&d; fur&d;ur &d;onne o&d;re  &d;&ae;t he eac sie on his weorcum &amp; &d;eawum sua micle fur&d;ur. 
 Eac him mon scolde sellan &d;a breos&d; &d;&ae;s neates toeacan &d;&ae;m boge  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he geleornige &d;&ae;t he selle Gode his agne breos&d;  &d;&ae;t is his innge&d;onc; 
 Nalles na &d;&ae;t an &d;&ae;t he on his breostum &d;ence &d;&ae;tte ryht sie  ac eac &d;a spone &d;e his &d;eawa giema&d; to &d;&ae;m illcan mid his godum biesenum. 
 Ne wilnige he nanes eor&d;lices ofer &d;&ae;t  ne he him ne ondr&ae;de nanne eor&d;licne ege &d;yses andweardan lifes  ac ge&d;ence he &d;one inncundan ege Godes  &amp; forsio &ae;lce olicunge &d;isses middangeardes  &amp; eac his ege for &d;&ae;re wynsuman suetnesse Godes. 
 For&d;on &d;urh &d;a uplecan stefne w&ae;s beboden on &d;&ae;re &ae; &d;&ae;t se sacerd scolde beon f&ae;ste bew&ae;fed on b&ae;m sculdrum mid &d;&ae;m m&ae;ssehr&ae;gle. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he bio simle gestrymed &amp; gefr&ae;twod wi&d; &ae;lce frecenesse ge g&ae;stlice ge mennisclice &amp; wi&d; &ae;lce orsorgnesse besuapen mid &d;yssum m&ae;genum  sua sua Paulus cu&ae;&d;: Ga&d; ge gew&ae;pnode &ae;g&d;er ge on &d;a sui&d;ran hond  ge on &d;a winstran mid &d;&ae;m w&ae;pnum ryhtwisnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne he higa&d; to &d;&ae;m godcundum &d;ingum anum  &d;&ae;t he ne &d;yrfe an nane healfe anbugan to nanum fullicum &amp; synlicum luste  ne eac ne &d;yrfe bion to upah&ae;fen for nanum wlencum ne for nanre orsorgnesse  ne hine ne gedrefe nan wuht wi&d;erweardes  ne hine ne geloccige nan oliccung to hiere willan  ne hine ne ge&d;rysce nan wi&d;ermodnes to ormodnesse. 
 Gif &d;onne mid nanum &d;issa ne bi&d; onw&ae;ced his innge&d;onc  &d;onne bi&d; hit swutul &d;&ae;t he bi&d; sui&d;e gerisenlice besuapen mid swi&d;e wlitige oferbr&ae;delse on b&ae;m sculdrum. 
 &D;&ae;t hr&ae;gl w&ae;s beboden &d;&ae;t scolde bion geworht of purpuran &amp; of tweobleom derodine &amp; of twispunnenum twine linenum &amp; gerenod mid golde &amp; mid &d;&ae;m stane iacincta  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t w&ae;re getacnod on hu mislecum &amp; on hu monigfaldum m&ae;genum se sacerd scolde scinan beforan Gode  mannum to biesene. 
 &AE;res&d; alra glengea &amp; ymes&d; scolde scinan gold on his hr&ae;gle. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte on his mode scine ealra &d;inga fyrmes&d; ongit wisdomes. 
 Toeacan &d;&ae;m golde ealra glenga fyrmes&d; on his hr&ae;gle w&ae;s beboden &d;&ae;t scolde bion se giem iacinctus  se is lyfte onlicus&d; on hiwe. 
 Se &d;onne tacna&d; &d;&ae;t eall &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;s sacerdes ondgit &d;urhfaran m&ae;ge  sie ymb &d;a hefonlican lufan  n&ae;s ymbe idelne gilp  &d;yl&ae;s him losige &d;&ae;t heofenlice ondgit  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he sie geh&ae;fted mid &d;&ae;m luste his selfes heringe. 
 Eac &d;&ae;m golde &amp; &d;&ae;m line w&ae;s ongemang purpura  &d;&ae;t is cynelic hr&ae;gl  for&d;&ae;m hit tacna&d; kynelicne anwald. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ge&d;ence se sacerd  &d;onne he o&d;re men healice l&ae;r&d;  &d;&ae;t he eac on him selfum healice of&d;rysce &d;a lustas his un&d;eawa  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he kynelic hr&ae;gl h&ae;f&d;  &d;&ae;t he eac sie kyning ofer his agne un&d;eawas  &amp; &d;a cynelican ofersui&d;e; 
 &amp; ge&d;ence he simle sie sua &ae;&d;ele sua un&ae;&d;ele su&ae;&d;er he sie &d;a &ae;&d;elu &d;&ae;re &ae;fterran acennesse  &d;&ae;t is on &d;&ae;m fulluhte  &amp; simle atiewe on his &d;eawum &d;a &d;ing &d;e he &d;&ae;r Gode gehet  &amp; &d;a &d;eawas &d;e him mon &d;&ae;r bebead. 
 Be &d;&ae;m &ae;&d;elum &d;&ae;s g&ae;stes Petrus cu&ae;&d;: Ge sint acoren kynn Gode &amp; cynelices preosthades. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m anwalde  &d;e we sculon ure un&d;eawas mid ofercuman  we magon beon getrymede mid Iohannes cuide &d;&ae;s godspelleres  &d;e he cu&ae;&d;: &d;a &d;e hine onfengon he salde him anwald &d;&ae;t hie meahton beon Godes bearn. 
 &D;a medomnesse &d;&ae;re strengio se salmscop ongeat  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Dryhten  sui&d;e sui&d;e sint geweor&d;ode mid me &d;ine friend  &amp; sui&d;e is gestrangod hiera ealdordom; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;&ae;t mod &d;inra haligra bi&d; a&d;ened sui&d;e healice &amp; sui&d;e stranglice to &d;e  &d;onne &d;onne o&d;rum monnum &d;ync&d; &d;&ae;t hie m&ae;stne demm &amp; m&ae;ste scande &d;rowigen  &amp; hie forsewenuste bio&d; for worulde. 
 On &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gle w&ae;s toeacan golde &amp; iacinc&d;e &amp; purpuran  dyrodine twegera bleo. 
 &D;&ae;t tacna&d; &d;&ae;tte eal &d;a god &amp; &d;a m&ae;genu &d;e heo do&d; beon gewlitegode mid &d;&ae;re lufan Godes &amp; monna beforan &d;&ae;m eagum &d;&ae;s ecean Deman  &d;&ae;tte se spearca &d;ara godra weorca &d;e her tuincla&d; beforan mannum  bierne healice licge on &d;&ae;re inncundan lufan beforan &d;&ae;m dieglan Deman. 
 Sio lufu &d;onne hio lufa&d; &ae;tsomne &ae;g&d;er ge God ge his niehstan  hio scin&d; sui&d;e smicere on tw&ae;m bleom sua sua twegea bleo godwebb. 
 Se &d;onne se &d;e sua higa&d; ealneweg to andweardnesse his scippendes  &amp; agiemeleasa&d; &d;a giemene his nihstena  o&d;&d;e eft sua singallice folga&d; &d;&ae;re giemenne his niehstena  &d;&ae;t he agiemeleasa&d; &d;a godcundan lufe  &d;onne h&ae;f&d; he anforl&ae;ten &d;&ae;t twegea bleo godwebb &d;&ae;t he habban sceolde on &d;&ae;m halgan hr&ae;gle  gif he au&d;er &d;issa forl&ae;t. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; a&d;ened on &d;a lufan &ae;g&d;er ge Godes ge his niehstena  ne bi&d; hit &d;onne nohtes hwon buton forh&ae;fdnesse anre  &d;&ae;t he his lichoman suence &amp; hl&ae;nige. 
 For&d;on is toeacan &d;&ae;m twiblion godwebbe &d;&ae;t scyle beon twi&d;r&ae;wen twin on &d;&ae;m m&ae;ssegierelan. 
 Of &d;&ae;re eor&d;an cyme&d; &d;&ae;t fleax  &d;&ae;t bi&d; hwites hiwes. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g &d;onne elles beon getacnod &d;urh &d;&ae;t fleax butan lichoman cl&ae;nnes  sio sceal scinan of cl&ae;nre heortan? 
 For&d;&ae;m bi&d; gef&ae;s&d;nod &d;&ae;t ge&d;r&ae;wene twin to &d;&ae;m wlite &d;&ae;s m&ae;ssehr&ae;gles  for&d;am sio cl&ae;nnes bi&d; &d;onne to fulbeorhtum wlite becumen  &d;onne &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc bi&d; gesuenced &d;urh f&ae;rh&ae;fdnesse  &amp; &d;onne betweox o&d;rum m&ae;genum bi&d; &d;ionde sio earnung &d;&ae;s gesuenctan fl&ae;sces  sua sua on &d;&ae;m m&ae;ssehr&ae;gle scien&d; ongemang o&d;rum bleon &d;&ae;t tweo&d;r&ae;wene twin. 
 Hu se lareow sceal bion gesceadwis on his swigean &amp; nytwyr&d;e on his wordum. 
 Sie se lariow gemetf&ae;s&d; &amp; gescadwis &amp; nyttwyr&d;e on his wordum  &d;&ae;tte he ne suigige &d;&ae;s &d;e nyttwyr&d;e sie to sprecanne  ne &d;&ae;t ne sprece &d;&ae;t he suigigean scyle. 
 For&d;&ae;m sua sua unw&ae;rlicu &amp; giemeleaslicu spr&ae;c menn dwele&d;  sua eac sio ungemetgode suige &d;&ae;s lareowes on gedwolan gebring&d; &d;a &d;e he l&ae;ran meahte  gif he sprecende beon wolde. 
 Oft eac &d;a unwaran lareowas for ege ne durron cleopian  ondr&ae;da&d; him sumra monna un&d;onc  ne durron for&d;on ryht freolice l&ae;ran &amp; unforwandodlice sprecan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;ness cu&ae;&d;: Ne healde ge mid suelcum eornoste &d;a heorde suelce hirdas scoldon  ac hyrena &d;eawe ge fleo&d;  &amp; hyda&d; eow mid &d;&ae;re suigean  sua se hyrra &d;onne he &d;one wulf gesieh&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce o&d;wat Dryhten &d;urh &d;one witgan  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Dumbe hundas ne magon beorcan. 
 Ond eft he cidde  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ne come ge no togenes minum folce &d;&ae;t ge meahton standan on minum gefeohte for Israhela folce  ne ge &d;one weall ne trymedon ymbe hira hus on &d;&ae;m d&ae;ge &d;e him nied&d;earf w&ae;s. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t he fare togeanes Israhela folce him mid to feohtanne &d;&ae;t he wi&d;stande mid his spr&ae;ce &d;am unryhtwillendum &d;e &d;yses middangeardes walda&d; mid freore &amp; unforwandodlicre stefne  for gescildnesse his heorde. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t he him mid feohte on &d;&ae;m d&ae;ge &d;e him nied&d;earf sie  &d;&ae;t he wi&d;stonde ealle m&ae;gene &d;&ae;m &d;e on woh wiellen for &d;&ae;re ryhtwisnesse lufan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s eft gecueden to &d;&ae;m scyldegan folce: Eowre witgan eow witgodan dysig &amp; leasunga  &amp; noldon eow gecy&d;an eowre unryhtwisnesse  &d;&ae;t hie eow gebrohten on hreowsunge. 
 &D;a godan lareowas beo&d; oft genemnede on halgum gewritum wietgan  for&d;&ae;m hie gerecca&d; &d;is andwearde lif fleonde  &amp; &d;&ae;t towearde gesueotoligea&d;. 
 &D;a &d;onne &d;e sio godcundde stefn &d;reade  &amp; cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hie scolden leasunga witgian  &d;&ae;t sindon &d;a &d;a &d;e him ondr&ae;da&d; &d;&ae;t hie menn for hira scyldum &d;reagen  ac mid ie&d;elre olicunge orsorgnesse gehata&d; &d;&ae;m scyldegan  &amp; mid nanum &d;ingum nylla&d; geopenian &d;&ae;m syngiendum hiera unryht  ac suigia&d; &d;ara &d;reaunga. 
 &D;&ae;t word &d;&ae;re &d;reaunge is c&ae;g  for&d;&ae;m hit oft anlyc&d; &amp; geopena&d; &d;a scylde &d;e se him self &ae;r nyste se hie &d;urhteah. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Paulus &d;&ae;t se lareow sceolde beon miehtig to tyhtanne on halwende lare  &amp; eac to &d;reanne &d;a &d;e him wi&d;stondan wiellen. 
 Eft w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh Zacharias: Sio &ae; sceal beon soht on &d;&ae;s sacerdes mu&d;e  &amp; his weleras gehal&d;a&d; &d;&ae;t andgit  for&d;&ae;m he bi&d; Godes boda to &d;am folce. 
 For&d;am myndgode Dryhten &d;urh Essaiam &d;one witgan &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Cleopa &amp; ne blin  hefe up &d;ine stefne sua &d;es bime. 
 For&d;&ae;m se se &d;e &d;one sacerdhad onfeh&d;  he onfeh&d; friccan scire &amp; foreryneles &d;a her ierna&d; beforan kyningum  &amp; bodigea&d; hira f&ae;relt &amp; hiera willan hlydende. 
 Sua sculun &d;a sacerdas nu faran hlydende &amp; bodiende beforan &d;&ae;m egeslican deman &d;e him sui&d;e andrysnlic &ae;fter g&ae;&d;. 
 Gif &d;onne se sacerd bi&d; ungerad &d;&ae;s lareowdomes  hw&ae;t forstent &d;onne his gehlyd? 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g he bodigean ma &d;onne se dumba fryccea? 
 Ac for &d;eosum w&ae;s geworden &d;&ae;t se halega g&ae;s&d; on tungena onlicnesse gesette ofer &d;a apostolas  for&d;&ae;m butan tweon &d;one &d;e he gefyl&d; he gede&d; &d;&ae;t he bi&d; sui&d;e hr&ae;&d;e ymbe hine sprecende. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s beboden Moyse &d;&ae;t se sacerd scolde bion mid bellum behangen. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe &d;a stefne &d;&ae;re lare  &d;yl&ae;s he abelge mid &d;&ae;re suigean &d;one dom &d;&ae;s Sceaweres. 
 Hit is awriten &d;&ae;t he scolde inngongende &amp; utgongende beforan Gode to &d;am halignessum beon gehiered his sueg  &d;yl&ae;s he swulte. 
 Hit is gecueden &d;&ae;t se sacerd scolde sweltan  gif se sueg n&ae;re of him gehiered &ae;g&d;er ge inngongendum ge utgongendum  for&d;on he geniet &d;one dieglan deman to irre  gif he inng&ae;&d; butan &d;am swege &d;&ae;re lare. 
 Hit w&ae;s awriten &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gl w&ae;re behongen mid bellum. 
 Hw&ae;t elles getacna&d; &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gl butan ryht weorc? 
 Daui&d; se witga &d;&ae;t cy&d;de  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Sien &d;ine sacerdas gegierede mid ryhtwisnesse. 
 On &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gle w&ae;ron bellan hangiende. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t &d;a weorc &d;&ae;s sacerdes &amp; eac se sueg his tungan clypien ymb lifes weg. 
 Ac &d;onne se lareow hine gegearwa&d; to &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce  behalde he hine geornlice &d;&ae;t he w&ae;rlice sprece; 
 For&d;on gif he unendebyrdlice onet mid &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce  &amp; wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he &d;y wisra &d;ynce  &d;onne is wen &d;&ae;t he gewundige &d;a heortan &d;ara gehirendra mid &d;&ae;re wunde  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he hie gedwele&d; &amp; unwislice geiec&d; &d;a idelnesse &d;e he of aceorfan sceolde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes cu&ae;&d;: Habba&d; ge sealt on ieow  &amp; sibbe habba&d; betweoh iow. 
 &D;urh &d;&ae;t sealt is getacnod &d;a word wisdomes. 
 Se &d;onne se &d;e fundige wislice to sprecanne  ondr&ae;de he him sui&d;lice  &d;yl&ae;s his spr&ae;c gescynde &d;a anmodnesse &d;ara &d;e &d;&ae;rto hlysta&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Paulus: Ne wilnien ge mare to witenne &d;onne iow &d;earf sie  ac wita&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t iow gemetlic sie &amp; iower ondefenu sien to witenne. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden mid &d;&ae;re godcundan stefne &d;&ae;t on &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gle scoldon hangigan bellan &amp; ongemang &d;&ae;m bellum reade apla. 
 Hw&ae;t elles is getacnod &d;urh &d;a readan apla buton sio anmodnes ryhtes geleafan? 
 Sua se &ae;ppel bi&d; betogen mid anfealdre rinde  &amp; &d;eah monig corn oninnan him h&ae;f&d;  sua sio halige cirice unrim folces befeh&d; mid anfealde geleafan  &amp; &d;a habba&d; sua&d;eah sui&d;e misleca geearnunga &d;e &d;&ae;rinne wunigea&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m ge&d;ence se lariow &d;&ae;t he unw&ae;rlice for&d; ne r&ae;se on &d;a spr&ae;ce. 
 Ymbe &d;&ae;t &d;e we &ae;r spr&ae;con sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes &d;urh hie selfe cleopade to &d;&ae;m apostolum  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Habba&d; ge seaLt on iow &amp; sibbe betweoh iow. 
 Sio anlicnes w&ae;s gecueden &d;&ae;t sceolde bion on &d;&ae;s sacerdes hr&ae;gle &d;a readan appla ongemang &d;am bellum. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte &d;urh eall &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t we &ae;r spr&ae;con sie underfangen &amp; w&ae;rlice gehealden sio anmodnes &d;&ae;s godcundan geleafan. 
 Se lareow sceal mid geornfullice ingehygde fore&d;encean na &d;&ae;t an &d;&ae;tte he &d;urh hine nan woh ne bodige  ac eac &d;&ae;t he nane &d;inga &d;&ae;t ryht to sui&d;e &amp; to ungemetlice &amp; to unaberendlice ne bodige  for&d;&ae;m oft &d;&ae;t m&ae;gen &d;&ae;re lare wier&d; forloren  &d;onne mon mid ungedafenlicre &amp; unw&ae;rlicre oferspr&ae;ce &d;a heortan &amp; &d;&ae;t andgiet gedwele&d; &d;ara &d;e &d;&ae;rto hlysta&d;  ond eac se lariow bi&d; gescinded mid &d;&ae;re oferspr&ae;ce  &d;onne he ne conn ge&d;encean hu he nyttwyr&d;licost l&ae;ran m&ae;ge &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;rto hlystan willa&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecueden &d;urh Moyses &d;&ae;tte se wer se &d;e &d;rowude oferflownesse his s&ae;des  &amp; &d;&ae;t unnytlice agute  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne w&ae;re uncl&ae;ne. 
 Sua eac &d;a word &d;&ae;re lare beo&d; s&ae;d  &amp; hi gefealla&d; on &d;a heortan &d;e hiera hlyst  sua nytt sua unnyt  su&ae;&d;er hie beo&d;. 
 &D;urh &d;a earan &d;a word bio&d; onfangen  &amp; on &d;&ae;m mode hie beo&d; acennedu &d;urh &d;&ae;t ondgiet. 
 For&d;&ae;m heton woroldwise menn wordsawere &d;one &ae;&d;elan lareow Paulus. 
 Se &d;onne se &d;e &d;ola&d; flowednesse his s&ae;des he bi&d; uncl&ae;ne gecueden. 
 Sua eac se &d;e oferspr&ae;ce bi&d;  he bi&d; nohte &d;on l&ae;s mid &d;&ae;re besmiten. 
 Gif he &d;onne endebyrdlice his spr&ae;ce for&d;bring&d;  &d;onne m&ae;g he cennan mid &d;am &d;&ae;t tuder ryhtes ge&d;ohtes on &d;ara tohlystendra heortan. 
 Gif &d;onne unw&ae;rlice sio lar toflew&d; &d;urh oferspr&ae;ce  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t s&ae;d unnnyt agoten  n&ae;s to nanre kenninge &d;&ae;s cynrenes  ac to uncl&ae;nnesse &amp; to ungerisnum. 
 Be &d;am Paulus cu&ae;&d;  &d;a he manode his cneoht &d;&ae;t he scolde standan on &d;&ae;re lare  he cu&ae;&d;: Ic &d;e bebeode beforan Gode &amp; &d;&ae;m h&ae;lendum Criste  se &d;e demende is cucum &amp; deadum  &amp; ic &d;e beode &d;urh his tocyme &amp; &d;urh his rice  &d;&ae;t &d;u stande on &d;issum wordum  &amp; hie l&ae;re &ae;g&d;er ge ged&ae;ftlice ge eac unged&ae;ftlice. 
 &D;eah he cu&ae;de unged&ae;ftelice  he cu&ae;&d; &d;eah &ae;r ged&ae;ftelice  for&d;&ae;m sio ofersmeaung mir&d; &d;a unwisan &d;e hit gecnawan ne magon  &amp; gede&d; &d;a spr&ae;ce unnytte &d;&ae;m tohlystendum &d;onne sio unged&ae;ftnes hit ne cann eft ged&ae;ftan. 
 Hu se lareow sceal bion eallum monnum efn&d;rowiende &amp; fore&d;encende on hiora earfo&d;um. 
 Ac sie se lareow eallum monnum se niehsta &amp; eallum monnum efn&d;rowiende on hira gesuincum  &amp; sie he for ealle up a&d;ened mid &d;&ae;re godcundan foresceawunge his innge&d;ances  &d;&ae;tte &d;urh &d;a mildheortnesse his arf&ae;s&d;nesse &d;&ae;t he tio on hine selfne o&d;erra monna scylda  &amp; eac &d;a heanesse &d;&ae;re sceawunga his innge&d;onces he hine selfne oferstige mid &d;&ae;re gewilnunge &d;ara ungesewenlicra &d;inga  &amp; &d;&ae;tte hie sua healicra &d;inga wilnigende ne forsio his niehstan untrume &amp; scyldige  ne eft for hiera untrymnesse ne forl&ae;te &d;&ae;t he ne wilnige &d;&ae;s hean. 
 For &d;ysum w&ae;s geworden &d;&ae;tte Paulus  &d;eah &d;e he w&ae;re gel&ae;ded on neorxna wong he arimde &d;a diogolnesse &d;&ae;s &d;riddan hefones  ond sua&d;eah for &d;&ae;re sceawungge &d;ara ungesewenlicra &d;inga &d;eah &d;e he up a&d;ened w&ae;re on his modes scearpnesse  ne forhogde he &d;&ae;t he hit eft gecierde to &d;am fl&ae;sclican burcotum  &amp; gestihtode hu men scoldon &d;&ae;rinne hit macian  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: H&ae;bbe &ae;lc monn his wif  &amp; &ae;lc wif hiere ciorl; 
 &amp; doo &d;&ae;t wif &d;&ae;m were &d;&ae;t hio him mid ryhte doon sceal  &amp; he hire sua some  &d;yl&ae;s hie on unryht h&ae;men. 
 &amp; hwene &ae;fter he cui&d;: Ne untreowsige ge no eow betweoxn  buton huru &d;&ae;t ge eow geh&ae;bben sume hwile  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e ge eowru gebedu &amp; eowra offrunga doon wiellen  &amp; eftsona cirra&d; to eowrum ryhth&ae;mede. 
 Loca nu hu se halega wer  se &d;e sua f&ae;s&d;lice geimpod w&ae;s to &d;&ae;m hefenlicum diogolnessum  &amp; sua&d;eah for mildheortnesse w&ae;s &d;onon gecierred to smeaganne hu fl&ae;sclicum monnum gedafonode on hira burcotum &amp; on hiera beddum to donne; 
 &amp; sua sui&d;e sua he w&ae;s upah&ae;fen to &d;&ae;m ungesewenlicum  he &d;eah gehwyrfde his heortan eage  &amp; for mildheortnesse gebigde his mod to untrumra monna diogolnessum. 
 Hefonas he &d;urhfor mid his modes sceawunga  &amp; sua&d;eah &d;one ymbhogan ne forlet &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sclican beddgemanan; 
 For&d;&ae;m he w&ae;s gefeged mid &d;&ae;re lufan Godes &amp; monna &ae;g&d;er ge to &d;am hiehstum &d;ingum ge to &d;&ae;m ny&d;emestum. 
 He w&ae;s on himselfum mid &d;&ae;s halgan g&ae;stes m&ae;gene sui&d;e healice up abrogden  &amp; &d;eah eor&d;licum monnum emnlice for arf&ae;s&d;nesse &amp; for nied&d;earfe w&ae;s geuntrumod. 
 For&d;&ae;m he cu&ae;&d;: Hwa bi&d; geuntrumod &d;&ae;t ic ne sie eac geuntrumod; 
 O&d;&d;e hwa bi&d; gesciended &d;&ae;t ic eac &d;&ae;s ne scamige? 
 Eft he cu&ae;&d; be &d;&ae;m ilcan: &d;onne ic w&ae;s mid Iudeum ic w&ae;s suelc hie. 
 Ne cu&ae;&d; he &d;&ae;t for&d;y&d;e he wolde his treowa &amp; his geleafan forl&ae;tan su&ae; su&ae; hie  ac he wolde atiewan his arf&ae;s&d;nesse  &d;a he licette hine selfne &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re ungeleaffull  ac on &d;&ae;m he geleornode hu he scolde o&d;rum monnum miltsian &d;e he ge&d;ohte hu he wolde &d;&ae;t mon him miltsode gif he suelc w&ae;re. 
 &amp; eft he cu&ae;&d;: &d;eah we nu ofer ure m&ae;&d; &d;encen &amp; smeagean  &d;&ae;t we doo&d; for Gode; 
 &D;onne we hit eft gemetl&ae;ca&d;  &d;onne do&d; we &d;&ae;t for eow. 
 He ongeat &d;&ae;t he oferstag hine selfne on &d;&ae;re sceawunge &d;&ae;re godcundnesse  &amp; eft hine selfne ofdune astiggende he cu&d;e gemetgian his hieremonnum. 
 Be &d;&ae;m eac Iacobus se heahf&ae;der  &d;a he smirede &d;one stan &d;e &ae;t his heafdum l&ae;g to tacne &d;&ae;t he eft wolde his irfe &d;&ae;r geteo&d;ian  for &d;&ae;re gesih&d;e &d;e he on &d;&ae;m swefne geseah  &d;a he &ae;t &d;&ae;m stane sl&ae;pte. 
 He geseah ane hl&ae;dre standan &ae;t him on eor&d;an. 
 O&d;er ende w&ae;s uppe on hefenum  &amp; &ae;t &d;&ae;m uferran ende Dryhten hlinode  &amp; englas stigon up &amp; ofdune on &d;a hl&ae;dre. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;a godan lareowas upsceawiende no &d;&ae;t an wilnia&d; secean &amp; sceawian &d;&ae;t halige heafod &d;&ae;re halgan gesomnunge  &d;&ae;t is Dryhten  ac wilna&d; for mildheortnesse &d;&ae;t hie ofdune astigen to his limum. 
 For&d;&ae;m Moyses oft eode inn &amp; ut on &d;&ae;t templ  for&d;&ae;m he w&ae;s &d;&ae;rinne getogen to &d;&ae;re godcundan sceawunga  &amp; &d;&ae;rut he w&ae;s abisgod ymb &d;&ae;s folces &d;earfe. 
 &D;&ae;rinne he sceawode on his mode &d;a diogolnesse &d;&ae;re godcundnesse  ond &d;onon utbrohte &d;&ae;m folce  &amp; cy&d;de hw&ae;t hie wyrcean &amp; healdan scoldon. 
 &amp; symle ymb &d;&ae;t &d;e hine &d;onne tueode  &d;onne orn he eft innto &d;&ae;m temple  &amp; fr&ae;gn &d;&ae;s Dryhten beforan &d;&ae;re earce &d;e se haligdom on w&ae;s &d;&ae;s temples. 
 He astealde on &d;&ae;m bisene &d;&ae;m reccerum &d;e nu siendon. 
 Hie sculon  &d;onne hie ymb hw&ae;t tueo&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e hie &d;&ae;rute don sculon  cierran eft to hira agnum innge&d;once  &amp; &d;&ae;r God ascian  su&ae; su&ae; Moyses dyde beforan &d;&ae;re earce on &d;&ae;m temple. 
 Gif hie &d;onne giet &d;&ae;r tueona&d;  gongen &d;onne to &d;&ae;m halgan gewritum  frine &d;ara hw&ae;t hie don o&d;&d;e l&ae;ran scylen. 
 For&d;&ae;m sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes self  &d;&ae;t is Kris&d;  &d;a he on eor&d;an w&ae;s  he hine geb&ae;d on muntum &amp; on dioglum stowum  &amp; on burgum he worhte his wundru  mid &d;&ae;m he strewede &d;one weg &d;&ae;re onhyrenesse &d;&ae;m godum lariowum  &d;&ae;t hie ne scolden forhyggean &d;one geferscipe &d;ara synfulra &amp; &d;ara ungetydra  &d;eh &d;e hi selfe wilnien &d;&ae;s heahstan. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne sio lufu for mildheortnesse nie&d;erastige&d;  &amp; hio hie ge&d;ied to his niehstena &d;earfe  &d;onne hio sui&d;e wunderlice upastige&d;; 
 &amp; sua micle sua hio estelicor ofdune astige&d;  sua hio ie&d;elicor upastige&d;; 
 Suelce hie sculon hie selfe atiowan  &d;a &d;e o&d;rum  fore beo&d;  &d;&ae;tte &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde sien him dyrren hira dieglan &d;ing for scome geandettan. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne &d;a y&d;a &d;ara costunga &d;a synfullan &d;rowia&d;  &d;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen iernan &amp; fleon to &d;&ae;s lareowes mode him to ondettunge  su&ae; su&ae; cild to his moder greadan  &amp; &d;a scylda &d;e hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie mid besmitene sien  mid his fultume &amp; ge&d;eahte hie m&ae;gen a&d;wean cl&ae;nran &d;onne hie &ae;r &d;&ae;re costunge w&ae;ren  mid &d;&ae;m tearum &d;ara gebeda a&d;w&ae;gen. 
 For&d;&ae;m eac w&ae;s &d;&ae;t &d;e beforan &d;&ae;m temple stod &ae;ren ceac onuppan twelf &ae;renum oxum  &d;&ae;tte &d;a menn &d;e into &d;&ae;m temple gan woldon meahten hira honda &d;wean on &d;&ae;m mere. 
 Se ceac w&ae;s sua micel &d;&ae;t he oferhelede &d;a oxan ealle  buton &d;a heafudu totodon ut. 
 Hw&ae;t getacnia&d; &d;onne twelf oxan buton &d;a XII apostolas  &amp; si&d;&d;an ealle &d;a endebyrdnessa &d;ara biscopa &d;e &d;&ae;r&ae;fter fylgea&d;? 
 Bi &d;on w&ae;s gecueden on &d;&ae;re &ae;: Ne forbinden ge na &d;&ae;m &d;yrstendum oxum &d;one mu&d;. 
 &D;one cwide Paulus geryhte eft to biscepum &d;ara openlican weorc we gesio&d;  ac we nyton hwelc hira innge&d;onc bi&d; beforan &d;&ae;m &d;earlwisan deman on &d;&ae;m dieglan edleanum. 
 &D;a &d;eah &d;onne hi ni&d;erastiga&d; to a&d;weanne hiera niehstena scylda  &d;onne hie him ondetta&d;  hie beo&d; onlicost suelce hi beren &d;one ceak beforan &d;&ae;re ciricean dura  sua sua &d;a oxan dydon beforan &d;&ae;m temple; 
 &D;&ae;tte sua hwelc sua inweard higige to gangenne on &d;a duru &d;&ae;s ecean lifes  he &d;onne ondette &ae;lce costunge &d;e him on becume &d;am mode his scriftes beforan &d;&ae;m temple; 
 Ond su&ae; su&ae; &d;ara monna honda &amp; fet w&ae;ren a&d;w&ae;gene on &d;&ae;re ealdan &ae; on &d;&ae;m ceake beforan &d;&ae;m temple  sua &d;onne nu we a&d;wean ures modes honda &amp; ure weorc mid &d;&ae;re ondetnesse. 
 Oft eac gebyre&d; &d;onne se scrift ongit &d;&ae;s costunga &d;e he him ondette&d; &d;&ae;t eac self bi&d; mid &d;&ae;m ilcum gecostod. 
 Hw&ae;t &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter on &d;&ae;m ceake w&ae;s gedrefed  &d;onne &d;&ae;r micel folc hiera fet &amp; honda on &d;wogon. 
 Sua bi&d; &d;&ae;s sacerdes mod &d;onne &d;&ae;r bi&d; micel folc on a&d;w&ae;gen hira scylda &d;urh his lare. 
 &D;onne he underfeh&d; &d;&ae;t fenn &d;ara &d;weandra  him &d;ync&d; suelce he forleose &d;a smyltnesse his cl&ae;nnesse. 
 Ac nis &d;&ae;t na to andr&ae;danne &d;&ae;m hirde  for&d;&ae;m&d;e Dryhten hit eall swi&d;e smealice ge&d;enc&d;  &amp; him forgief&d; &d;&ae;t he sua micle ie&d;elicor bi&d; gefri&d;od from his agnum costungum sua he mildheortlicor bi&d; gesuenced mid o&d;erra monna costungum. 
 Hu se reccere sceal bion &d;&ae;m weldondum monnum for ea&d;modnesse gefera &amp; wi&d; &d;ara yfelena un&d;eawas str&ae;c for ryhtwislicum andan. 
 Se ealdormonn sceal l&ae;tan hine selfne gelicne his hieremonnum: he sceal bion hira gefera for ea&d;modnesse &d;ara &d;eah &d;e wel don:he sceal bion wi&d; &d;ara agyltendra un&d;eawas upah&ae;fen for &d;&ae;m andan his ryhtwisnesse  &amp; &d;&ae;tte he on n&ae;negum &d;ingum hine beteran ne do &d;&ae;m godum; 
 &amp; &d;eah &d;onne he ongiete &d;a scylda &d;ara &d;weortiemena  &d;onne ge&d;ence he &d;one ealdordom his onwealdes; 
 &amp; eft ongean &d;a godan &amp; &d;a wellibbendan forsio he his ealdordom su&ae; sui&d;e &d;&ae;t he on allum &d;ingum &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde sien l&ae;te him gelice  &amp; ne wene he nanes &d;inges hine selfne beteran; 
 &amp; eft wi&d; &d;a wi&d;erweardan ne ondr&ae;de he &d;&ae;t he begonge his ryhtwisnesse  su&ae; su&ae; ic geman &d;&ae;t ic io s&ae;de on &d;&ae;re bec &d;e Morales Iob hatte. 
 Ic cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &ae;ghwelc monn w&ae;re gelice o&d;rum acenned  ac sio ungelicnes hira geearnunga hie tieh&d; sume behindan sume  &amp; hira scylda hi &d;&ae;r gehabba&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t &d;onne &d;a ungelicnesse &d;e of hira un&d;eawum for&d;cyme&d;  se godcunda dom ge&d;enc&d; &d;&ae;tte ealle men gelice beon ne magon  ac wile &d;&ae;t simle se o&d;er beo ar&ae;red from &d;&ae;m o&d;rum. 
 For&d;&ae;m ealle &d;a &d;e fore o&d;rum bieon sculon ne sculon hi na sua sui&d;e ne sua oft ge&d;encean hiera ealderdomes sua hie sculon ge&d;encean hu gelice hie beo&d; o&d;rum monnum on hira gecynde; 
 &amp; ne gefeon hie na &d;&ae;t hie ofer o&d;re menn bion moten sua sui&d;e sua &d;&ae;s &d;&ae;t hie o&d;rum monnum m&ae;gen nyttoste beon. 
 Hw&ae;t hit is ges&ae;d &d;&ae;t ure ealdan f&ae;deras w&ae;ron ceapes hierdas. 
 Ond eac Dryhten cu&ae;&d; to Noe &amp; to his bearnum: Weahsa&d; ge &amp; monigfaldia&d; &amp; gefylla&d; eor&d;an  &amp; iower ege &amp; broga sie ofer ealle eor&d;an nitenu. 
 Ne cu&ae;&d; he no ofer o&d;re menn ac ofer nietenu  &d;a he w&ae;s forboden ofer menn  &d;a he w&ae;s aliefed ofer nietenu. 
 Se monn is on gecynde betera &d;onne dysig nietenu  ac he ne bi&d; na betera &d;onne o&d;re menn. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit n&ae;s na gecueden &d;&ae;t hie ne scoldon o&d;re menn ondr&ae;dan  ac nietenu. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit is ungecyndelicu ofermodgung &d;&ae;t se monn wilnige &d;&ae;t hine his gelica ondr&ae;de  &amp; sua&d;eah hit is nied&d;earf &d;&ae;t mon his hlaford ondr&ae;de  &amp; se cneoht his magister. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne &d;a lareowas ongita&d; &d;&ae;t &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde beo&d; him to hwon God andr&ae;da&d;  &d;onne is &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie gedon &d;&ae;t hi huru him menniscne ege ondr&ae;den  &d;&ae;t hie ne durren syngian &d;a &d;e him ne ondr&ae;da&d; &d;one godcundan dom. 
 Ne ofermodgia&d; &d;a scirmenn na for&d;y  &d;eah hi for &d;yslicum wielnien &d;&ae;t hie andrysne sien  for&d;on hi ne seca&d; na hira selfra gielp on &d;am  ac hioraN hieremonna ryhtwisnesse hie wilnia&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;m hi wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie andrysne sien &d;&ae;m &d;e on woh libba&d;; 
 &amp; ofer &d;a hi sculon ricsian n&ae;s na sua ofer menn ac sua sua ofer nietenu  for&d;on&d;e hie be sumum d&ae;le wildorlice beo&d;. 
 Hie sculon for&d;y ofdr&ae;dde licgean astreahte o&d;rum monnum under&d;iodde sua sua nietenu. 
 For &d;iosum &d;onne oft gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t se reccere on his mode wir&d; upah&ae;fen  &amp; wier&d; a&d;unden on ofermetto  &d;onne he sua sui&d;e o&d;re oferhlifa&d; &d;&ae;tte ealle licggea&d; under his willan  ond eall &d;&ae;t he bebeode&d; bi&d; sui&d;e hra&d;e gefylled to his nytte; 
 Ond gif hw&ae;t welgedones bi&d;  &d;onne cnoda&d; him &d;&ae;t ealle &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde bio&d; mid herenesse; 
 &amp; gif he hw&ae;t yfeles de&d;  ne wi&d;cui&d; &d;am nan mann  ac heriga&d; oft sua sui&d;e sua hie hit lean scoldon; 
 &amp; mid &d;y wyr&d; &d;&ae;t mod besuicen &amp; gen&ae;t mid &d;&ae;ra olicunga &d;e him under&d;iedde beo&d; &d;&ae;t he bi&d; up ofer hine selfne ah&ae;fen on his mode; 
 Ond &d;onne he bi&d; utane ymbhringed mid ungemetlicre heringe  he bi&d; innan aidlad &d;&ae;re ryhtwisnesse  &amp; forgiet hine selfne &d;onne he tol&ae;tt  &amp; f&ae;gna&d; ongeagn &d;ara o&d;erra word ond gelief&d; &d;&ae;t he suelc sie suelce he gehier&d; &d;&ae;t his olicceras secga&d; &d;&ae;t he sie  n&ae;s suelc scuelc his selfes gescadwisnes sceolde ongietan &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re. 
 Ac forsieh&d; &d;a &d;e him under&d;iodde beo&d;  &amp; ne m&ae;g ongietan &d;a &d;e him beo&d; on gecynde &amp; on &d;eawum gelice  ac wen&d; &d;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe hie ofer&d;ungne on his lifes gearnunga sua he hi h&ae;f&d; oferstigene mid &d;am hliete his anwaldes  ond wen&d; he sua micle ma wite &d;onne o&d;re menn  sua he gesih&d; &d;&ae;t he mare m&ae;g doon &d;onne o&d;re menn. 
 &amp; &d;onne hine selfne sua healice upahefe&d; on sumum &d;ingum  ond sua&d;eah bi&d; getieged to o&d;rum monnum mid onlicre gecynde  &d;eah he forsio &d;&ae;t he him onlocige. 
 Ac sua he wier&d; self to &d;&ae;s onlicnesse &d;e awriten is &d;&ae;t he gesio &ae;lce ofermetto  se is kyning ofer eall &d;a bearn oferhygde. 
 Se wilnode synderlices ealdordomes  &amp; forsieh &d;a geferr&ae;ddene o&d;erra engla &amp; hira lif  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ic wille wyrcean min setl on nor&d;d&ae;le  &amp; wielle bion gelic &d;&ae;m hiehstan  ond &d;a wunderlice dome gewear&d; &d;&ae;t he geearnode mid his agne innge&d;once &d;one pytt &d;e he on aworpen wear&d;  &d;a he hine his agnes &d;onces upahof on sua healicne anwald. 
 Butan tweon &d;onne se monn oferhy&d; &d;&ae;t he beo gelic o&d;rum monnum  &d;onne bi&d; he gelic &d;&ae;m wi&d;erweardan &amp; &d;&ae;m aworpnan diofule. 
 Sua sua Sawl Israhela kyning &d;urh ea&d;modnesse he geearnode &d;&ae;t rice  ond for &d;&ae;s rices heanesse him weoxon ofermetto. 
 For ea&d;modnesse he w&ae;s ah&ae;fen ofer o&d;re menn  ond f&ae;r ofermettum he w&ae;s aworpen. 
 Dryhten &d;&ae;t gecy&d;de &d;a &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;a &d;u &d;e selfum &d;uhtest unwenlic  &d;a ic &d;e gesette eallum Israhelum to heafde. 
 &AE;res&d; him &d;uhte selfum &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re sui&d;e unmedeme  ac si&d;&d;an he understungen &amp; awre&d;ed w&ae;s mid &d;ys hwilendlican onwalde  he &d;uhte him selfum sui&d;e unlytel &amp; sui&d;e medeme. 
 For&d;&ae;m he hine &ae;thof from o&d;erra monna geferr&ae;denne  ond hine dyde o&d;rum monnum sua ungelicne. 
 For&d;y he ongeat &d;&ae;t he ma mehte &d;onne &ae;nig o&d;er  &d;a wende he &d;&ae;t he eac mara w&ae;re. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;s wunderlicu gemetgung &d;&ae;tte &d;a &d;a he him selfum w&ae;s lytel ge&d;uht  &d;a w&ae;s he Gode micel ge&d;uht  ond &d;a &d;a he w&ae;s him selfum micel ge&d;uht  &d;a w&ae;s he Gode lytel ge&d;uht. 
 Sua oft &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod a&d;int on ofermettum for &d;&ae;re menige &d;&ae;s folces &d;e him under&d;ied bi&d;  hit bi&d; gewemmed mid &d;&ae;s anwaldes heanesse. 
 &D;one anwald m&ae;g wel reccan se &d;e &ae;g&d;er ge hine habban cann ge wi&d;winnan. 
 Wel hine rec&d; se &d;e conn wel str&ae;c bion &amp; ah&ae;fen wi&d; &d;a unryhtwisan &amp; wi&d; &d;a scyldgan &amp; wel emn wi&d; o&d;re menn  ond he hine na bettran ne de&d;. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mennisce mod bi&d; oft upahafen  &d;eah hit mid nane anwalde ne sie underled; 
 Ac hu micle ma wenstu &d;&ae;t hit wolde  gif &d;a wlenca &amp; se anwald &d;&ae;r w&ae;re to gemenged. 
 &amp; &d;eah sui&d;e ryhte stihta&d; &d;one anwald se &d;e geornlice conn ongietan &d;&ae;t he of him gadrige &d;&ae;t him st&ae;lwier&d;e sie  &amp; wi&d; &d;&ae;t winne &d;&ae;t him dere&d;  &amp; ongite hine selfne  ond ongiete &d;&ae;t he bi&d; self o&d;rum monnum gelic  ond &d;eah ahebbe hine ofer &d;a scyldgan mid andan &amp; mid wr&ae;ce. 
 We magon eac fullecor ongietan &amp; tosceadan &d;a spr&ae;ce  gif we sceawia&d; &d;a biesene &d;&ae;s forman hierdes  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s sanctus Petrus. 
 &D;urh Godes giefe he onfeng &d;one ealdordom &d;&ae;re halgan ciericean  ond &d;eah he wi&d;soc &d;&ae;t hine mon to ungemetlice weor&d;ode. 
 &D;a &d;a Cornelius for ea&d;modnesse wel dyde &d;&ae;t he hine astrehte beforan him  he &d;eah hine selfne ongeat him gelicne  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Aris  ne do sua; 
 Hu  ne iom ic monn sua ilce sua &d;u? 
 Ac &d;a &d;a he ongeat &d;a scylde on Annanian &amp; on Saffiram  sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice he o&d;iewde hu micelne onwald he h&ae;fde ofer o&d;re menn  &d;a he hira lif &d;urh &d;a smeanga &d;&ae;s halgan g&ae;stes ongeat  &amp; hine &d;a mid his worde geslog  &amp; mid &d;y anwalde gecy&d;de &d;&ae;t he w&ae;s ieldes&d; ofer &d;a halgan cirican &amp; strenges&d; wi&d; scylda. 
 &D;&ae;t rice &amp; &d;one anwald he na ne angeat wi&d; Cornelius  &d;a &d;a he hine sua sui&d;lice weor&d;ian wolde; 
 He wolde him &ae;tf&ae;stan his ea&d;metto  &amp; mid &d;y he geearnode &d;&ae;t he &d;uhte &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re his gelica. 
 He cu&ae;&d; to him &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re his gelica: &d;&ae;r he gecy&d;de his ea&d;modnesse; 
 Ond eft on Annaniam &amp; on Saffiram gecy&d;de his ni&d; &amp; his onwald mid &d;&ae;re wr&ae;ce. 
 Ond eft sanctus Paulus ne ongeat he na hine selfne beteran o&d;rum godum monnum  &d;a &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ne sint we nane waldendas eowres geleafan. 
 Ac sint fultemend eowres gefean  for&d;am&d;e ge stonda&d; on geleafan Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: We sint emnlice on &d;am &d;e we ongieta&d; &d;&ae;t ge stonda&d;. 
 Eft he spr&ae;c suelce he nysse &d;&ae;t he a fur&d;or w&ae;re &d;onne o&d;re bro&d;or  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: We sint gewordene suelce lytlingas betueox eow. 
 Ond eft he cu&ae;&d;: We sint eowre &d;eowas for Cristes lufan. 
 Ac &d;onne he gemette &d;a scylde &d;e he stieran scolde  hr&ae;dlice he gecy&d;de &d;&ae;t he w&ae;s magister &amp; ealdormonn. 
 &D;&ae;t he cy&d;de &d;a he cu&ae;&d; on his epistolan to Galatum: Hw&ae;&d;er wille ge &d;&ae;t ic cume to eow  &d;e mid gierde &d;e mid monn&d;w&ae;re g&ae;ste? 
 Suelce he cu&ae;de: Hw&ae;&d;er ic cume &d;e mid ege &d;e mid lufe? 
 &D;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t rice wel gereht  &d;onne se &d;e &d;&ae;r fore bi&d; sui&d;or wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he ricsige ofer monna un&d;eawas &d;onne ofer o&d;re gode menn. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;a ealdermenn &d;reagea&d; &d;a scyldgan  &d;onne is him micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte &d;urh &d;a lare &amp; &d;urh &d;one ege &d;e hie niede don sculon mid hiera anwalde gestiran &d;ara scylda. 
 Ond &d;eahhw&ae;&d;re  &d;yl&ae;s he his ea&d;modnesse forleose  ge&d;ence he &d;&ae;t he bi&d; self sui&d;e gelic &d;am ilcan monnum &d;e he &d;&ae;r &d;reata&d; &amp; hen&d;; 
 Ond eac we magon suigende ge&d;encean on urum inngehygde  &d;eah we hit ne sprecen  &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; beteran &d;onne we  &amp; &d;&ae;s wier&d;e &d;&ae;t we hie fur&d;or don  &d;eah we to &d;am gesette sien &d;&ae;t we hie &d;reagean scylen  &amp; &d;urh us scylen bion hiora scylda gestiered mid cr&ae;fte &amp; mid lare. 
 Ac eft &d;onne we selfe gesyngia&d;  ne &d;rea&d; us nan monn  ne fur&d;um ane worde ne t&ae;l&d;. 
 For&d;am we beo&d; mid Gode sua micle sui&d;or gebundne sua we for monnum orsorglicor ungewitnode syngia&d; buton &ae;lcre wrace. 
 Ac &d;onne we ure hieremenn l&ae;ra&d; &amp; &d;reagea&d;  sua micle ma we hie gefreoga&d; &ae;fter &d;am godcundan dome  sua we her hiera synna wreca&d; sui&d;or; 
 Ond sua&d;eah on &d;&ae;re heortan is a sio ea&d;modnes to healdanne &amp; eac on weorcum to l&ae;ranne; 
 &amp; betuh &d;&ae;m tw&ae;m is eallenga to ge&d;encenne &d;&ae;t we to ungemetlice &d;a ea&d;modnesse ne healden  &d;yl&ae;s se anweald aslacie &d;&ae;s recendomes  ond &d;&ae;t we ure hieremenn sua gearige sua we hie eft geegesian m&ae;ge. 
 &D;one ealdordom &amp; &d;&ae;t riceter &d;e se reccere for monigra monna &d;earfe underfeh&d; he hine sceal eowian utan  &amp; he sceal healdan his ea&d;modnesse innan. 
 Eahtige he hine selfne on his innge&d;once suelcne suelcne he ondr&ae;tt &d;&ae;t he sie. 
 Ond &d;eah hit on sumum &d;ingum getacnad sie &d;&ae;t he hwelc gerisenlic wundor wyrcean m&ae;ge  gedo he &d;eah &d;&ae;t his hieremenn ongieten &d;&ae;t he sie ea&d;mod on his innge&d;once  &d;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen &d;&ae;m onhyrigean  ond on his ealdorlicnesse hie ongieten &d;&ae;t hie him m&ae;gen ondr&ae;dan. 
 &D;a &d;e ofer o&d;re bio&d; giemen hie geornlice &d;&ae;tte sua micle sua hira onwald bi&d; mara gesewen ofer o&d;re menn &d;&ae;t hie sua micle ma sien innan ge&d;ryccede mid ea&d;modnesse  &d;yl&ae;s &d;&ae;t ge&d;oht hine ofersui&d;e &amp; on lustfulnesse his mod geteo hwelces un&d;eawes  &d;&ae;t he hit m&ae;ge &d;onne to his willan gewealdan  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he him &ae;r to un&d;eawum his agenne willan under&d;eodde  &amp; him ge&d;afade &d;&ae;t hit mid anwalde him moste oferricsian  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t ofsetene mod mid &d;&ae;re lustfulnesse his anwaldes ne sie getogen to upahafenesse. 
 Bi &d;am w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte gecueden &d;urh sumne wisne monn  he cu&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m o&d;rum: To ealdormenn &d;u eart gesett  ne beo &d;u &d;eah to upahafen  ac bio suelce an &d;inra hieremonna. 
 Ond eft be &d;am ilcan cu&ae;&d; sanctus Petrus: Ne sint we nane waldendas &d;isses folces  ac we sint to bisene gesette urre heorde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan eft sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;ness  &d;&ae;t is Crist  &d;urh hine selfne cu&ae;&d;  &d;a he us speon to &d;&ae;m hiehstan geearnungum  he cu&ae;&d;: Wite ge &d;&ae;tte &d;ioda kyningas bio&d; &d;&ae;s folces waldendas  ond &d;a &d;e &d;one anwald bega&d; hi beo&d; hlafordas gehatene; 
 Ne sie hit &d;onne na sua betweoxn eow  ac sua hwelc sua wille betweoxn eow fyrmest beon  se sceal beon eower &d;egn  ond sua hwelc sua wille betweoxn eow m&ae;st beon  sie se eower &d;eow. 
 Sua sua monnes sunu  cu&ae;&d; Crist be him selfum  ne com he na to &d;am on eor&d;an &d;&ae;t him mon &d;enade  ac &d;&ae;t he wolde &d;enian. 
 For &d;eosun illcan is eac ges&ae;d on &d;&ae;m godspelle hwelc wite scolde &d;rowian se upahafena &d;egn &ae;fter &d;am anfangnan rice; 
 He cu&ae;&d; &d;onne: Se yfela &d;eow cui&d; on his mode: Hit bi&d; long hwonne se hlaford cume; 
 Ic m&ae;g slean &amp; ierman mine heafodgem&ae;ccan. 
 Itt him &d;onne &amp; drinc&d; mid &d;am druncenwillum monnum  ond l&ae;t his hlafordes gebod to giemelieste. 
 &D;onne cym&d; his hlaford on &d;&ae;m d&ae;ge &d;e he ne wen&d;  ond on &d;a tiid &d;&ae;t he hine &ae;r nat; 
 H&ae;f&d; hine &d;onne si&d;&d;an for &ae;nne licettere. 
 &amp; sui&d;e ryht de&d; for &d;&ae;re licettunge &d;e he licette &d;&ae;t he wolde habban &d;a &d;enunga &d;eawas &amp; &d;eodscipe to l&ae;ranne; 
 Ond &d;a he &d;&ae;t h&ae;fde  &d;a wolde he hit habban him to agnum anwalde  ond dyde him &d;&ae;t riceter to sida &amp; to gewunan. 
 Ond sua&d;eah oft agylta&d; &d;a ealdormenn efnsui&d;e on &d;am &d;e he bi&d; to ea&d;mod &d;am yflan mannan  ond l&ae;t hine him to gelicne  &amp; licett wi&d; hie ma to geferr&ae;denne &d;onne toealdordome. 
 Sui&d;e ryhte se bi&d; geteald to &d;&ae;m liceterum se &d;e on lareowes onlicnesse &d;a &d;enenga &d;&ae;s ealdordomes gecier&d; to hlaforddome  &amp; gemaca&d; &d;&ae;t his ege &amp; his onwald wier&d; to gewunan &amp; to landsida on his scire. 
 Ond &d;eah hwilum giet sui&d;or hie syngia&d; on &d;am &d;e hie healda&d; ma geferr&ae;denne &amp; efnlicnesse &d;onne ealdordom wi&d; &d;a yfelan &amp; &d;a unryhtwisan. 
 Sua Heli se sacerd dyde. 
 He w&ae;s mid leasre mildheortnesse ofersui&d;ed &d;&ae;t he nolde witnian his agne suna &d;a hie agylton  ac beforan &d;am &d;earlwisan Deman he ofslog &ae;g&d;er ge &d;a suna ge hine selfne mid&d;am&d;e he ge&d;afade &d;a scylde unwitnode. 
 Hit w&ae;s onlicost suelce sio godcunde stemn to him cu&ae;de: &d;u weor&d;as&d; &d;ine suna ma &d;onne me. 
 Ond eft &d;urh &d;one witgan w&ae;s gecid hierdum  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t sceap &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r sceoncforad w&ae;s ne spilcte ge &d;&ae;t  ond &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r forloren w&ae;s ne sohte ge &d;&ae;t  ne ham ne brohtan. 
 Se bring&d; ham &d;one forlorenan se &d;e mid geornfulnesse &d;&ae;re hierdelican giemenne &d;one &d;e afiel&d; on synne eft gehwyrf&d; &amp; ar&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he stent on ryhtwisnesse. 
 Hw&ae;t se foreda sconca bi&d; gewri&d;en mid &d;&ae;m bende  sua beo&d; &d;a synna mid &d;am lareowdome gebundne. 
 Sua sua sio wund wile toberan  gif hio ne bi&d; gewri&d;en mid wr&ae;de  sua willa&d; &d;a synna weax&ae;nde toflowan  gif hie ne beo&d; gebundne hwilum mid str&ae;clice lareowdome. 
 Ond sua&d;eah oft sio wund bi&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e wierse &amp; &d;y mare  gif hio bi&d; unw&ae;rlice gewri&d;en  &amp; him bi&d; &d;&ae;t sar &d;e gefredre  gif sio wund bi&d; to ungemetlice f&ae;ste gewri&d;en. 
 Sua is eac &d;earf &d;&ae;t se lareow  se bi&d; saule l&ae;ce  &d;ara synna wunde stirende gemetlice gewri&d;e on his hieremonnumm  ond &d;eah sua geornlice begaa &d;a ryhtwisnesse &d;&ae;s lareowdomes wi&d; &d;a gyltendan &d;&ae;t he ne forl&ae;te his mildheortnesse. 
 Ond eac him is to giemenne &d;&ae;t he &ae;tiewe his hieremonnum &d;&ae;t he sie hiera f&ae;der &amp; reccere on lare  &amp; hiera modur on mildheortnesse  &d;&ae;t he huru ne sie to str&ae;c on &d;&ae;re lare  ne to sl&ae;c on &d;&ae;re mildheortnesse. 
 Sua sua we io cu&ae;don on &d;eawa bocum be Iobe &d;&ae;t &ae;g&d;er w&ae;re unnyt ge mildheortnes ge steor  gif hie anlipe w&ae;ron  buton hi butu &ae;tsomne sien. 
 For&d;&ae;m scel bion on &d;&ae;m reccere &d;&ae;t he sie ryhtlice &amp; mildheortlice r&ae;dende his hieremonnum &amp; mildheortlice witniende. 
 For &d;ioson ilcan w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte sio So&d;f&ae;stnes self cu&ae;&d;  &d;&ae;t is Crist  &d;a he l&ae;rde &d;urh &d;a tielunga &d;&ae;s Samaritaniscan ymb &d;one gewundedan  &d;e mon l&ae;dde helfcuicne to &d;&ae;m gies&d;huse  &amp; b&ae;d &d;&ae;t mon scolde &ae;g&d;er ge win ge ele giotan on his wunde. 
 Witodlice &d;&ae;t win slit &d;a wunde  &amp; se ele hie gesme&d; &amp; geh&ae;l&d;. 
 &D;is is &d;earf &d;&ae;t se &d;e wunde lacnigean wille giote win on  &d;&ae;t sio re&d;nes &d;&ae;s wines &d;a forrotedan wunde suge &amp; cl&ae;nsige  &amp; eft ele  &d;&ae;t se hie lie&d;e &amp; geh&ae;le. 
 Sua eac &d;am lareowe is to monianne &d;a lie&d;nesse wi&d; &d;a re&d;nesse  &amp; of &d;am gemonnge wyrce gemetunge  &d;&ae;t he mid ungemetlicre grimsunge his hieremonna wunda to sui&d;e ne slite ne ne ice  ne eft for ungemetlicre mildheortnesse he hie ne l&ae;te unwri&d;ena. 
 Sui&d;e wel ymb &d;&ae;t tacna&d; sio earc on &d;&ae;re ealdan &ae;. 
 On &d;&ae;re w&ae;ron &d;a st&ae;nenan bredu &d;e sio &ae; w&ae;s on awriten mid tien bebodum  &amp; wac sio gierd mid &d;&ae;m bredum  &amp; eac se sweta mete &d;e hie heton monna  se him cuom of hefonum. 
 Sua eac  gif &d;ara haligra gewrita &amp;git bi&d; on &d;am breostum &d;&ae;s godan recceres  &d;onne sceal &d;&ae;r bion gierd. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he &d;reage his hiremenn. 
 &amp; eac sceal bion on &d;&ae;m breostum &d;&ae;s monnan suetnes. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he him sie lie&d;e. 
 Be &d;iosum illcan cu&ae;&d; Daui&d; to Gode: &d;in gierd &amp; &d;in st&ae;f me afrefredon. 
 Mid gierde mon bi&d; geswungen  &amp; mid st&ae;fe he bi&d; awre&d;ed. 
 Gif &d;&ae;r &d;onne sie gierd mid to &d;reageanne  sie &d;&ae;r eac st&ae;f mid to wre&d;ianne: sie &d;&ae;r eac lufu  n&ae;s &d;eah to hnesce; 
 Sie &d;&ae;r eac re&d;nes  n&ae;s &d;eah to sti&d;; 
 Sie &d;&ae;r eac onda  n&ae;s &d;eah to ungemetlice grim; 
 Sie &d;&ae;r eac arf&ae;s&d;nes  n&ae;s &d;eah wandigendre &d;onne hit gedafenlic sie; 
 &D;&ae;tte &d;onne sio ryhtwisnes &amp; sio mildheortnes hi gegadrige on &d;&ae;m anwalde &d;&ae;s recceres  &amp; &d;&ae;t mod his hieremonna oliccende egesige &amp; &d;reatigende olicce. 
 Hu se lareow ne sceal &d;a inneran giemenne gewanian for &d;&ae;re uterran abisgunge  ne eft &d;a uterran ne forl&ae;te he for &d;&ae;re inneran. 
 Ne forl&ae;te se reccere &d;a inneran giemenne &d;&ae;s godcundan &d;iowdomes for &d;&ae;re abisgunge &d;ara uterra weorca  ne eac ne gewanige he na &d;one ymbhogan &d;&ae;re innera scire for &d;&ae;re abisgunge &d;&ae;re uterran; 
 &D;yl&ae;s he sie geh&ae;ft mid &d;am uterran  o&d;&d;e eft mid &d;am inneran anum abisegad  &d;&ae;t he ne m&ae;ge &d;urhteon his niehstum &d;&ae;t he him utan don scolde. 
 Monige &d;eah nylla&d; na ge&d;encean &d;&ae;t hi beo&d; o&d;rum bro&d;rum ofergesett  &amp; him fore bion scoldon on godcundum &d;ingum; 
 Ac mid ealre heortan geornfulnesse begonga&d; &d;a woroldcundan giemenne  &amp; f&ae;gnia&d; &d;&ae;s &d;&ae;t hie &d;a habba&d; to begongenne; 
 &amp; &d;onne  &d;onne hie hie ne habba&d;  d&ae;ges &amp; niehtes hie fundia&d; to bigietenne  &amp; beo&d; sui&d;e gedrefede on hira mode for&d;am&d;e him &d;onne wona bi&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e hie habban woldon. 
 Ac &d;onne him eft gelimp&d; &d;&ae;t hi &ae;mtige beo&d; &d;&ae;re scire  &d;onne bio&d; hie sui&d;ur on hira mode gesuenced for &d;&ae;m &ae;mtan; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t w&ae;re his willa &d;&ae;t he moste ymb swincan  ond &d;ync&d; him gesuinc &d;&ae;t he bi&d; butan woroldgesuincium. 
 &amp; sua hit gebyre&d;  &d;onne he f&ae;gna&d; &d;&ae;t he sie abisgod mid worold&d;ingum  &d;&ae;t he ne conn o&d;re l&ae;ran &d;a godcundan wisan &d;e he l&ae;ran scolde. 
 For&d;on a&d;reat &d;a hieremenn ryhtes lifes  &d;onne hie wilnia&d; g&ae;stlice libban  be &d;&ae;m yfelum bisenum &d;e se de&d; &d;e him fore beon sceolde. 
 &D;onne &ae;tsporna&d; hie  &amp; weor&d;a&d; mid &d;&ae;m ascrencte. 
 Sua eac &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;t heafod bi&d; unhal eall &d;a limu bio&d; idelu  &d;eah hie hale sien  sua eac bi&d; se here eal idel  &d;onne he on o&d;er folc winnan sceal  gif se heretoga dwola&d;; 
 Sua eac &d;onne se biscep beg&ae;&d; &d;a &d;eninga &d;e eor&d;lice deman sceoldon  &d;onne ne tyht nan mon his hieremonna mod ne ne bilt to g&ae;stlicum weorcum  ne nan mon hiera scylda ne &d;rea&d;  ac se hierde bi&d; idel &d;e scolde &d;&ae;re heorde gieman. 
 For&d;y ne magon &d;a hieremenn begietan &d;&ae;t leoht &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;stnesse  for&d;&ae;m &d;onne sio giornfulnes eor&d;licra &d;inga abisga&d; &d;&ae;t &amp;git  &amp; ablent &d;&ae;s modes eagan mid &d;&ae;re costunga &d;&ae;m folce  sua sua dust de&d; &d;&ae;s lichoman eagan on sumra mid &d;odene. 
 For&d;&ae;m sui&d;e ryhtlice se Aliesend monna cynnes  &d;a he us stierde urra womba oferfylle  he cu&ae;&d;: Behealda&d; eow &d;&ae;t ge ne gehefegien eowre heortan mid ofer&ae;te &amp; oferdrynce &amp; mid monigfaldre gieminge &d;isse worolde. 
 &amp; eac he geicte &d;&ae;rto ege  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;yl&ae;s eow hr&ae;dlice on becume se f&ae;rlica domes d&ae;g. 
 &D;&ae;s d&ae;ges tocyme hwelc he beo he cy&d;de  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: He cym&d; sua sua grin ofer ealle &d;a &d;e eardia&d; ofer eor&d;an. 
 Ond eft he cu&ae;&d;: Ne m&ae;g nan mon twam hlafordum hieran. 
 Ond eac cu&ae;&d; Paulus  &d;a &d;a he wolde arwier&d;ra monna mod from &d;isses middangeardes geferr&ae;denne ateon  sui&d;e sui&d;e he him wi&d;br&ae;d  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ne scyle nan Godes &d;eow hine selfne to ungemetlice bindan on woruldscipum  &d;yl&ae;s he mislicige &d;&ae;m &d;e he &ae;r hine selfne gesealde. 
 &D;a &d;a he l&ae;rde &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;re ciricean &d;egnas scoldon stilnesse &d;&ae;re &d;enunga habban  &d;a l&ae;rde he hi eac hu hie hie ge&ae;mettian scoldon o&d;erra weorca; 
 He cu&ae;&d;: Gif ge ymb woroldcunde domas beon scylen  &d;onne nime ge &d;a &d;e on &d;&ae;m hirede unweor&d;uste sien  &amp; setta&d; &d;a to domerum  &d;&ae;t hie strienen &amp; stihtien ymb &d;a eor&d;lican &d;ing  &d;a &d;e ne beo&d; sua sui&d;e geweor&d;ode mid &d;&ae;m g&ae;stlicum giefum. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: Gedo&d; &d;&ae;t hie sien on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum nytte  gif hie on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum ne cunnen. 
 Be &d;&ae;m eac Moyses  se &d;e w&ae;s Gode sua weor&d; &d;&ae;t he oft wi&d; hine selfne spr&ae;c  &ae;t sume cierre Githro his sueor  &d;eah he h&ae;&d;en &amp; el&d;iodig w&ae;re  hine t&ae;lde &amp; s&ae;de &d;&ae;t he on dyslicum gesuincum w&ae;re mid &d;&ae;s folces eor&d;lican &d;eowote  ac l&ae;rde hine &d;&ae;t he gesette o&d;re for hine to demenne betweox &d;&ae;m folce ymbe hira geflita  &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re &d;&ae;s &d;e freorra to ongietanne &d;a dieglan &amp; &d;a g&ae;stlican &d;ing  &d;&ae;t he meahte &d;&ae;t folc &d;y wislicor &amp; &d;y r&ae;dlicor l&ae;ran; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;a hlafordas &amp; &d;a recceras scoldon &d;encean ymb &d;&ae;t helicuste  &amp; &d;a under&d;ioddan scoldon don &d;&ae;t unweor&d;licre. 
 &D;a recceras sceolon bion beforan &d;&ae;m folce sua sua monnes eage beforan his lichoman  his weg &amp; his st&ae;pas to sceawianne. 
 &D;onne is &d;earf &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t dust &d;isse eor&d;lican giemenne ne a&d;is&d;rige &d;&ae;t eage &d;&ae;s recceres  for&d;&ae;m ealle &d;a &d;e ofer o&d;re bio&d;  bio&d; heafda &d;ara &d;e &d;&ae;runder bio&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t heafod sceal wisian &d;&ae;m fotum  &d;&ae;t hie st&ae;ppen on ryhtne weg: ufone sceal &d;&ae;t heafod giman &d;&ae;t &d;a fet ne asliden on &d;&ae;m f&ae;relte  for&d;&ae;m  gif &d;a fet weor&d;a&d; ascrencte  eal se lichoma wier&d; gebiged  &amp; &d;&ae;t heafod gecym&d; on &d;&ae;re eor&d;an. 
 Hu gerades m&ae;g &d;onne se biscep brucan &d;&ae;re hirdelican are  gif he self drohta&d; on &d;am eor&d;licum tielongum &d;e he o&d;rum monnum lean sceolde? 
 For&d;&ae;m ryhtan edleane Dryhten &d;reade &d;urh &d;one witgan  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Suelc &d;&ae;t folc bi&d;  suelc bi&d; se sacerd. 
 &D;onne bi&d; se sacerd suelc suelc &d;&ae;t folc bi&d;  &d;onne he &d;&ae;t ilce de&d; &d;&ae;t hie do&d;  &amp; his on &d;a ilcan wisan tiela&d; &d;e hie do&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t ongeat Heremias se witga  &d;a &d;a he sui&d;e sarlice weop  &amp; spr&ae;c suelce &d;&ae;t templ w&ae;re eal toworpen; 
 He cu&ae;&d;: Eala  hwy is &d;is gold adeorcad? 
 &amp; &d;&ae;t &ae;&d;eleste hiew hwy wear&d; hit onhworfen? 
 Toworpne sint &d;a stanas &d;&ae;s temples  &amp; licggea&d; &ae;t &ae;lcre str&ae;te ende. 
 Hu&ae;t tacna&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t gold &d;e is sua diorwyr&d;e ofer eall ondweorc  buton &d;a heanesse &d;&ae;s haligdomes? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t getacna&d; &d;&ae;t &ae;&d;ele hiew buton &d;a arwyr&d;nes &d;&ae;re &ae;fes&d;nesse  &d;e eallum monnum is to lufigenne? 
 Hw&ae;t getacnia&d; eac &d;a stanas &d;&ae;s halgan huses buton &d;one had &d;&ae;re halgan endebyrdnesse? 
 Hw&ae;t getacna&d; eac sio rume str&ae;t butan &d;one widan weg &d;isses andwerdan lifes? 
 Be &d;am ruman wege sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes  &d;&ae;t is Crist  &d;urh hine selfne he cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t is sui&d;e rum weg &amp; widgille &d;e l&ae;t to f&ae;rwyrde. 
 Ac &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t gold asueartod  &d;onne sio halignes monnes lifes bi&d; mid eor&d;licum weorcum gewemmed. 
 Ond &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t &ae;&d;eleste hiw onhworfen  &d;onne se &ae;ht &d;ara godra weorca  &d;e he &ae;r beeode  bi&d; gewanod  for&d;&ae;m&d;e menn &ae;r wendon &d;&ae;t he &ae;f&ae;s&d;lice drohtode. 
 Ac &d;onne hwelc &ae;fter halgum hade hine selfne f&ae;stlice geimpa&d; on eor&d;licum weorcum  &d;onne bi&d; hit suelc &d;&ae;t f&ae;gere hiw &d;&ae;s goldes sie onhworfen  &amp; hit sie ablacod &amp; forsewen for monna eagum. 
 &amp; &d;a giemmas &d;ara halignessa licggea&d; toworpne &ae;fter str&ae;ta endum. 
 &D;onne licggea&d; &d;a giemmas toworpne &ae;fter str&ae;tum  &d;onne &d;a menn &d;e hie selfe to &d;&ae;re ciricean wlite &ae;mtegian sceoldon on &d;&ae;m dieglum &d;enungum &d;&ae;s temples  &d;onne hie ute wilnia&d; &d;ara rumena wega &d;isse worulde. 
 So&d;lice &d;a gimmas &d;ara halignessa to &d;&ae;m w&ae;ron gemacod &d;&ae;t hi scoldon scinan on &d;&ae;s hiehstan sacerdes hr&ae;gle betwux &d;am halegestan halignessum. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;a sacerdas to &ae;f&ae;s&d;nessum &amp; weor&d;unga ures Aliesendes ne b&ae;da&d; &d;a &d;e him under&d;iedde bio&d; mid hira lifes geearnungum  &d;onne ne beo&d; hira &d;&ae;re halegestan halignesse gimmas on &d;&ae;m gerenum &d;&ae;s biscepes gierelan  ac licggea&d; toworpne &ae;fter str&ae;tum  &d;onne &d;a hadas &d;&ae;re halgan endebyrdnesse beo&d; forgiefene &d;&ae;m widgillan wegum hiera agenra lusta  &amp; beo&d; getigede to eor&d;licum tielengum. 
 Eac is to witanne &d;&ae;t he ne cu&ae;&d; na &d;&ae;t &d;a giemmas w&ae;ren forsceadne &ae;fter &d;&ae;m str&ae;tum  ac &ae;t &d;ara str&ae;ta endum; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;eah hie woroldcundlice drohtigen  hie wilinia&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;yncen &d;a betstan  ond &d;eah hie gan on &d;one ruman weg hiera agnes willan &amp; lustfulnesse  hie wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie mon h&ae;bbe for &d;a betstan &amp; &d;a halgestan. 
 &amp; sua&d;eah hwilum sint to ge&d;afianne for nied&d;earfe &d;as eor&d;lican tielunga  &amp; n&ae;fre &d;eah to sui&d;e ne lufige  &d;yl&ae;s hie gehefegien &d;&ae;s monnes mod &d;e hi to sui&d;e lufa&d;  &d;&ae;t he for &d;&ae;re byr&d;enne gehefegad &amp; ofersui&d;ed  ne sie besenced of &d;&ae;m ymestun to &d;&ae;m nio&d;emestum. 
 Ond sua&d;eah monige underfo&d; heorde  &amp; &d;eah wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie beon freo &amp; &ae;mtige synderlice him selfum to g&ae;stlicum weorcum  &amp; noldon beon abisgode nane wuht on eor&d;licum &d;ingum. 
 &D;a &d;onne hie eallinga agiemeleasia&d; &d;one ymbhogan woruldcundra &d;inga  &d;onne ne gefultuma&d; he nawuht to his hieremonna nied&d;earfe. 
 For&d;&ae;m wyr&d; oft forsewen &d;ara monna lar  &d;onne hie t&ae;la&d; &amp; hatiga&d; hiera hieramonna un&d;eawas  &amp; ne doo&d; him nan o&d;er god &d;isse weorolde; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t word &d;&ae;re lare ne m&ae;g &d;urhfaran &d;&ae;s w&ae;dlan heortan  gif he n&ae;f&d; &d;a are &d;e he on beon m&ae;ge. 
 Ac &d;onne grew&d; &d;&ae;t s&ae;d sui&d;e wel &d;ara worda  &d;onne sio mildheortnes &d;&ae;s lareowes ge&d;w&ae;n&d; &amp; gelec&d; &d;a breost &d;&ae;s gehierendes. 
 For&d;&ae;m is nied&d;earf &d;&ae;m reccere &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge &amp; cunne o&d;erra monna innge&d;onc giendgeotan &amp; gew&ae;terian  &amp; hie eac on hiera nied&d;earfum utane besio. 
 Sua sculon &d;a hierdas weallan ymb &d;a geornfulnesse &d;&ae;re inneran &d;earfe his hieremonna  &d;&ae;t he ne forl&ae;te &d;a giemenne hira uterran &d;earfe. 
 Niede sceal bion gebrocen &d;&ae;t mod &d;ara hieremonna  gif se lareow &amp; se hierde agiemeleasa&d; &d;&ae;t he hiera utan ne helpe. 
 Be &d;&ae;m se forma hierde sanctus Petrus geornfullice monode  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Ic  eower emn&d;eowa &amp; Cristes &d;rowunge gewita  ic eow healsige &d;&ae;t ge feden Godes heorde &d;e under eow is. 
 Sui&d;e hr&ae;&d;e &ae;fter &d;on he gecy&d;de hw&ae;&d;er he m&ae;nde  &d;e &d;&ae;s modes foster &d;e &d;&ae;s lichoman  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ungeniedde  mid eowrum agenum willan  ge sculon &d;encean for eowre heorde Godes &d;onces  nals na for frace&d;lecum gestreonum. 
 Mid &d;&ae;m wordum fullice he us warode &amp; l&ae;rde &d;&ae;tte &d;onne hie gefylden &amp; gebeten &d;a w&ae;dle hiera hieremonna  hie ne wurdon self ofsl&ae;gene mid &d;am sueorde &d;&ae;re gitsunge  &d;&ae;tte &d;onne hira niehstan &d;urh hie beo&d; gereorde &amp; gearode &d;&ae;t hie selfe ne f&ae;sten &d;&ae;s hlafes ryhtwisnesse. 
 &D;as ilcan geornfulnesse &d;ara hierda sanctus Paulus aweahte  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Se &d;e ne gim&d; &d;ara &d;e his beo&d;  &amp; huru Godes &d;eowa  he wi&d;s&ae;c&d; Godes geleafan  &amp; he bi&d; treowleas. 
 &amp; sua&d;eah betuoxn &d;issum simle is to ondr&ae;denne &amp; geornlice to behealdenne  &d;onne hie &d;a uterran &d;ing don sculon  &d;&ae;t hie ne sien &d;&ae;m innecundan inge&d;once afierrede; 
 For&d;&ae;m oft &d;a heortan &d;ara reccera  sua sua we &ae;r cu&ae;don  &d;onne hie mid &d;issum hwilendlicum &d;ingum hie selfe abisegia&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;m unw&ae;rlice &d;iowia&d;  hi &d;onne l&ae;ta&d; acolian &d;a innecundan lufan  &amp; ne ondr&ae;da&d; him na &d;&ae;t hie forgieten &d;&ae;t hie underfengon &d;one recedom monna saula. 
 Ac hit is &d;earf &d;&ae;tte sio giemen  &d;e hie hira hiremonnum utan don scylen  sie wel gemetgod. 
 Be &d;&ae;m sui&d;e wel w&ae;s gecueden to Ezechiele &d;&ae;m witgan &d;&ae;tte &d;a sacerdas ne scoldon no hiera heafdu scieran mid scierseaxum  ne eft hi ne scoldon hira loccas l&ae;tan weaxan  ac hie scoldon hie efsigean mid scearum. 
 Sui&d;e ryhte &d;a sacerdas sint gehatene sacerdas  &d;&ae;t is on Englisc cl&ae;nseras  for&d;&ae;m hie sculon latteowdom gearwian &d;&ae;m geleaffullum &amp; him sculon fore beon. 
 &D;&ae;t feax &d;onne on hira heafde getacna&d; &d;a uterran ge&d;ohtas  &d;&ae;t grew&d; &amp; scin&d; ofer &d;&ae;m br&ae;gene  &amp; his mon &d;eah ne gefred; 
 &D;a giemen &d;ises andweardan lifes &d;&ae;t getacna&d;. 
 Sua giemeleaslice oft sceaca&d; ure ge&d;ohtas from us  &d;&ae;t we his fur&d;um ne gefreda&d;  &d;on ma &d;e mon his feax m&ae;g gefredan butan &d;am felle  for&d;&ae;m we oft ymb ungedafenlice wisan smeagea&d;. 
 Ond sua&d;eah ealle &d;a &d;e for o&d;rum beon sculon  sculon habban giemenne &d;issa uterrena &d;inga  ond &d;eah ne sien hi to f&ae;ste to gebundene. 
 Sui&d;e ryhte w&ae;s &d;&ae;m sacerde forboden &d;&ae;t he his heafod sceare  &amp; eac &d;&ae;t he his feax lete weaxan; 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he ealle &d;a ge&d;ohtas of his mode ne aceorfe &d;e he scyle his hieremonnum to nytte habban  ne eft he ne l&ae;te forweahsan to sui&d;e to unnytte &amp; to unryhte. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecueden &d;&ae;t se efsigenda efsode his heafod  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he sua geornfullice sie ymb &d;a giemenne &d;issa hwilendlicra &d;inga sua sua hit nied&d;earf sie  ond &d;eah sua sua he m&ae;ge hie i&d;elice butan sare of aceorfan &d;&ae;t hie to ungemetlice ne forweaxen; 
 &D;yl&ae;s  &d;onne &d;&ae;t lif &d;&ae;s lichoman bi&d; gescil&d;ed  &d;&ae;t innege&d;onc sie gebunden to &d;&ae;re heortan for &d;&ae;re ungemetgunge &d;&ae;s ymbehogan &d;ara uterra &d;inga; 
 Sua sindon &d;a loccas to sparienne &d;&ae;m sacerde &d;&ae;t hi &d;a hyde behelien  &amp; &d;eah &d;&ae;t he hie forceorfe &ae;r  &ae;r hie on &d;a eagan feallen. 
 &D;&ae;tte se reccere his godan weorc for gielpe anum ne do  ac ma for Godes lufan. 
 Betueox &d;issum is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t se reccere geornlice wacige &amp; &d;ence &d;&ae;t hine ne cnysse sio wilnung &d;&ae;t he scyle monnum licigean; 
 For&d;am  &d;onne he geornlice ongiett &d;a inneran &amp; &d;a g&ae;stlican &d;ing on his inge&d;once  &amp; sui&d;e wel gieme&d; &d;ara uterra &d;inga  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne ma ne wilnige &d;&ae;t he self licige his hieremonnum &d;onne Gode; 
 &D;yl&ae;s &d;onne he mid godum weorcum bi&d; underwre&d;ed  &amp; from woruldmonnum ongiten suelce he sie &ae;l&d;iedig on &d;iosum middangearde  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne for &d;&ae;re wilnunga his agnes gielpes &amp; heringe ne weor&d;e &ae;l&d;iodig from Gode. 
 Se bi&d; eallinga Godes gewinna se se &d;e wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe &d;a weor&d;unga for his godan weorcum &d;e God habban sceolde &ae;t &d;&ae;m folce. 
 Hw&ae;t we genoh georne witon &d;&ae;t se esne &d;e &ae;renda&d; his woroldhlaforde wifes  &d;&ae;t he bi&d; diernes gelires scyldig wi&d; God  &amp; wi&d; his hlaford eallenga forworht  gif he wilna&d; &d;&ae;t hio hine lufige  &amp; he hire licige bet &d;onne se &d;e hine &amp; &d;&ae;t feoh &d;ider sende. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;&ae;t selflice gegriep&d; &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s recceres  &amp; he wilna&d; ungemetlice licigean  &d;onne ber&ae;st he oft on ungemetlice cueminge  &amp; bi&d; hwilum to ungemetlice sme&d;e  hwilum to ungemetlice re&d;e. 
 &D;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t mod awacod &d;&ae;s recceres  &d;onne he gesih&d; &d;&ae;t his hieremen agylta&d;  &amp; he nyle hie arasian  &d;yl&ae;s hira lufu aslacige  &amp; he him &d;e wirs licige. 
 Ac &d;one gedwolan his hieremonna &d;e he stieran sceolde he oft to sui&d;e ge&d;afa&d;  &d;onne he ne dear hie &d;reagean for &d;&ae;re olicunge. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecueden &d;urh &d;one witgan: Wa &d;&ae;m &d;e willa&d; under &ae;lcne elnbogan lecggean pyle &amp; bolster under &ae;lcne hneccan menn mid to gefonne. 
 Se lege&d; pyle under &ae;lces monnes elnbogan  se &d;e mid li&d;um oliccungum wile l&ae;cnian &d;a men &d;e siga&d; on &d;isses middangeardes lufan  o&d;&d;&ae;t hie afealla&d; of hiera ryhtwisnessum. 
 &D;onne bi&d; se elnboga underled mid pyle &amp; se hnecca mid bolstre  &d;onne &d;&ae;m synfullan menn bi&d; oftogen &d;&ae;t hine mon sti&d;lice arasige. 
 &D;onne hine mon ne cnys&d; mid nanre re&d;nesse ne nanre wi&d;ercue&d;nisse  &d;onne ge&d;afa&d; him mon on &d;&ae;re hnescean olecunge &d;&ae;t he hine sui&d;e softe res&d; on his agnum gedwolan. 
 Ac &d;a recceras &d;e hira agnes gilpes gierna&d;  &d;&ae;m hie ge&d;afiga&d; &d;yllic &d;e hie ondr&ae;da&d; &d;&ae;t him derian m&ae;ge &ae;t &d;&ae;m gielpe  &amp; him oftion m&ae;ge &d;isses eor&d;lican weor&d;scipes. 
 Ac &d;a &d;e hi wena&d; &d;&ae;t him nan wuht la&d;es ne wi&d;erweardes don ne m&ae;ge  &d;a hie sui&d;e sti&d;lice arasigea&d;  &amp; mid ealle of&d;ryscea&d;; 
 Ond hie n&ae;fre bilwitlice willa&d; monigean  ac hie ofergieta&d; &d;&ae;re hirdelican lufan  &amp; egesia&d; hie &amp; &d;reatigea&d; mid onwalde sua sua hlafordas. 
 &D;as &d;onne w&ae;ron &d;urh &d;one witgan sui&d;e ryhtlice ge&d;reade mid &d;&ae;re godcundan stefne  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ge budon sui&d;e riclice &amp; sui&d;e agendlice. 
 &D;&ae;t is be &d;&ae;m &d;e ma lufigea&d; hie selfe &amp; hiera agenne weor&d;scipe &d;onne hiera Hlafurdes. 
 Hie &d;onne ahebba&d; hie ofer hiera hieremenn  &amp; &d;encea&d; a hw&ae;t hie don m&ae;gen  &amp; ne &d;encea&d; no hw&ae;t hie don scoldon  &amp; ne ondr&ae;da&d; &d;one dom &d;e &d;&ae;r&ae;fter fylg&d;; 
 Ac sui&d;e scamleaslice gielpa&d; &d;isses hwilendlican onwaldes  &amp; lica&d; him &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t unaliefede do&d; aliefedlice  &amp; hiera hieremonna him nan ne wi&d;cui&d;. 
 Se &d;onne &d;e wilna&d; woh to donne  &amp; wilna&d; &d;eah &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;s o&d;re menn sugigen  he &d;onne bi&d; him selfum gewuta &d;&ae;t he wilna&d; ma &d;&ae;t hine mon lufige &d;onne ryhtwisnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m nan man nis &d;e eallunga sua libban m&ae;ge &d;&ae;t he hwilum ne agylte. 
 Se &d;onne wilna&d; sui&d;ur &d;&ae;t mon lufige so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse &d;onne hine selfne  se &d;e wilna&d; &d;&ae;t mon nanre ryhtwisnesse fore him ne wandige. 
 For &d;iosum &d;ingum sanctus Petrus anfeng sui&d;e lustlice Paules t&ae;linge. 
 Ond eft Daui&d; se kyning anfeng sui&d;e ea&d;modlice his agnes &d;egnes cease  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s Nathan se witga. 
 For&d;&ae;m eac &d;a godan recceras  &d;onne hie ne reccea&d; hw&ae;&d;er mon hie selfe synderlice &amp; ungemetlice lufige  hie wena&d;  &d;eah hira hieremenn hie mid ryhte heregen for hiera agnum gewyrhtum  &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t don for lufan &amp; for ea&d;modnesse  nals for his geearnungum. 
 &D;onne is sui&d;e micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t we mid micle cr&ae;fte betueox &d;issum gemetgien &d;a gemetgunge &d;&ae;s reccedomes  &d;&ae;tte &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod &d;ara under&d;iedra hw&ae;thwugu ryhtlices ongitan m&ae;g  &d;&ae;t hit &d;onne sua bald sie for his freodome &d;&ae;t hit ne gewende on selflice &amp; on ofermetto  &d;onne his hlaford him to ungemetlicne anwald forgief&d; his spr&ae;cce  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne for&d;&ae;m ne forgiete ne ne forl&ae;te his ea&d;modnesse. 
 Ond &d;eah wel gedafona&d; &d;&ae;tte &d;a godan recceras wilnigen &d;&ae;t hie monnum licigen  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte &d;urh &d;a licunga hi m&ae;gen gedon &d;&ae;tte hiera Dryhten licige &d;&ae;m folce  &amp; hie m&ae;gen geteon &d;urh &d;a eahtunge &d;e hie mon eahtige hira niehstan to &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse lufan; 
 Nalles for&d;&ae;m anum &d;e hie wilnigen &d;&ae;t hi mon synderlice lufige  ac swelce sio hira lufu si sum weg &d;urh &d;one hie m&ae;gen l&ae;dan &d;a heortan &d;e hie gehiran willa&d; to &d;&ae;re lufan ures Scippendes. 
 Ac hit is &d;eah sui&d;e earfe&d;d&ae;de &d;&ae;t mon lustlice &d;one lareow gehieran wille &d;e mon ne lufa&d;. 
 For&d;on se &d;e for o&d;re beon sceal  he sceal tilian &d;&ae;t he licige  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge beon gehiered. 
 &amp; &d;eah &d;a his lufe ne sece he no for him selfum  &d;yl&ae;s he sie ongieten &d;&ae;t he sie wi&d;erwinna on &d;&ae;re diegelnesse his ge&d;ohtes  &d;&ae;s &d;e he bi&d; gesewen &d;eow on his &d;enunge. 
 &D;&ae;t sui&d;e wel sanctus Paulus geopenude  &d;a he us cy&d;de &d;a degolnesse his geornfulnesse  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Sua sua ic wilnige on eallum &d;ingum &d;&ae;t ic monnum cueme &amp; licige. 
 &amp; sua&d;eah eftsona he cu&ae;&d;: Gif ic monnum cueme &amp; licige  &d;onne ne beo ic no Godes &d;eow. 
 Hw&ae;t &d;onne Paulus &ae;g&d;er ge licode ge ne licode; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e on &d;&ae;m &d;e he wilnode licigean  nals no he  &d;eah&d;e he cu&ae;de  ac &d;urh hine he wilnode &d;&ae;t sio so&d;f&ae;stnes monnum licode. 
 &D;&ae;tte se reccere sceal geornlice wietan &d;&ae;tte oft &d;a un&d;eawas leoga&d;  &amp; licetta&d; &d;&ae;t hi sien gode &d;eawas. 
 Eac sceal se reccere witan &d;&ae;t &d;a un&d;eawas beo&d; oft geliccette to godum &d;eawum &amp; to m&ae;genum &d;urh leasunga. 
 Monig mon de&d; micel f&ae;sten  &amp; h&ae;f&d; &d;one hlisan &d;&ae;t he hit do for forh&ae;fdnesse  &amp; de&d; hit &d;eah for hneawnesse &amp; for feohgitsunge. 
 Monig bi&d; agieta his goda &amp; wilna&d; mid &d;y geearnigan &d;one hlisan &d;&ae;t he sie rumgiful  &amp; wena&d; menn &d;&ae;t he hit do for kystum  &amp; bi&d; &d;eah for gielpe ma &d;onne for lufan. 
 &amp; oft eac ungemetlico forgifnes bi&d; gelicet  &d;&ae;t mon wene&d; &d;&ae;t hit sie mildheortnes. 
 Ond oft eac ungemetlicu irsung bi&d; gelicet  &d;&ae;t menn wena&d; &d;&ae;t hit sie ryhtwislic anda. 
 Oft mon bi&d; sui&d;e rempende  &amp; r&ae;s&d; sui&d;e dollice on &ae;lc weorc &amp; hr&ae;dlice  &amp; &d;eah wena&d; men &d;&ae;t hit sie for arodscipe &amp; for hw&ae;tscipe. 
 Oft mon bi&d; sui&d;e wandigende &ae;t &ae;lcum weorce &amp; sui&d;e l&ae;tr&ae;de  &amp; wena&d; menn &d;&ae;t hit sie for suarmodnesse &amp; for unarodscipe  &amp; bi&d; &d;eah for wisdome &amp; for w&ae;rscipe. 
 For&d;&ae;m is micel nied&d;earf &d;&ae;t se reccere &d;a &d;eawas &amp; &d;a un&d;eawas cunne wel toscadan  &d;yl&ae;s se hneawa &amp; se gitsigenda f&ae;gnige &d;&ae;s &d;&ae;tte menn wenen &d;&ae;t he sie gehealdsum on &d;&ae;m &d;e he healdan scyle o&d;&d;e d&ae;lan. 
 O&d;&d;e eft se gielpna &amp; se agita for his goda mierringe gielpe  &amp; wene &d;&ae;t he sie kystig &amp; mildheort. 
 O&d;&d;e eft se &d;afetere  se &d;e wile forgiefan &d;&ae;t he wrecan sceolde  to ecum witum geteo his hieremenn. 
 O&d;&d;e eft se &d;e ungemetlice wric&d; &d;a scylda  &d;&ae;t he self sui&d;ur on &d;&ae;m ne gesyngige. 
 O&d;&d;e eft &d;&ae;t he ryhtlice &amp; sti&d;lice wrecan sceolde  &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t ne forielde  &d;yl&ae;s se ryhtwislica anda acolige  &d;&ae;t he hit eft sua ea&d;e wrecan ne m&ae;ge  &d;&ae;tte for&d;y to ungemetlice ne sie geli&d;od &d;&ae;m scyldgan  &d;yl&ae;s him &d;&ae;s godan weorces lean losige &d;e he mid &d;&ae;re steore geearnian sceolde. 
 Hu gesceadwis se reccere sceal bion on his &d;reaunga &amp; on his oleccunga  &amp; eac on his hatheortnesse &amp; on his mon&d;w&ae;rnesse. 
 Eac is to wietanne &d;&ae;tte hwilum bi&d; god w&ae;rlice to mi&d;anne his hieremonna scylda &amp; to licettanne suelce he hit nyte; hwilum eft to secganne; hwilum  &d;eah hit mon cu&d;lice wite  hit is to forberanne; 
 Hwilum eft smealice &amp; geornlice to seccanne; 
 Hwilum li&d;elice to &d;reatianne; 
 Hwilum sui&d;lice &amp; str&ae;clice to &d;rafianne. 
 Monige sint  swa swa we &ae;r cu&ae;don  &d;e mon sceal w&ae;rlice liccettan  &amp; &d;eahhw&ae;&d;re eft cy&d;an  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t hie ongieten &d;&ae;t hie mon t&ae;le  &amp; &d;&ae;t ea&d;modlice ge&d;afigen  &amp; &d;onne &d;a scylda &d;e hie diogollice on him selfum forbera&d; hie geornlice on hiera agnum inge&d;once sceawigen  &amp; on him selfum demen &amp; wrecen  &amp; hie forscamige &d;&ae;t hie eft sua don; 
 &D;onne bi&d; he self geladod wi&d; hine selfne mid his agenre scame &amp; mid his ge&d;ylde &amp; eac mid his recceres. 
 Be &d;&ae;re ildinge sui&d;e wel Dryhten &d;reade Iudeas  &d;a he &d;urh &d;one witgan cu&ae;&d;: Ge sindon leogende: n&ae;ron ge no min gemunende  ne ge no ne ge&d;ohton on eowerre heortan &d;&ae;t ic suugode  suelce ic hit ne gesawe. 
 He ilde  &amp; &d;afode &d;a scylda  &amp; &d;eah he him gecy&d;de; 
 &D;eah &d;e he wi&d; &d;a scyldgiendan swugode  he hit him &d;eah suigende ges&ae;de. 
 Ac monige scylda openlice witene beo&d; to forberanne  &d;onne &d;&ae;s &d;inges tima ne bi&d; &d;&ae;t hit mon sidelice gebetan m&ae;ge. 
 Swa se l&ae;ce  &d;onne he on untiman lacna&d; wunde  hio wyrmse&d; &amp; rota&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m buton he &d;one timan aredige &d;&ae;s l&ae;cedomes &d;onne bi&d; hit swutol &d;&ae;t se lacnigenda forlies&d; &d;one cr&ae;ft his l&ae;cedomes. 
 Ac &d;onne se lareow ieldende sec&d; &d;one timan &d;e he his hieremenn sidelice on &d;reatigean m&ae;ge  &d;onne bi&d; hit swutol &d;&ae;t he bier&d; on his ge&d;ylde &d;a byr&d;enne hira scylda. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is swi&d;e wel gecueden &d;urh &d;one salmsceop  he cw&ae;&d;: &d;a synfullan bytledon uppe on minum hrygge. 
 He sarette &d;&ae;tte &d;a synfullan sceoldon bytlan onuppan his hrycge  swelce he openlice cu&ae;de: &d;onne ic man geryhtan ne m&ae;g &amp; hine gel&ae;ran  &d;onne bi&d; me suelce ic hine b&ae;re uppe on minum hrycge. 
 Ac manegu diglu &d;ing sindon nearolice to smeageanne  &d;&ae;tte se reccere m&ae;ge ongietan be sumum tacnum on his hieremonna mode eal &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r gehyddes lutige  &amp; on &d;&ae;m anbide &d;e he hira fandige  &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge hwilum ongietan micel of lytlum. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte to Ezechiele &d;&ae;m witgan gecueden: &d;u monnes sunu  &d;urh&d;yrela &d;one wag. 
 &D;a ic &d;a &d;one wah &d;urh&d;yreludne h&ae;fde  cu&ae;&d; se witga  &d;a iewde he me ane duru beinnan &d;&ae;m wealle  &amp; cu&ae;&d; to me: Gong inn  geseoh &d;a scande &amp; &d;a wierrestan &d;ing &d;e &d;as menn her do&d;. 
 Ic &d;a eode inn  &amp; geseah &d;&ae;r &d;a anlicnessa eallra creopendra wuhta &amp; ealra anscunigendlicra nietena  &amp; ealle &d;a hearga Israhela folces w&ae;ron atiefrede on &d;&ae;m wage.

 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecueden: Gong inn  &amp; geseoh &d;a heards&ae;l&d;a &amp; &d;a sconde &d;e &d;as her do&d;.

 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s eac gecueden: Ic &d;a eode inn  &amp; geseah &d;a anlicnessa ealra creopendra wuhta &amp; eac onscuniendlicra nietena. 
 &D;a creopendan wuhta getacnigea&d; &d;a eor&d;lican ge&d;ohtas. 
 &D;a nietenu &d;onne beo&d; hw&ae;thwuguningas from eor&d;an ah&ae;fen  &amp; sua&d;eah onluta&d; to &d;&ae;re eor&d;an for&d;&ae;m hie sculon bi &d;&ae;re libban. 
 &D;a creopendan &amp; &d;a scnicendan licgea&d; mid ealle lichoman on eor&d;an. 
 &D;a nietenu &d;onne  &d;eah hie maran sien  hie beo&d; sui&d;ur ah&ae;fen from eor&d;an  &amp; sua&d;eah for &d;&ae;re gewilnunge hiera giefernesse hie simle locigea&d; to &d;&ae;re eor&d;an. 
 &D;a creopendan wuhta beinnan &d;am wage getacnia&d; &d;a inge&d;oncas &d;e wealca&d; in &d;&ae;s monnes mode  &d;e &ae;fre willa&d; licgean on &d;&ae;m eor&d;licum gewilnungum. 
 &D;a nietenu &d;onne &d;e he geseah binnan &d;&ae;m wage getacnigea&d; &d;onne mon hw&ae;t ryhtlices &amp; gerisenlices ge&d;enc&d;  &d;onne ne lige&d; he eallinga on &d;&ae;re eor&d;an sua &d;a creopendan wuhta  ac bi&d; hw&ae;thwugu upah&ae;fen sua &d;&ae;t neat from eor&d;an; 
 Ac for &d;&ae;re gewilnunga woroldgielpes &amp; gietsunga he onlytt ungerisenlice to &d;issum eor&d;licum  sua &d;&ae;t neat for gifernesse onlyt to &d;&ae;re eor&d;an. 
 Eac w&ae;s gesewen on &d;&ae;m wage atifred ealle &d;a heargas Israhela folces  &amp; eac sio gietsung &d;e sanctus Paulus cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t w&ae;re hearga &amp; idelnesse gefera. 
 Sui&d;e ryhtlice hit w&ae;s awriten &ae;fter &d;&ae;m nitenum &d;&ae;t &d;a heargas w&ae;ron atiefrede  for&d;am &d;eah &d;e ful monige mid gerisenlicum weorcum arisen from eor&d;an  mid ungerisenlicum gewilnungum &d;issa worold&d;inga hie hie selfe alecgea&d; on eor&d;an.
