 Eac is to wietanne &d;&ae;t &ae;res&d; bi&d; se wah &d;urh&d;yrelod  &amp; si&d;&d;an mon wyrc&d; duru to. 
 Gif sio &d;onne ontyned bi&d;  &d;onne m&ae;g mon geseon gif &d;&ae;r hwelc dieglu scond inne bi&d;  sua se witga dyde. 
 Feorrane &d;u meaht geseon  gif se wah bi&d; &d;yrel  ac &d;u ne meaht geseon hw&ae;t &d;&ae;rinne bi&d; gehyddes  buton &d;u &d;a duru ontyne. 
 Sua &d;u meaht &ae;lcne un&d;eaw on &d;&ae;m menn &ae;res&d; be sumum tacnum ongietan  hw&ae;s &d;u wenan scealt  &ae;r he hit mid wordum o&d;&d;e mid weorcum cy&d;e. 
 Sie&d;&d;an he hit &d;onne mid &d;ara aw&d;rum cy&d;  &d;onne bi&d; sio duru &d;&ae;re unryhtwisnesse ontyned &d;&ae;t &d;u meaht geseon eall &d;&ae;t yfel openlice &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;rinne luta&d;. 
 Monige hira &d;onne sindon sui&d;e li&d;elice to &d;reageanne  &d;onne he of yfelum willan ne gesynga&d;  ac of unwisdome &amp; ungewisses o&d;&d;e ungewealdes o&d;&d;e of fl&ae;sclicum gecynde o&d;&d;e of wacmodnesse &amp; of unbieldo o&d;&d;e of untrymnesse modes o&d;&d;e lichoman. 
 For&d;&ae;m is sui&d;e micel nied&d;earf &d;&ae;t mon mid micelre gemetgunge suelcra scylda &d;reaunga geli&d;ige &amp; gemetgie  for&d;&ae;m&d;e we ealle  &d;e hwile &d;e we libba&d; on &d;issum deadlican fl&ae;sce  &d;&ae;re tidernesse &amp; &d;&ae;re hnescnesse ures fl&ae;sces we beo&d; under&d;iedde. 
 Bi him selfum &ae;lc mon sceal ge&d;encean hu he o&d;rum deman wille  &d;yl&ae;s he sie ongieten &d;&ae;t he sie onstyred &amp; on&ae;led mid &d;&ae;m andan his hieremonna un&d;eawa  &amp; h&ae;bbe hine selfne forgietenne. 
 Be &d;&ae;m sui&d;e wel Paulus us manode  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Gif hwa sie abisegod mid hwelcum scyldum  ge &d;onne &d;e g&ae;s&d;lice sindon gel&ae;ra&d; &d;a suelcan mid monn&d;w&ae;rnesse g&ae;ste; 
 Gesceawia&d; eow selfe  &d;yl&ae;s eow becume costung. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de; 
 &D;onne eow mislicia&d; &d;a mettrumnessa &d;a ge on o&d;rum monnum geseo&d;  &d;onne ge&d;ence ge hw&ae;t ge sien &amp; hwelce ge sien; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t ge eower mod gemetgien on &d;&ae;m ni&d;e  &d;onne ge eow selfum ondr&ae;da&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t ge on o&d;rum monnum t&ae;la&d;. 
 Ond &d;eah sindon monige sui&d;e sui&d;e to &d;reageanne  &d;onne hie selfe nylla&d; ongietan hiera scylda  &d;&ae;t hi &d;onne gehieren &d;reagende of &d;&ae;s lariowes mu&d;e hu micle byr&d;enne hie habba&d; on hiera scyldum; 
 &D;onne hie willa&d; him selfum &d;&ae;t yfel &d;&ae;t hie &d;urtugon to sui&d;e gelihtan  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne ondr&ae;den for &d;&ae;s lareowes &d;reaunga &d;&ae;t hie hit him gehefegigen. 
 &D;&ae;t &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;s recceres ryht &d;&ae;t he &d;urh &d;a stemne his lariowdomes &ae;tiewe &d;&ae;t wuldor &d;&ae;s uplican e&d;les  &amp; hu moniga digla costunga &d;&ae;s ealdan feondes lutigea&d; on &d;ys andweardan life he eac geopenige  ond &d;&ae;t he his hieremonna yfelu to hnesclice forberan ne sceal  ac mid miclum andan &amp; re&d;nesse him stiere  &d;yl&ae;s he sie scyldig ealra hira scylda  &d;onne him hiera na ne of&d;ync&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecueden to Ezechiele: Nim sume tigelan  &amp; lege beforan &d;e  &amp; writ on hiere &d;a burg Hierusalem. 
 &amp; sona &ae;fter &d;&ae;m he cu&ae;&d;: Besitta&d; hie utan  &amp; wyrcea&d; o&d;er f&ae;sten wi&d; hie  &amp; bera&d; hiere hl&ae;d to  &amp; send &d;&ae;rto gefylcio  &amp; &d;ersca&d; &d;one weall mid rammum. 
 &amp; eft he him t&ae;hte to fultome &d;&ae;t he him gename ane iserne hearstepannan  &amp; sette betweoh hine &amp; &d;a burg for iserne weall. 
 Hw&ae;t tacna&d; &d;onne Ezechhiel se witga buton &d;a lareowas  to &d;&ae;m is gecueden: Genim &d;e ane tigelan  &amp; lege beforan &d;e  &amp; writ on hiere &d;a burg Hierusalem? 
 &D;a halgan lareowas &d;onne him nima&d; tigelan  &d;onne hie &d;ara eor&d;licra monna heortan underfo&d; to l&ae;ranne. 
 &D;onne hie lecgea&d; &d;a tieglan beforan hie  &d;e him beboden w&ae;s &d;&ae;t hi scolden &d;a ceastre Hierusalem on awritan  &d;onne hie behealda&d; ealle &d;a innge&d;oncas hiora modes  &amp; sui&d;e geornlice giema&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;a eor&d;lican heortan gel&ae;ren  &amp; him &ae;tiewen hwelc sie &d;&ae;re uplican sibbe gesieh&d;e  &amp; hu on idelnesse man ongiett Godes &d;&ae;t hefonlice wundor  gif he ne ongiett hu monega costunga &d;&ae;s lytegan feondes him on fealla&d;. 
 Sui&d;e wel he hit geicte mid &d;ysum  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ymbsitta&d; &d;a burg sui&d;e gebyrdelice  &amp; getrymia&d; eow wi&d; hie. 
 &D;a halgan lareowas ymbsitta&d; &d;a tieglan  &d;e sio burg Hierusalem on atiefred bi&d;  &d;onne hi &d;am menniscan mode  &d;e &d;eah &d;&ae;t uplice lif sec&d;  &ae;tiewa&d; hu manega him on &d;ys andweardum life frecenlice wi&d;erwearde un&d;eawas him wi&d;feohta&d;  &amp; hu &ae;ghwelc syn bi&d; s&ae;tigende &d;&ae;s &d;iondan monnes. 
 &amp; su&ae; su&ae; se here sceolde bion getrymed onbutan Hierusalem  su&ae; sculon beon getrymed &d;a word &d;&ae;s sacerdes ymbutan &d;&ae;t mod his hieremonna. 
 &amp; ne sceal he no &d;&ae;t an bodigan his hieremonnum hu &d;a synna him wi&d;winna&d;  ac he him sceal eac cy&d;an mid hwelcum cr&ae;ftum he him wi&d;stondan m&ae;g. 
 Swi&d;e ryhtlice w&ae;s se eaca &d;&ae;r to gedon  &d;a mon to &d;&ae;m witgan cu&ae;&d;: Wyrcea&d; f&ae;sten ymb &d;a burg. 
 Wiotodlice f&ae;sten wyrc&d; se halga lariow ymb &d;a burg &d;&ae;s modes &d;e he gel&ae;r&d; &d;one cr&ae;ft hu hit m&ae;g costingum wi&d;stondan  &amp; him eac ges&ae;g&d; hu &d;&ae;m monnum &d;e him m&ae;gen &amp; cr&ae;ft wiex&d;  hu him eac hwilum eakia&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;m m&ae;genum &d;a costunga. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte gecueden: Bera&d; hire to hl&ae;d  &amp; ymbsitta&d; hie  &amp; ga&d; to mid rammum. 
 &D;onne bire&d; &ae;lc lareow hl&ae;d to &d;&ae;s monnes mode  &d;onne he him gecy&d;&d; hu sio byr&d;en wiex&d; &amp; hefega&d;. 
 Eac he ar&ae;&d; ceastre wi&d; Hierusalem  &d;onne he &d;&ae;m ryhtlicum innge&d;once his hieremonna fores&ae;g&d; &d;a dieglan s&ae;tenga &d;&ae;s lytegan feondes  &d;e he him wenan m&ae;g. 
 &amp; eac he bier&d; rammas ymbutan &d;&ae;t mod his hieremonna  &d;onne he him gecy&d; mid hu scearplicum costungum we sint &ae;ghwonon utan behrincgde  &amp; se weall ures m&ae;genes &d;urh&d;yrela&d; mid &d;an scearpan ramman &d;ara costunga. 
 Ond sua&d;eah nu  &d;eah se lareow &d;is eall smealice &amp; openlice gecy&d;e  ne forstent hit him noht  ne him nohte &d;on ma ne beo&d; forl&ae;tna his agna synna  buton he sie on&ae;led mid ryhtwislicum andan wi&d; his hieremonna scylda. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is git sui&d;e ryhtlice gecueden to &d;&ae;m witgan: Genim &d;e ane iserne hierstepannan  &amp; sete betweoxn &d;e &amp; Hierusalem for iserne weall. 
 &D;urh &d;a pannan is getacnod se wielm &d;&ae;s modes  &amp; &d;urh &d;&ae;t isern &d;&ae;t m&ae;gen &d;ara &d;reatunga. 
 Hw&ae;t is &d;ienga &d;e bieterre sie on &d;&ae;s lareowes mode  o&d;&d;e hit sui&d;ur gehierste &amp; gegremige &d;onne se anda &d;e for ryhtwisnesse bi&d; upah&ae;fen? 
 Mid &d;isse pannan hierstinge w&ae;s Paulus onb&ae;rned  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Hwa bi&d; medtrum  &d;&ae;t ic ne sie eac for his &d;ingum seoc? 
 O&d;&d;e hwa bi&d; gescended  &d;&ae;t me for&d;&ae;m ne scamige? 
 Ond sua hwelc sua mid &d;am Godes andan bi&d; on&ae;led  ne bi&d; he for giemeleste gehiened  ac he bi&d; stranglice wi&d; &d;a getrymed on ecnesse. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte gecueden to &d;&ae;m witgan: Sete iserne weall betuh &d;e &amp; &d;a burh. 
 &D;a isernan hierstepannan he t&ae;hte for iserne weall to settanne betuh &d;&ae;m witgan &amp; &d;&ae;re byrig  for&d;am nu &d;a recceras &ae;tiewa&d; sua strangne andan &d;y hie wiella&d; &d;&ae;t hie hiene eft h&ae;bben on &d;&ae;m ecan life betux him &amp; hiera hieremonnum to isernum wealle  &d;&ae;t is to gewitnesse &d;&ae;t hit him ne licode  &d;eah he hit gebetan ne meahte. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne &d;&ae;s recceres mod wyr&d; to re&d;e on &d;&ae;re &d;reaunga  &d;onne abiers&d; &d;&ae;r hwilum hw&ae;thwugu ut &d;&ae;s &d;e he sugian sceolde. 
 Ond oft eac gelimpe&d;  &d;onne he to sui&d;e &amp; to &d;earllice &d;reapian wile his hieremenn  &d;&ae;t his word beo&d; gehwyrfedo to unnyttre oferspr&ae;ce. 
 &D;onne sio &d;reaung bi&d; ungemetgad  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s agyltendan mid ormodnesse ge&d;rysced. 
 For&d;&ae;m is micel &d;earf  &d;onne se re&d;a reccere ongiett &d;&ae;t he his hieremonna mod sui&d;ur gedrefed h&ae;f&d; &d;onne he scolde  &d;&ae;t he sona for&d;&ae;m hreowsige  &d;&ae;t he &d;urh &d;a hreowsunga gemete forgiefnesse beforan &d;&ae;re So&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse &d;&ae;s &d;e he &d;urh &d;a geornfulnesse his andan gesyngade. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce Dryhten God us bisnade &d;urh Moysen  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Gif hwa gonge bilwitlice mid his friend to wuda treow to ceorfanne  &amp; sio &ae;cs &d;onne awient of &d;&ae;m hielfe  &amp; sua ungeweal&d;es ofslie&d; his geferan  he &d;onne sceal fleon to anra &d;ara &d;reora burga &d;e to fri&d;stowe gesette sint &amp; libbe  &d;yl&ae;s hwelc &d;ara niehstena &d;&ae;s ofsl&ae;genan for &d;&ae;m sare his ehte  &amp; hine &d;onne gefoo &amp; ofslea. 
 To wuda we ga&d; mid urum freondum sua oft sua we sceawia&d; ura hieremonna un&d;eawas; 
 &amp; bilwitlice we heawa&d; &d;one wudu  &d;onne we &d;ara gyltendra scylda mid arf&ae;s&d;&d;es inge&d;onces lare anweg aceorfa&d;. 
 Ac sio &ae;cs wint of &d;am hielfe  &amp; eac us of &d;&ae;re honda  &d;onne &d;onne sio lar wint on re&d;nesse sui&d;ur &d;onne mon niede scyle. 
 Sio &ae;cs wient of &d;&ae;m hielfe  &d;onne of &d;&ae;re &d;reatunga ga&d; to sti&d;lico word  &amp; mid &d;am his freond gewunda&d;  o&d;&d;e ofslieh&d;  &d;onne he hine on unrotnesse o&d;&d;e on ormodnesse gebring&d; mid his edwite  &d;eah he hit for lufum do  &d;&ae;t he geopenige his un&d;eawas. 
 Sua&d;eah &d;&ae;t ge&d;reatade mod bi&d; sui&d;e ra&d;e gehwierfed to fiounga  gif him mon to ungemetlice mid &d;&ae;re &d;reapunga oferfylg&d; sui&d;ur &d;onne mon &d;yrfe. 
 Ac se se &d;e unw&ae;rlice &d;one wuda hiew&d;  &amp; sua his freond ofslieh&d;  him bi&d; nid&d;earf &d;&ae;t he fleo to &d;ara &d;reora burga anre  &d;&ae;t on sumere &d;ara weor&d;e genered  &d;&ae;t he mote libban; 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he gehweorfe to hreowsunga  &amp; sua fleo to &d;ara &d;reora burga sumere  &d;&ae;t is tohopa &amp; lufu &amp; geleafa. 
 Se to anra &d;ara burga geflieh&d;  &d;onne m&ae;g he bion orsorg &d;&ae;s monnsliehtes; 
 &D;eah hine &d;&ae;r meten &d;a niehstan &d;&ae;s ofsl&ae;genan  ne slea&d; hi hiene na: for&d;&ae;m &d;onne se &d;earla &amp; se ryhtwisa Dema cym&d;  se &d;e hine on urne geferscipe &d;urh fl&ae;sces gecynd gemengde  ne wriec&d; he mid nanum &d;ingum &d;a scylde on him  for&d;&ae;m under his forgiefnesse hine gefrie&d;ode sio lufu &amp; se geleafa &amp; se tohopa. 
 Hu swi&d;e se reccere sceal beon on his smeaunga abisgod ymb &d;a halgan &ae;. 
 Ac eall &d;iss areda&d; se reccere sui&d;e ryhte  &d;onne he for godes lufum &amp; for Godes ege de&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he de&d;  &amp; &ae;lce d&ae;ge geornfullice smea&d; &d;a bebodu halegra gewrita  &d;&ae;tte on him sie uppar&ae;red se cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;re giemenne ymbe &d;a foresceawunga &d;&ae;s hefonlican lifes  &d;onne singallice &d;isse eor&d;lican drohtunge gewuna wile toweorpan  buton hine sio myndgung &d;ara haligra gewrita onbryrde; 
 For&d;&ae;m se eor&d;lica geferscipe hine tieh&d; on &d;a lufe his ealdan ungewunan  he sceal simle higian &d;&ae;t he weor&d;e onbryrd &amp; geedniwad to &d;&ae;m hefonlican e&d;le. 
 Ac his mod bi&d; sui&d;e ie&d;egende &amp; sui&d;e abisgad mid eor&d;licra monna wordum  for&d;am hit is openlice cu&d; &d;&ae;tte sio uterre abisgung &d;issa worold&d;inga &d;&ae;s monnes mod gedref&d;  &amp; hine scofett hidres &d;&ae;dres  o&d;&d;&ae;t he afiel&d; of his agnum willan; 
 Ac him bi&d; &d;earf &d;&ae;t he hine genime simle be &d;&ae;re leornunge haligra gewrita  &amp; be &d;am arise. 
 For &d;iosum &d;ingum manade Paulus Timotheum his cniht  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: &d;onne ic cume  &d;onne beo &d;u abisgad ymbe r&ae;dinge. 
 &amp; eft Dauit be &d;am ilcan spr&ae;c  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Loca  Dryhten  hu sui&d;e ic lufige &d;ine &ae;; 
 Ealne d&ae;g &d;&ae;t bi&d; min smeaung. 
 Eft bi &d;ys ilcan Dryhten bebead Moyse hu he scolde beran &d;a earce  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Wyrc feower hringas &ae;lgyldene  &amp; ahoh hie sui&d;e f&ae;ste on &d;a feower hyrnan &d;&ae;re earce; 
 &amp; hat wyrcean twegen stengas of &d;&ae;m treowe  &d;e is haten sethim  &d;&ae;t ne wyr&d; n&ae;fre forrotad; 
 &amp; befoh utan mid golde: &amp; sting ut &d;urh &d;a hringas bi &d;&ae;re earce sidan  &d;&ae;t hie man m&ae;ge beran on &d;am  &amp; l&ae;t hi stician &d;&ae;ron; 
 Ne tio hie mon n&ae;fre of. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g &d;onne elles seo earc tacnian buton &d;a halgan ciricean  on &d;&ae;re sculon hangian &d;a feower hringas on &d;am feower hyrnum  &d;&ae;t sint &d;a feower hyrnan &d;ises middangeardes  binnan &d;&ae;m is tobr&ae;dd Godes folc  &d;&ae;t is utan begyrdd mid &d;am feower godspellum? 
 &D;a saglas &d;onne  &d;e mon &d;a earce big beran sceal  sticia&d; eallne weg inn on &d;am hringum &d;a earce mid to beranne  &d;a beo&d; geworht of &d;&ae;m treowe sethim  &d;&ae;t n&ae;fre ne rota&d;. 
 Sua sindon to seceanne stronge &amp; una&d;rotene lareowas &amp; &d;urhwuniende on &d;&ae;re lare haligra boca  &d;a simle sculon bion bodiende ymbe &d;a anmodnesse &d;&ae;re halgan gesomnunga  sua sua &d;a anbestungne saglas &d;a earce bera&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon &d;a earce bere on &d;&ae;m saglum  &d;&ae;tte &d;a godan lareowas &d;a halgan gesomnunge l&ae;rende &d;a niwan &amp; &d;a ungeleaffullan mod mid hira lare gel&ae;de to ryhtum geleafan. 
 &D;a saglas is beboden &d;&ae;t scoldon beon mid golde befongne. 
 &D;&ae;t is  &d;onne &d;a lareowas mid wordum o&d;re menn l&ae;rat  &d;&ae;t hi eac selfe on hira agnum weorcum biorhte scinen. 
 Be &d;am saglum is sui&d;e gesceadlice gecueden &d;&ae;t hie sculon simle stician on &d;am hringum  &amp; n&ae;fre ne moton him beon ofatogene  for&d;&ae;m is micel nied&d;earf &d;&ae;tte &d;a &d;e beo&d; gesette to &d;&ae;re &d;enunga &d;&ae;s lareowdomes &d;&ae;t hi n&ae;fre ne gewiten from &d;&ae;re geornfulnesse &d;&ae;re r&ae;dinge &amp; leornunge haligra gewrita. 
 For&d;&ae;m is eac gecueden &d;&ae;tte simle &d;a ofergyldan saglas sceolden stician on &d;&ae;m gyldnum hringum  &d;yl&ae;s hine &ae;nig wuht g&ae;lde ungearowes  &d;onne mon &d;a earce beran scolde. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;onne &d;ara lareowa hieremenn hw&ae;thwugu g&ae;s&d;lices to him seca&d;  &amp; hi frina&d;  &d;onne is sui&d;e micel scand gif he &d;onne f&ae;r&d; secende hw&ae;t he sellan scyle  &d;onne he iowan scolde &d;&ae;t him mon to asca&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne sticia&d; &d;a saglas sui&d;e singallice on &d;&ae;m hringum  &d;onne &d;a lareowas simle on hira heortum smeaga&d; &d;a halgan gewritu. 
 Ond &d;onne hi hebba&d; sui&d;e arodlice &d;a earce up  &d;onne hi sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice bio&d; gearwe to l&ae;ranne &d;&ae;tte &d;onne &d;earf bi&d;. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m sui&d;e wel se forma hierde &d;&ae;re halgan ciricean  &d;&ae;t is sanctus Petrus  manode o&d;re hierdas  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Bio&d; simle gearwe to l&ae;ranne &amp; to forgiefanne &ae;lcum &d;ara &d;e iow ryhtlice bidde ymbe &d;one tohopan &d;e ge habba&d; on eow. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: Ne bregden ge no &d;a stengas of &d;&ae;m hringum  &d;yl&ae;s sio earc si ungearo to beranne. 
 Hu micel scyle bion &d;&ae;t toscead  &amp; hu mislice mon scyle menn l&ae;ran mid &d;&ae;m cr&ae;fte &d;&ae;s lareowdomes. 
 Nu &d;onne o&d; &d;iss we rehton hwelc se hierde bion sceal; 
 Nu we him willa&d; cy&d;an hu he l&ae;ran sceal  sua sua hit lange &ae;r us &d;&ae;re eadegan gemynde wer Gregorius l&ae;rde  se w&ae;s o&d;rum noman genemned Nanzanzenus  he cu&ae;&d;: Ne gedafena&d; hit no &d;&ae;t we ealle menn on ane wisan l&ae;ren  for&d;am hie ne sint ealle anes modes &amp; anra &d;eawa. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft sio ilce lar &d;e o&d;rum hielpe&d;  hio dere&d; &d;&ae;m o&d;rum; 
 Sua sua manegra cynna wyrta &amp; grasu beo&d; gegaderad  &t;e sumu neat batiga&d; fore  sumu cuela&d;; 
 Sua sua mid li&d;re wis&d;lunga mon hors gestille&d;  sua eac mid &d;&ae;re illcan wistlunga mon m&ae;g hund astyrigean; 
 Sua beo&d; eac monige l&ae;cedomas &d;e sume adle gelytlia&d;  &amp; sume gestrongia&d;; 
 Sua eac hlaf &d;e strongra monna m&ae;gen gemicla&d;  he gelytla&d; cilda. 
 For &d;&ae;re ungelicnesse &d;ara hieremonna sculun beon ungelic &d;a word &d;&ae;s lareowes  &d;&ae;t he hiene selfne ge&d;eode to eallum his hieremonnum  to &ae;ghwelcum be his andefne  &amp; &d;eah hw&ae;&d;re sua sui&d;e sua he of &d;&ae;re &ae;we &amp; of &d;&ae;re ryhtan lare ne cerre. 
 Hw&ae;t cue&d;e we &d;onne hwelce sin &d;a innge&d;oncas monna buton suelce sumere hearpan strengas a&d;enede  &d;a se hearpere sui&d;e ungelice tieh&d; styre&d;  &amp; mid &d;y gede&d; &d;&ae;t hi nanwuht ungelice &d;&ae;m sone ne singa&d; &d;e he wilna&d;? 
 Ealle he gret mid anre honda  &d;y &d;e he wile &d;&ae;t he anne song singen  &d;eah he hie ungelice styrige. 
 Sua sceal &ae;ghwelc lareow to anre lufan &amp; to anum geleafan mid anre lare &amp; mid mislicum manungum his hieremonna mod styrigean. 
 On o&d;re wisan mon sceal manian weras  on o&d;re wif; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan ealde  on o&d;re giong; &amp; on o&d;re wisan earme  on o&d;re eadige;

 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a under&d;ieddan  on o&d;re &d;a ofer o&d;re gesettan; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;eowas  on o&d;re &d;a hlafurdas; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a woroldwisan  on o&d;re &d;a dysegan;

 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a ofermodan  on o&d;re &d;a wacmodan; 
 Ond on o&d;re wisan &d;a unge&d;yldegan  on o&d;re wisan &d;a ge&d;yldegan; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a welwillendan  on o&d;re &d;a &ae;fstegan; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a bilwitan  on o&d;re &d;a felaspr&ae;can; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a halan  on o&d;re &d;a unhalan; 
 Ond on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e for ege forbera&d; &d;&ae;t hi yfel ne do&d;  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e sua aheardiga&d; &d;&ae;t hi hit for nanum ege ne forl&ae;ta&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a sui&d;e suigean  on o&d;re &d;a felaidelspr&ae;c&ae;n; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a slawan  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e beo&d; to hrade; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a man&d;u&ae;ran  on o&d;re &d;a gramb&ae;ran;

 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a anwillan  on o&d;re &d;a ungest&ae;&d;&d;egan &amp; unf&ae;s&d;r&ae;dan; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a ofergifran  on o&d;re &d;a f&ae;stendan; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e mildheortlice hira agen sella&d;  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e &ae;fter o&d;erra monna ierfe flita&d;  &amp; hie reafigea&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e nohw&ae;&d;er ne o&d;erra monna ne reafia&d;  ne hiera agen rumedlice ne d&ae;la&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hira agen rumedlice sella&d;  &amp; ne forl&ae;ta&d; &d;eah &d;&ae;t hie o&d;erra monna ne reafien; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a ungemodan  on o&d;re &d;a gemodan; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a wrohtgeornan &d;e cease wyrcea&d;  &amp; on o&d;re &d;a gesibsuman; 
 Ond on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e &d;a word &d;&ae;re halgan &ae; ryhte ne ongieta&d;  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e hi ryhtlice ongieta&d;  &amp; &d;eah for ea&d;modnesse wandia&d; &d;&ae;t hi hit ne spreca&d;; 
 Ond on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e fullfremede ne beo&d; nohw&ae;&d;er ne on ieldo ne on wisdome  &amp; &d;eah for hr&ae;dwilnesse to fo&d;  &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e medomlice &amp; wel magon l&ae;ran  &amp; him &d;eah ondr&ae;da&d; for ea&d;modnesse  &d;&ae;t hie hit for&d;y forl&ae;ta&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;isse hwilendlican are wilnia&d;  &amp; him nan gesuinc ne &d;ync&d; &d;&ae;t hi hie h&ae;bben  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e him &d;ync&d; micel earfo&d;u &amp; micel gesuinc to habbanne  &amp; hiera sua&d;eah wilnia&d;; 
 Ond on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e beo&d; mid synscipe gebundene  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e beo&d; frio &d;ara benda; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a &d;urhtogenan synna wepa&d;  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e &d;a ge&d;ohtan wepa&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a &ae;rgedonan wepa&d;  &amp; &d;eah ne forl&ae;ta&d;  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e hi forl&ae;ta&d;  &amp; sua&d;eah ne wepa&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a unaliefedan &d;ing do&d;  &amp; hie eac heriga&d;  &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hie t&ae;la&d;  &amp; hi sua&d;eah ne forl&ae;ta&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e mid sumere unryhtwilnunga beo&d; f&ae;ringa hr&ae;dlice ofersui&d;ede  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e on &d;&ae;re synne ealnu weg licga&d;  mid ge&d;eahte to gebundene; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a lytlan scylda oftr&ae;dlice wyrcea&d;  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a lytlan forga&d;  &amp; &d;eah hwilum &d;a maran wyrcea&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e nan god nylla&d; onginnan  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e hit onginnan willa&d;  &amp; n&ae;fre ne geendiga&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e dearninga yfel do&d;  &amp; god eawunga  &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hira god hela&d; &d;e hie do&d;  &amp; ne recca&d; &d;eah menn wenen &d;&ae;t hie yfel don  &amp; eac mid sumum &d;ingum gedo&d; &d;&ae;t menn wena&d; &d;&ae;t hi yfel don. 
 Hu nytt rehton we nu &amp; rimdon &d;a c&ae;gan  buton we eac feawum wordum &ae;tiewen hw&ae;t hie healden  &amp; sua we swiotolus&d; m&ae;gen &ae;fter gereccan? 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne weras  on o&d;re wif. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne weras  on o&d;re wif. 
 &D;a weras mon sceal hefiglecor &amp; sti&d;lecor l&ae;ran  &amp; &d;a wif leohtlecor; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t &d;a weras higigen to maran byr&d;enne  &amp; &d;a wif mid oleccunga weor&d;en on gebrohte. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a iungan  on o&d;re &d;a ealdan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to l&ae;ranne &d;a iungan  on o&d;re &d;a ealdan; 
 For&d;&ae;m oftor mid re&d;re manunga beo&d; &d;a iungan nytwyr&d;e gedone  &amp; &d;a ealdan mid li&d;elicre bene  sua hit awriten is on &d;&ae;re &ae;we: Ne &d;reata &d;u no &d;one ealdan  ac healsa hine sua sua &d;inne f&ae;der. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a welegan  on o&d;re &d;a w&ae;dlan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a w&ae;dlan  on o&d;re &d;a welegan. 
 &D;a w&ae;dlan sint to frefranne &amp; to retanne  &d;yl&ae;s hi sien to ormode for hira earfe&d;um. 
 &D;a o&d;re sint to breganne  &d;yl&ae;s hi sien for hiera wlencum to upah&ae;fene. 
 To &d;&ae;m w&ae;dlan w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh Dryhten to &d;&ae;m witgan: Ne ondr&ae;d &d;u &d;e  for&d;&ae;m &d;u ne weor&d;es&d; gescended. 
 &amp; sui&d;e hr&ae;&d;e eac &ae;fter &d;&ae;m he him olecte  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;u earma  &d;u &d;e eart mid &d;y storme &amp; mid &d;&ae;re yste onwend &amp; oferworpen  &d;e ic geceas on &d;am ofne &d;e &d;u on w&ae;re asoden  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s on &d;inum ierm&d;um. 
 Ac sanctus Paulus &d;reade &d;a welegan  &d;a he cu&ae;&d; to his gingrum: Secga&d; &d;&ae;m welegum gind &d;isne middangeard &d;&ae;t hi to ofermodlice ne &d;encen  ne to wel ne truwigen &d;issum ungewissum welum. 
 Be &d;&ae;m we magon sui&d;e swutule oncnawan &d;&ae;t se ea&d;modnesse lareow  &d;a &d;a he ymb &d;a welegan spr&ae;c  na ne cu&ae;&d;: Bidda&d;  ac: Secga&d;  &amp; bebeoda&d;. 
 &amp; eac we magon oncnawan &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t &d;a earman &amp; &d;a untruman sient to retanne  &amp; &d;a ofermodan &amp; &d;a upahafenan ne sient no to weor&d;ianne  ac &d;a mon sceal swa micle ma hatan &d;onne biddan sua man ongiet &d;&ae;t hie for &d;issum woruldwlencum bio&d; sui&d;ur upahafene &amp; on ofermettum a&d;undene. 
 Be &d;&ae;m Crist cu&ae;&d; on his godspelle: Waa ieow welegum  &d;e eower lufu eall &amp; eower tohopa is on eowrum woruldwelum  &amp; ne giema&d; &d;&ae;s ecan gefean  ac gefeo&d; ealle mode &d;isses andweardan lifes genyhte. 
 Ac &d;&ae;s is &d;earf &d;&ae;t mon &d;one frefre &d;e on &d;&ae;m ofne asoden bi&d; his ierm&d;a  &amp; se is to &d;reatiganne &amp; to breganne  se &d;e bi&d; upahafen mid &d;y gefean &amp; mid &d;y gielpe &d;isse worulde; 
 &D;&ae;tte &d;a sorgfullan ongieten &d;&ae;t him becuma&d; &d;a welan &d;e him gehatene sint  &d;eah hi hi &d;onne git ne geseon; 
 &amp; eac &d;a welegan ongieten &d;&ae;tte &d;a welan &d;e hie onlocia&d; &amp; habba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &d;a habban ne magon. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m lareowe is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t he ongiete hwa earm sie  hwa eadig  &amp; hwone he l&ae;ran scyle sua earmne  &amp; hwane sua eadigne. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft se welega &amp; se w&ae;dla habba&d; sua gehweorfed hira &d;eawum &d;&ae;t se welega bi&d; ea&d;mod &amp; sorgfull  &amp; se w&ae;dla bi&d; upah&ae;fen &amp; selflice. 
 For&d;&ae;m sceal se lareow sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice wendan his tungan ongean &d;&ae;t &d;e he ongiet &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;s monnes innge&d;onc bi&d;  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t se earma upahafena sie mid his wordum ge&d;reatod &amp; gescended  &d;onne he ongiet &d;&ae;t hine ne magon his ierm&d;a ge&d;reatigan &amp; geea&d;medan. 
 Ac sua micle li&d;elecor he sceal olecan &d;&ae;m welegan ea&d;modan sua he ongiet &d;&ae;t he ea&d;modra bi&d;  &d;onne hine ne magon &d;a welan forwlencean  &d;e &ae;lcne ofermodne o&d;hebba&d;. 
 &amp; oft eac mon sceal &d;one welegan ofermodan to him loccian mid li&d;elicre olicunga  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he hine to ryhte geweeme; 
 For&d;&ae;m oft hearda wunda beo&d; mid li&d;um be&d;engum gehnescode &amp; geh&ae;lede  &amp; eac &d;a wod&d;raga &d;&ae;s ungewitfullan monnes se l&ae;ce gestil&d; &amp; geh&ae;l&d; mid &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he him olec&d; &ae;fter his agnum willan. 
 Ne sculon we eac forgietan hu hit w&ae;s be Saule &d;&ae;m kyninge: &d;onne him se wi&d;erwearda g&ae;s&d; on becom  &d;onne gefeng Dauid his hearpan  &amp; gestillde his wod&d;raga mid &d;&ae;m glige. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g &d;onne elles tacnian Saules ungewitfullnes buton &d;a upahafenesse &d;ara welegena? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t is elles getacnod &d;urh Dauid buton ea&d;modlic lif haligra monna? 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne se uncl&ae;na g&ae;s&d; becom on Saul  Dauid &d;onne mid his sange gemetgode &d;a wod&d;rage Saules. 
 Sua &d;onne  &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod &d;ara ricena for upah&ae;fenesse bi&d; to ierre gehwierfed  &d;onne is cynn &d;&ae;tte we for hira modes h&ae;lo olicende hi on smyltnesse gebringen mid ure spr&ae;ce  sua sua Dauid dyde Saul mid &d;&ae;re hearpan. 
 Hwilum eac &d;onne mon &d;&ae;m ricum cidan sceal  &ae;res&d; mon sceal sprecan asciende  suelce he be o&d;rum menn sprece &amp; ascie  &amp; gehiere hu be &d;&ae;m deman wille. 
 &D;onne mon &d;onne ongiete &d;&ae;t he ryhte gedemed h&ae;bbe  &amp; he wene &d;&ae;t he ryht be o&d;rum gedemed h&ae;bbe  &d;onne secge him mon sui&d;e ged&ae;ftelice for his agnum scyldum  &d;yl&ae;s &d;&ae;t a&d;undne mod for &d;issum hwilendlicum anwalde hit gebelge wi&d; &d;one &d;e him cit  ac &d;&ae;t he mid his agnum wisdome &amp; mid his agnum wordum &d;one suiran gebiege his agenra ofermetta  &d;&ae;tte he nane lade ne m&ae;ge findan  ac sie sua mid his agnum wordum gebunden. 
 For&d;&ae;m com Nathan to cidanne &d;&ae;m cyninge Dauide  &amp; licette  suelce he ymb sumes &d;earfan &amp; sumes earmes monnes ryht spr&ae;ce  &amp; sohte &d;&ae;s cyninges dom  &amp; wolde &d;&ae;t he &ae;res&d; hine be o&d;rum menn gedemde  &amp; si&d;&d;an gehierde his agne scylde  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he eft ne meahte &d;&ae;m ilcan dome wi&d;cue&d;an. 
 &amp; eac se haliga monn ongeat &ae;g&d;er ge &d;&ae;s cyninges scylde ge eac his hatheortnesse &amp; gedyrstignesse  wolde hine &d;a &ae;res&d; gebindan mid his agenre ondetnesse  &amp; forh&ae;l him &d;&ae;t he hine eft &d;reatian wolde. 
 Sua se l&ae;ce hyd his isern wi&d; &d;one monn &d;e he sni&d;an wile; 
 Wen&d;  gif he hit him iewe  &d;&ae;t he him nylle ge&d;afigean &d;&ae;t he hine sni&d;e. 
 Ac grapa&d; sui&d;e f&ae;gre ymbutan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he sni&d;an wile  &amp; sni&d; swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice. 
 Sua se witga dyde &d;one cyning mid his wordum: ic wene &d;&ae;t he hine snide slaulecor  gif he him &ae;r s&ae;de &d;&ae;t he hine sni&d;an wolde; 
 &D;y hit w&ae;s betre &d;&ae;t he grapude mid &d;&ae;m bispelle  &ae;r&d;on&d;e he cidde  sua se l&ae;ce grapa&d;  &amp; straca&d;  &amp; hyt his seax &amp; hw&ae;t  &ae;r&d;on&d;e he stingan wille. 
 Se l&ae;ce  &d;onne he cym&d; &d;one untruman to sni&d;anne  &ae;res&d; he sceawa&d; &d;&ae;t cumbl  &amp; si&d;&d;an hine tweona&d; ymb &d;&ae;s untruman ge&d;yld  hw&ae;&d;er he ge&d;afian m&ae;ge &d;&ae;t hine mon sni&d;e. 
 Hyt &d;onne his l&ae;ceseax under his cla&d;um o&d;&d;&ae;t he hine wunda&d;: wile &d;&ae;t he hit gefrede  &ae;r he hit geseo; 
 For&d;&ae;m he wen&d;  gif he hit &ae;r geseo  &d;&ae;t he hit wille forsacan. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a gladan  on o&d;re &d;a unrotan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a bli&d;an  on o&d;re &d;a unrotan. 
 &D;&ae;m oferbli&d;um is to cy&d;anne &d;a unrotnessa &d;e &d;&ae;r&ae;fter cuma&d;  &amp; &d;am unbli&d;um sint to cy&d;anne &d;a gefean &d;e him gehatene sindon. 
 Geliorngen &d;a bli&d;an on &d;&ae;re &d;reaunga &d;&ae;t hie him ondr&ae;den  &amp; gehieren &d;a unbli&d;an &d;a lean &d;&ae;s gefean &d;e hie tohopia&d;. 
 To &d;&ae;m bli&d;an is gecueden: Wa eow &d;a nu hlieha&d;  for&d;am ge sculon eft wepan. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a unrotan &d;one cuide &d;e him is to gecueden &d;urh &d;one illcan lareow  &d;&ae;t is Crist  he cu&ae;&d;: Eft ic eow geseo  &amp; &d;onne blissia&d; eowre heortan  &amp; eowerne gefean eow nan mon &ae;t ne genim&d;. 
 Monige beo&d; &d;eah bli&d;e &amp; eac unbli&d;e &d;ara &d;e for nanum woruld&d;ingum nahw&ae;&d;er do&d;  buton for &d;&ae;s blodes styringe &amp; for lichoman medtrymnesse. 
 Sua&d;eah is &d;&ae;m to cy&d;anne  &d;&ae;t hi hie warenigen &ae;g&d;er ge wi&d; &d;a ungemetlican blisse ge wi&d; &d;a ungemetlican unrotnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m hira &ae;g&d;er astyre&d; sumne un&d;eaw  &d;eah hie ungewealdes cumen of &d;&ae;s lichoman medtrymnesse. 
 &D;&ae;m oferbli&d;an oft folga&d; firenlus&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;m unrotan ierre. 
 For&d;&ae;m is micel nied&d;earf &d;&ae;t mon hiene wi&d; &d;&ae;t irre an &amp; wi&d; &d;a ungemetlican s&ae;l&d;a warenige  ac eac wi&d; &d;&ae;t &d;e forcu&d;re bi&d;  &d;e &d;&ae;r&ae;fter cym&d;  &d;&ae;t is fierenlus&d; &amp; unryhtlicu iersung  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t mon iersige on o&d;erne for his gode. 
 &D;onne is micel &d;earf  &d;onne him mon &d;issa tuega hw&ae;&d;er on&d;r&ae;tt sui&d;ur &d;onne o&d;er  &amp; wi&d; &d;&ae;t wien&d;  &d;&ae;t he sua sui&d;e wi&d; &d;&ae;t winne sua he on &d;&ae;t o&d;er ne befealle  &d;e he him &ae;r l&ae;s ondred. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a ealdormen  on o&d;re wisan &d;a hieremenn. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint &d;onne to manianne &d;a under&d;ioddan  on o&d;re &d;a ofergesettan. 
 &D;a under&d;ieddan mon sceal sua l&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hie elles ne sien gen&ae;t ne geirmed  &amp; &d;a ofersettan mon sceal sua manian &d;&ae;t se hiera folgo&d; hine ne o&d;hebbe. 
 &amp; &d;a under&d;ioddan &d;&ae;t hie wiers ne don &d;onne him man bebeode  ond &d;a ofergesettan &d;&ae;t hi him to unaberendlice ne beoden. 
 &amp; &d;a un&d;er&d;ieddan &d;&ae;t hi him ea&d;modlice underlicgen  &amp; &d;a ofergesettan &d;&ae;t hie gemetlice him ofer sien  &d;&ae;t hi magon eac be &d;isse bisene ongietan &d;&ae;t him is to gecueden: Bearn  beo ge under&d;iodde eowrum ieldrum magum on Dryhtne. 
 &D;&ae;m ofergesettan is to gecueden: Ne gremigen ge eowru bearn. 
 Geleornigen eac &d;a bearn &d;&ae;t hi sua hieren hira ieldrum sua sua hie selfe wieten on hira innge&d;once beforan &d;&ae;s dieglan Deman eagum &d;&ae;t hi hit for Gode don  &amp; &ae;t Gode &d;a lean habban willen. 
 Geleornigen eac &d;a f&ae;deras &amp; &d;a hlafurdas &d;&ae;t hie wel libbende gode bisene astellen &d;&ae;m &d;e him under&d;iedde sien. 
 Eac sculun wietan &d;a ofer o&d;re gesettan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie unaliefedes &d;urhteo&d;  &amp; o&d;re men bi &d;am biesenia&d;  sua manegra wieta hie beo&d; wyr&d;e beforan &d;&ae;m o&d;rum sua sua he monna on won gebrohte  buton he eft self gesuice  &amp; sua monige gecierre sua he m&ae;s&d; m&ae;ge. 
 For&d;&ae;m him is sui&d;e micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t he sua micle w&ae;rlicor hine healde wi&d; scylda swa he gere witan m&ae;g &d;&ae;t he no ana ne forwier&d;  &d;onne he o&d;rum yfele bisene stele&d;.

 Hit is god &d;&ae;t ge hit nu witon. 
 N&ae;ron naht &ae;metige  &d;eah ge wel ne dyden. 
 For&d;&ae;m he spr&ae;c &d;as word &d;e he wolde &d;ara scamleasna scylda t&ae;lende geopenian  &amp; &d;ara scamf&ae;stena giemelieste he wolde mid li&d;elicum wordum gedieglan. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a ofermodan &amp; &d;a upah&ae;fenan on hira mode  on o&d;re wisan &d;a earmheortan &amp; &d;a wacmodan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a modgan &amp; &d;a fortruwodan  on o&d;re &d;a unmodgan &amp; &d;a un&d;ristan. 
 &D;a fortruwodan  &d;onne hie him selfum to sui&d;e truwia&d;  hie forsio&d; o&d;re menn  &amp; eac forcue&d;a&d;. 
 &D;a lytelmodan &d;onne &amp; &d;a un&d;ristan  &d;onne hie ongieta&d; hiera unb&ae;ldo &amp; hiera unmiehte  hie weor&d;a&d; oft ormode. 
 &D;a modgan &d;onne &amp; &d;a fortruwudan  eall hiera agen &d;&ae;t hie synderlice &d;encea&d; o&d;&d;e do&d; hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t sie &d;&ae;t betste: ac &d;a unmodigan &amp; &d;a ungedyrstigan wena&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t sui&d;e forsewenlic sie &d;&ae;tte hie do&d;  &amp; for&d;on weor&d;a&d; oft ormode. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m lareowe is swi&d;e smealice to underseceanne be &d;&ae;m weorcum &d;ara ofertruwedena  &d;&ae;t hie him gecy&d;en &d;&ae;tte on &d;am &d;ingum &d;e hie him selfum sua sui&d;e liciga&d;  &d;&ae;t hie Gode mislicia&d;. 
 Swa we magon betst &d;a gedyrstigan gel&ae;ran &d;&ae;tte   &d;onne hie wenen &d;&ae;t hie h&ae;bben betst gedon  &d;&ae;t we him &d;onne secgen &d;&ae;t hie h&ae;bben wierst gedon  &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne hie wenen &d;&ae;t hie &d;one gilp &amp; &d;&ae;t lof begieten h&ae;bben &d;&ae;t hie &ae;r wilnodon  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne h&ae;bben mid &d;y scame geholode. 
 Hwilum eac  &d;onne &d;a fortruwudan &amp; &d;a anwillan wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie nane scylde &d;urhtogen n&ae;bben  &d;onne magon we hi sua ra&d;os&d; to ryhte gecierran &d;&ae;t we him sume opene scylde  &d;e &ae;r &d;urhtogen w&ae;re  healfunga o&d;wieten  &d;&ae;t hie for&d;&ae;m scamige  for&d;&ae;m of &d;&ae;re scylde &d;e he hine &d;onne bereccan ne m&ae;ge  he ongiete &d;a he &d;onne de&d;  &d;eah him &d;onne &d;ynce &d;&ae;t he nan yfel ne do. 
 &D;a fortruwodnesse &amp; &d;a anwilnesse an Corinctheum paulus ongeat sui&d;e wi&d;erweardne wi&d; hine  &amp; betweoh him selfum sui&d;e a&d;undene &amp; upah&ae;fene; 
 Sua &d;&ae;tte sume cu&ae;don &d;&ae;t hie w&ae;ron Apollan  sume cu&ae;don &d;&ae;t hi w&ae;ron Saules  sume Petres  sum cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re Cristes. 
 Ac Paulus &d;a sona &d;a uncl&ae;nan scylde beforan him alLum s&ae;de  &d;e an hiera ealra gewitnesse gedon w&ae;s  &amp; &d;agiet ungebet; 
 He cu&ae;&d;; 
 We gehierdon betueoxn eow unryhth&ae;med  ge sua unryht sua we fur&d;um betwuxn h&ae;&d;num monnum ne hierdon  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t ge sume h&ae;fdon eowre steopmodur  &amp; ge &d;&ae;s n&ae;fdon nane sorge  &amp; noldon from eow adon &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;t dydon  ac w&ae;ron sua upah&ae;fene sua ge &ae;r w&ae;ron. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: Hw&ae;t wille ge for eowerre fortruwodnesse &amp; for eowerre anwilnesse cue&d;an  hw&ae;s o&d;&d;e hw&ae;s ge sien? 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e on eowerre towesnesse ge habba&d; gecy&d;ed &d;&ae;t ge ures nanes ne siendon. 
 Ac &d;a lytelmodan &amp; &d;a un&d;riestan we magon &d;y ie&d; on &d;&ae;m wege gebringan godra weorca  gif we healfunga &amp; &d;eah be sumum d&ae;le heora godan weorc secgea&d;  for&d;&ae;m  &d;onne we hira yfel t&ae;la&d;  &d;&ae;t we eac hira god herigen  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t we hira modes mearuwnesse gesti&d;igen mi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie gehiren &d;&ae;t we hi herigen  &amp; &d;&ae;tte eft sien hira scyl&d;a ge&d;reade mid &d;am &d;&ae;t we hie t&ae;len. 
 Oft we magon beon sua nyttran &ae;t him  gif we hie myndgia&d; hira godna weorca  &amp; &d;a secgea&d;  &amp; gif we hw&ae;t ongieta&d; on him ungesceadwislices gedoon  ne sculon we no hi &d;reagean suelce hie hit gedoon h&ae;bben  &d;eah hit gedon sie  ac we sculon him forbeodan &d;&ae;t hie huru sua ne don  suelce hit &d;onne giet gedon ne sie  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t sio hering &d;e we &ae;r heredon us gefultume &d;&ae;t we hie wi&d;ermode ne gedon mid &d;&ae;re t&ae;linge  ac &d;&ae;t sio hering getrymme &amp; gemetgige &d;&ae;s wacmodan &amp; &d;&ae;s un&d;ristan monnes mod wi&d; &d;a t&ae;linge. 
 Be &d;am se ilca Paulus cu&ae;&d;  &d;a he ongeat &d;&ae;t folc &d;e Salonicensa hatte  &d;&ae;t hie on his lare f&ae;ste w&ae;ron  &amp; &d;eah he ongeat &d;&ae;t hi gedrefde w&ae;ron mid wacmodnesse  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie wendon &d;&ae;t hit near worulde endunge w&ae;re &d;onne hit w&ae;re; 
 &D;a ongon he &ae;res&d; herigean on him &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he f&ae;s&d;r&ae;des wiste  &amp; sona &ae;fter &d;on sui&d;e li&d;elice hierdde &d;a &d;e he unf&ae;s&d;rade wisse  &amp; &d;us cu&ae;&d;: We sculon simle secgan Gode &d;oncas for eow bro&d;ur  sua sua hit wel wier&d;e is  for&d;&ae;m&d;e eower geleafa h&ae;f&d; ofer &d;ungen sui&d;e monigra o&d;erra monna  &amp; eower lufu is betweoxn eow sui&d;e genyhtsumu  sua &d;&ae;t we apostolas sint sui&d;e gefeonde ealle for eowrum geleafan &amp; for eowrum ge&d;ylde. 
 Ac sona &ae;fter &d;&ae;re li&d;elican spr&ae;ce he cu&ae;&d;: Ic eow healsige bro&d;ur for &d;&ae;m tocyme Dryhtnes H&ae;lendan Kristes &amp; for ure gesomnunge &d;&ae;t ge no to hr&ae;dlice ne sien astyrede from gewitte  ne eow to sui&d;e ne ondr&ae;da&d; for nanes monnes wordum ne for nanes witgan g&ae;ste  ne &d;eah eow hwelc &ae;rendgewrit cume  suelce hit from us send sie  &amp; &d;&ae;ron cy&d;e &d;&ae;t se domes d&ae;g neah sie. 
 Sua gedyde se so&d;f&ae;sta lareow &d;&ae;t hie &ae;res&d; gehierdon &d;a heringe &d;e him licode for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie &ae;fter &d;&ae;m &d;e lus&d;licor gehierden &d;a lare  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t lof hie to &d;&ae;m getrymede &d;&ae;t sio manung hie eft ne &d;rycte. 
 &D;a he ongeat &d;&ae;t hie w&ae;ron onstryede mid &d;&ae;m wenan &d;&ae;t hi &d;&ae;s endes sua neah wendon  &d;a spr&ae;c he suelce he hit &d;agiet nyste &d;&ae;t hie hit him &d;a io ondredon  ac forbead him &d;&ae;t hit ne scolde sua weor&d;an  &amp; wolde &d;&ae;t hie wenden &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;s &d;e unt&ae;lwyr&d;ran w&ae;ren &d;e hie wendon &d;&ae;t he nyste hira leohtmodnesse &amp; hira unf&ae;s&d;radnesse. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a unge&d;yldgan  &amp; on o&d;re &d;a ge&d;yldgan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a unge&d;yldgan  on o&d;re wisan &d;a ge&d;yldegan. 
 &D;&ae;m unge&d;yldegum is to secganne &d;&ae;t hie ne agimeleasigen &d;&ae;t hi hira mod gebridligen  &d;&ae;t hi ne hlipen unwillende on &d;&ae;t scorene clif un&d;eawa; 
 Sua hit oft gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t sio hatheortness &amp; sio hr&ae;dwilnes &d;&ae;t mod gebring&d; on &d;&ae;m weorce &d;e hine &ae;r nan willa to ne spon  &amp; de&d; &d;eah sua astyred  suelce he hit ungewisses o&d;&d;e ungewealdes doo  &d;&ae;t him eft gehreowe&d;  si&d;&d;an he hit wat. 
 For&d;&ae;m him is to secgganne &d;&ae;t hie weor&d;a&d; oft ascrencte on &d;&ae;m scyfe &d;&ae;re styringe hira modes  &d;&ae;t hi hira selfra ne agon &d;y mare geweald &d;e o&d;erra monna  &amp; sui&d;e seldon magon ongietan hira &ae;gen yfel  &ae;r&d;on hi hit &d;urhtogen habba&d;. 
 Ac gif he &d;onne &d;&ae;re styringe ne wi&d;stent  &d;onne gescient he &d;a godan weorc &d;e he oft &ae;r on stillum mode &d;urhteah  &amp; sua ungleaulice for &d;&ae;m scyfe &d;&ae;re styringe sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice towierp&d; &d;a godan weorc &d;e he longe &ae;r fore&d;onclice timbrede  &amp; &d;a ge&d;yld &d;e his modur &amp; hierde ealra m&ae;gena for &d;&ae;m unwrence &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde forlet  &amp; eac &d;&ae;t m&ae;gen &d;&ae;re so&d;an lufan he forlet. 
 Hit is awriten on Paules bocum &d;&ae;t sio Godes lufu sie ge&d;yld  &amp; se &d;e ge&d;yldig ne sie  &d;&ae;t he n&ae;bbe &d;a Godes lufe on him. 
 For&d;&ae;m for &d;&ae;m un&d;eawe &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde wir&d; utadrifen sio fostermodur &ae;lcre leornunga &amp; &ae;lces cr&ae;ftes  &amp; &ae;ghwelces lareowes lar wihx&d; &d;urh his ge&d;ylde  &ae;ghwelc monn bi&d; onfunden sua micle l&ae;s gel&ae;red &d;onne o&d;er sua he bi&d; unge&d;yldegra. 
 Ne m&ae;g he no ryhtlice ge&d;yld l&ae;ran  buton he self ge&d;yldelice o&d;erra monna tionan ge&d;olige. 
 Hwilum eac gebyre&d; for &d;&ae;m un&d;eawe &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t mod wier&d; gesticced mid &d;&ae;re scylde gielpes  &amp; he ne m&ae;g ge&d;yldgian &d;&ae;t he for &d;isse worulde sie foresewen  ac gif he hw&ae;t diogollice for Gode to goode gedyde  &d;onne ne m&ae;g he ge&d;yldgian &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t forhele  ac wier&d; &d;onon gielpen  &amp; ongienne&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t cy&d;an &d;onne he ne m&ae;g ge&d;olian &d;&ae;t hine menn forsion  ac geopena&d; hit mid gielpe. 
 Be &d;am is awriten &d;&ae;t betera beo se ge&d;yldega wer &d;onne se gielpna  for&d;&ae;m&d;e him bi&d; leofre scande to &d;olianne &d;onne &d;&ae;t god to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;t he deogollice de&d;  &d;yl&ae;s he for &d;&ae;m un&d;eawe &d;&ae;s gielpes hit forleose. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m gielpnan bi&d; leofre &d;&ae;t he secge on hine selfne gif he hw&ae;t godes wat  ge &d;eah he nyte hw&ae;t he so&d;es secge  him is &d;eah leofre &d;&ae;t he leoge &d;onne him mon &ae;nigra ungerisna to wene. 
 Ac he forl&ae;t &d;onne &amp; towierp&d; eal &d;a godan weorc &d;e he &ae;r worhte  &d;onne he forl&ae;t &d;a ge&d;ylde. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhtlice beboden Ezechiele &d;&ae;m witgan &d;&ae;t he scolde &d;one Godes alter habban uppan aholodne &d;&ae;t he meahte on healdan &d;a offrunga &amp; &d;a lic &d;e mon brohte to &d;&ae;m weobude; 
 For&d;&ae;m  gif se weobud ufan hol n&ae;re  &amp; &d;&ae;r wind to come  &d;onne tostencte he &d;a lac. 
 Hw&ae;t elles getacna&d; &d;&ae;t weobud buton ryhtwisra monna saula? 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e nu eal &d;&ae;t se ryhtwisa to gode de&d; eal hit bi&d; beorht to lacum beforan Godes eagum  sua io w&ae;s eall sio offrung uppe on &d;&ae;t wiebed broht. 
 Hw&ae;t tacna&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t holh on &d;&ae;m weobude buton godra monna ge&d;yld? 
 For&d;am  &d;onne mon his mod geea&d;modga&d; &d;&ae;t he wi&d;erweardnesse &amp; scande forbere  &d;onne geeacna&d; he sum holh on his mode sua sua &d;&ae;t weobud h&ae;f&d; on him uppan. 
 Holh w&ae;s beboden &d;&ae;t sceolde beon on &d;&ae;m weobude uppan  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t wind ne meahte &d;a lac tostencean  &d;e mon on &d;&ae;t weobud legde. 
 &D;&ae;t tacna&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t ge&d;yld sceal gehealdan &d;ara gecorenra monna mod  &d;&ae;tte hit ne astyrige se wind &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde  &d;yl&ae;s hit forleose &d;a godan weorc &d;e he &ae;r geworht h&ae;fde. 
 Wel hit w&ae;s gecueden &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t holh sceolde beon on &d;&ae;m weobude anre elne brad &amp; anre elne long  for&d;&ae;m butan tweon se &d;e &d;a ge&d;ylde ne forl&ae;t  he gehilt micle anmodnesse. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Bere eower &ae;lc o&d;re byr&d;enne betweoxn eow  &d;onne gefylle ge Godes &ae;. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne Godes &ae; &d;&ae;t mon h&ae;bbe lufe &amp; ge&d;yld  &d;&ae;t micelne beam on &d;inum agnan. 
 Sio gedrefednes &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde on &d;&ae;m mode &d;&ae;t is se smala ci&d;  ac se yfela willa on &d;&ae;re heortan &d;&ae;t is se greata beam. 
 &D;one unge&d;yldegan &d;onne sui&d;e lytel scur &d;&ae;re costunga m&ae;g onhreran  sua sua lytel wind m&ae;g &d;one ci&d; awecgan  ac &d;one yfelan f&ae;s&d;r&ae;dan willan fulneah nan wind ne m&ae;g awecgan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Dryhten: &d;u licettere  aweorp &ae;res&d; of &d;inum agnum eagan &d;one greatan beam  &amp; cunna si&d;&d;an hw&ae;&d;er &d;u m&ae;ge adon &d;one ci&d; of &d;ines bro&d;ur eagan. 
 Suelce he cu&ae;de to &d;&ae;m unryhtwisan mode  &d;e innan bi&d; gnornigende  &amp; utan licet ge&d;yld: Adoo &ae;res&d; from &d;e &d;a byr&d;enne &d;&ae;s yfelan willan  &amp; t&ae;l si&d;&d;an o&d;erne for his unge&d;ylde &amp; for his leohtmodnesse; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;onne &d;u ne wilnas&d; &d;&ae;t &d;u oferswi&d;e &amp; forl&ae;te &d;a licettunge on &d;e selfum  &d;onne meaht &d;u &d;y wyrs ge&d;yldgian o&d;res monnes yfel. 
 &amp; oft &d;eah gebyre&d; &d;&ae;m ge&d;yldgan  &d;eah him mon hw&ae;t wi&d;erweardes doo  o&d;&d;e he hwelce scande gehiere bi him selfum  &d;&ae;t he &d;onne nawuht &ae;t &d;am cierre ne bi&d; onstyred  ac geb&ae;r&d; sua ge&d;yldelice suelce he hit h&ae;bbe mid ealre heortan forl&ae;ten. 
 Ac &d;onne he hit eft ofman &ae;fter lytlum f&ae;ce  &d;onne of&d;ync&d; him &d;&ae;s ilcan &d;e he &ae;r forb&ae;r  &amp; bi&d; eft on&ae;led mid &d;y fyre &d;&ae;s sares. 
 Sec&d; &d;onne &amp; smea&d; hu he hit gewrecan m&ae;ge  &amp; &d;a monn&d;w&ae;rnesse &d;e he &ae;r &d;urhtogen h&ae;fde eft &d;eahtigende on yfel gewend. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m m&ae;g beon sui&d;e hra&d;e geholpen from his lareowe  gif he him s&ae;g&d; hwonon &d;&ae;t cym&d;  &amp; hu se lytega dioful styre&d; gewinn &amp; gefeoht betweoxn him twam: o&d;erne he l&ae;r&d; &d;&ae;t he onginne sume scande bi &d;&ae;m o&d;rum o&d;&d;e sprecan o&d;&d;e don  o&d;erne he l&ae;r&d; &d;&ae;t he &d;a scande forgielde. 
 Ac hit gebyre&d; oftos&d; &d;&ae;t se bi&d; ofersui&d;ed  se &d;e &d;urh diofles lare &ae;res&d; bi&d; on&ae;led mid &d;y unryhtan ni&d;e  &d;eah he sua ne wene  &d;onne he hit &ae;res&d; ongin&d;; 
 &amp; se h&ae;f&d; oftos&d; &d;one weor&d;scipe  se &d;e &ae;r ge&d;yldelic &d;a scande forb&ae;r. 
 Ac &d;onne se diobul h&ae;f&d; &d;one &ae;rran gewunnenne  &amp; he bi&d; under his geoc gegan  &d;onne went he mid ealle cr&ae;fte ongen &d;&ae;s o&d;res ge&d;yld  &d;e him &d;onne giet wi&d;win&d;  &amp; bi&d; sui&d;e sorig  for&d;&ae;m he on &d;&ae;m forman gefeohte hiene ne meahte ofsceotan mid &d;&ae;m bismere  &d;e he &d;urh &d;one o&d;erne him to sende. 
 L&ae;tt &d;onne an &d;&ae;t gefeoht sua openlice sume hwile  &amp; ongien&d; hine diogollice l&ae;ran  &amp; slitan his innge&d;onc  &amp; bit &d;&ae;re tide  hwonne he &d;&ae;s wier&d;e sie &d;&ae;t he hine besuican mote. 
 For&d;&ae;m he hine ne meahte mid openlicum gefeohte ofersui&d;an  s&ae;ta&d; &d;onne diogollice  &amp; sec&d; hu he hine m&ae;ge gefon. 
 Se ge&d;yldiga &d;onne eft  &d;onne &d;&ae;t gestilled bi&d;  &d;onne went he eft ongean mid his mode  &amp; geman &d;one demm o&d;&d;e &d;&ae;t bismer  &d;&ae;t him &ae;r gedon w&ae;s  &amp; &d;onne sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice &amp; sui&d;e ungemetlice eahta&d; eall &d;&ae;t him &ae;r gedon w&ae;s  &amp; hit &d;onne sui&d;e unaberendlic tala&d;  &amp; mid sua micelre murcunga his agen mod gedref&d;  &d;&ae;tte oft &d;one ge&d;yldegestan scama&d; &d;&ae;s siges &d;e he ofer &d;one dioful h&ae;fde mid his ge&d;ylde  &amp; he &d;onne sua gebunden fram &d;am diofle sarga&d; &d;&ae;s  &amp; him of&d;ync&d; &d;&ae;t he hit sua emne &amp; sua ge&d;yldelice forb&ae;r &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t bismer ne forgeald  &d;enc&d; &d;&ae;s timan hwonne he hit wyrs geleanian m&ae;ge. 
 Ac hwam beo&d; &d;onne &d;as &d;yllecan geliccran &d;onne &d;&ae;m folce &d;e on cl&ae;num felda weor&d;licne sige gefeohta&d;  &amp; eft innan hira burgum f&ae;ste belocene &d;urh hiera giemelieste hie l&ae;ta&d; gebindan  o&d;&d;e suelce hie &ae;r l&ae;gen on longre medtrymnesse  &amp; hie &d;eah gewierpten  &amp; eft cume an lytel febbres  &amp; hie ofslea? 
 &D;a ge&d;yldegan sint to manianne &d;&ae;tte hie hira heortan getrymigen &ae;fter &d;&ae;s miclan sige  &amp; &d;a burg hira modes wi&d; st&ae;lherigas behealden  &amp; mid wighusum gef&ae;s&d;nige  suelce he him &d;&ae;re adle edcier sui&d;ur ondr&ae;de &d;onne &d;one fruman  &d;yl&ae;s se lytega fiond &ae;fter fierste sui&d;ur f&ae;gnige &d;&ae;t he hine mid his lotwrencium besuice  &d;eah he hine &ae;r openum gefeohte ofercome  &amp; him &d;one sti&d;an suiran forbr&ae;ce. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a welwillendan  &amp; on o&d;re &d;a &ae;festgan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a welwillendan  on o&d;re &d;a &ae;fstegan. 
 &D;a welwillendan sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie sua f&ae;genigen o&d;ra monna godra weorca &d;&ae;t hie eac selfe &d;&ae;s ilcan lyste  &amp; sua gielpen hiera niehstena d&ae;da &d;&ae;t hie him eac onhyrigen. 
 Nimen him bisene on hira godan weorcum  &amp; icen hie simle mid hira agenum  &d;yl&ae;s hie sien to o&d;erra monna gefeohte holde haweras  &amp; don him selfe nawuht  &amp; &d;onne eft &ae;fter &d;am gefeohte sie butan &ae;ghwelcum edleane on &d;ys andweardan life. 
 Se &d;e nu on &d;&ae;m gefeohte &d;isses andweardan lifes nile suincan  ne his selfes plion  he ongiet eft hine selfne ofercymenne &amp; gesciendne  &d;onne he gesieh&d; &amp; gehier&d; &d;a weor&d;igan &d;e &ae;r wel ongunnon  &d;a &d;a he idel w&ae;s. 
 Sui&d;e sui&d;e we gesyngia&d;  gif we o&d;erra monna welgedona d&ae;da ne lufiga&d; &amp; ne heriga&d;  ac we nabba&d; &d;eah nane mede &d;&ae;re heringe  gif we be sumum d&ae;le nella&d; onginnan &d;&ae;t we onhyrigen &d;&ae;m &d;eawum &d;e us on o&d;rum monnum licia&d; be d&ae;le &d;e we m&ae;gen. 
 For&d;&ae;m is to secganne &d;&ae;m welwillendan monnum &d;&ae;t hi habba&d; sua micle mede o&d;erra monna godra weorca  gif hie him nanwuht ne onhyrigea&d;  sua we habba&d; &d;&ae;s hleahtres  &d;onne we hlieha&d; gligmonna unnyttes cr&ae;ftes. 
 We heriga&d; hira cr&ae;ftas  &amp; &d;eah nylla&d; hi habban  for&d;&ae;m we hiera nabba&d; nan lof. 
 We wundria&d; hu wel hie licia&d; for hira cr&ae;fte  &amp; &d;eah ne wilniga&d; no &d;&ae;t we sua licigen. 
 &D;&ae;m welwillendum is to secganne  &d;onne hie gesio&d; hiera geferena god weorc  &d;&ae;t hie eac &d;encen to him selfum  &amp; ne fortruwigen hie for o&d;erra monna weorcum  &d;yl&ae;s hie herigen hiera godan weorc  &amp; onscunigen &d;&ae;t hie selfe sua don. 
 &D;&ae;s &d;y wyrse wite hie sculon habban on ende &d;e him lica&d; &d;&ae;t mon wel doo  &amp; nylla&d; &d;&ae;m onhyrigean be sumum d&ae;le. 
 Ac &d;a &ae;fstegan sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hu blinde hi beo&d;  &d;onne hie beo&d; unrote for o&d;erra monna godan weorcum  &amp; for hira ryhtum gefean beo&d; unbli&d;e  for&d;&ae;m hie beo&d; sui&d;e unges&ae;lige  &d;onne hie yfelia&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e o&d;re menn godiga&d;  &amp; &d;onne hie geseo&d; &d;ara o&d;erra ges&ae;l&d;a eaciende  &d;onne &d;ync&d; him &d;&ae;t hie wiellen acuelan for &d;&ae;re medtrymnesse &d;&ae;s o&d;res ges&ae;lignesse  sua he bi&d; genierwed on his mode. 
 Hwa m&ae;g beon unges&ae;ligra &d;onne se &ae;fstiga? 
 &D;onne &d;u gesiehs&d; &d;&ae;t he bi&d; utan gedrefed  hu micle ma wenstu &d;&ae;t he sie innan for &d;&ae;s o&d;res gode. 
 &D;&ae;t god &d;&ae;t se o&d;er &d;onne de&d;  &d;&ae;t meahte beon eac his god  &d;eah he hit &d;onne git don ne meahte  gif he hit wolde lufigean on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum. 
 Ealle &d;a &d;e wunigea&d; on anum geleafan &amp; on anum willan hie beo&d; sua sua manegu limu on anum menn  &amp; &ae;lc h&ae;f&d; &d;eah sundernytte  &amp; &d;eah &d;a limu mislice tod&ae;lde sin  &ae;lc hira bi&d; on o&d;res nytte swa some swa on his selfes. 
 &D;onon hit gewyr&d; &d;&ae;t se fot gesieh&d; &d;urh &d;&ae;t eage  &amp; &d;&ae;t eage st&ae;p&d; on &d;&ae;m fotum  &d;a earan gehiera&d; for &d;one mu&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;s mu&d;es tunge sceal faran on &d;ara earena &d;earfe  &amp; sio womb sceal fulteman &d;&ae;m hondum  &amp; sio hond sceal wyrcean for &d;a wambe. 
 On &d;&ae;s lichoman gesceafte we underfengon ealle &d;a &d;enunga &d;e we nu &d;iowia&d; &amp; wyrcea&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit is micel sceand  gif we nylla&d; licittan &d;&ae;t we sien &d;&ae;t we sindon  for&d;&ae;m butan tweon &d;&ae;t bi&d; ure &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t we lufigea&d; on o&d;rum monnum  &d;eah we hit selfe don ne m&ae;gen  &amp; &d;&ae;t o&d;re menn on us lufigea&d;  &d;&ae;t bi&d; hira. 
 Ge&d;encen be &d;ysum &d;a &ae;fstigan hu micel m&ae;gen bi&d; on &d;&ae;re lufe &d;&ae;t hio gede&d; &d;&ae;t o&d;erra monna gesuinc &amp; hira weorc bi&d; ure butan &ae;lcum gesuince ures lichoman. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m &ae;fstegum is to secganne  gif hie hie nylla&d; healdan wi&d; &d;&ae;m &ae;fste  &d;&ae;t hie weor&d;a&d; besencte on &d;a ealdan unryhtwisnesse &d;&ae;s lytegan fiondes  &d;e bi him awriten is &d;&ae;tte for his &ae;feste dea&d; become ofer ealle eor&d;an. 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e he hefonrice mid his agenre scylde forworhte  &d;a of&d;uhte him &d;&ae;tte menn w&ae;ron to &d;&ae;m gesceapene  &amp; icte &d;a his agne scylde mid &d;&ae;m &ae;fste  &d;&ae;t he tiolode menn forl&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hie wurden eac forlorene sua he w&ae;s. 
 Eac sint to l&ae;ranne &d;a &ae;fstigan &d;&ae;tte hie ongieten under hu micelre frecenesse hie liecga&d;  &amp; hu hie icea&d; hira forwyrd  &d;onne hie of hira heortan nylla&d; aweorpan &d;one &ae;fst  ac hine healda&d;  o&d;&d;&ae;t hie afealla&d; on opene scylde  sw&ae; sw&ae; Cain dyde. 
 Ne gefiolle he no on sw&ae; opene scylde &d;&ae;t he his bro&d;ur ofsloge  gif he &ae;r ne ge&ae;fstgode &d;&ae;tte his bro&d;ur lac w&ae;ron &d;ancweor&d;licor onfongne &d;onne his. 
 Be &d;am is awriten &d;&ae;t Dryhten besawe to Abele &amp; to his lacum  &amp; nolde to Caine ne to his lacum. 
 &D;a wear&d; Cain sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice irre  &amp; hnipode ofdune  &amp; se anda &d;a &d;e he h&ae;fde to his bre&d;er  for&d;&ae;m&d;e his lac w&ae;ron onfangne &amp; his n&ae;ron  se anda wear&d; to s&ae;de &d;&ae;s bro&d;ursl&ae;ges  for&d;&ae;m him eglde &d;&ae;t he w&ae;s betra &d;onne he  &amp; &d;ohte  sua he eft gedyde  &d;&ae;t he hine ofsloge  wurde si&d;&d;an to &d;&ae;m &d;e hit meahte. 
 For&d;&ae;m is to secganne &d;&ae;m &ae;fstegum sua hw&ae;t o&d;res godes sua on him ongieten bi&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten &d;&ae;tte &d;is fl&ae;sclice lif sie &ae;fes&d;  &amp; he sie &d;&ae;re fl&ae;sclican heortan h&ae;lo  &amp; &d;eah &d;a ban for him forrotigen. 
 Hw&ae;t getacna&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc buton unf&ae;s&d; weorc &amp; hnesce  &amp; hw&ae;t &d;a ban buton stronglice geworht weorc? 
 Oft &d;eah gebyre&d; &d;&ae;tte sume  &d;a &d;e welwillende beo&d; on monegum weorcum  unf&ae;ste beo&d; ongietene  &amp; sume beo&d; beforan monna eagum gesewen suelce he f&ae;s&d;licu &amp; stranglecu weorc wyrce  &amp; &d;eah  &d;eah he swa do beforan monnum  for &d;am andan o&d;erra monna godena weorca  he bi&d; aswunden oninnan him selfum. 
 For&d;y is wel gecueden &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sclice lif sie &d;&ae;re heortan h&ae;lo  for&d;&ae;m se &d;e gehielt his unsceadfulnesse &amp; his godan willan  &d;eah he hw&ae;t tiederlices o&d;&d;e yfelra weorca utan doo  he m&ae;g &d;&ae;t &ae;t sumum cierre betan. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t is sui&d;e ryhte gecueden be &d;&ae;m banum &d;&ae;t hie forrotigen for &d;&ae;m &ae;fste  for&d;&ae;m for &d;&ae;s &ae;fstes scylde forweor&d;a&d; &d;a godan weorc  &d;eah &d;e hie beforan monna eagum &d;yncen trumlice gedon. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t &d;a ban forrotigen for &d;&ae;m &ae;fste &d;&ae;t he forleose sum sui&d;e god weorc for &d;&ae;m &ae;fste. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a bilwitan  on o&d;re &d;a &d;weoran &amp; &d;a lytegan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a biliwitan  on o&d;re &d;a lytegan. 
 &D;a bilewitan sint to herigenne  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie simle suinca&d; on &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi tieligea&d; &d;&ae;t hie ne sculen leasunga secgan. 
 Hie mon sceal eac l&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hi hwilum suigien &d;&ae;s so&d;es  for&d;&ae;m  sua sua sio leasung simle deret &d;&ae;m secggendum  sua dere&d; eac hwilum sumum monnum &d;&ae;t so&d; to gehierenne. 
 For&d;&ae;m ure Dryhten gemetgode mid suigean his spr&ae;ce beforan his &d;egnum  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Fela ic h&ae;bbe eow to secganne  ac ge hit ne magon nu giet aberan. 
 &D;y sint to manianne &d;a bilwitan anfealdan &d;&ae;tte  sua sua hie &d;a leasunga nyttwyr&d;lice fleo&d;  &d;&ae;t hie eac &d;&ae;t so&d; nytwyr&d;lice secgen  &amp; geicen &d;a god hira anfealdnesse mid w&ae;rscipe  &amp; sua tilige &d;&ae;re orsorgnesse mid &d;&ae;re anfealdnesse &d;&ae;tte he &d;one ymbe&d;onc &d;&ae;s w&ae;rscipes ne forl&ae;te. 
 Be &d;am cw&ae;&d; se &ae;&d;ela lareow sanctus Paulus: Ic wille &d;&ae;t ge sien wise to gode &amp; bilwite to yfele. 
 Ond eft be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Dryhten &d;urh hine selfne to his gecorenum: Beo ge swa ware sua sua n&ae;dran &amp; sua bilwite sua culfran. 
 For&d;&ae;m on &d;ara acorenra monna heortan sceal &d;&ae;re n&ae;dran lytignes &amp; hire ni&d; &d;&ae;re culfran biliwitnesse gescirpan  &amp; eft &d;&ae;re culfran biliwitnesse sceal gemetgian &d;&ae;re n&ae;dran w&ae;rscipe &amp; hire ni&d;  &d;yl&ae;s hine se w&ae;rscipe &amp; se anda gel&ae;de on ealles to micle hatheortnesse  o&d;&d;e eft sio bilewitnes &amp; sio anfealdnes hine to ungeornfulne gedoo to ongietanne  &d;yl&ae;s he weor&d;e besolcen. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t mon sceal monian &d;a lytegan  &amp; him secgan &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hu hefig &d;&ae;t twiefalde gesuinc bi&d; &d;&ae;t hie him selfe &d;urh hira agena scylda hira agnes gewealdes him on geteo&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t hie eallneg r&ae;swa&d; &amp; ondr&ae;da&d; &d;&ae;t hi mon t&ae;lan wille  &amp; beo&d; eallneg mid &d;&ae;m ymbe&d;oncan abisgode &amp; ofdr&ae;dde. 
 O&d;er is &d;ara gesuinca &d;&ae;t hi simle secea&d; endelease ladunga  hu hie &d;onne bereccan m&ae;gen. 
 Ac nis nan scild trumra wi&d; &d;&ae;t tuiefalde gesuinc &d;onne mon sie untwiefeald  for&d;&ae;m&d;e nawuht nis ie&d;re to gesecganne  ne eac to geliefanne &d;onne so&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne hwa on &d;a leasunga befeh&d;  &d;onne ne m&ae;g he of  ac sceal &d;onne niede &d;encean hu he hie gelicettan m&ae;ge  &amp; gewerga&d; &d;onne his heortan sui&d;e hearde mid &d;y gesuince. 
 Be &d;&ae;m gesuince spr&ae;c se salmscop  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t gesuinc hira agenra welena hie ge&d;ryc&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m se ilca feond se &d;e nu &d;&ae;t mod &d;urh &d;a bisuiculan olicunga forl&ae;re&d;  he hit eft mid sui&d;e grimmum edleane ge&d;rysc&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh Ieremias &d;one witgan: Hie l&ae;rdon hira tungan  &amp; wenedon to leasunge  &amp; swuncon on unryhtum weorce. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: &d;a &d;e meahton Godes friend beon butan gesuince  hie suuncon ymb &d;&ae;t hu hie meahton gesyngian. 
 Wietodlice  &d;onne hwa nyle bielwitlice libban butan gesuince  he wile geearnian mid his gesuince his agenne dea&d;. 
 Ac monige menn  &d;onne him beo&d; un&d;eawas on anfundene  &d;onne anscuniga&d; hie &d;&ae;t mon wite hwelce hie sien  &amp; wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie hie gehyden &amp; beheligen under &d;&ae;m ryfte &d;&ae;re leasunga  ge fur&d;um &d;ara scylda &d;e openlice beo&d; gesewena  hie wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie scylen hie beladian sua georne &d;&ae;tte oft se &d;e wilna&d; hiera un&d;eawas arasian  bi&d; openlice besuicen &amp; ablend mid &d;&ae;m miste &d;&ae;re leasunga  sua &d;&ae;t him fulneah &d;ync&d; &d;&ae;tte his nawuht sua ne sie sua sua he &ae;r witodlice be him wende. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ryhtlice bi Iudeum w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh &d;one witgan ymb &d;&ae;t synfulle mod &d;e hit simle wile ladian  he cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r se iil h&ae;fde his holh. 
 Se iil getacna&d; &d;a twiefealdnesse &d;&ae;s uncl&ae;nan modes &d;e hit symle lytiglice lada&d;  sua sua se iil  &ae;r&d;&ae;m he gefangen weor&d;e  mon m&ae;g gesion &ae;g&d;er ge his fet ge his heafod ge eac eall &d;&ae;t bodig  ac sona sua hiene mon gefeh&d;  sua gewint he to anum cliewene  &amp; tih&d; his fet sua he inmest m&ae;g  &amp; gehyt his heafod  sua &d;&ae;tte betwuh hondum &d;u nast hw&ae;r him aw&d;er cym&d;  o&d;&d;e fet o&d;&d;e heafod  &amp; &ae;r  &ae;r &d;u his o onhriene  &d;u meahtes geseon &ae;g&d;er ge fet ge heafod. 
 Swa do&d; &d;a lytegan &amp; &d;a uncl&ae;nan mod: &d;onne him bi&d; sum un&d;eaw on onfunden  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;s iles heafud gesewen; 
 &D;onne mon m&ae;g ongietan of hwam hit &ae;res&d; com  &amp; for hw&ae;m. 
 &amp; &d;onne beo&d; &d;a fet gesewene  &d;onne mon ongiet mid hwelcum st&ae;pum &d;&ae;t nawht w&ae;s &d;urhtogen  ac &d;eah &d;&ae;t uncl&ae;ne mod sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice feh&d; on &d;a ladunga  &amp; mid &d;&ae;re behele&d; his fet &amp; &d;a st&ae;pas his unnyttan weorces. 
 &D;onne he tieh&d; his heafod in to him  &d;onne he mid wunderlicre ladunga &ae;tiew&d; &d;&ae;t he fur&d;um n&ae;fre &d;&ae;t yfel ne ongunne  sua he hit h&ae;f&d; mid his lotwrencium bewunden oninnan him selfum  suelce se lareow h&ae;bbe an cliwen on his honda sui&d;e nearwe &amp; sui&d;e smealice gefealden  &amp; nyte hw&ae;r se ende sie  sua feor &amp; sua f&ae;ste hit bi&d; gefealden oninnan &d;&ae;s synnfullan monnes inge&d;once  &amp; mid his lote bewunden  &d;&ae;tte se lareow &d;&ae;s yfeles &d;e he stieran scolde  &d;eah &d;e he hit &ae;r wis&d;e  &d;&ae;t he hit &d;onne nat  &amp; eall &d;&ae;t he &ae;r t&ae;lwyr&d;lices geseah mid &d;am forhwirfdan gewunan &d;&ae;re unryhtan ladunge he bi&d; amierred &d;&ae;t he hit eal endemes forl&ae;t  &amp; his nanwuht nat. 
 Wietodlice se il h&ae;f&d; his holh on &d;&ae;s unnyttan monnes heortan  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t yfelwillende mod gefielt hit self twiefald oninnan him selfum  &amp; gehyt hine on &d;&ae;m &d;iestran mid &d;&ae;re ladunge  sua se iil hine selfne gehyt on him selfum. 
 Gehieren &d;a uncl&ae;nan &amp; &d;a lytegan hu hit awriten is on Salomonnes bocum &d;&ae;tte se libbe getreowlice se &d;e bilwitlice libbe. 
 &D;&ae;t is se truwa micelre orsorgnesse  biliwitnes &amp; anfealdnes his weorca. 
 Gehira&d; hw&ae;t of &d;&ae;s wisan Salomonnes mu&d;e w&ae;s gecueden; 
 He cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;s Halgan G&ae;stes lar wille fleon leasunga. 
 Gehira&d; eac &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;r&ae;fter awriten is &d;&ae;tte he h&ae;bbe his ge&d;eaht &amp; his sundorspr&ae;ce mid &d;&ae;m bilwitum &amp; mid &d;&ae;m anfealdum. 
 &D;onne spric&d; God to &d;&ae;m menn  &d;onne he onlieht &d;&ae;t mennisce mod mid his agenre andweardnesse  &amp; him his dieglan &d;ing geopena&d;. 
 &D;onne is eac gecueden &d;&ae;tte God spr&ae;ce to &d;&ae;m bilwitum  &d;onne he mid &d;&ae;m uplicum &amp; mid &d;&ae;m dieglum &d;ingum hira mod onlieht mid &d;&ae;m sciman his giefe &amp; his fandunga &amp; eac his tiehtinge. 
 &D;&ae;t beo&d; &d;onne ealles sui&d;us&d; &d;a mod &d;a &d;e nan sceadu ne ge&d;iestra&d; &d;&ae;re twiefaldnesse. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t is &d;eah syndrig yfel twiefaldra monna &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne hie o&d;re menn mid hira lote bismria&d;  &d;onne gielpa&d; hie &amp; f&ae;genia&d; &d;&ae;s  suelce hi sien micle w&ae;rran &amp; wisran &d;onne hie  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie ne ge&d;encea&d; &d;a &d;earlan edlean  ac f&ae;gnia&d; irmingas hiera agnes dysiges &amp; hearmes. 
 Gehiren eac &d;a ilcan mid hwelcum ymbe&d;once godcundes onwaldes hie &d;reade Soffonias se witga  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Giet cym&d; se micla &amp; se m&ae;ra &amp; se egeslica Godes d&ae;g  se d&ae;g bi&d; irres d&ae;g &amp; &d;iestra d&ae;g &amp; mistes &amp; gebreces &amp; biemena d&ae;g &amp; gedynes ofer ealla truma ceastra &amp; ofer ealle hea hwammas. 
 Hw&ae;t getacnia&d; &d;onne &d;a truman ceastra butan hwurfulu mod  getrymedu &amp; ymbtrymedu mid lytelicre ladunge  &d;&ae;t him ne magon to cuman &d;a speru &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse  &d;&ae;t sindon haligra gewrita manunga? 
 Wi&d; &d;a speru &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;stnesse hie hie scilda&d;  &d;onne hi mon t&ae;lan wile &amp; arasian for hira un&d;eawum. 
 Hw&ae;t getacnia&d; &d;onne &d;a hean hwammas buton uncl&ae;nu &amp; twiefeald mod? 
 For&d;&ae;m &ae;lc wag bi&d; gebieged twiefeald on &d;&ae;m heale. 
 Sua bi&d; &d;&ae;s monnes heorte: &d;onne he &d;a bilewitnesse &amp; &d;a anfealdnesse flih&d;  he gefielt his mod mid wore &amp; mid unnytre twiefealdnesse  &amp; eac &d;&ae;tte wierse bi&d;  he hine ahef&d; on his ge&d;ohte on gielp &amp; on ofermetto for &d;&ae;m w&ae;rscipe his agenre scylde  &amp; de&d; his agenne un&d;eaw him to weor&d;scipe. 
 &D;onne cym&d; se Dryhtnes domes d&ae;g &amp; wrace d&ae;g ofer &d;a truman ceastra &amp; ofer &d;a hean hwammas  &d;onne &d;&ae;t ierre &d;&ae;s ytemestan domes &d;a menniscan heortan towyrp&d;  &d;a &d;e nu sindon betynede &amp; getrymede mid lytelicum ladungum wi&d; &d;a so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse  &amp; arafa&d; &d;&ae;t cliwen &d;&ae;re twifaldan heortan. 
 &D;onne fealla&d; &d;a truman ceastra  &d;onne &d;a mod &d;e Dryhtne ungeferu sint weor&d;a&d; gesciende. 
 &D;onne fealla&d; &d;a hean hwammas  &d;onne &d;a heortan &d;e hie ahebba&d; for &d;&ae;re tuiefealdnesse &d;&ae;s unryhtan w&ae;rscipes &d;urh ryhtlicne cuide &amp; dom weor&d;a&d; ofdune aworpne. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&t;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a halan  on o&d;re &d;a unhalan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a truman  on o&d;re &d;a untruman. 
 &D;a truman sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie gewilnigen mid &d;&ae;s licuman trumnesse &d;&ae;t him ne losige sio h&ae;lo &d;&ae;s modes  &d;yl&ae;s him &d;y wirs sie  gif hie &d;a trumnesse &d;&ae;re Godes giefe him to unnyte gehweorfa&d;  &amp; &d;yl&ae;s hie si&d;&d;an geearnigen sua micle hefigre wite sua hie nu egeleaslicor &amp; unnytlicor bruca&d; &d;&ae;re mildheortlican Godes giefe. 
 For&d;on sint to manianne &d;a halan &d;&ae;t hie ne forhycgen &d;&ae;t hie her on worulde on &d;&ae;re hwilendlican h&ae;lo him geearnigen &d;a ecan h&ae;lo. 
 Ymb &d;a hwilendlican tida sanctus Paulus spr&ae;c  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Nu is hiersumnesse tima &amp; nu sint h&ae;lnesse dagas. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a halan &d;&ae;t hie Gode wilnigen to licianne &d;e hwile &d;e hie m&ae;gen  &d;yl&ae;s hie eft ne m&ae;gen  &d;onne hie willen. 
 For&d;on w&ae;s gesprecen &d;urh &d;one wisan Salomonn bi &d;&ae;m Wisdome &d;&ae;t se Wisdom wille sona fleon &d;one &d;e hine flieh&d;  &d;onne he hine ful oft &ae;r to him cleopa&d;  &amp; he fors&ae;c&d; &d;&ae;t he him to cume. 
 Ac eft  &d;onne he &d;one Wisdom habban wolde  &amp; his wilna&d;  &d;onne cui&d; se Wisdom to him: Ic eow cleopode &ae;r to me  ac ge me noldon &ae;t cuman; 
 Ic r&ae;hte mine hond to eow  nolde iower nan to locian; 
 Ac ge forsawon eall min ge&d;eaht  &amp; leton eow to giemeleste  &d;onne ic eow cidde. 
 Hw&ae;t sceal ic &d;onne buton hliehchan &d;&ae;s  &d;onne ge to lose weor&d;a&d;  &amp; habban me &d;&ae;t to gamene  &d;onne eow &d;&ae;t yfel on becym&d; &d;&ae;t ge eow &ae;r ondredon? 
 Ond eac cui&d; se Wisdom eft: &d;onne hie to me clipia&d;  &d;onne nylle ic hie gehieran. 
 On uhtan hie arisa&d;  &amp; me secea&d;  ac hi me ne finda&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne se mon his lichoman h&ae;lo forsih&d;  &d;onne &d;onne he wel trum bi&d; to wyrceanne &d;&ae;t he &d;onne wile  &d;onne &d;onne him eft sio h&ae;l losa&d;  &d;onne gefred he &ae;res&d; hwelc heo to habbanne w&ae;s &d;a hwile &d;e he hi h&ae;fde  &amp; wilna&d; hire to late &amp; on untiman  &d;onne he &ae;r nolde hie gehealdan  &d;a &d;a he hi h&ae;fde. 
 For&d;&ae;m eft sui&d;e ryhtlice Salomonn cu&ae;&d;: Ne l&ae;t &d;u to &ae;l&d;iodigum &d;inne weor&d;scipe  ne on &d;&ae;s w&ae;lhreowan hond &d;in gear  &d;yl&ae;s fremde menn weor&d;en gefylled of &d;inum gesuince  &amp; &d;in m&ae;gen sie on o&d;res monnes gewealdum  &amp; &d;u &d;onne sargige for&d;&ae;m on las&d;  &d;onne &d;in lichoma beo to lore gedon  &amp; &d;in fl&ae;sc gebrosnod. 
 Hwa is &d;onne from us fremde butan &d;a awiergdan g&ae;stas  &d;a &d;e from &d;&ae;s hefencundan F&ae;der e&d;le adrifene sindon? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t is ure weor&d;scipe on &d;issum eor&d;licum lichoman buton &d;&ae;t we sint gesceapene &ae;fter &d;&ae;re biesene ures Scippendes? 
 &amp; hw&ae;t is elles se w&ae;lhreowa buton &d;a aworpnan englas  &d;e hie selfe mid hiera ofermettum on dea&d;es wite gebrohton? 
 &amp; on &d;one ilcan dea&d; hie wilnia&d; eal moncynn to forspananne &amp; to forl&ae;danne. 
 Hw&ae;t tacna&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t word elles &d;&ae;t mon ne selle his weor&d;scipe fremdum menn buton &d;&ae;tte se &d;e to Godes bisene gesceapen is  &d;onne he &d;a tid his lifes on gewil &d;ara awierdena g&ae;sta gehwierf&d;; 
 &amp; his gear gesele&d; w&ae;lhreowum  se se &d;e in yfelra &amp; wi&d;erweardra onwald forl&ae;t &d;a hwile his lifes? 
 Ond eac cu&ae;&d; Salomonn &d;&ae;t fremde ne scolden beon gefyllede ures m&ae;genes  &amp; ure gesuinc ne scolde beon on o&d;res monnes anwalde. 
 Sua hwa &d;onne sua on &d;isse worulde h&ae;f&d; Fulle h&ae;le his lichoman  &amp; nyle wisdomes &amp; cr&ae;ftes on his mode tiligan  ac suince&d; on &d;&ae;n &d;&ae;t he leornige un&d;eawas &amp; fremme  ne fyl&d; se no his agen hus godra cr&ae;fta  ac fremdra hus he fyl&d;  &d;&ae;t sint uncl&ae;ne g&ae;stas. 
 Wiotodlice &d;a &d;e hira lif on firenluste &amp; on ofermodnesse geendiga&d;  ne gefylla&d; hie godra rim  ac awiergedra g&ae;sta. 
 &D;onne is &ae;fter &d;&ae;m gecueden &d;&ae;t he sargige &ae;t niehstan  &d;onne his lichoma &amp; his fl&ae;sc sie gebrosnod  for&d;&ae;m oft sio h&ae;lo &d;&ae;s lichoman on un&d;eawas wier&d; gecierred  ac &d;onne he &d;&ae;re h&ae;lo benumen wier&d; mid monigfaldum sare &d;&ae;s modes &amp; &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sces  se lichoma &d;onne wier&d; gedrefed  for&d;&ae;m sio saul  &d;onne hio hire un&d;onces geb&ae;dd wier&d; &d;&ae;t yfel to forl&ae;tanne &d;&ae;t hio &ae;r longe on woh hire agnes &d;onces gedyde  sec&d; &d;onne &d;a forlorenan h&ae;lo  &amp; wilna&d; &d;&ae;re  suelce he &d;onne wel &amp; nytwyr&d;lice libban wolde  gif he for&d; moste. 
 Murcna&d; &d;onne for&d;y &d;&ae;t he Gode nolde &d;iowigan &d;a hwile &d;e he meahte  for&d;on he &d;onne &d;one demm his giemelieste mid nanum gesuince gebetan ne m&ae;g  buton him &d;urh his hreowsung &amp; &d;urh Godes miltse geholpen weor&d;e. 
 For&d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; se sealmscop: &d;onne God hie slog  &d;onne sohton hie hine. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a mettruman &d;&ae;t hie ongieten &amp; gefreden &d;&ae;t hie sua micle ma beo&d; Godes bearn  &amp; he hie sua micle ma lufa&d; sua he hie sui&d;ur mana&d; &amp; suing&d;  for&d;&ae;m  gif he &d;&ae;m gehiersuman mannum n&ae;fde geteohchad his e&d;el to sellanne  hwie wolde he hie mid &ae;negum unget&ae;sum l&ae;ran ? 
 For&d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Dryhten to Iohanne &d;am godspellere &d;urh his engel  he cu&ae;&d;: Ic &d;reage &amp; suinge &d;a &d;e ic lufige. 
 For&d;&ae;m eac cu&ae;&d; Salomonn: Sunu min  ne agiemeleasa &d;u Godes suingan  ne &d;u ne beo werig for his &d;reaunge  for&d;&ae;m&d;e God lufa&d; &d;one &d;e he &d;rea&d;  &amp; suinge&d; &ae;lc bearn &d;e he underfon wile. 
 Be &d;am ilcan se salmscop cu&ae;&d;: Sui&d;e monigfalde sint ryhtwisra monna earfo&d;u. 
 Be &d;&ae;m eac se eadega Iob cw&ae;&d; on his earfe&d;um  &amp; geomriende cliopode to Dryhtne  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Gif ic ryhtwis w&ae;s  ne ahof ic me no for&d;y  &amp; &d;eah ic eom gefylled mid broce &amp; mid ierm&d;um. 
 Eac is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;m mettrumum  gif hie willen geliefan &d;&ae;tte Godes rice hiera sie  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne her on worulde &d;oligen earfe&d;u &d;&ae;m timum &d;e hie &d;yrfen  sua sua mon sceal on el&d;iode. 
 Be &d;ys ilcan is gecueden on kyninga bocum  sua sua hit geworden w&ae;s  &amp; eac us to bisene. 
 Hit is gecueden &d;&ae;tte &d;a stanas on &d;&ae;m m&ae;ran temple Salomonnes w&ae;ron sua wel gefegede &amp; sua emne gesnidene &amp; gesme&d;de  &ae;r hie mon to &d;&ae;m stede brohte &d;e hie on standan scoldon  &d;&ae;tte hie mon eft si&d;&d;an on &d;&ae;re halgan stowe sua tosomne gesette &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r nan monn ne gehierde ne &ae;xe hlem ne bietles sueg. 
 &D;&ae;t &d;onne tacna&d; us &d;&ae;tte we scylen beon on &d;isse &ae;l&d;eodignesse utane beheawene mid suingellan  to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t we eft sien geteald &amp; gefeged to &d;&ae;m gefogstanum on &d;&ae;re Godes ceastre butan &d;&ae;m hiewete &ae;lcre suingean  &d;&ae;tte sua hw&ae;t sua nu on us unnytes sie  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t aceorfe sio suingelle from us  sua &d;&ae;tte si&d;&d;an an sibb Godes lufe butan &ae;lcum ungerade us sui&d;e f&ae;ste gebinde &amp; gefege tosomne. 
 &D;onne sint eac to manianne &d;a unhalan &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen mid hu monigfaldum unget&ae;sum &amp; mid hu heardum brocum us swinga&d; &amp; &d;reaga&d; ure worldcunde f&ae;dras &amp; hlafordas  for&d;&ae;m &d;e hie wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t we him ge&d;w&ae;re sien  &amp; eac hira irfes wier&d;e sien  &amp; hie us &d;e bli&d;ran beon m&ae;gen. 
 Ac hwelc wite sceal us &d;onne to hefig &d;yncan &d;&ae;re godcundan &d;reaunga wi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e we m&ae;gen geearnian &d;one hefonlican e&d;el &d;e n&ae;fre to lore ne weor&d;e&d;  &amp; for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t we m&ae;gen forbugan &d;&ae;t wite &d;&ae;t n&ae;fre ne wier&d; geendod? 
 For&d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Ure fl&ae;sclican f&ae;dras l&ae;rdon us  &amp; we hie ondredon; 
 Hie &d;readon us  &amp; we weor&d;odon hie. 
 Hu micle sui&d;or sculon we &d;onne beon gehiersume &d;&ae;m &d;e ure g&ae;sta F&ae;der bi&d; wi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t we moten libban on ecnesse. 
 Ure fl&ae;sclican f&ae;dras us l&ae;rdon to &d;&ae;m &d;e hira willa w&ae;s  ac &d;&ae;t w&ae;s to sui&d;e scortre hwile  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;ios woruld is sui&d;e l&ae;nu  ac se g&ae;s&d;lica F&ae;der he us l&ae;r&d; nytwyr&d;licu &d;ing to underfonne  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t we geearnigen &d;&ae;t ece lif. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a mettruman &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen hu micel h&ae;lo &d;&ae;t bi&d; &d;&ae;re heortan &d;&ae;t se lichoma sie medtrum  for&d;&ae;m sio medtrymnes &d;&ae;t mod gehwierf&d; gehwelces monnes hine selfne to ongietanne  &amp; &d;&ae;t gode mod &d;e sio h&ae;lo ful oft aweg adrief&d; &d;&ae;t gemynd &d;&ae;re medtrymnesse geedniewa&d;  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t mod &d;e ofer his m&ae;&d; bi&d; upah&ae;fen gemyne of &d;&ae;m suingum &d;e &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc &d;ola&d; to hw&ae;m eal monncynn gesceapen is. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;re sui&d;e ryhte getacnod &d;urh Balaham on &d;&ae;re lettinge his f&ae;reltes  gif he mid his hiersumnesse Godes stemne &amp; his gebodum fullice folgian wolde  &amp; on his willan fore. 
 Baloham &d;onne fulgeorne feran wolde &d;&ae;r hine mon b&ae;d  ac his estfulnesse witteah se esol &d;e he onuppan s&ae;t. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;s for&d;&ae;m&d;e se assa geseah &d;one engel ongean hine standan  &amp; him &d;&ae;s f&ae;reltes forwiernan  &d;one &d;e &d;&ae;t mennisce mod geseon ne meahte. 
 Sua eac  &d;onne &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc bi&d; gelett mid sumum broce  hit getacna&d; &d;&ae;m mode for &d;&ae;re suingan hw&ae;t Godes willa bi&d;  &d;one illcan willan &d;e &d;&ae;t mod hwilum ongietan m&ae;g &d;e ofer &d;&ae;m fl&ae;sce sitt  &amp; his wealdan sceolde  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc oft l&ae;tt &d;a geornfulnesse &amp; &d;one willan &d;&ae;s &d;iondan modes her on worulde. 
 Sua mon oft lett fundigendne monna  &amp; his f&ae;relt g&ae;l&d;  sua g&ae;l&d; se lichoma &d;&ae;t mod  o&d;&d;&ae;t he gebrocad wier&d; mid sumre mettrymnesse  &amp; &d;onne &d;urh &d;a mettrymnesse getacna&d; se lichoma &d;&ae;m mode &d;one ungesewenan engel &d;e him togenes stent  &amp; him wiern&d; his unnyttan f&ae;relta &d;urh &d;&ae;s lichoma mettrymnesse. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; sanctus Petrus sui&d;e ryhtlice: &d;&ae;t dumbe &amp; &d;&ae;t geh&ae;fte neat &d;reade &d;one witgan for his yfelan willan  &d;a hit cleopode sua sua monn  &amp; mid &d;y gestierde &d;&ae;m witgan his unryhtre &amp; dyslicre wilnunga. 
 &D;onne &d;rea&d; &d;&ae;t dumbe neat &d;one unwisan monn  &d;onne &d;&ae;t gebrocode fl&ae;sc gel&ae;r&d; &d;&ae;t upah&ae;fene mod to ryhttre &amp; to nyttwyr&d;re ea&d;modnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m ne meahte Balaham geearnian &d;a Godes giefe &d;e he biddende w&ae;s &d;a he Israhela folc wirgean wolde &amp; for hine selfne gebiddan; 
 For&d;&ae;m he wear&d; untyg&d;a &d;e he hwierfde his stemne nales his mod: &d;&ae;t w&ae;s &d;&ae;t he spr&ae;c o&d;er  o&d;er &d;&ae;t he sprecan wolde. 
 Eac sint &d;a seocan to monianne &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hu micel Godes giefu him bi&d; &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sces gesuinc  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hit &ae;g&d;er ge &d;a gedonan synna aweg a&d;wieh&d;  ge hine eac &d;ara gelett &d;e he don wolde  gif he meahte  for&d;&ae;m &d;onne he bi&d; gesargod on &d;&ae;s lichoman wundum  &d;onne gewyrcea&d; &d;a wunda on &d;&ae;m gebrocodan mode hreowsunge wunda. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m is eac awriten on Salomonnes cuidbocum &d;&ae;t sio wund wolde halian  &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e heo wyrmsde. 
 &D;onne aflew&d; &d;&ae;t sar of &d;&ae;re wunde mid &d;y wormse  &d;onne &d;&ae;t sar &d;&ae;re suingellan &d;issa woruldbroca a&d;wieh&d; &ae;g&d;er ge &d;a ge&d;ohtan synna ge &d;a gedonan of &d;&ae;re saule. 
 Eac cu&ae;&d; Salomon &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t illce beo bi &d;&ae;m wundum &d;e beo&d; oninnan &d;&ae;re wambe. 
 &D;&ae;re wambe nama getacna&d; &d;&ae;t mod  for&d;&ae;m sua sua sio wamb gemielt &d;one mete  sua gemielt &d;&ae;t mod mid &d;&ae;re gescadwisnesse his ge&d;eahtes his sorga. 
 Of Salomonnes cuidum we namon &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;re wambe nama scolde tacnian &d;&ae;t mod  &d;a &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;s monnes lif bi&d; Godes leohtf&ae;t; 
 &D;&ae;t Godes leohtf&ae;t gindsec&d; &amp; gindlieht ealle &d;a diogolnesse &d;&ae;re wambe. 
 Suelce he cu&ae;de: &ae;res&d; he hiene onlieht mid his leohtf&ae;te  &d;onne he hiene gelieff&ae;s&d;  &amp; eft he hine onlieht  &d;onne he hiene on&ae;l&d; mid &d;&ae;m tapure &d;&ae;s godcundan lieges. 
 &D;&ae;t bi&d; &d;onne  &d;onne he de&d; &d;&ae;t he ongiet his agne unnytte &d;eawas &amp; ge&d;ohtas &d;e wen is &d;&ae;t he &ae;r h&ae;fde  &d;eah he hit ge&d;encean ne meahte. 
 &D;&ae;t worms &d;onne &d;ara wunda &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t broc &d;&ae;s lichoman  &amp; &d;&ae;t sar innan &d;&ae;re wambe  &d;&ae;t tacna&d; &d;a sorge &d;&ae;s modes. 
 Sio sorg &d;onne asw&ae;p&d; aweg &d;&ae;t yfel of &d;&ae;m mode. 
 &D;onne we beo&d; butan &d;&ae;m mode on &d;&ae;m lichoman gesuencte  &d;onne beo we suigende gemanode mid &d;&ae;re mettrymnesse ura synna to gemunanne  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;onne bi&d; broht beforan ures modes eagan eall &d;&ae;t we &ae;r yfeles gedydon  for&d;&ae;m sua se lichoma sui&d;ur utan &d;rowa&d;  sua &d;&ae;t mod sui&d;ur innan hreowsa&d; &d;&ae;s unnyttes &d;e he &ae;r dyde. 
 For&d;&ae;m gelimp&d; &d;&ae;tte &d;urh &d;a openlican wunda &amp; &d;urh &d;&ae;t gesewene sar &d;&ae;s lichoman bi&d; sui&d;e wel a&d;w&ae;gen sio diegle wund &d;&ae;s modes  for&d;&ae;m sio diegle wund &d;&ae;re hreowsunga h&ae;l&d; &d;a scyl&d;e &d;&ae;s won weorces. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a mettruman to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie gehealden &d;a strenge &d;&ae;re ge&d;ylde. 
 Him is to secgeanne &d;&ae;t hie unablinnendlice ge&d;encen hu monig yfel ure Dryhten &amp; ure Alisend ge&d;olode mid &d;am ilcan mannum &d;e he self gesceop  &amp; hu fela edwites &amp; unnyttra worda he forb&ae;r  &amp; hu manige hleorsl&ae;geas he underfeng &ae;t &d;&ae;m &d;e hine bismredon. 
 Se ilca se &d;e &ae;lce d&ae;g saula gereafa&d; of &d;&ae;s ealdan feondes honda  se ilca se &d;e us &d;wieh&d; mid &d;y halwyndan w&ae;tre  se na ne forbeag mid his nebbe &d;ara triowleasena monna spatl  &d;onne hie him on &d;&ae;t nebb sp&ae;tton. 
 Se ilca se us gefreo&d; mid his forespr&ae;ce from ecum witum  se ilca suigende ge&d;afode swingellan. 
 Se &d;e us sealde ece are betwuxn his engla geferscipe  he ge&d;afode &d;&ae;t hine mon mid fyste slog. 
 Se &d;e us geh&ae;le&d; from &d;&ae;m stice urra synna  he ge&d;afode &d;&ae;t him mon sette &d;yrnenne beag on &d;&ae;t heafud. 
 Se &d;e us oferdrenc&d; mid &d;&ae;s ecan lifes li&d;e  he gefandode geallan biternesse  &d;a hine &d;yrstte. 
 Se &d;e for us geb&ae;d to his F&ae;der  &d;eah he him emnmiehtig sie on his godhade  &d;a &d;a him mon on bismer to geb&ae;d  &d;a swugode he. 
 Se se &d;e deadum monnum lif gearuwa&d;  &amp; he self lif is  he becom to dea&d;e. 
 Forhwy &d;onne sceal &ae;nigum menn &d;yncan to re&d;e o&d;&d;e to unie&d;e &d;&ae;t he Godes suingellan ge&d;afige for his yfelum d&ae;dum  nu God self sua fela yfeles ge&d;afode  sua sua we &ae;r cu&ae;don  for monncynne? 
 Hwa sceal &d;onne  &d;ara &d;e hal &amp; good andgiet h&ae;bbe  Gode un&d;oncfull beon  for&d;&ae;m  &d;eah he hine for his synnum suinge  ne se ne for butan suingellan of &d;ys middangearde se &d;e butan &ae;lcre synne w&ae;s &amp; giet is?
