 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e him ondr&ae;da&d; Godes swingellan o&d;&d;e monna  &amp; for&d;y forl&ae;ta&d; &d;&ae;t hie yfel ne do&d;; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e beo&d; swa aheardode on unryhtwisnesse &d;&ae;t hi mon ne m&ae;g mid nanre &d;reaunge ge&d;reatian. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e him suingellan ondr&ae;da&d;  &amp; for&d;&ae;m unscea&d;fullice libba&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e on hiera unryhtwisnessum sua aheardode beo&d; &d;&ae;t hie mon mid nanre swingellan gebetan ne m&ae;g. 
 &D;&ae;t is to cy&d;anne &d;e him swingellan ondr&ae;da&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;issa eor&d;licena goda to sui&d;e ne gietsien  &d;eah hie geseon &d;&ae;t &d;a yfelan hie h&ae;bben ongemong him  for&d;&ae;m hie sint &ae;g&d;rum gem&ae;ne ge yfelum monnum ge godum; 
 &amp; ne fleon eac &d;is andwearde yfel  suelce hie hit adriogan ne m&ae;gen  for&d;on&d;e hit oft gode menn her on worlde dreoga&d;. 
 Eac hie sint to monianne  gif hie geornlice wilnigen &d;&ae;t him yfel &d;ing losie  &d;onne beo him sui&d;e egefull &d;&ae;t ece wite; 
 Nalles &d;eah sua egeful &d;&ae;t hie ealneg &d;urhwunigen on &d;&ae;m ege  ac mid &d;am fostre &d;&ae;re Godes lufan hie sculon up arisan &amp; weaxan a ma &amp; ma to lufigeanne &d;a godcundan weorc. 
 For&d;&ae;m Iohannis se godspellere cw&ae;&d; on his &ae;rendgewrite  ic cw&ae;&d;: Sio fulfremede Godes lufu adrife&d; aweg &d;one ege. 
 &amp; eft cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Ne underfengon ge no &d;one Gast &ae;t &d;&ae;m fulluhte to &d;eowigeanne for ege  ac ge hine underfengon to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t ge Gode geagenudu bearn beon scielen  for&d;y we cliepia&d; to Gode  &amp; cwe&d;a&d;  F&ae;der  F&ae;der. 
 For&d;&ae;m cwi&d; eft eac se ilca lariow: &d;&ae;r se Dryhtnes gast is  &d;&ae;r is freodoom. 
 Gif &d;onne hwelc mon forbire&d; his synna for &d;&ae;m ege anum &d;&ae;s wites  &d;onne nafa&d; &d;&ae;s ondr&ae;dendan monnes mod nanne gastes freodom  for&d;&ae;m  gif he hit for &d;&ae;s wites ege ne forlete  butan tweon he fulfremede &d;a synne. 
 &D;onne nat &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;t him bi&d; freodom forgiefen  &d;onne hit bi&d; gebunden mid &d;&ae;s &d;eowutes ege. 
 &D;eah monn nu good onginne for sumes wites ege  hit mon sceal &d;eah geendigean for sumes godes lufum. 
 Se &d;e for &d;&ae;m anum god de&d; &d;&ae;t he sumre &d;reaunge yfel him ondr&ae;tt  se wilna&d; &d;&ae;tte nan &d;ing ne sie &d;e he him ondr&ae;dan &d;yrfe  &d;&ae;t he &d;y orsorglicor dyrre don unnyttlicu &d;ing &amp; unalifedu. 
 &D;onne bi&d; sui&d;e sweotol &d;&ae;tte him &d;onne losa&d; beforan Gode his ryhtwisnes  &d;onne he &d;urh his agene geornfulnesse gesynga&d; unniedenga  &d;onne bi&d; sui&d;e sueotul &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t good na ne dyde &d;&ae;r he hit for &d;&ae;m ege dorste forl&ae;tan. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t &d;onne sint to monianne &d;a menn &d;e suingellan ne magon forwiernan ne na gelettan hiera unryhtwisnesse. 
 Hie beo&d; to &d;reageanne &amp; to swinganne mid swa micle maran wite sua hie ungefredelicor beo&d; aheardode on hiera un&d;eawum. 
 Oft eac &d;a swelcan monn sceal forsion mid eallum forsewennessum  &amp; unweor&d;ian mid &ae;lcre unweor&d;nesse  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte sio forsewennes him ege &amp; ondrysnu on gebringe  &amp; eft &ae;fter &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hiene sio godcunde manung on wege gebringe  &amp; hine to hyhte gehwierfe. 
 &D;onne sint eac &d;&ae;m ilcan monnum sui&d;e &d;earllice to recceanne &d;a godcundan cwidas  &d;&ae;t hie bi &d;am oncnaw&ae;n  &d;onne hie ge&d;encen &d;one ecean dom  to hw&ae;m hiera agen wise wir&d;. 
 Eac hie sculon gehieran &d;&ae;t on him bi&d; gefylled Salomonnes cwide &d;e he cw&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: &d;eah &d;u portige &d;one dysegan on pilan  swa mon corn de&d; mid piilst&ae;fe  ne meaht &d;u his dysi him from adrifan. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce sarette se witga  &d;a &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: &d;u hie tobr&ae;ce  &amp; &d;eah hie noldon underfon &d;ine lare. 
 Eft bi &d;&ae;m ilcan cw&ae;&d; Dryhten: Ic ofslog &d;is folc  &amp; to forlore gedyde  &amp; hie hie &d;eah noldon onwendan from hiera woom wegum  &d;&ae;t is  from hiera yfelum weorcum. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m ilcan eft cw&ae;&d; se witga: &d;is folc nis no gewend to &d;&ae;m &d;e hie swing&d;. 
 Ymb &d;&ae;t ilce sargode se witga  sua sua god lareow de&d;  &d;onne he his gingran suing&d;  gif hit him nauht ne forstent. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; se witga: We lacnodon Babylon  &amp; hio &d;eah ne wear&d; geh&ae;led. 
 &D;onne bi&d; Babylon gelacnad  nales &d;eah fullice geh&ae;led  &d;onne &d;&ae;s monnes mod for his unryhtum willan &amp; for his won weorcum gehier&d; sceamlice &d;reaunga  &amp; sceandlice suingellan underfeh&d;  &amp; &d;eahhw&ae;&d;re oferhyg&d; &d;&ae;t he gecierre to bettran. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce eac Dryhten o&d;wat Israhela folce  &d;a hie w&ae;ron gehergeode &amp; of hiera earde al&ae;dde  &amp; swa&d;eah noldon gesuican hiera yfelena weorca  ne hie noldon awendan of hiera won wegum; 
 &D;a cw&ae;&d; Dryhten: &d;iss Israhela folc is geworden nu me to sindrum &amp; to are &amp; to tine &amp; to iserne &amp; to leade inne on minum ofne. 
 Suelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Ic hie wolde gecl&ae;nsian mid &d;&ae;m gesode &d;&ae;s broces  &amp; wolde &d;&ae;t hie wurden to golde &amp; to seolufre  ac hie wurdon gehwierfde inne on &d;am ofne to are &amp; to tine &amp; to isene &amp; to leade  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie noldon on &d;&ae;m gesuincium hie selfe gecirran to nyttum &d;ingum  ac &d;urhwunedon on hiera un&d;eawum. 
 Witodlice &d;&ae;t ar  &d;onne hit mon slih&d;  hit bi&d; hludre &d;onne &ae;nig o&d;er ondweorc. 
 Sua bi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e sui&d;e gnorna&d; on &d;&ae;re godcundan suingellan  he bi&d; on middum &d;&ae;m ofne gecirred to are. 
 &D;&ae;t tin &d;onne  &d;onne hit mon mid sumum cr&ae;fte gemeng&d;  &amp; to tine gewyrc&d;  &d;onne bi&d; hit swi&d;e leaslice on siolufres hiewe. 
 Sua hwa &d;onne sua licet on &d;&ae;re swingellan  he bi&d; &d;&ae;m tine gelic inne on &d;&ae;m ofne. 
 Se bi&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;m isene gelic inne on &d;&ae;m ofne  se &d;e for &d;&ae;re suingellan nyle his &d;weorscipe forl&ae;tan  ac ofan his nihstan his lifes. 
 &D;&ae;t lead &d;onne is hefigre &d;onne &ae;nig o&d;er andweorc. 
 For&d;y bi&d; inne on &d;&ae;m ofne geworden to leade se se &d;e sua bi&d; ge&d;rysced mid &d;&ae;re hefignesse his synna &d;&ae;t he fur&d;um on &d;&ae;m broce nyle al&ae;tan his geornfulnesse &amp; &d;as eor&d;lican wilnunga. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m ilcan is eft awriten: &d;&ae;r w&ae;s sui&d;e sui&d;lic gesuinc  &amp; &d;&ae;r w&ae;s micel swat agoten  &amp; &d;eah ne meahte monn him of animan &d;one miclan rust  ne fur&d;um mid fyre ne meahte hiene mon aweg adon. 
 He us stiere&d; mid fyres broce  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wolde from us adon &d;one rust urra un&d;eawa  ac we &d;eah for &d;&ae;m broce &d;&ae;s fyres nylla&d; al&ae;tan from us &d;&ae;t rust &d;ara unnyttra weorca  &d;onne we on &d;&ae;re suingellan nylla&d; gebetan ure un&d;eawas. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; eft se witga: Idel w&ae;s se blawere  for&d;on hiera awirgdan weorc ne wurdon from him asyndred. 
 Eac is to witanne &d;&ae;tte oft &d;&ae;m bi&d; gestiered mid man&d;w&ae;rlicre manunga  &d;&ae;m &d;e monn mid heardre suingellan gecirran ne m&ae;g  &amp; &d;a &d;e ne magon &d;rouunga gestieran yfelra weorca  eft hie hie forl&ae;ta&d; for li&d;elicre olicunga  sua sua &d;a seocan  &d;a &d;e mon oft ne m&ae;g gelacnian mid &d;&ae;m drencium strangra wyrta gemanges  &d;a ful oft beo&d; mid wlacum watre gelacnode  &amp; on &d;&ae;re ilcan h&ae;lo gebrohte &d;e hie &ae;r h&ae;fdon. 
 Sua beo&d; eac ful oft &d;a wunda mid ele geh&ae;lda  &d;a &d;e mon mid gesnide gebetan ne meahte. 
 &amp; eac se hearda stan  se &d;e a&d;amans hatte  &d;one mon mid nane isene ceorfan ne m&ae;g  gif his mon onhrin&d; mid buccan blode  he hnesca&d; ongean &d;&ae;t li&d;e blod to &d;&ae;m sui&d;e &d;&ae;t hine se cr&ae;ftega wyrcean m&ae;g to &d;&ae;m &d;e he wile. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e to swi&d;e swige beo&d;  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e willa&d; to fela idles &amp; unnyttes gespr&ae;can. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a sui&d;e suigean  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e beo&d; aidlode on oferspr&ae;ce. 
 &D;a sui&d;e suigean mon sceal l&ae;ran &d;&ae;tte hie  &d;onne &d;onne hie sumne un&d;eaw unw&ae;rlice fleo&d;  &d;&ae;t hie ne sien to wyrsan gecirde  &amp; &d;&ae;ron befealdne  sua him oft gebyre&d;  &d;onne hie hiora tungan ungemetlice gemidlia&d; &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; micle hefiglicor gedrefde on hiera heortan &d;onne &d;a oferspr&ae;cean  for&d;&ae;m for &d;&ae;re suigean hiora ge&d;ohtas beo&d; aweallene on hiora mode  for&d;&ae;m hie hie selfe nida&d; to healdonne ungemetlice swigean  &amp; for&d;&ae;m beo&d; sui&d;e for&d;rycte. 
 For&d;&ae;m gebyre&d; oft &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; sua micle ungest&ae;&d;&d;elicor toflowene on hiera mode sua hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie stilran &amp; orsorgtran beon m&ae;gen for hiera suigean. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e mon ne m&ae;g utane on him ongietan for hiera suigean hw&ae;t mon t&ae;le  hie beo&d; innane oft ahafene on ofermettum  swa &d;&ae;t hie &d;a felasprecan forseo&d;  &amp; hie for nauht do&d;  &amp; ne ongieta&d; na hu sui&d;e hie onluca&d; hiera mod mid &d;&ae;m un&d;eawe ofermetta  &d;eah hie &d;&ae;s lichoman mu&d; belucen; 
 &D;eah sio tunge ea&d;modlice licge  &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; sui&d;e upahafen  &amp; sua micle freolicor he t&ae;l&d; on his inge&d;once ealle o&d;re menn sua he l&ae;s ongitt his agene uncysta. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a sui&d;e suigean ; 
 &D;&ae;t hie geornlice tiligen to wietanne &d;&ae;t him nis na &d;&ae;s anes &d;earf to &d;enceanne hwelce hie hie selfe utane eowien mannum  ac him is micle mare &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen hwelce hi hie innan geeowigen Gode  &amp; &d;&ae;t hi swi&d;or him ondr&ae;den for hiera ge&d;ohtum &d;one diglan Deman  &d;e hie ealle wat  &d;onne hie him ondr&ae;den wi&d; hiera wordum &amp; d&ae;dum hiera geferena t&ae;linge. 
 Hit is awriten on Salomonnes cwidum: Sunu min  ongiet minne wisdom &amp; minne w&ae;rscipe  &amp; behald &d;in eagean &amp; &d;in earan to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte &d;u m&ae;ge &d;in ge&d;oht gehealdan. 
 For&d;&ae;m nan wuht nis on us unstilre &amp; ungest&ae;&d;&d;igre &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod  for&d;&ae;m hit gewitt sua oft fram us sua us unnytte ge&d;ohtas to cuma&d;  &amp; &ae;fter &ae;lcum &d;ara toflew&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; se psalmsceop: Min mod &amp; min wisdom me forlet &amp; eft he gehwearf to him selfum  &amp; wear&d; on his agenum gewitte  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &d;in &d;eow h&ae;f&d; nu funden his wisdom  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he hine gebidde to &d;e. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne monn his mod geh&ae;ft  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hit &ae;r gewunode to fleonne hit gemet. 
 Oft eac &d;a sui&d;e suigean  &d;onne hie monige unnytte ge&d;ohtas innan habba&d;  &d;onne weor&d;a&d; hie him to &d;y maran sare innan  gif hie hi ut ne spreca&d;  ond hwilum gebyre&d;  gif he hit ged&ae;ftelice as&ae;g&d;  &d;&ae;t he mid &d;y his sorge gebet. 
 Hw&ae;t we wieton &d;&ae;t sio diegle wund bi&d; sarre &d;onne sio opene  for&d;am &d;&ae;t worsm &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;rinne gehweled bi&d;  gif hit bi&d; utforl&ae;ten  &d;onne bi&d; sio wund geopenod to h&ae;lo &d;&ae;s sares. 
 Eac sculon weotan &d;a &d;e ma swugia&d; &d;onne hie &d;yrfen  &d;&ae;tte hie hiera sorge ne geiecen mid &d;y &d;&ae;t hie hiora tungan gehealden. 
 Eac hie sint to manianne  gif hie hiera nihstan lufien swa sua hie selfe  &d;&ae;t hie him ne helen forhwy hi hie t&ae;len on hiera ge&d;ohte  for&d;&ae;m sio spr&ae;c cym&d; hiora &ae;g&d;rum to h&ae;lo  for&d;am&d;e hie &ae;g&d;er ge &d;&ae;t gehwelede on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum geopena&d; &amp; utforl&ae;t  &d;&ae;t he wier&d; &d;onon geh&ae;led  ge &d;one o&d;erne gel&ae;r&d;  &amp; his un&d;eawa gestier&d;. 
 Se &d;e &d;onne hw&ae;t yfeles ongiet on his nihstan  &amp; hit forswuga&d;  he de&d; sua sua se l&ae;ce &d;e gesceawa&d; his freondes wunde  &amp; nyle hie &d;onne gelacnigan. 
 Hu  ne bi&d; he &d;onne swelce he sie his slaga  &d;onne he hine m&ae;g geh&ae;lan  &amp; nyle? 
 For&d;&ae;m is sio tunge gemetlice to midliganne  nales ungemetlice to gebindanne. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten: Se wisa suiga&d;  o&d; he ongiet &d;&ae;t him bi&d; nyttre to sprecanne. 
 Nis hit nan wundur  &d;eah he swugie  &amp; bide his timan  ac &d;onne he nytwyr&d;ne timan ongiet to sprecenne  he forsih&d; &d;a swigean  &amp; spric&d; eall &d;&ae;t he nytwyr&d;es ongiet to sprecanne. 
 &amp; eft hit is awriten on Salomonnes bocum  &d;&ae;m &d;e Ecclesiastis hatton  &d;&ae;tte hwilum sie spr&ae;ce tiid  hwilum swigean. 
 For&d;&ae;m is gesceadwislice to &d;enceanne hwelcum tidum him gecopust sie to sprecanne  &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne he sprecan wille  he his tungan gehealde &d;&ae;t hio ne racige on unnytte spr&ae;ca  ne eft ne aseolce &d;&ae;r he nytte sprecan m&ae;g. 
 Be &d;&ae;m sui&d;e wel cw&ae;&d; se psalmsceop: Gesete Dryhten hirde minum mu&d;e &amp; &d;a duru gest&ae;&d;&d;ignesse. 
 Ne b&ae;d he no &d;&ae;t he hine elle fortynde mid gehale wage  ac he b&ae;d dura to  &d;&ae;t he meahte hwilum ontynan  hwilum betynan. 
 &D;y we sculon geleornian &d;&ae;t we sui&d;e w&ae;rlice gecope tiid aredigen  &amp; &d;onne sio stemn gesceadwislice &d;one mu&d; ontyne  &amp; eac &d;a tid gesceadwislice aredigen &d;e sio suige hine betynan scyle. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to l&ae;ranne &d;a oferspr&ae;cean &d;&ae;t hie wacorlice ongieten fram hu micelre ryhtwisnesse hie beo&d; gewietene  &d;onne hie on monigfealdum wordum slidriga&d;. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mennisce mod h&ae;f&d; w&ae;tres &d;eaw. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;ter  &d;onne hit bi&d; gepynd  hit micla&d; &amp; uppa&d; &amp; funda&d; wi&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e hit &ae;r from com  &d;onne hit flowan ne mot &d;ider hit wolde. 
 Ac gif sio pynding wier&d; onpennad  o&d;&d;e sio wering wir&d; tobrocen  &d;onne toflew&d; hit eall  &amp; ne wier&d; to nanre nytte  buton to fenne. 
 Sua de&d; &d;&ae;s monnes mod  &d;onne hit gesceadwislice ne can his swigean gehealdan  ac hit abric&d; ut on idle oferspr&ae;ce  &amp; wier&d; swa monigfealdlice on &d;&ae;m tod&ae;led  suelce hit eall lytlum ri&d;um torinne  &amp; ut of him selfum aflowe  &d;&ae;t hit eft ne m&ae;ge in to his agnum ondgiete &amp; to his inge&d;once gecirran. 
 &D;&ae;tte ne bi&d; for&d;&ae;m&d;e hit bi&d; tod&ae;led &amp; to monigfealda spr&ae;ca  suelce he self hine selfne ute betyne from &d;&ae;re smeaunga his agnes inge&d;onces  &amp; sua nacodne hine selfne eowige to wundigeanne his feondum  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he ne bi&d; belocen mid nanum gehieldum nanes f&ae;stenes. 
 Swa hit awriten is on Salomonnes cwidum &d;&ae;tte se mon se &d;e ne m&ae;g his tungan gehealdan sie gelicost openre byrig  &d;&ae;re &d;e mid nane wealle ne bi&d; ymbworht. 
 For&d;&ae;m sio burg &d;&ae;s modes  &d;e mid nanre suigean ne bi&d; bityned sceal sui&d;e oft gefredan hiere feonda speru  for&d;&ae;m hio &ae;tiewe&d; hie selfe sui&d;e opene hiere feondum  &d;onne hio hie selfe toweorpe&d; ut of hiere selfre mid unnyttum wordum  &amp; hio bi&d; micle &d;e ie&d;re to oferfeohtanne &d;e hio self fieht wi&d; hie selfe mid oferspr&ae;ce to fultome &d;&ae;m wi&d;feohtende  for&d;&ae;m hio bi&d; oft oferfohten butan &ae;lcum gesuince. 
 Oft &d;onne &d;&ae;t hefige mod glit ni&d;or &amp; ni&d;or st&ae;pm&ae;lum on unnyttum wordum  o&d; hit mid ealle afiel&d;  &amp; to nauhte wir&d;; 
 For&d;&ae;m hit &ae;r hit nolde behealdan wi&d; unnyt word  hit sceal &d;onne niedinga afeallan for &d;&ae;m slide. 
 &AE;t &ae;restum lyst &d;one monn unnyt sprecan be o&d;rum monnum  &amp; &d;onne &ae;fter firste hine lyst t&ae;lan &amp; slitan &d;ara lif butan scylde &d;e he &d;onne ymbspricd  o&d;&d;&ae;t hit on last of his tungan ut abirst to openum bismere &d;&ae;m o&d;rum. 
 Swa he s&ae;w&d; &d;one sticel &d;&ae;s andan  o&d;&d;&ae;t &d;&ae;rof aweox&d; towesnes  &amp; of &d;&ae;re towesnesse bi&d; &d;&ae;t fyr on&ae;led &d;&ae;re feounga  &amp; sio feoung adw&ae;sc&d; &d;a sibbe. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh &d;one wisan Salomon  &d;&ae;tte se se &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter utforlete w&ae;re fruma &d;&ae;re towesnesse. 
 Se forl&ae;t ut &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter  se &d;e his tungan stemne on unnyttum wordum l&ae;tt toflowan. 
 Ac se wisa Salomon s&ae;de &d;&ae;tte sui&d;e deop pol w&ae;re gewered on &d;&ae;s wisan monnes mode  &amp; sui&d;e lytel unnyttes utfleowe. 
 Ac se se &d;e &d;one wer bric&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter utforl&ae;t  se bi&d; fruma &d;&ae;s geflites. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne se &d;e his tungan ne gemidla&d;  se towierp&d; anmodnesse. 
 Eft cw&ae;&d; Salomon: Se gemetga&d; irre  se &d;e &d;one disigan h&ae;tt geswugian. 
 For&d;&ae;m se n&ae;fre ne m&ae;g ryhtwisnesse &amp; gesceadwisnesse healdan  se &d;e ofersprecol bi&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t tacnode se salmsceop  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Se oferspr&ae;cea wer ne wier&d; he n&ae;fre geryht ne gel&ae;red on &d;isse worlde. 
 Eft cw&ae;&d; Salomon bi &d;&ae;m ilcan: Ne bi&d; n&ae;fre sio oferspr&ae;c butan synne. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; eac Essaias se witga  he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;tte sio suyge w&ae;re &d;&ae;re ryhtwisnesse fultum &amp; midwyrhta. 
 &D;&ae;t &d;onne tacna&d; &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;s modes ryhtwisnes bi&d; toflowen  &d;e nele forhabban &d;a ungemetgodan spr&ae;ce. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Iacobus se apostol: Gif hwa teochha&d; &d;&ae;t he &ae;f&ae;st sie  &amp; nyle gemidlian his tungan  &d;&ae;t mod lih&d; him selfum  for&d;&ae;m his &ae;f&ae;stnes bi&d; sui&d;e idlu. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d;: Sie &ae;ghwelc mon sui&d;e hr&ae;d &amp; sui&d;e geornful to gehieranne  &amp; sui&d;e l&ae;t to sprecenne. 
 Eft bi &d;am ilcan he gecy&d;de hw&ae;t &d;&ae;re tungan m&ae;gen is  he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hio w&ae;re unstille  yfel &amp; dea&d;berendes atres full. 
 &amp; eft us manode sio So&d;f&ae;stnes &d;urh hie selfe  &d;&ae;t is Crist  he cu&ae;&d;: &ae;lces unnyttes wordes &d;ara &d;e men spreca&d; hie sculon ryht awyrcean on domes d&ae;ge. 
 &D;&ae;t bi&d; &d;onne openlice unnyt word  &d;&ae;tte gescedwise menn ne magon ongietan &d;&ae;t hit belimpe to ryhtwislicre &amp; to nytwyr&d;licre &d;earfe au&d;er o&d;&d;e eft uferran dogore o&d;&d;e &d;onne. 
 Gif we &d;onne sculon ryht agildan unnyttra worda  hwelc wite wene we &d;&ae;t se felaspr&ae;cea scyle habban &d;e simle on oferspr&ae;ce synga&d;? 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e bio&d; to late  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e bio&d; to hrade. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e beo&d; to late  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e beo&d; to hrade. 
 &D;a slawan sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie ne forielden &d;one timan for hiera sl&ae;w&d;e &d;e hie tiola on don m&ae;gen. 
 &D;a hradan &d;onne sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie to unw&ae;rlice ne onetten  &d;yl&ae;s hie forhradien &d;one betestan timan  &amp; hiera mede for&d;&ae;m forleosen. 
 &D;am slawum &d;onne is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;tte oft  &d;onne we nella&d; hw&ae;thwugu nytwyr&d;es don  &d;onne &d;onne we magon  &d;&ae;tte hwilum eft cym&d; sio tid ymb lytel f&ae;c &d;&ae;tte we &d;onne willa&d;  &amp; ne magon. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne we forslawia&d; &d;one gecopestan timan  &d;&ae;tte we &d;onne ne beo&d; on&ae;lde mid &d;&ae;re lustb&ae;rnesse ures modes  &d;onne bistil&d; sio sl&ae;w&d; on us  &amp; ricsa&d; &d;onne ofer us  o&d;&d;&ae;t hio us awyrtwala&d; from &ae;lcre lustb&ae;rnesse godra weorca. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh Salomon &d;one snottran: Sio sl&ae;w&d; giett sl&ae;p on &d;one monnan. 
 Se slawa ongit hw&ae;t him ryht bi&d; to donne  swelce he ealneg wacige  &amp; swa&d;eah he aslawa&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he nawuht ne wyrc&d;  ac sio sl&ae;w&d; him giet on &d;one sl&ae;p  cw&ae;&d; Salomonn  for&d;&ae;m  &d;eah he ryhtlice &d;ence  lytlum &amp; lytlum he forlist &d;&ae;t gode andgiet  &d;onne he forl&ae;tt &d;a geornfulnesse &d;&ae;s go&d;an weorces. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan is eft sui&d;e ryhte gecweden: &d;&ae;t ungeornfulle mod &amp; &d;&ae;t toslopene hyngre&d;  for&d;&ae;m hie n&ae;fre ne beo&d; gereorde mid godum weorcum  ne hie nella&d; hie geh&ae;ftan &amp; gepyndan hiora mod  swelce mon deopne pool gewerige  ac he l&ae;t his mod toflowan on &d;&ae;t ofdele giemelieste &amp; ungesceadwisnesse &ae;fter eallum his willum  &amp; ne geh&ae;ft hit na mid &d;am gesuincium godra weorca  ac hit wir&d; gewundod mid &d;&ae;m hungre &d;&ae;s ny&d;emestan &amp; &d;&ae;s fulestan ge&d;ohtes; 
 &D;onne hit flih&d; &d;&ae;t hit sie gebunden mid ege &amp; mid lare  &d;onne tostret hit on yfelre &amp; on unnytte wilnunga  &amp; h&ae;f&d; &d;&ae;s sui&d;e micelne hunger. 
 Be &d;&ae;m eft wrat Salomon  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &ae;lc idel mon liofa&d; &ae;fter his agnum dome. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan eft sio So&d;f&ae;stnes  &d;&ae;t is Crist  he cw&ae;&d; on his godspelle: &d;onne an uncl&ae;ne gast bi&d; adrifen of &d;&ae;m men  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t hus cl&ae;ne. 
 Ac gif he eft cym&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t hus idel gemett  he hit gefylle&d; mid sui&d;e monigum. 
 Oft se slawa  &d;onne he ag&ae;l&d; &amp; forielt &d;&ae;t weorc &d;e him nied&d;earf w&ae;re to wyrceanne  &d;onne &d;yncea&d; him sumu weorc sui&d;e hefug  sumu sui&d;e unw&ae;rlico  &amp; donne he wen&d; &d;&ae;t he funden h&ae;bbe hw&ae;t he ryhtlice ondr&ae;de  &d;onne wile he gereccean &d;&ae;t he noht unryhtlice hit ne forsl&ae;wde  &d;onne him &d;ync&d; &d;&ae;t he ryhte lade funden h&ae;bbe. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte gecweden &d;urh Salomon &d;one snottran: For ciele nele se slawa erian on wintra  ac he wile biddan on sumera  &amp; him mon nele &d;onne sellan. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t se slawa nylle erian for ciele  &d;&ae;t hwa sie gebunden mid hefignesse &d;&ae;re sl&ae;w&d;e  &d;&ae;t hine ne lyste sum nytwyr&d;e weorc wyrcean. 
 For&d;&ae;m is gecweden &d;&ae;t se slawa for &d;&ae;m ege &d;&ae;s cieles nylle erigean  for&d;&ae;m we oft for &d;&ae;m ege lytles yfeles forl&ae;ta&d; micel god. 
 Hit is sui&d;e wel be &d;&ae;m gecweden &d;&ae;t he eft bedecige on sumera  &amp; him mon &d;onne noht ne selle. 
 Sua bi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e nu on godum weorcum ne sw&ae;t  &amp; sui&d;e ne suince&d;: eft &d;onne sio sunne  &d;&ae;t is Crist  on domes d&ae;ge on m&ae;stum wielme &ae;tiew&d;  &d;onne bi&d; he idel  gif he on &d;&ae;m sumra bidt ingonges in hefonrice. 
 Be &d;&ae;m men w&ae;s eft sui&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh Salomon &d;one snottran  he cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e him ealneg wind ondr&ae;t  he s&ae;w&d; to seldon; 
 &amp; se &d;e him &ae;lc wolcn ondr&ae;dt  ne rip&d; se n&ae;fre. 
 Hw&ae;t getacna&d; &d;onne se wind buton &d;a costunga &d;&ae;s awirgdan g&ae;stes  &amp; hw&ae;t &d;&ae;t wolc &d;e bi&d; astyred from &d;&ae;m winde buton &d;a wi&d;erweardnesse unryhtwisra monna? 
 Se wind drife&d; &d;&ae;t wolcn. 
 Sua de&d; se uncl&ae;na g&ae;st mid his winde; 
 He onstyre&d; unryhtwise men. 
 We cw&ae;don &ae;r &d;&ae;t se sceolde lytel sawan  se de him &d;one wind ondrede; 
 &amp; eft lytel ripan  se &d;e him &d;a wolc ondrede. 
 Hw&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;tte sua hwelc sua him ondr&ae;t o&d;&d;e deofles costunga o&d;&d;e yfelra monna ehtnesse  &amp; for&d;y forl&ae;t &d;&ae;t he hw&ae;thwugu godes ne do  &d;onne nau&d;er ne he her &d;a corn godra weorca ne s&ae;w&d;  ne he eft n&ae;nne sceaf ne rip&d; &d;&ae;s ecean edleanes. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;m &d;e beo&d; to hrade  &d;onne hie forhradiga&d; &d;one timan godes weorces  &d;&ae;t hie forp&ae;ra&d; &d;&ae;m edleane  &amp; oft befealla&d; on micel yfel  &d;onne hie nabba&d; &d;a gesceadwisnesse &d;&ae;t hie cunnen &d;&ae;s &d;inges timan aredian  ne fur&d;um ne giema&d; hw&ae;t hie don  o&d;&d;e hwonne hie hw&ae;t don  ac hwilum hit gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t hie hit eft ongieta&d;  &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e hit gedon bi&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &ae;r sua don ne sceoldon. 
 To swelcum monnum Salomon w&ae;s sprecende  &d;a he his cnieht l&ae;rde  he cw&ae;&d;: Sunu min  ne doo &d;u nan wuht butan ge&d;eahte  &d;onne ne hriw&d; hit &d;e  &d;onne hit gedon bi&d;; 
 Ac l&ae;t simle gan &d;in eagean beforan &d;inum fotum. 
 &D;onne st&ae;ppa&d; &d;a eagan beforan &d;&ae;m fotum  &d;onne &d;&ae;t ryhte &amp; &d;&ae;t gesceadwislice ge&d;eaht g&ae;&d; beforan weorcum. 
 Ac se &d;e agimeleasa&d; &d;&ae;t he &d;ence  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e he do  se st&ae;p&d; for&d; mid &d;am fotum  &amp; winca&d; mid &d;&ae;m eagum. 
 He g&ae;&d; on &d;one weg  ac he nat on hw&ae;t he g&ae;&d;  ac he wir&d; sui&d;e ra&d;e on fielle. 
 Sua wir&d; se &d;e beforan &d;&ae;m st&ae;pum his weorca ne loca&d; mid &d;&ae;m eagum gesceadwisra ge&d;eahtes. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a mon&d;w&ae;ran  on o&d;re &d;a gramb&ae;ran. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a monn&d;w&ae;ran  on o&d;re &d;a gramb&ae;ran. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft gebyre&d; &d;&ae;m mon&d;w&ae;ran  &d;onne he wier&d; riece ofer o&d;re menn  &d;&ae;t he for his monn&d;w&ae;rnesse aslawa&d;  &amp; wier&d; to unbeald  for&d;&ae;m sio bieldo &amp; sio monn&d;w&ae;rnes bio&d; swi&d;e anlice. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft  &d;onne mon l&ae;t toslupan &d;one ege &amp; &d;a lare sui&d;ur &d;onne hit &d;earf sie for wacmodnesse  &d;onne wier&d; gehnescad &d;onone sio &d;reaung &d;&ae;s anwaldes. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a weamodan &amp; &d;a gramb&ae;ran  for&d;&ae;m  &d;onne hie underfo&d; &d;one folgo&d;  &d;onne tyht hie &amp; greme&d; &d;&ae;t ierre &d;&ae;t hie wealwia&d; on &d;a wedenheortnesse  &amp; &d;urh &d;&ae;t wier&d; toslieten sio stilnes hiera hieremonna modes  &amp; bi&d; gedrefed sio smyltnes hiera lifes. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne &d;&ae;t ierre &ae;f&d; anwald &d;&ae;s monnes  &d;onne gehries&d; he on sume scylde  sua &d;&ae;t he self nat hu&ae;t he on &d;&ae;t irre de&d;. 
 &D;a irran nyton hw&ae;t hie on him selfum habba&d;  &amp; eac &d;&ae;tte wierse is  &d;&ae;tte hie ful oft wena&d; &d;&ae;tte hiera hierre sie ryhtwislic anda &amp; manung sumre ryhtwisnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t hiera un&d;eawas sien sum god cr&ae;ft  &d;onne gadria&d; hie hie &amp; iecea&d; butan &ae;lcum ege. 
 Oft eac &d;a mon&d;w&ae;ran weor&d;a&d; sua besolcne &amp; sua wlace &amp; sua slawe for hira monn&d;w&ae;rnesse &d;&ae;t hie ne anhaga&d; nane wuht nyttwyr&d;es don. 
 Oft eac &d;a gramb&ae;ra leoga&d; him selfum  &d;onne hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie ryhtne andan h&ae;bben. 
 Oft eac sio godnes &d;&ae;re monn&d;w&ae;rnesse bi&d; diegellice gemenged wi&d; sleacnesse. 
 Oft eac &d;a gramb&ae;ran wena&d; &d;&ae;t hiera un&d;eaw sie sumes ryhtwislices andan wielm. 
 Ac we sculon manian &d;a man&d;w&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hie h&ae;bben &d;a monn&d;w&ae;rnesse  &amp; fleon &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r sui&d;e neah liege&d; &d;&ae;re monn&d;w&ae;rnesse  &d;&ae;t is sleacnes. 
 &D;a gramb&ae;ran we sculon monian &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hw&ae;t hie on him selfum habba&d;. 
 &D;a monn&d;w&ae;ran we sculon monian &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hw&ae;t hi nabba&d;. 
 Ne forl&ae;ten &d;a ierran &d;one andan  ac ge&d;encen &d;&ae;t he sie gesceadwislic &amp; gemetlic. 
 Leornia&d; hine &d;a man&d;w&ae;ran &amp; lufiga&d;  o&d;&d;&ae;t hie hiene h&ae;bben. 
 Lytligen &d;a gramb&ae;ran hiera gedrefednesse. 
 &D;a mon&d;w&ae;ran sint to monianne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice tiligen &d;&ae;t hie h&ae;bben ryhtwislicne andan. 
 &D;a gramb&ae;ran sint to monianne  &d;e wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie ryhtwislicne andan h&ae;bben  &d;&ae;t hie &d;one gemengen wi&d; monn&d;w&ae;rnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m us &ae;tiede se Halga G&ae;s&d; &ae;g&d;er ge on culfran onlicnesse ge on fyres  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;lcne &d;ara &d;e he gefyl&d;  he hiene on&ae;l&d; &ae;g&d;er ge mid &d;&ae;re culfran bilewitnesse &amp; mann&d;w&ae;rnesse ge mid &d;&ae;s fyres re&d;nesse. 
 Ne bi&d; se no gefylled &d;&ae;s Halgan G&ae;s&d;&ae;s se &d;e on &d;&ae;re smyltnesse his mon&d;w&ae;rnesse forl&ae;t &d;one wielm ryhtwislices andan  o&d;&d;e eft on &d;&ae;m wielme &d;&ae;s andan forl&ae;t &d;one cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;re monn&d;w&ae;rnesse. 
 Ic wene &d;&ae;t we m&ae;gen &d;is openlicor gecy&d;an gif we sanctus Paulus lare sume ongemong secga&d;  for&d;&ae;m he h&ae;fde twegen gingran sui&d;e gelices willan &amp; on eallum &d;ingum sui&d;e onlice  &amp; he hie &d;eah l&ae;rde sui&d;e ungelice. 
 O&d;er hira w&ae;s haten Timotheus  o&d;er Titus. 
 He cu&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m Timotheo: L&ae;re hie  &amp; healsa  &amp; t&ae;l hira un&d;eawas  &amp; &d;eah ge&d;yldelice. 
 To &d;&ae;m Tite he cu&ae;&d;: L&ae;r &d;&ae;t folc  &amp; &d;reata  &amp; t&ae;l  &amp; hat  &d;&ae;t hie wieten &d;&ae;t ge sume anwald habba&d; ofer hie. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;nde sanctus Paulus  &d;a he his lare sua cr&ae;ftelice toscead  &amp; &d;one o&d;erne l&ae;rde &d;&ae;t he him anwald ontuge  o&d;erne he l&ae;rde ge&d;yld  buton &d;&ae;t he ongeat Titum hwene mon&d;w&ae;rran &amp; ge&d;yldigran &d;onne he sceolde  &amp; Timotheus he ongeat hatheortran &d;onne he sceolde? 
 Titum he wolde on&ae;lan mid ryhtwislicum andan  Timotheum he wolde gemetgian. 
 O&d;rum he wolde geiecean &d;&ae;t him wana w&ae;s  o&d;rum he wolde oftion &d;&ae;s &d;e he to fela &ae;fde. 
 O&d;erne he draf sui&d;e geornfullice mid sticele  o&d;rum he wi&d;teah mid bridle. 
 Wietodlice se m&ae;ra landbegenga  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s sanctus Paulus  he underfeng &d;a halgan gesomnunga to plantianne &amp; to ymbhweorfanne  sua se ceorl de&d; his ortgeard. 
 Sumu treowu he watrode  to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie &d;y sui&d;ur sceolden weaxan. 
 Sume he cearf &d;onne him &d;uhte &d;&ae;t hie to sui&d;e weoxsen  &d;yl&ae;s hie to &d;&ae;m forweoxen &d;&ae;t hie forseareden  &amp; &d;y unw&ae;s&d;mb&ae;rran w&ae;ren. 
 Sumu twigu he lehte mid w&ae;tere  &d;onne hie to hwon weoxson  &d;&ae;t hie &d;y sui&d;ur weaxan sceolden. 
 Ac &d;a irsunga sindun sui&d;e ungelica: o&d;er bi&d; suelce hit sie irres anlicnes  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t mon wielle &ae;t o&d;rum his yfel a&d;reatigan  &amp; hine on ryhtum gebringan  o&d;er bi&d; &d;&ae;t ierre &d;&ae;t mon sie gedrefed on his mode butan &ae;lcre ryhtwisnesse; 
 O&d;er &d;ara irsunga bi&d; to ungemetlice &amp; to ungedafenlice atyht on &d;&ae;t &d;e hio mid ryhte irsian sceall  o&d;er on &d;&ae;t &d;e hio ne sceal bi&d; ealneg to sui&d;e onb&ae;rned. 
 Eac is to wietanne &d;&ae;tte hw&ae;thwugu bi&d; betweoh &d;&ae;m irsiendan &amp; &d;&ae;m unge&d;yldgan  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t &d;a unge&d;yldgan ne magon aberan nanwuht &d;&ae;s la&d;es &d;e him mon on leg&d; o&d;&d;e mid wordum o&d;&d;e mid d&ae;dum  &d;a iersigendan &d;onne him to getio&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;tte hie ea&d;e butan bion meahton: &d;eah hie nan mann mid la&d;e ne grete  hie wiella&d; griellan o&d;re menn to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie niede sculon  &amp; secea&d; &d;a &d;e hie fleo&d;  &amp; styriga&d; geflitu &amp; geciid  &amp; f&ae;gnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie moten suincan on unge&d;w&ae;rnesse. 
 &D;a suelcan we magon ealra betest geryhtan mid &d;y &d;&ae;t we hie forbugen  &d;onne &d;onne hie beo&d; anstyred mid hiera ierre  for&d;&ae;m  &d;onne hie sua gedrefede bio&d;  hie nyton hw&ae;t hie &d;onne gehiera&d;  &d;eah him mon stiere  ac eft  &d;onne hie hie selfe ongieta&d;  hie onfoo&d; &d;&ae;re lare sua micle lus&d;licor sua him mon &ae;r ge&d;yldelicor forb&ae;r hiera irre  &amp; sua micle ma scamia&d; hiera un&d;eawes sua hiene mon &ae;r ge&d;yldelicor forb&ae;r. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mod  &d;a hwile &d;e hit bi&d; oferdruncen &d;&ae;s ierres  eal &d;&ae;t him mon ryhtes s&ae;g&d;  hit &d;ync&d; him woh. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t wif &d;e Abigall hatte sui&d;e herigendlice forsuigode &d;&ae;t dysig hiere fordruncnan hlafordes  se w&ae;s haten Nabal  &amp; eft  &d;a him &d;&ae;t li&d; gescired w&ae;s  full herigendlice hio hit him gecy&d;de  &amp; he for&d;&ae;m sua micle bet his agen dysig oncnew sua he undruncenra w&ae;s. 
 Sua eac  &d;onne &d;&ae;t gelimp&d; &d;&ae;t &d;a iersigendan menn o&d;rum monnum oferfylgea&d; to &d;on sui&d;e &d;&ae;t hit mon forberan ne m&ae;g  ne sceal mon no mid openlice edwite him wi&d;slean  ac bi sumum d&ae;le arwier&d;elice wandigende sui&d;e w&ae;rlice stieran. 
 &D;&ae;t we magon openlicor gecy&d;an  gif we &ae;fneres d&ae;da sume herongemong secga&d;  hu Assael hine unw&ae;rlice mid anwealde &d;reatode  &amp; him oferfylgde. 
 Hit is awriten &d;&ae;t &AE;fnere cw&ae;de to Assaele: Gecier la  &amp; gesuic  ne folga me &d;&ae;t ic &d;e ne dyrre ofstingan. 
 He forhogde &d;&ae;t he hit gehierde  &amp; nolde hine forl&ae;tan. 
 &D;a &d;ydde &ae;fner hine mid hindewerde sceafte on &d;&ae;t sm&ae;l&d;earme &d;&ae;t he w&ae;s dead. 
 Hw&ae;s onlicnesse h&ae;fde Assael &d;a buton &d;ara &d;e hiera hatheortnes hie sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice on f&ae;rspild gel&ae;d? 
 &D;a &d;onne hie ber&ae;sa&d; on suelce weamodnesse hie sindon sua micle w&ae;rlicor to ferbuganne sua mon ongiet &d;&ae;t hie on maran ungewitte beo&d;. 
 &D;&ae;s &ae;fneres noma &d;e &d;one o&d;erne fleah is on ure ge&d;iode f&ae;der leohtf&ae;t. 
 &D;&ae;t getacna&d; &d;&ae;tte &d;ara lareowa tungan &d;e &d;&ae;t uplice leoht bodia&d;  &d;onne hie ongieta&d; hwelcne monnan gesuencedne mid irre &amp; mid hatheortnesse onb&ae;rnedne  &amp; &d;onne forwandiga&d; &d;&ae;t hie mid &d;&ae;m kycglum hiera worda ongean hiera ierre worpigen  sua sua &ae;fner wandade &d;&ae;t he nolde &d;ane slean &d;e hine draf. 
 Sua  &d;onne &d;onne &d;a hatheortan hie mid nane fore&d;once nylla&d; gestillan  ac sua wedende folgia&d; hwam sua sua Assael dyde &ae;fnere  &amp; n&ae;fre nylla&d; gesuican  &d;onne is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;tte se  se &d;a hatheortnesse ofercuman wielle  &d;&ae;tte he hiene ongean ne hathierte  w&ae;rlice hine pynge mid sumum wordum  &d;&ae;t he on &d;&ae;m ongietan m&ae;ge be sumum d&ae;le his un&d;eaw. 
 For&d;&ae;m &ae;fner  &d;a &d;a he ongean &d;one cirde &d;e hine draf  ne ofstong he hiene no mid &d;y speres orde  ac mid hindewerdum &d;am sceafte. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne suelc mon mid forewearde orde stinge  &d;&ae;t mon openlice &amp; unforwandodlice on o&d;erne r&ae;se mid t&ae;linge &amp; mid &d;rafunga. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon mid hindewearde sceafte &d;one &d;ydde &d;e him oferfylge  &d;&ae;t mon &d;one weamodan li&d;elice mid sumum &d;ingum gehrine  suelce he hine wandigende ofersui&d;e. 
 Sua sua Assael sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice gefeol  sua &d;&ae;t ahrerede mod  &d;onne hit ongiet &d;&ae;t him mon birg&d; mid &d;&ae;re gesceadlican andsuare  hit bi&d; get&ae;sed on &d;&ae;t inge&d;onc  &amp; mid &d;&ae;re li&d;elican manunga to &d;am aredod &d;&ae;t hit sceal sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice afeallan of &d;&ae;re weamodnesse &d;e hit &ae;r on ah&ae;fen w&ae;s. 
 Se &d;e &d;onne sua forbyg&d; &d;one wielm &amp; &d;one onr&ae;s his hatheortnesse  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hine mon slea mid li&d;elicre andsuare  &d;onne bi&d; his un&d;eaw ofsl&ae;gen butan &ae;lcre nied&d;rafunga  sua sua Assael w&ae;s dead butan orde. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a ea&d;modan  on o&d;re wisan &d;a upah&ae;fenan on hira mode. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a ea&d;modan  on o&d;re &d;a upah&ae;fenan. 
 &D;&ae;m ea&d;modum is to cy&d;anne hu micel sio heanes is &amp; hu so&d;lic &d;e hie to hopia&d;  &amp; eac habba&d;. 
 &D;&ae;m upah&ae;fenum is to cy&d;anne hwelc nawuht &d;es woruldgielp is &d;e hie clyppa&d; &amp; lufia&d;  &amp; his nawuht habba&d;  &d;eah hie wenen &d;&ae;t hie hiene h&ae;bben. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan hu ece &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hie wilnia&d;  &amp; hu gewitende &amp; hu unagen &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hie onscunia&d;. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a upah&ae;fenan hu gewitende &d;a &d;ing sint &d;e hie gietsia&d;  &amp; hu eciu &d;a sint &d;e hie forhycga&d;  &amp; forleosan willa&d;. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse stemne  &d;&ae;t is Crist ure lareow  he cu&ae;&d;: &ae;lc &d;ara &d;e bi&d; geea&d;med  he bi&d; upah&ae;fen. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a upah&ae;fenan on hiera mode hw&ae;t he eft cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d;: &ae;lc &d;ara &d;e hine selfne upahefe&d;  he wier&d; gehined. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan hw&ae;t Salomon cu&ae;&d;: Sio ea&d;modnes iern&d; beforan &d;&ae;m gielpe  &amp; heo cym&d; &ae;r &ae;r &d;a wyr&d;myn&d;u. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a upah&ae;fenan on hira mode hu he eft cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d;: &ae;r &d;&ae;s monnes hryre bi&d; &d;&ae;t mod upah&ae;fen. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan hw&ae;t God cu&ae;&d; &d;urh Essaim &d;one witgan  he cu&ae;&d;: To hw&ae;m locige ic buton to &d;&ae;m ea&d;modum &amp; to &d;&ae;m stillum &amp; to &d;&ae;m &d;e him ondr&ae;da&d; min word? 
 Gehieren &d;a upah&ae;fenan hw&ae;t Salomon cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t ofermodga&d; &d;ios eor&d;e &amp; &d;is dus&d;? 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan hw&ae;t on psalmum gecueden is  &d;&ae;tte Dryhten locige to &d;&ae;m ea&d;modan. 
 Gehieren &d;a upah&ae;fenan: Dryhten ongiet sui&d;e feorran &d;a heahmodnesse. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan hw&ae;t Crist cu&ae;&d;: Ne com ic to &d;on on eor&d;an &d;&ae;t me mon &d;enode  ac to &d;on &d;&ae;t ic wolde &d;egnian. 
 Gehieren &d;a upah&ae;fenan hw&ae;t Salomon cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &ae;lces yfles fruma w&ae;re ofermetta. 
 Gehieren &d;a ea&d;modan &d;&ae;tte Cris&d; ure Aliesend hiene selfne geea&d;medde emne o&d; &d;one dea&d;. 
 Gehieren &d;a upah&ae;fenan hw&ae;t awriten is be hira heafde &amp; be hiera lareowe  &d;&ae;t is dioful: hit is awriten &d;&ae;t he sie kyning ofer eal &d;a oferhydigan bearn  for&d;&ae;m his ofermedu is fruma ures forlores  &amp; se or&d;onc &d;e we mid aliesde siendon is Godes ea&d;modnes. 
 Se ure fiond &d;onne he w&ae;s gesceapen ongemang eallum o&d;rum gesceaftum  ac he wilnode &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re ongieten upah&ae;fen ofer ealle o&d;re gesceafte. 
 Ac se ure Aliesend  &d;e mara is &amp; m&ae;rra eallum gesceaftum  he hine gemedomode to bionne betwuix &d;&ae;m l&ae;s&d;um &amp; &d;&ae;m gingestum monnum. 
 &D;&ae;m ea&d;modum is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne hie hie selfe sui&d;us&d; ea&d;meda&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie &d;onne astiga&d; to Godes anlicnesse. 
 Secga&d; eac &d;&ae;m upah&ae;fenum &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne hie hie selfe upahebba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne afealla&d; on &d;a biesene &d;&ae;s aworpnan engles. 
 Ac hw&ae;t is &d;onne forcu&d;re &d;onne sio upah&ae;fenes? 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne heo bi&d; atyht ofer hire andefnu  &d;onne bi&d; heo afeorrod sui&d;e feor from &d;&ae;re so&d;an heanesse. 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g &d;onne hierre bion &d;onne sio so&d;e ea&d;modnes? 
 Sio  &d;onne hio nie&d;emes&d; gebyge&d;  &d;onne bi&d; hio gelicos&d; hiere Dryhtne  se wuna&d; ofer eallum &d;&ae;m hiehstum gesceaftum. 
 &D;onne is &d;eah betwux &d;issum twam sum &d;ing &d;e mon w&ae;rlice sceal ge&d;encean  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t sume menn onderfo&d; ea&d;modnesse hiw  sume ofermodnesse  sua sua hie nyton. 
 Sume  &d;a &d;a wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie ea&d;mode sien  hie do&d; for ege &d;one weor&d;scipe mannum &d;e hie Gode don scoldon. 
 Oft eac &d;a upah&ae;fenan  &d;eah hie hwilum unforwandodlice sprecen  &d;onne hie hwelces un&d;eawes stiran sculon  &d;onne gesugia&d; hie for ege  &amp; tiohchia&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t scyle bion for ea&d;mettum  &amp; &d;onne hie spreca&d;  &d;onne wena&d; hie &d;&ae;t hie sprecen for unforwandodlicre &amp; orsorglicre ryhtwisnesse. 
 Ac hit bi&d; oftor for &d;&ae;re unge&d;ylde hiera upah&ae;fenesse. 
 &D;a ea&d;modan &d;onne bio&d; oft ge&d;rycte mid &d;&ae;re synne &d;&ae;s eges  &d;onne hie ne durron un&d;eawas t&ae;lan  &amp; licetta&d; &d;eah &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t don &d;urh ea&d;modnesse. 
 Ac &d;a upah&ae;fenan  &d;onne hie licetta&d; &d;&ae;t him ne sie nawuhtes cearu ofer &d;a ryhtwisnesse  weor&d;a&d; &d;onne unmidlode sua &amp; a&d;undene geniedde mid hiera upah&ae;fenesse &d;&ae;t hie &d;a t&ae;la&d; &amp; &d;reatiga&d; &d;e hie &d;reatian ne sceoldon  o&d;&d;e &d;a &d;e hie &d;reatigan sceoldon sui&d;ur &d;reatia&d; &d;onne hie sceolden. 
 For&d;&ae;m sint to manianne &d;a upah&ae;fenan &d;&ae;t hie ne sien bealdran &amp; orsorgran &d;onne hie scylen  ond &d;a ea&d;modan sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie ne sien sui&d;ur under&d;iedde &d;onne hie mid ryhte scylen  &d;yl&ae;s &d;a modgan &d;a forespr&ae;ce &d;&ae;re ryhtwisnesse gehwierfen to ofermodnesse  o&d;&d;e eft &d;a ea&d;modan &d;onne hie ma wilnia&d; o&d;rum monnum under&d;iedde beon &d;onne hie &d;yrfen  weor&d;en geniedde hiera un&d;eawas to herianne &amp; to weor&d;ianne. 
 Eac is to ge&d;encanne &d;&ae;tte mon m&ae;g oft &d;y bet &d;a ofermodan &d;reatian  gif hie mon ongemang &d;&ae;re &d;reatunga fet mid sumere heringe. 
 Him mon sceal cy&d;an &d;ara goda sum &d;e hie on him habba&d; o&d;&d;e &d;ara sum &d;e hie habban meahton  gif hie n&ae;fden. 
 Sua we magon betes&d; of aceorfan &d;&ae;t us on him mislica&d;  &d;&ae;t we &ae;res&d; gedon &d;&ae;t hie gehieren &ae;t us hw&ae;thwugu &d;&ae;s &d;e him licige  &amp; mid &d;y hiera mod getion to us  &d;&ae;t hit sie &d;e lus&d;b&ae;rre to gehieranne sua hw&ae;t sua we him au&d;er o&d;&d;e lean o&d;&d;e l&ae;ran wiellen. 
 For&d;&ae;m hie beo&d; to myndgianne &d;ara goda &d;e hie &ae;r dydon  &d;&ae;t hie sien &d;e lus&d;b&ae;rran to gehieranne &d;&ae;t him mon &d;onne beodan wielle. 
 Swa swa wildu hors  &d;onne we hie &ae;res&d; gefangnu habba&d;  we hie &d;accia&d; &amp; straciad mid bradre han&d;a &amp; lemia&d;  to &d;on &d;&ae;t we eft on fierste hie moten mid gierdum fullice gel&ae;ran &amp; &d;a temian. 
 Sua eac se l&ae;ce  &d;onne he bietre wyrta de&d; to hwelcum drence  he hie gesuet mid hunige  &d;yl&ae;s he &d;a bieternesse &d;&ae;re wyrte &d;e hine geh&ae;lan sceal &ae;t fruman gefrede  ac &d;onne se sw&ae;c &d;&ae;re bieternesse bi&d; bediegled mid &d;&ae;re swetnesse  &d;onne bi&d; se dea&d;b&ae;ra w&ae;ta on &d;&ae;m menn ofsl&ae;gen mid &d;&ae;m biteran drence. 
 Sua mon sceal on &d;&ae;m upah&ae;fenum monnum &d;one fruman &amp; &d;one ingong &d;&ae;re &d;reatunga &amp; &d;&ae;re t&ae;linge gemetgian  &amp; wi&d; heringe gemengan  &d;&ae;tte hie for &d;&ae;re licunga &d;&ae;re heringe &amp; &d;&ae;re olicunga &d;e hie lufigea&d; eac ga&d;afigen &d;a t&ae;linge &amp; &d;a &d;reaunga &d;e hie onscunia&d;. 
 Oft we magon eac &d;a upah&ae;fenan &d;y bet gel&ae;ran to urum willan  gif we him cy&d;a&d; hu micle &d;earfe we hiera habba&d;  suelce we maran &d;earfe h&ae;bban &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;eon &d;onne hie selfe  &amp; we hie &d;onne bidda&d; &d;&ae;t hie for urum &d;ingum hira un&d;eawa gesuicen; 
 &D;y ie&d;elicor bi&d; sio upah&ae;fenes to gode gehwierfed  gif hie ongieta&d; &d;&ae;t hiera eac o&d;re men &d;urfon. 
 Be &d;&ae;m se ilca Moyses &d;e God self l&ae;rde  &amp; hine l&ae;dde &d;urh &d;&ae;t westen mid &d;y fyrenan sweore on nieht  &amp; on d&ae;g mid &d;y sweore &d;&ae;s wolcnes  he wolde Obab his sweor ob &d;&ae;s h&ae;&d;endomes si&d;um al&ae;dan  &amp; hie wol&d;e under&d;iodan &ae;lmihtigum Gode. 
 He cu&ae;&d;: We willa&d; nu faran to &d;&ae;re stowe &d;e God us gehaten h&ae;f&d;  ac far mid us  &d;&ae;t we &d;e m&ae;gen wel don  for&d;&ae;m&d;e God h&ae;f&d; sui&d;e wel gehaten Israhela folce. 
 &D;a andsuarode he him  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Ic nelle mid &d;e faran  ac ic wille faran to minre cy&d;&d;e  &amp; to &d;&ae;m londe &d;e ic on geboren w&ae;s. 
 &D;a andswarade him Moyses: La  ne forl&ae;t us  ac beo ure la&d;eow  &d;u cans eal &d;is westen  &amp; was&d; hw&ae;r we wician magon. 
 Ne spr&ae;c he hit no for&d;y&d;e his mod auht genierwed w&ae;re mid &d;&ae;re uncy&d;&d;e &d;&ae;s si&d;f&ae;tes  for&d;&ae;m hit w&ae;s geweor&d;ad mid &d;&ae;m andgiete godcundes wisdomes  &amp; w&ae;s him self witga  for&d;am hine God hiewcu&d;licor on eallum &d;ingum &amp; &d;eawum innan l&ae;rde &d;onne o&d;re menn mid his gelomlicre tospr&ae;ce  &amp; utane he hine ne l&ae;rde mid &d;&ae;m sweore &d;&ae;s wolcnes. 
 La ah &d;eahhw&ae;&d;re se fore&d;ancula wer  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he spr&ae;c to &d;&ae;m upah&ae;fenan  he b&ae;d his fultumes  swelce him nied&d;erf w&ae;re; 
 &amp; b&ae;d &d;eah for &d;&ae;s o&d;res &d;earfe  for&d;&ae;m he tiohchode him ma to fultemanne; 
 He sohte hine him to lat&d;eowe on &d;&ae;m wege  for&d;&ae;m he teohchode hine to l&ae;danne on lifes weg. 
 Ac he dyde sua sua ofermod gefera de&d;: he sceolde beon &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce sua micle gef&ae;genra sua him mare &d;earf w&ae;s  &amp; &d;&ae;s &d;e gef&ae;genra &d;e he him sua ea&d;modlice &amp; sua arlice to spr&ae;c  he sceolde bion him micle &d;y ea&d;modra &amp; his larum &d;e sui&d;ur under&d;ied. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a anwillan  on o&d;re &d;a ungest&ae;&d;&d;egan &amp; unf&ae;s&d;r&ae;da. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a anfealdan str&ae;can  on o&d;re &d;a unbealdan. 
 &D;&ae;m anfealdan str&ae;cum is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;t hie bet ne truwien him selfum &d;onne hie &d;yrfen  &d;onne hi for&d;y nylla&d; ge&d;afan beon o&d;erra monna ge&d;eahtes. 
 &D;&ae;m unbealdum is to cy&d;anne hu giemelease hie bio&d; &d;onne hie hie selfe to sui&d;e forsio&d;  for&d;&ae;m hie mon &ae;t &ae;lcum cierre m&ae;g for hira leohtmodnesse of hiera agnum ge&d;eahte awendan. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m anstr&ae;cum is to cy&d;anne  &d;&ae;r hie ne wenden &d;&ae;t hie selfe beteran &amp; wisran w&ae;ren &d;onne o&d;re menn  &d;&ae;t hie ne l&ae;ten hiera ge&d;eaht &amp; hiera wenan sua feor beforan ealra o&d;erra monna wenan. 
 Ac &d;&ae;m unbealdum is to ky&d;anne  gif hie be &ae;negum d&ae;le wolden ge&d;encean hw&ae;t hie selfe w&ae;ren  &d;onne ne leten hie no hie eallinga on &ae;lce healfe gebigean  ne fur&d;um no awecggan  &d;eah &d;e hie mon manigfealdlice &amp; mislice styrede  sua sua wac hreod &amp; idel  &d;e &ae;lc hwi&d;a windes m&ae;g awecggan. 
 Ac to &d;&ae;m anstr&ae;cum is gecueden &d;urh sanctus Paulus: Ne sculon ge no &d;yncan eow selfum to wise. 
 Ond eft he cu&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m unbealdum: Ne l&ae;te ge eow &ae;lcre lare wind awecggan. 
 To &d;&ae;m anstr&ae;cum is gecueden &d;urh Salomon: Hie eta&d; &d;one w&ae;s&d;m hiera &ae;gnes weges. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;onne hie beo&d; gefyllede mid hiera &ae;gnum ge&d;eahte. 
 Eft cu&ae;&d; Salomon be &d;&ae;m unbealdum: Dysigra monna mod bi&d; sui&d;e unemn &amp; sui&d;e ungelic  ond &d;&ae;s wisan monnes mod bi&d; sui&d;e emn  &amp; simle him selfum gelic. 
 He bi&d; simle ryhtes ge&d;eahtes ge&d;afa  for&d;&ae;m he bi&d; sui&d;e arod &amp; sui&d;e gere&d;re on ryhtum weorcum. 
 Ac &d;ara monna mod bi&d; sui&d;e unemn  for&d;&ae;m hit gede&d; hit self him selfum sui&d;e ungelic for &d;&ae;re gelomlican wendinge  for&d;&ae;m hit n&ae;fre eft ne bi&d; &d;&ae;t hit &ae;r w&ae;s. 
 Eac is to wietanne &d;&ae;tte sume un&d;eawas cuma&d; of o&d;rum un&d;eawum sua ilce sua hie comon &ae;r of o&d;rum. 
 For&d;y us is to wietanne &d;&ae;t we magon hie sua i&d;es&d; mid &d;reaunga gebetan  gif we &d;one biteran wille &ae;t &d;&ae;m &ae;sprynge forwyrcea&d; &amp; adryga&d;  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;re anwilnesse &ae;wilm is ofermetta  &amp; of &d;&ae;re leohtmodnesse cym&d; sio twiefealdnes &amp; sio unbieldo. 
 &D;a anstr&ae;can &d;onne sint to monianne &d;&ae;t hie ongieten &d;a upah&ae;fenesse hiora modes  &amp; geornlice tiligen &d;&ae;t hie hie selfe oferwinnen  &d;yl&ae;s &d;onne hie oferhygga&d; &d;&ae;t hie sien oferreahte utane mid o&d;erra manna ryhtum spellum &amp; larum  hie &d;onne sien innan geh&ae;fte mid ofermetum. 
 Eac hie sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte Crist  &d;e simle anes willan w&ae;s &amp; God f&ae;der  us salde bisne urne willan to brecanne  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ne sece ic no minne willan  ac mines f&ae;der  &d;e me hider sende. 
 &amp; eac he gehett &d;&ae;t he sua don wolde  &d;onne he eft come on &d;&ae;m ytemestan d&ae;ge  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wolde &d;&ae;t we nu &d;e bett underfengen &d;one cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;re lare. 
 &D;&ae;t he cy&d;de  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Ne m&ae;g ic nane wuht don mines agnes &d;onces  ac sua ic deme sua ic minne F&ae;der gehiere. 
 Ac hwy sceal &ae;nigum menn &d;onne &d;yncean to orgellic &d;&ae;t he onbuge to o&d;res monnes willan  &d;onne Godes agen sunu  &d;onne he cym&d; mid his m&ae;gen&d;rymme to demanne  &amp; his wuldor to &ae;tiewanne  he cy&d;de &d;&ae;t he no &d;onne of him selfum ne demde  ac of &d;&ae;m &d;e hine sent? 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a unbealdan &amp; &d;a unf&ae;s&d;r&ae;dan &d;&ae;t hie hera mod mid stillnesse &amp; gest&ae;&d;&d;ignesse gestrongien. 
 Sona asearia&d; &d;a twigu &d;&ae;re hwurfulnesse  gif &ae;res&d; se wyrtruma bi&d; forcorfen &ae;t &d;&ae;re heortan  &d;&ae;t is sio leohtmodnes. 
 &D;y mon sceal f&ae;s&d;ne weal wyrcean  &d;y mon &ae;r gehawige &d;&ae;t se grund f&ae;s&d; sie  &d;&ae;r mon &d;one grundweall onlecgge. 
 &D;y sceal eac bion ofersui&d;ed sio unf&ae;s&d;r&ae;dnes &amp; sio unbieldo &d;ara ge&d;ohta  &d;y mon hine bewarige wi&d; &d;a leohtmodnesse. 
 &D;&ae;re leohtmodnesse &amp; &d;&ae;re leasmodnesse sanctus Paulus hine ladode  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Wene ge nu &d;&ae;t ic &ae;nigre leohtmodnesse bruce  o&d;&d;e &d;&ae;tte ic &d;ence &ae;fter woruldluste  o&d;&d;e wene ge &d;&ae;t &ae;g&d;er sie mid me ge gise ge nese? 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de &d;&ae;t hine ne meahte nan scur &d;&ae;re hwurfulnesse astyrigean  for&d;&ae;m he &d;&ae;re leohtmodnesse un&d;eawes nanwuht n&ae;fde. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e hie selfe forgiefa&d; gifernesse  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e do&d; forh&ae;fdnesse. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manigenne &d;a gifran  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e forh&ae;fdnesse do&d;  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;m ofergifrum wile fylgean ofersprecolnes &amp; leohtlicu weorc &amp; leaslicu &amp; wr&ae;nnes  &amp; &d;&ae;m swi&d;e f&ae;stendan oft folga&d; unge&d;yld  &amp; hwilum eac ofermetta. 
 Gif &d;am gifran ungemetlicu spr&ae;c ne eglde  &d;onne ne burne se weliga &d;e sui&d;ur on &d;&ae;re tungan &d;e on o&d;rum limum  se &d;e on &d;&ae;m godspelle ges&ae;d is &d;&ae;tte &ae;lce d&ae;ge symblede  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s se se &d;e cw&ae;&d;: F&ae;der Habraham  miltsa me  &amp; onsend Ladzarus  &d;&ae;tte he gew&ae;te his ytemestan finger on w&ae;ttre  &amp; mid &d;&ae;m gecele mine tungan  for&d;&ae;m ic eom cwielmed on &d;ys liege. 
 Mid &d;y worde w&ae;s getacnod &d;&ae;tte &d;a &d;e &ae;lce d&ae;g symblia&d;  on &d;&ae;re tungann sui&d;ur syngia&d; &d;onne on o&d;rum limum  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he w&ae;s eall biernende  &amp; &d;eah &d;a tunga sui&d;ust m&ae;nde  &amp; him &d;&ae;re kelnesse b&ae;d. 
 Ond eft &d;&ae;m gifrum sui&d;e hr&ae;dlice him willa&d; fylgan leohtlicu weorc &amp; unnyte. 
 &D;&ae;t tryme&d; sio halige &ae;  &d;&ae;r hio cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t folc s&ae;t  &ae;t  &amp; dranc  &amp; si&d;&d;an aryson  &amp; eodon him plegean. 
 Sua oft se ofer&ae;t wier&d; gehwierfed to fierenluste  for&d;&ae;m &d;onne sio womb bi&d; full &amp; a&d;ened  &d;onne bid aweaht se anga &d;&ae;re wr&ae;nnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden to &d;&ae;m lytegan feonde  &d;e &d;&ae;s &ae;restan monnes mod ontynde on &d;&ae;s &ae;ples gewilnunge  &amp; hit &d;a gewearp mid synne grine  to &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden mid &d;&ae;re godcundan stemne: On &d;inre wambe &amp; on &d;inum breostum &d;u scealt snican. 
 Suelce he openlice cu&ae;de: On giefernesse &amp; on unnytum ge&d;ohtum &d;u ricsas&d; ofer &d;a menniscan heortan. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;m &d;e on giefernesse ongietene beo&d; wile folgian fierenlust. 
 &D;&ae;t cy&d;de se witga  &d;a he &d;&ae;t openlice s&ae;de &d;&ae;tte sua gewear&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t gebiecnede &d;&ae;t &d;a giet diegle w&ae;s  he cu&ae;&d;: Koka ealdormon towearp &d;a burg &ae;t Hierusalem. 
 &D;ara koka ealdormon bi&d; sio womb  for&d;&ae;m eall hiera gesuinc &amp; hiera &d;enung belimpe&d; to hiere  hu heo weor&d;e mid swotlecustum mettum gefylled. 
 &D;a weallas &d;onne Hierusalem getacnia&d; &d;a m&ae;genu &d;&ae;re saule. 
 &D;a m&ae;genu beo&d; ar&ae;redu mid wilnunge to &d;&ae;re uplican sibbe. 
 Ac &d;ara koka ealdormon towierp&d; &d;a weallas Hierusalem. 
 &D;&ae;t is  &d;onne &d;onne sio wamb bi&d; a&d;ened mid fylle for giefernesse  &d;onne towierp&d; hio &d;urh fierenlustas &d;a m&ae;genu &d;&ae;re saule. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t &d;onne is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;m f&ae;stendum  gif &d;&ae;s modes forh&ae;fdnes ful oft mid unge&d;yl&d;e ne ascoke &d;a sibbe of &d;&ae;m sceate &d;&ae;re smyltnesse  &d;onne ne cu&ae;de sanctus Petrus to his cnihtum sua sua he cu&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Nu ge habba&d; geleafan  wyrcea&d; nu god weorc  &amp; habba&d; &d;onne wisdom  &amp; on &d;am wisdome habba&d; forh&ae;fdnesse  &amp; eac l&ae;ra&d;  &amp; huru on &d;&ae;re forh&ae;fdnesse ge&d;ylde. 
 Ne cu&ae;de he no sua  gif he ne ongeate &d;&ae;t him w&ae;s &d;&ae;s wana  ac for&d;y&d;e he ongeat &d;&ae;t sio unge&d;yld oft dere&d; &d;&ae;m mannum &d;e micle forh&ae;fdnesse habba&d;  &d;a l&ae;rde he &d;&ae;t hie huru sceoldon &d;a habban toeacan &d;&ae;re forh&ae;fdnesse. 
 Gif eac sio scyld &d;ara ofermetta ne gewundode &d;y oftor &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s f&ae;stendan  &d;onne ne cu&ae;de no sanctus Paulus: Se &d;e f&ae;stan wille  ne t&ae;le he no &d;one &d;e ete. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d; to Kolosensum  &d;a he ongeat &d;&ae;t hie gulpun hiera f&ae;stennes: Oft &d;onne mon ma f&ae;st &d;onne he &d;yrfe  &d;onne eowe&d; he utan ea&d;modnesse  &amp; for &d;&ae;re ilcan ea&d;modnesse he ofermodga&d; innan micle &d;y hefelicor. 
 Gif &d;&ae;t mod ful oft ne a&d;unde on ofermettum for &d;&ae;re forh&ae;fdnesse  &d;onne ne talode se ofermoda Phariseus to sua micle m&ae;gene &d;a forh&ae;fdnesse sua he dyde  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Ic f&ae;ste tuwa on wican. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a ofergifran  &d;eah hie ne m&ae;gen &d;one un&d;eaw forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;re gifernesse &amp; &d;&ae;re oferwiste  &d;&ae;t he huru hine selfne ne &d;urhstinge mid &d;y sweorde unryhth&ae;medes  ac ongiete hu micel leohtmodnes &amp; leasfer&d;nes &amp; oferspr&ae;c cyme&d; of &d;&ae;re oferwiste  &d;yl&ae;s he hit mid &d;&ae;m o&d;rum yfele geiece  &amp; eac &d;onne he his wambe sua hnesclice olec&d;  &d;&ae;t he for&d;&ae;m ne weor&d;e w&ae;lhreowlice gefangen mid &d;&ae;m grinum uncysta. 
 Ac we sculun ge&d;encean  sua oft sua we ure hand do&d; to urum mu&d;e for giefernesse ofergemet  &d;&ae;t we geedniwia&d; &amp; gemyndgia&d; &d;&ae;re scylde &d;e ure ieldesta m&ae;g us on forworhte  &amp; we beo&d; sua micle fier gewitene fram urum &ae;fterran M&ae;ge &d;e us eft ge&d;ingode  sua we oftor aslida&d; on &d;&ae;m un&d;eawe. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a f&ae;stendan &d;&ae;t hie huru geornlice giemen  &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r hie fleo&d; &d;one un&d;eaw &d;&ae;re gifernesse  &d;&ae;tte of &d;&ae;m gode ne weor&d;e wyrse yfel akenned  &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc hl&ae;na&d;  &d;&ae;t mod ne ber&ae;se on unge&d;yld  &amp; &d;onne sie unnyt &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc sie oferswi&d;ed  gif &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; mid &d;&ae;m ierre oferswi&d;ed. 
 Oft eac  &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s f&ae;stendan bi&d; mid &d;y irre ofseten  &d;onne cym&d; sio blis seldhwanne  suelce hio sie cuma o&d;&d;e el&d;eodig  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; mid &d;y ierre gewemmed  &amp; for&d;&ae;m forlies&d; &d;&ae;t god &d;&ae;re forh&ae;fdnesse  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he hine no ne beheold wi&d; &d;a g&ae;stlican scylde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s sui&d;e ryhte gecueden &d;urh &d;one witgan: On eowrum f&ae;stendagum bi&d; ongieten eower willa. 
 &amp; sona &d;&ae;r&ae;fter he cu&ae;&d;: To gemotum &amp; to gecidum &amp; to iersunga &amp; to fystgebeate ge f&ae;sta&d;. 
 Willa belimp&d; to blisse simle &amp; &d;&ae;t fystgebeat to irre. 
 On iedelnesse &d;onne bi&d; se lichoma mid f&ae;stenne gesuenced  &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; forl&ae;ten &amp; onstyred &amp; tod&ae;led ungedafenlice &amp; unendebyrdlice on un&d;eawas. 
 Ond &d;eah hie sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie no hiera f&ae;sten ne gewanigen  ne eft ne wenen &d;&ae;t hit anlipe full healic m&ae;gen sie beforan &d;&ae;m dieglan Deman  &d;yl&ae;s hie wenen &d;&ae;t hit anlipe micellre geearnunge m&ae;gen sie  &amp; &d;onne weor&d;en on hiera mode for&d;y to upah&ae;fene. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh Essaias &d;one witgan: Ne geceas ic no &d;is f&ae;sten  ac &d;yllic f&ae;sten ic geceas: brec &d;&ae;m hyngriendum &d;inne hlaf  &amp; &d;one widfarendan &amp; &d;one w&ae;dlan l&ae;d on &d;in hus. 
 Be &d;&ae;m we magon ge&d;encean hu lytelu sio forh&ae;fdnes bi&d; gesewen  gif hio ne bi&d; mid o&d;rum goodum weorcum geiced. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cu&ae;&d; Iohel se witga: Gehalgia&d; eower f&ae;sten. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his f&ae;sten gehalgige  &d;&ae;t he hit geice mid o&d;rum godum weorcum; 
 &D;onne m&ae;g he eowian &d;&ae;r Gode sui&d;e gelicweor&d;e forh&ae;fdnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;m f&ae;stendum &d;&ae;t hie wieten &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne Gode sui&d;e licwyr&d;e forh&ae;fdnesse brienga&d;  &d;onne hie &d;earfendum monnum sella&d; hiera ondliefene &d;one d&ae;l &d;e hi him selfum oftio&d;. 
 Ac us is sui&d;e geornlice to gehieranne hw&ae;t Dryhten &d;reatigende cu&ae;&d; to Iudeum &d;urh Sacharias &d;one witgan; 
 He cu&ae;&d;: Eall &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t ge f&ae;stun &amp; weopun on &d;&ae;m fiftan &amp; on &d;am siofo&d;an mon&d;e nu hundsiofantig wintra  ne f&ae;ste ge &d;&ae;s nawuht me  &amp; &d;onne ge &ae;ton  &d;onne &ae;te ge eow selfum  &amp; &d;onne ge druncon  &d;onne druncon ge eow selfum. 
 Ne f&ae;s&d; se no Gode ac him selfum  se &d;e &d;&ae;t nyle &d;earfum sellan &d;&ae;t he &d;onne on m&ae;le l&ae;f&d;  ac wile hit healdan eft to o&d;rum m&ae;le  &d;&ae;t he eft m&ae;ge his wambe mid gefyllan. 
 Ac sua he sceal etan &d;&ae;tte hine sio gewilnung &d;&ae;re gifernesse of his modes f&ae;s&d;r&ae;dnesse ne gebrienge  ne eft sio &d;r&ae;s&d;ing &d;&ae;s lichoman &d;&ae;t mod ne ascrence mid upah&ae;fenesse. 
 Gehieren &d;a oferetolan &d;a word &d;e Krist of his agnum mu&d;e cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d;: Behealda&d; eow &d;&ae;t eowre heortan ne sin gehefegode mid ofer&ae;te &amp; druncennesse &amp; on to monigfaldum ymbehogan &d;isse worulde  &d;yl&ae;s eow on &d;&ae;m weorcum gemete se re&d;a &amp; se egeslica d&ae;g  se cym&d; ofer ealle eor&d;waran unge&d;inged  sua sua grin. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a f&ae;stendan hw&ae;t he eft cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d;: Ne geuncl&ae;nsa&d; &d;&ae;t no &d;one mon &d;&ae;t on his mu&d; g&ae;&d;  ac &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t of his mu&d;e g&ae;&d;  &d;&ae;t hine geuncl&ae;nsa&d;. 
 Gehieren &d;a oferetolan hw&ae;t sanctus Paulus cu&ae;&d;: Fulga nu se mete &d;&ae;re wambe willan  &amp; sio wamb &d;&ae;s metes  &d;onne towyrp&d; God &ae;g&d;er. 
 &amp; eft he cu&ae;&d;: Ne gewunigen ge to oferetolnisse &amp; to oferdruncennisse. 
 &amp; eft he cu&ae;&d;: Se ofermete ne bef&ae;s&d; us n&ae;bre Gode. 
 Gehieren eft &d;a f&ae;stendan hw&ae;t he to him cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;m cl&ae;num w&ae;re eal cl&ae;ne  &amp; &d;&ae;m uncl&ae;num n&ae;re nan wuht cl&ae;ne. 
 Gehiren eft &d;a oferetolan hw&ae;t he to him cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;tte hira wamb w&ae;re hiera God  &amp; hie dydon hiera bysmer him to wyr&d;scipe. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a f&ae;stendan hw&ae;t he to him cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;m forh&ae;bbendum hwilum gebyrede &d;&ae;t hie gewieten of hiera geleafan  &amp; forbeoda&d; monnum &d;&ae;t hie hiwien  &amp; &d;a mettas &d;e God self gesceop to etanne geleaffullum monnum  &d;&ae;m &d;e ongieta&d; so&d;f&ae;s&d;nisse  &amp; Gode &d;oncia&d; mid goodum weorcum his giefa. 
 Gehieren &d;a oferetolan hw&ae;t sanctus Paulus cw&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hit w&ae;re good &d;&ae;t mon foreode fl&ae;sc &amp; win for bisene his bro&d;rum. 
 Gehiren &d;a f&ae;stendan hw&ae;t he eft cu&ae;&d;  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t ge moston drincan gewealden wines for eowres magan mettrymnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m he &d;&ae;t cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he wolde &d;&ae;t &d;a oferetolan geleornoden &d;&ae;t hie to ungemetlice ne wilnoden fl&ae;scmetta  ond eft &d;a f&ae;stendan ne forsawen &d;a etendan  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie &d;&ae;re Godes giefe bruca&d; &d;a &d;e o&d;re forbera&d;. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e hiora agnu &d;ing mildheortlice sella&d;  &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;onne giet wilniad o&d;erra monna gereafigan. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e hira god mildheortlice sella&d;  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;onne giet flieta&d; &ae;fter o&d;erra monna  &amp; hie reafia&d;. 
 To manienne sint &d;a &d;e hiera mildheortlice sella&d; &d;&ae;tte hie ne a&d;inden on hiora mode to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi hi h&ae;bben ofer &d;a &d;e hie hiora sella&d;  ne hie selfe &d;y beteran ne taligen &d;e &d;a o&d;re  &d;eah &d;a o&d;re be him libben. 
 Ac &d;a eor&d;lican hlafordas sint to &d;&ae;m gesette &d;&ae;t hie &d;a endebyrdnesse &amp; &d;a &d;egnunga hiora hieredum gebrytnige  &amp; hie gerecce  &amp; &d;&ae;t folc is to &d;&ae;m gesett &d;&ae;t hie scylen be hira r&ae;dum libban. 
 &D;&ae;m hlafordum is beboden &d;&ae;t hie him doon &d;&ae;t hira &d;earf sie  &amp; &d;&ae;m &d;egnum is beboden &d;&ae;t hie him &d;&ae;t to genyhte don &d;&ae;t hie him sellen. 
 &amp; &d;eah oft agylta&d; &d;a hlafordas  &amp; &d;a menn wunia&d; on Godes hyldo &d;a &d;e ryhtwise beo&d;  &amp; &d;a habba&d; his unhyldo &d;e hit him bryhttian sceoldon  &amp; &d;a beo&d; butan ierre &d;e be hiera giefum libban sculon. 
 Eac sint to manienne &d;a &d;e &d;onne mildheortlice sella&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne habba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne angieten &d;&ae;t hie sint gesette &d;&ae;m hefencundan Gode to &d;eningmannum  to d&ae;lanne &d;as l&ae;nan god. 
 For&d;&ae;m hie hie sculon sua micle estelicor d&ae;lan sua hie ongieta&d; &d;&ae;t him l&ae;nre &amp; unagenre bi&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;r d&ae;la&d;  for&d;&ae;m hie magon ongietan &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; to hiera &d;enunga gesette Godes giefe to d&ae;lanne. 
 Hwy sculon hie &d;onne beon for&d;&ae;m upah&ae;fene &amp; a&d;undene on hira mode? 
 Him w&ae;re &d;onne micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie leten Godes ege hie geea&d;medan. 
 &amp; eac him is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;t hie to unweor&d;lice ne d&ae;len &d;&ae;t him bef&ae;s&d; bi&d;  &d;yl&ae;s hie awuht sellen &d;&ae;m &d;e hie nanwuht ne sceoldon  o&d;&d;e nan wuht &d;&ae;m &d;e hie hw&ae;thwugu sceoldon  o&d;&d;e eft fela &d;am &d;e hie lytel sceoldon  o&d;&d;e lytel &d;&ae;m &d;e hie micel sceoldon  &d;yl&ae;s hie unnytlice forweorpen &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie sellen for hira hr&ae;dhydignesse  o&d;&d;e him eft hefiglice of&d;ynce &d;&ae;s &d;e hie sealdon  &amp; hi scylen selfe beon biddende  &amp; for&d;y weor&d;en geunrotsode  o&d;&d;e hie eft her wilnigen &d;ara leana &d;&ae;s &d;e hie on &ae;lmessan sella&d;  &d;yl&ae;s sio gidsung &d;&ae;s l&ae;nan lofes adw&ae;sce &d;&ae;t leoht &d;&ae;re giofolnesse  o&d;&d;e eft sio giofolness sie gemenged wi&d; unrotnesse  o&d;&d;e he eft for &d;&ae;m giefum  &d;e him &d;onne &d;ynce&d; &d;&ae;t he sui&d;e wel atogen h&ae;bbe  his mod sui&d;ur f&ae;gnige &amp; blissige &d;onne hit gemetlic o&d;&d;e gedafenlic sie. 
 Ac &d;onne hie hit eall ryhtlice ged&ae;led h&ae;bben  &d;onne ne teon hie nanwuht &d;&ae;s lofes &amp; &d;&ae;s ge&d;onces to him  &d;yl&ae;s hie hit eal forleosen  &d;onne hie hit ged&ae;led h&ae;bben  ne him selfum ne tellen to m&ae;gene hiora freodom; 
 Ac gehieren hw&ae;t awriten is on &d;&ae;m &ae;rendgewrite sancte Petres: Gif hwa &d;enige  &d;enige he suelce he hit of Godes m&ae;gene &d;enige  n&ae;s of his selfes  &d;yl&ae;s he to ungemetlice f&ae;genige for his godum weorcum. 
 Ac gehieren hw&ae;t awriten is on Kristes bocum  hit is awriten: &d;onne ge eall h&ae;bben gedoon &d;&ae;t eow beboden is  &d;onne cue&d;e ge &d;&ae;t ge sien unnytte &d;eowas  for&d;&ae;m ge &d;&ae;t an worhton &d;&ae;t ge niede scoldon. 
 &amp; eft  &d;yl&ae;s &d;a rummodnessa sio unrotnes gewemme  gehiera&d; &d;one cuide &d;e sanctus Paulus cu&ae;&d; to Corinctheum  he cu&ae;&d; &d;&ae;tte &d;one gladan giefan God lufode. 
 &amp; eft  &d;yl&ae;s hie for &d;&ae;m gedale &d;&ae;s feos wilnigen &d;isses l&ae;nan lifes  gehieren hie &d;one cwide &d;e on Cristesbocum awriten is  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t sio winestre hand ne scyle witan hw&ae;t sio sui&d;re do. 
 &D;&ae;t is  &d;onne &d;onne he his &ae;lmessan d&ae;l&d;  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r ne sie wi&d; gemenged nan gielp &d;isses andweardan lifes  ne he ne scrife &d;&ae;s hlisan buton hu he ryhtos&d; wyrce. 
 Ne he ne gieme hwelce hylde he mid &d;&ae;re &ae;lmessan gewriexle  ac gehiren hw&ae;t awriten is on cristesbocum  he cu&ae;&d;: &d;onne &d;u h&ae;bbe gegearwod underngiefl o&d;&d;e &ae;fengiefl  ne la&d;a &d;u no &d;&ae;rto &d;ine friend  ne &d;ine bro&d;or  ne &d;ine cu&d;an  ne &d;ine welegan neahgeburas  &d;yl&ae;s hie &d;e don &d;&ae;t selfe. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;u feorme gierwe on &ae;lmessan la&d;a &d;&ae;rto w&ae;dlan &amp; wanhale &amp; healte &amp; blinde  &d;onne bis &d;u eadig  for&d;&ae;m hie nyton mid hwam hie hit &d;e forgielden. 
 &amp; &d;&ae;tte mon &d;onne &d;urhteon m&ae;ge  &d;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t ne forilde  ac gehieren hw&ae;t awriten is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is awrieten &d;&ae;t mon ne scyle cwe&d;an to his friend: Ga  &amp; cum to morgenne  &d;onne selle ic &d;e hw&ae;thwugu  gif he hit him &d;onne sellan m&ae;ge. 
 Ond eft  &d;yl&ae;s mon unnytlice mierre &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe  gehieren menn &d;isne cwide: Heald &d;ine &ae;lmessan  &d;yl&ae;s &d;u hie forweorpe. 
 &amp; eft &d;a &d;e to lytel sella&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e micles &d;orfton  sculon gehieran sancte Paules cuide  he cu&ae;&d;: Se &d;e lytel s&ae;w&d; he lytel rip&d;. 
 &amp; &d;eah ne selle mon to fela &d;&ae;m &d;e lytles &d;yrfe  &d;yl&ae;s hwa him self weor&d;e to w&ae;dlan  &amp; him &d;onne gehreowe sio &ae;lmesse. 
 Be &d;am cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Ne beo ge o&d;rum monnum sua gifole &d;&ae;t hit weor&d;e eow selfum to gesuince  ac ofer &d;&ae;t &d;e ge selfe genog h&ae;bben  sella&d; &d;&ae;t &d;earfum  &amp; mid &d;y hiera w&ae;dle gebeta&d;  &d;&ae;tte sua ielce sua hie beo&d; her gefyllede mid ure genyhtsumnesse  we beon eac mid hiera genyhtsumnesse. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne hiera genihtsumnes Godes milts  &d;a geearna&d; se se on his g&ae;ste bi&d; w&ae;dla. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;&ae;s sellendan mod ne cann &d;a w&ae;delnesse ge&d;olian  &d;onne him micles oftogen bi&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e he habban wolde; 
 &D;onne oncann he hiene selfne for &d;&ae;re hr&ae;dhydignesse &d;e he &ae;r to fela sealde. 
 For&d;y mon scel &ae;r ge&d;encean  &ae;r he hw&ae;t selle  &d;&ae;t he hit eft forberan m&ae;ge butan hreowe  &d;yl&ae;s he forleose &d;a lean &d;&ae;s &d;e he &ae;r sealde  &amp; &d;&ae;t mod eac weor&d;e wirs forloren &d;urh &d;a gnornunga. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a nanwuht ne sella&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e hie lytles hw&ae;thwugu scoldon  hw&ae;t to him gecweden is on &d;&ae;m godspelle  hit is gecweden: Sele &ae;lcum &d;ara &d;e &d;e bidde. 
 Eft gehieren &d;a &d;a &d;e hw&ae;thwugu sella&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e hie nane wuht ne scoldon  hw&ae;t to him gecueden is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is gecueden: Sele &d;in good  &amp; na &d;eah &d;am synnfullum. 
 Doo wel &d;&ae;m ea&d;modum  &amp; &d;am arleasum nanwuht. 
 Ond eft hit is gecweden on Tobius bocum: Sete &d;in win  &amp; lege &d;inne hlaf ofer ryhtwisra monna byrgenne  &amp; ne et his nanwuht  ne ne drinc mid &d;&ae;m synfullum. 
 Se &d;onne itt &amp; drinc&d; mid &d;&ae;m synfullum  &amp; him sel&d; his hlaf &amp; his win  se &d;&ae;m unryhtwisan fultuma&d;  &amp; hine ara&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he unryhtwis bi&d;. 
 Sua eac monige welige menn on &d;ys middangearde l&ae;ta&d; cuelan hungre Cristes &d;earfan  &amp; feda&d; yfle gliigmenn mid oferwiste  &amp; beo&d; to ungemetlice kystige. 
 &D;a &d;onne &d;e hira hlaf sella&d; &d;&ae;m synfullum &d;e &d;earfende beo&d;  nalles no for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie synnfulle beo&d;  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie menn beo&d;  &amp; &d;earfende beo&d;  ne sel&d; se no synfullum his hlaf  ac ryhtwisum  gif he on him ne lufa&d; his yfel  ac his gecynd  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he bi&d; man swa same sua he. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a &d;e nu hiera mildheortlice sella&d;  &d;&ae;t hie geornlice giemen &d;&ae;t hie eft &d;a synne ne gefremmen &d;e hie nu mid hira &ae;lmessan aliesa&d;  &d;yl&ae;s hie eft scilen don &d;&ae;t selfe. 
 Ne fortruwige he hiene &ae;t &d;&ae;re cipinge  ne wene he no &d;&ae;t Godes ryhtwisnes sie to ceape  swelce he hie m&ae;ge mid his peningum gebygcgean  &amp; don si&d;&d;an suelc yfel suelce hie willen butan &ae;lcre o&d;erre wrace  &d;a hwile &d;e hie peningas h&ae;bben mid to gieldanne. 
 Mare is &d;&ae;t mod &d;onne se mete  &amp; se lichoma &d;onne &d;&ae;t hr&ae;gl. 
 Ac &d;onne hwa &ae;g&d;er ge mete ge hr&ae;gl &d;earfendum rumodlice sel&d;  &amp; his mod &amp; his lichoman mid unryhtwisnesse besmit  &d;onne sel&d; he Gode &d;a l&ae;s&d;an ryhtwisnesse  &amp; oftieh&d; him &d;&ae;re m&ae;stan  &d;onne he synga&d; on his mode &amp; on his m&ae;gene  &amp; sel&d; &d;eah his &ae;lmessan: sel&d; Gode his &ae;hta  &amp; hine selfne diobule. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;onne giet wilnia&d; o&d;re menn to reafigeanne  &d;&ae;t hie geornlice gehieren &d;one cuide &d;e ges&ae;d is on &d;&ae;m godspelle  &d;&ae;t Dryhten cue&d;an wille  &d;onne he cym&d; to &d;&ae;m dome  he cui&d;: Me hyngrede  &amp; ge me nawuht ne sealdun etan. 
 Me &d;yrste  &amp; ge me ne sealdon drincan. 
 Ic w&ae;s cuma  &amp; ge me noldon onfon. 
 Ic w&ae;s nacod  &amp; ge me noldon bewreon. 
 Ic w&ae;s untrum &amp; on cearcerne  &amp; ge min noldon fandian. 
 &D;&ae;m monnum is gehaten &d;&ae;t he wille cue&d;an: Gewita&d; from me  awiergde  on ece fyr  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s gegearwod diofle &amp; his englum. 
 Ne scir&d; he no hw&ae;&d;er hie reafoden  o&d;&d;e hwelc o&d;er yfel fremeden  &amp; swa&d;eah cwi&d; &d;&ae;t hie scylen bion geh&ae;fte on ecum fyre. 
 Be &d;&ae;m we magon ge&d;encean hu micles wites &d;a beo&d; weor&d;e &d;e o&d;re menn reafia&d;  nu &d;a sua micel wite habba&d; &d;e hiora agen ungesceadwislice healda&d;. 
 Nu &d;a sua micel wite habba&d; &d;e hira agen nylla&d; sellan  ge&d;encea&d; &d;onne hwelces wites ge wenen &d;&ae;m &d;e o&d;re men reafia&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t wene ge hw&ae;t sio &d;urhtogene unryhtwisnes geearnige  nu sio un&d;urtogene arf&ae;s&d;nes swa micel wite geearna&d;? 
 Gehieren &d;a reaferas  &d;a &d;e higia&d; wi&d; &d;&ae;s &d;&ae;t hie willa&d; o&d;re menn bereafian  hw&ae;t be him gecweden is  hit is gecweden: Wa &d;&ae;m &d;e ealnig gadera&d; an hine selfne &d;&ae;t hefige fenn  &amp; gemonigfalda&d; &d;&ae;te his ne bi&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t monn gadrige &d;&ae;t &d;icke fenn on hine  &amp; hine mid &d;y gehefegige  &d;&ae;t se gitsere him on geheapige &d;a byr&d;enne eor&d;licra &ae;hta mid unryhte  &amp; his wor&d;ig &amp; his land mid unryhte ryme. 
 Ac hi scoldon gehiran &d;one cwide &d;e bi him gecweden is in Essaies bocum  hit is gecweden: Wa eow &d;e gadria&d; hus to huse  &amp; spanna&d; &d;one &ae;cer to &d;&ae;m o&d;rum o&d; &d;&ae;s landes mearce  swelce ge ane willen gebugean ealle &d;as eor&d;an. 
 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Hu feor wolde ge nu ryman eower land? 
 Wolde ge nu &d;&ae;t ge n&ae;fden nanne gemacan on &d;ys gem&ae;nan middangearde? 
 &D;u cuist nu &d;&ae;t &t;u wille geswican &d;on  &ae;r &d;e &d;u genoh h&ae;bbe. 
 Hwonne bi&d; &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t &d;e swa &d;ynce  o&d;&d;e hwonne bi&d; &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t &d;u nyte hw&ae;der &d;u maran wilnige? 
 Ac &d;u findst wi&d; hwone &d;u meaht flitan. 
 Ac gehiere ge feohgietseras hw&ae;t be eow gecweden is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is gecweden: Ne wyr&d; se gitsere n&ae;fre full feos  &amp; se &d;e woruldwelan lufa&d; ungesceadwislice  ne cym&d; him of &d;&ae;m nan w&ae;s&d;m. 
 Ac him meahte cuman  gif he hi to swi&d;e ne lufode  &amp; he hi wel wolde d&ae;lan. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e he hi her lufa&d; &amp; hielt  he hi eac her forl&ae;t butan &ae;lcum w&ae;s&d;me &amp; &ae;lcum edleane. 
 Ac &d;a &d;e wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hi her beon gefylde mid eallum welum &amp; mid &d;&ae;m willan beo&d; on&ae;lede  hie sculon gehieran &d;one cwide &d;e be him gecweden is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is gecweden: Se &d;e &ae;fter &d;&ae;m higa&d; &d;&ae;t he eadig sie on &d;isse worulde  ne bi&d; he unscea&d;ful  ac &d;a hwile &d;e he giern&d; &d;&ae;t he his weolan iece  he agiemeleasa&d; &amp; forgiet &d;&ae;t he forbuge his synna. 
 Swa swa fleogende fugel  &d;onne he gifre bi&d;  he gesih&d; &d;&ae;t &ae;s on eor&d;an  &amp; &d;onne for &d;&ae;m luste &d;&ae;s metes he forgiet &d;&ae;t grin &d;&ae;t he mid awierged wir&d;; 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;m gitsere. 
 He gesih&d; &d;one welan &d;e he wilna&d;  &amp; he ne gelief&d; &d;&ae;s grines &d;e he mid gebrogden wyr&d;  &ae;r&d;on he hit gefrede. 
 Ac &d;a &d;e wilnia&d; &d;isses middangeardes gestreona  &amp; nylla&d; wietan &d;one demm &d;e him &ae;fter cuman sceal  hie sculon gehieran &d;one cwide &d;e bi him gecweden is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is gecweden: &d;&ae;t ierfe &d;&ae;t ge &ae;rest &ae;fter hiegia&d;  &ae;t si&d;es&d;an hit bi&d; bed&ae;led &ae;lcre bledsunge. 
 On &d;ys andweardan life we onginna&d; &ae;res&d; libban to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t we &ae;t ytemestan onfon sumne d&ae;l bledsunge. 
 Se &d;onne &d;e wilna&d; &d;&ae;t wolde on &d;&ae;m angienne his lifes woroldspedig weor&d;an mid unryhte  se hine wile selfne bed&ae;lan &d;&ae;re bledsunge &amp; &d;&ae;s weolan on &d;&ae;m ytemestan d&ae;ge. 
 Ac &d;onne hie wilnia&d; &d;urh &d;a nawhtgitsunga &d;&ae;t hie hira woruldspeda ie icenn  &d;onne weor&d;a&d; hie bed&ae;lede &d;&ae;s ecean e&d;les ures F&ae;der. 
 Ac &d;a &d;e wilnia&d; feola to begietanne  &amp; eac &d;a &d;e magon begietan eall &d;&ae;t hie wilnia&d;  gehieren hw&ae;t Krist self cu&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t forstent &ae;nigum menn &d;&ae;t  &d;eah he mangige &d;&ae;t he ealne &d;isne middangeard age  gif he his saule forspildt? 
 Swelce sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes openlice cw&ae;de: Hwelc fremu bi&d; menn &d;&ae;t he gestriene eal &d;&ae;t him ymbutan sie  gif he forlies&d; &d;&ae;t him oninnan bi&d;  swelce he eall gegadrige &d;&ae;tte his ne sie  &amp; forspilde hine selfne? 
 Ac mon m&ae;g &d;y hra&d;or &d;ara reafera gitsunga gestillan  gif se lareow him gerec&d; hu fleonde &d;is andwearde lif is  &amp; hie gemyndga&d; &d;ara weligera &d;e lange striendon  &amp; lytle hwile brucon; 
 Hu hr&ae;dlice se f&ae;rlica dea&d; he on lytelre hwile bereafode &d;&ae;s &d;e hi on langre hwile mid unryhte strindon. 
 &D;eah hie hit hr&ae;dlice &ae;tsomne ne gestriendon  hie hit &d;eah swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice &ae;tsomne forluron &amp; his nawht mid him ne l&ae;ddon buton &d;a synne &d;ara yfelena weorca hie brohton to Godes dome. 
 Ac hit m&ae;g ea&d;e ges&ae;lan  gif we him swelc secga&d;  &d;&ae;t hie eac mid us &d;a o&d;re t&ae;len  &amp; hie &d;onne eft hira selfra gescamige  &d;onne hie gemuna&d; &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t ilce do&d; &d;&ae;t hie on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum t&ae;ldon. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e nohw&ae;&d;er ne o&d;erra monna ne wilnia&d;  ne hiora agen nylla&d; sellan; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e willa&d; sellan &d;&ae;t hi gestrina&d;  &amp; &d;eah nylla&d; geswican &d;&ae;t hi o&d;re men ne reafigen. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e nau&d;er ne o&d;erra monna ne wilnia&d;  ne hira agen nylla&d; sellan; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;e hira agen willa&d; sellan  &amp; &d;eah ne magon forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;t hie o&d;re menn ne reafigen. 
 Ac &d;a &d;onne &d;e hira agen nylla&d; sellan  ne eac o&d;erra monna ne gitsia&d;  hie sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;t &d;ios eor&d;e  &d;e him &d;&ae;t gestreon of com  eallum mannum is to gemanan geseald  &amp; for&d;&ae;m eallum mannum bring&d; gem&ae;nne foster. 
 Hw&ae;t se &d;onne unryhtlice tala&d;  se &d;e tala&d; &d;&ae;t he sie unscyldig  gif he &d;a good  &d;e us God teo gemanan sealde  him synderlice &ae;gna&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne hie nylla&d; sellan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie underfengon  &d;onne m&ae;sta&d; hie hie selfe on hira niehstena cwale  for&d;&ae;m hie nealice swa fela &d;earfena ofslea&d; swa hie i&d;elice mid hiera &ae;lmessan gehelpan meahton  gif hie woldon. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne &d;onne we &d;&ae;m &d;earfum hiera nied&d;earfe sella&d;  hiera &ae;gen we him sella&d;  nalles ure; 
 &amp; ryhtlicor we magon cwe&d;an &d;&ae;t we him gielden scylde &d;onne we him mildheortnesse don. 
 For&d;&ae;m sio So&d;f&ae;stnes  &d;&ae;t is Crist  &d;a &d;a he l&ae;rde &d;&ae;t mon &ae;lmessan w&ae;rlice sellan sceolde  &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Giema&d; &d;&ae;t ge eowre ryhtwisnesse ne don beforan monnum. 
 To &d;&ae;m cwide belimp&d; eac &d;&ae;s psalmscopes sang &d;e he sang  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Se tod&ae;l&d; his god  &amp; sel&d; &d;earfum  his ryhtwisnes wuna&d; on ecnesse. 
 Nolde he no &d;a rummodnesse hatan mildheortness  ac ryhtwisnes  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte us from &d;&ae;m gem&ae;nan gode geseald bi&d;  hit is cynn &d;&ae;t we &d;&ae;s eac gem&ae;nelice brucen. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Salomon: Se &d;e ryhtwis bi&d;  he bi&d; a sellende  &amp; no ne blin&d;. 
 Eac hie sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte se fiicbeam  &d;e on &d;&ae;m godspelle ges&ae;d is &d;&ae;tte nanne w&ae;s&d;m ne b&ae;re  stod unnyt; 
 For&d;&ae;m him wear&d; ierre se goda wyrhta for&d;&ae;m he ofergreow &d;&ae;t land butan w&ae;s&d;me. 
 &D;onne ofergrew&d; se fiicbeam &d;&ae;t lond  &d;onne se gitsere hyt &amp; hele&d; to unnytte &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t manegum menn to nytte weor&d;an meahte. 
 Swa se fiicbeam ofersceada&d; &d;&ae;t lond &d;&ae;t hit under him ne m&ae;g gegrowan  for&d;&ae;m hit sio sunne ne mot gescinan  ne he self nanne w&ae;s&d;m &d;&ae;rofer ne bire&d;  ac &d;&ae;t land bi&d; eal unnyt swa he hit oferbr&ae;t  swa bi&d; &d;&ae;m unnytwyr&d;an &amp; &d;&ae;m unwisan menn  &d;onne he mid &d;&ae;re scande his sl&ae;w&d;e oferbr&ae;t &d;a scire &d;e he &d;onne h&ae;f&d;  &amp; &d;onne nau&d;er ne &d;one folga&d; self nytne gedon nyle  ne &d;one tol&ae;tan &d;e hine &d;urh &d;a sunnan goodes weorces giendscinan wille  &amp; nytwyr&d;ne &amp; w&ae;s&d;mb&ae;rne gedon wille. 
 Ac manigra manna gewuna is &d;&ae;t hie hie mid &d;issum wordum ladia&d;  &amp; cue&d;a&d;: We bruca&d; ures &ae;gnes  ne gitsige we nanes o&d;res monnes. 
 Gif we nauht &d;&ae;s ne doo&d; &d;e us mon mid goode leanian &d;yrfe  ne do we eac nan woh &d;e us mon fore t&ae;lan &d;urfe. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m hie cue&d;a&d; &d;as word &d;e hie beluca&d; hiera modes earan ongean &d;a godcundan lare. 
 Hw&ae;t se weliga &d;e on &d;&ae;m godspelle get&ae;ld is  &amp; him bi gecweden is &d;&ae;t he &ae;lce d&ae;ge symblede  &amp; mid micelre wiste w&ae;re gefeormod  &amp; &ae;lce d&ae;ge geglenged mid purpuran &amp; mid hwitum hr&ae;gle  nis hit no ges&ae;d &d;&ae;t he for &d;y get&ae;led w&ae;re &d;y he o&d;re menn reafode  ac for&d;y&d;e he his &ae;genes ungemetlice breac  &amp; o&d;rum monnum nawuht ne sealde; 
 &amp; &d;eah &ae;fter &d;isse worulde he underfeng helle wite  nalles no for&d;y&d;e he awuht unaliefedes dyde  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e he &d;&ae;s aliefdan nanwuht nolde forl&ae;tan  ac his swi&d;e ungemetlice breac  &amp; hine selfne eallinga gesealde &d;iossum woruldwelum. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a f&ae;s&d;hafula &d;&ae;t hie ongieten &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t sindon &d;a forman l&ae;&d;&d;o &d;e hie Gode gedoon m&ae;gen  &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;m nawuht ne don &d;e him eall sealde &d;&ae;t hie habba&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; se psalmscop: He ne sealde Gode nanne metsceat for his saule ne n&ae;nne ge&d;ingsceat wi&d; his miltse. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne se medsceat wi&d; his saule &d;&ae;t he him gielde god weorc for &d;&ae;re giefe &d;e he him &ae;r sealde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan cw&ae;&d; Iohannes se godspellere: &ae;lc treow mon sceal ceorfan  &d;e goode w&ae;s&d;mas ne bir&d;  &amp; weorpan on fyr  &amp; forb&ae;rnan. 
 Nu is &d;onne sio &ae;xs aset on &d;ane wyrttruman &d;&ae;s treowes  ac ondr&ae;den him &d;one dynt swa neah  &d;a &d;e nauht to gode ne do&d;  &amp; &d;eah wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie sien unscyldige  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie nan la&d; ne do&d;. 
 Ac him is &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie forl&ae;ten &d;a orsorgnesse &amp; &d;&ae;t dysig hiera sl&ae;w&d;e  &d;yl&ae;s hie wyr&d;en awyrtwalode of &d;ys andwerdan life. 
 Swa swa &d;&ae;t treow &d;e &d;a wyrtruman beo&d; f&ae;rcorfene forseara&d;  swa hie magon ondr&ae;dan &d;&ae;t him weor&d;en &d;a wyrttruman f&ae;rcorfene on &d;ys andweardan life  gif hie for hiera giemeliste nylla&d; beran &d;a bleda godra weorca.
