 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a &d;e willa&d; sellan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie habba&d;  &amp; &d;eah nylla&d; forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;t hie o&d;re menn ne reafigen; 
 Hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen  ongemang &d;&ae;m &d;e hie wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie gifule &d;yncen  &d;&ae;t hie for &d;&ae;m godan hlisan &d;y forcu&d;ran ne weor&d;en  &d;yl&ae;s him gebyrige  swa swa we &ae;r bufan cw&ae;don  &d;onne hie hiera &ae;gen ungesceadwislice &amp; ungemetlice d&ae;len  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne for w&ae;dle weor&d;en on murcunga &amp; on unge&d;ylde  &d;&ae;t hie eft ongiennen gietsian &amp; reafian for hiera w&ae;dle. 
 Hwelc m&ae;g him mare unsl&ae;w&d; becuman &d;onne him becym&d; &d;urh &d;a &ae;lmessan  gif he hie to ungemetlice d&ae;l&d;  &amp; &d;urh &d;&ae;t wyr&d; eft gietsere? 
 Hu  ne bi&d; he &d;onne swelce he s&ae;we good  &amp; him weaxe of &d;&ae;m &ae;lc yfel? 
 Ac hie sint &ae;rest to manianne &d;&ae;t hie cunnen hiora &ae;gen gesceadwislice gehealdan  &amp; si&d;&d;an &d;&ae;t hie o&d;erra monna ne giernen; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e na se &d;orn &d;&ae;re gitsunga ne wyr&d; forsearod on &d;&ae;m helme  gif se wyrttruma ne bi&d; f&ae;rcorfen o&d;&d;e forb&ae;rned &ae;t &d;&ae;m stemne. 
 Swa wyr&d; eac gestiered &d;&ae;m gitsere &d;&ae;s reaflaces  gif he &ae;r &d;&ae;m gedale cann gemetgian hw&ae;t hine anhagige to sellanne  hw&ae;t he healdan scyle  &d;&ae;t he eft &d;&ae;t good &d;&ae;re mildheortnesse ne &d;yrfe gesciendan mid gidsunge &amp; mid reaflace. 
 Si&d;&d;an hie &d;onne &d;&ae;t geleornod h&ae;bben  &d;onne sint hie si&d;&d;an to l&ae;ranne hu hie scilen mildheortlice d&ae;lan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie ofer &d;&ae;t habba&d; &d;e hie hiora gitsunge mid gestillan sculon; 
 For&d;&ae;m  gif hie sua ne do&d;  &d;onne sculon hie eft niedenga gadrian o&d;er ierfe on &d;&ae;s ge wriexle &d;e hie &ae;r for mildheortnesse &amp; for rummodnesse sealdon  swelce hie setten &d;a synne wi&d; &d;&ae;re &ae;lmessan. 
 O&d;er is &d;&ae;t hwa for hreowsunge his synna &ae;lmessan selle  o&d;er is &d;&ae;t he for&d;y syngige &amp; reafige &d;y he tiohchie &d;&ae;t he eft scyle mid &d;y reaflace &ae;lmessan gewyrcean. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t nis nan &ae;lmesse  for&d;&ae;m hio nanne swetne w&ae;s&d;m for&d; ne bring&d;  ac sona on &d;&ae;m wyrtruman abiteria&d; &d;a bleda. 
 For&d;&ae;m Dryhten &d;urh Essaias &d;one witgan forcw&ae;&d; swelce &ae;lmessan  &amp; &d;us spr&ae;c: Ic eom Dryhten: ic lufige ryhte domas  &amp; ic hatige &d;a lac &d;e beo&d; on woh gereafodu. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d;: Arleasra offrung bi&d; awierged  for&d;&ae;m hie beo&d; brohte of unryhtum gestreonum &amp; of mand&ae;dum. 
 &amp; oft bi&d; genumen on &d;earfendum monnum &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie Gode sellen. 
 Ac Dryhten gecy&d;de &d;urh Salomon &d;one snottran hu micel his irsung &ae;fter &d;&ae;re d&ae;de bi&d;  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e me bring lac of earmes monnes &ae;htum on woh gereafodu  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t swelce hwa wille blotan &d;&ae;m f&ae;der to &d;ance &amp; to lacum his &ae;gen bearn  &amp; hit &d;onne cwelle beforan his eagum. 
 Hw&ae;t bi&d; &d;onne unaberendlicre to gesionne &d;onne &d;&ae;s bearnes cwalu beforan &d;&ae;s f&ae;der eagum? 
 Be &d;&ae;m we magon ongietan mid hu micle irre Dryhten ge&d;yldega&d; &d;a &ae;lmessan &d;e him man of reaflace bring&d;  nu he hie tealde gelice &d;&ae;s bearnes cwale beforan &d;&ae;s f&ae;der eagum. 
 Ac &d;a reaferas ge&d;encea&d; swi&d;e oft hu micel hie sella&d;  &amp; sui&d;e seldon hie willa&d; gemunan hu micel hie nima&d;  swelce hie &d;a metsceattas rimen &d;e hie Gode sellen  &amp; &d;a scylda willen forgietan &d;e hie wi&d; hiene geworhton. 
 Ac hie sceoldon gehieran &d;one cwide &d;e awriten is in Ageas bocum &d;&ae;s witgan; 
 He cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e medsceattas gadera&d;  he lege&d; hie on &d;yrelne pohchan. 
 An &d;yrelne pohchan se leg&d; &d;&ae;t he to metsceatte sellan &d;enc&d;  se &d;e wat hw&ae;r he hiene leget  &amp; nat hw&ae;r he hiene forlies&d;. 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e witan willa&d; hw&ae;t hie sella&d;  &amp; nylla&d; wietan mid hwelcum woo hie hit gestriendon o&d;&d;e forworhton; 
 For&d;&ae;m hie do&d; swelce hie hit on &d;yrelne pohchan f&ae;ten  for&d;&ae;m hie gemunan &d;one tohopan &d;e hie to &d;&ae;m gestreonum habba&d;  &amp; forgieta&d; hira demm &d;e him of &d;&ae;m gestreonum cym&d;  o&d;&d;e coom. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisa sint to manianne &d;a ge&d;w&ae;ran  on o&d;re &d;a unge&d;w&ae;ran. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manigenne &d;a gesibsuman  on o&d;re &d;a ungesibsuman. 
 &D;a ungesibsuman sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie gewisslice wieten &d;&ae;t hie na on to &d;&ae;s manegum goodum cr&ae;ftum ne beo&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &ae;fre m&ae;gen g&ae;s&d;lice beon  gif hie &d;urh ungemodnesse agiemeleasia&d; &d;&ae;t hie anmode beon nylla&d; on ryhte &amp; on gode. 
 Hit is awrieten on sancte Paules bocum &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;s g&ae;stes w&ae;s&d;m sie lufu &amp; gefea &amp; ryhtwislicu sibb. 
 Se &d;e &d;onne ne giem&d; hw&ae;&d;er he &d;a sibbe healde  &d;onne forsenc&d; he &d;one w&ae;s&d;m his g&ae;stes. 
 Eft cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: &d;onne betweoxn eow bi&d; yfel anda &amp; geflitu  hu ne beo&d; ge &d;onne fl&ae;sclice? 
 Ond eft he cu&ae;&d;: Secca&d; sibbe &amp; god to eallum mannum; 
 Butan &d;&ae;re ne m&ae;g nan man God gesion. 
 Ond eft he manode  &amp; cu&ae;&d;: Geornlice gebinde ge eow tosomne mid anmodnesse &amp; mid sibbe  &d;&ae;t ge sien gelices modes swa ge sint gelices lichoman sua sua ge ealle sint gela&d;ode to anum tohopan. 
 To &d;&ae;m gebanne &d;&ae;s tohopan nan monn m&ae;g cunnan  butan he &d;ider ierne mid anmodnesse wi&d; his niehstan. 
 &amp; &d;eah wel manige onfo&d; synderlicre giefe  &amp; &d;onne ofermodgiende forl&ae;ta&d; &d;a giefe &d;e mare is  &d;&ae;t is sio anmodnes; 
 Sua sua manige do&d;  gemidlia&d; hiera giefernesse  &amp; atemia&d; hira lichoman &d;&ae;t hie magon bet f&ae;stan &d;onne o&d;re  &amp; &d;onne for &d;&ae;m goodan cr&ae;fte forleosa&d; &d;one &d;e betera bi&d; &d;onne sio forh&ae;fdnes  &d;&ae;t is anmodnes. 
 Ac se &d;e wille ascadan &d;a forh&ae;fdnesse from &d;&ae;re anmodnesse  ge&d;ence se &d;one cwide &d;e se psalmscop cu&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Lofia&d; God mid tympanan &amp; on choro. 
 Se tympano bi&d; geworht of drygum felle  &amp; &d;&ae;t fell hlyt  &d;onne hit mon slieh&d;  &amp; on &d;&ae;m chore beo&d; manige menn gegadrode anes hw&ae;t to singanne anum wordum &amp; anre stefne. 
 Se &d;onne se &d;e his lichoman swenc&d;  &amp; &d;a anmodnesse wi&d; his niehstan forl&ae;t  se here&d; Dryhten mid timpanan  &amp; nyle mid choro. 
 Oft eac  &d;onne hwone mara wisdom upar&ae;&d; &d;onne o&d;re menn  &d;onne wile he hiene ascadan from o&d;erra monna geferr&ae;denne  &amp; sua micle sua he ma wat  &amp; wisra bi&d; &d;onne o&d;re menn  sua he ma dysega&d;  &amp; sui&d;ur wien&d; wi&d; &d;one cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;re anmodnesse. 
 Ac hie sceoldon gehieran &d;one cuide &d;e sio So&d;f&ae;s&d;nes self cw&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Habba&d; sealt on eow  &amp; habba&d; sibbe betweoxn eow. 
 &D;&ae;t sealt he nemde for wisdom  for&d;&ae;m he wolde &d;&ae;t we h&ae;fden &ae;g&d;er ge sibbe ge wisdom  for&d;&ae;m hit ne beo&d; nane cysta ne nan cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;t mon h&ae;bbe wisdom  &amp; nylle wilnian sibbe; 
 For&d;&ae;m sua sua he bet wat  swa he wyrs agylt  &amp; maran demm gedrih&d; him selfum mid &d;&ae;m lote. 
 He m&ae;g hine &d;y l&ae;s beladian &d;&ae;t he n&ae;bbe wite geearno&d; &d;y he meahte mid his wisdome w&ae;rlice &d;a synne forbugan  gif he wolde. 
 Ac him w&ae;s swi&d;e ryhte to gecueden &d;urh Iacobus &d;one apostol  he cw&ae;&d;: Gif ge h&ae;bben yfelne andan on eow &amp; teonan &amp; geflitu on eowrum mode  ne gilpe ge no  ne ne f&ae;gnia&d; &d;&ae;s  &amp; ne flita&d; mid eowrum leasungum wi&d; &d;&ae;m so&d;e; 
 For&d;&ae;m se wisdom nis ufan cumen of hefenum  ac he is eor&d;lic &amp; wildiorlic &amp; eac diofullic. 
 Ac se se &d;e of Gode cym&d;  he bi&d; godes willan &amp; gesibsum. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t he sie cl&ae;nes willan &amp; goodes  &d;&ae;t he cl&ae;nlice &amp; ryhtwislice ongiete &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he ongiete. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t he gesibsum sie  &d;&ae;t he hiene nanwuht ne ahebbe ofer his gelican  ne from hiera geferr&ae;denne ne &d;iede. 
 &D;&ae;m ungesibsuman is to cy&d;anne &d;&ae;t hie wieten &d;&ae;tte swa lange sua hie beo&d; from &d;&ae;re lufe a&d;ied hiera niehstena  &amp; him ungemode beo&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie nanwuht godes ne magon &d;a hwile Gode bringan to &d;ances. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten on Cristesbocum: Gif &d;u wille &d;in lac bringan to &d;&ae;m wiofude  &amp; &d;u &d;onne ryhte of&d;ence hw&ae;thwugu &d;&ae;s &d;e &d;in niehsta &d;e wi&d;erweardes gedon h&ae;bbe  forl&ae;t &d;onne an &d;in lac beforan &d;&ae;m weofude  &amp; fer &ae;rest &ae;fter him; 
 L&ae;t inc geseman &ae;r &d;u &d;in lac bringe; 
 Brieng si&d;&d;an &d;in lac. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hwa fare mid his mode &ae;fter his niehstan  &amp; him unne &d;&ae;t he to ryhte gecierre. 
 Of &d;issum bebode we magon ge&d;encean hu unaberendlic gylt sio towesnes bi&d;  &d;onne &d;a lac for&d;&ae;m beo&d; forsacene. 
 Nu man &ae;lc yfel m&ae;g mid goode adilegian  is &d;&ae;t &d;onne for micel scyld &d;&ae;t gede&d; &d;&ae;tte nan good ne bi&d; andfenge  buton mon &ae;r &d;&ae;t yfel forl&ae;te. 
 Ac &d;a ungesibsuman sint to manienne  gif hie nyllen hiera lichoman earan ontynan to gehieranne &d;a godcundan lare  &d;&ae;t hie ontynen hiera modes eagan  &amp; giemen &d;issa eor&d;licna gesceafta  hu &d;a fuglas  &d;e him gelice beo&d;  &amp; anes cynnes beo&d;  hu gesibsumlice hie fara&d;  &amp; hu seldon hie willa&d; forl&ae;tan hiera geferr&ae;denne  &amp; eac &d;a dumban nietenu  hu hie hie gadria&d; heapm&ae;lum  &amp; hie &ae;tsomne feda&d;. 
 Nu we magon gecnawan on &d;ara ungesceadwisra nietena gesibsumnesse hu micel yfel sio gesceadwislice gecynd &d;urh &d;a ungesibsumnesse gefreme&d;  &d;onne he on gesceadwislicum inge&d;once forlies&d; &d;&ae;t &d;a dumban nietenu gehealden habba&d; on hiera gecynde. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a gesibbsuman  &d;onne hie lufiga&d; &d;a sibbe &d;e hie her habba&d; sui&d;ur &d;onne hit &d;earf sie  &amp; ne wilnia&d; na &d;&ae;t hie to &d;&ae;re ecean sibbe becumen. 
 Ac sio stillnes &d;e hie &d;&ae;r wilnia&d; oft swi&d;e hefelice dere&d; hira inge&d;once  for&d;&ae;m swa him &d;ios stillnes &amp; &d;ios ie&d;nes ma lica&d;  sua him l&ae;s lica&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie to gela&d;ode sindon  &amp; sua hienne swi&d;ur lys&d; &d;isses andweardan  swa he l&ae;s sec&d; ymb &d;&ae;t ece. 
 Be &d;ysum ilcan cw&ae;&d; Crist &d;urh hiene selfne  &d;a &d;a he &d;as eor&d;lican sibbe toscead &amp; &d;a hefonlican  &amp; his apostolas spon of &d;issum andweardan to &d;&ae;m ecan  he cu&ae;&d;: Mine sibbe ic eow selle  &amp; mine sibbe ic l&ae;te to eow. 
 Swelce he cw&ae;de: Ic eow onl&ae;ne &d;as gewitendan  &amp; ic eow geselle &d;a &d;urhwiniendan. 
 Gif &d;onne &d;&ae;s monnes mod &amp; his lufu bi&d; behleapen eallunga on &d;a l&ae;nan sibbe  &d;onn ne m&ae;g he n&ae;bre becuman to &d;&ae;re &d;e him geseald is. 
 Ac swa is &d;ios andwearde sib to habbanne &d;&ae;t we hie sculon lufian  &amp; &d;eah oferhyggean  &d;yl&ae;s &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s &d;e hie lufa&d; on synne befealle  gif he hie to ungemetlice lufa&d;. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a gesibsuman &d;&ae;t hie to ungemetlice &d;&ae;re sibbe ne wilnigen  &d;yl&ae;s hie for &d;&ae;re wilnunga &d;isse eor&d;lican sibbe forl&ae;ten unt&ae;lde o&d;erra monna yfele un&d;eawas  &amp; hiene &d;onne selfne swa a&d;iede from &d;&ae;re sibbe his Scippendes mid &d;&ae;re ge&d;afunga &d;&ae;s unryhtes; 
 &D;yl&ae;s  &d;onne he him ondr&ae;dt &d;a towesnesse utane  he sie innan asliten from &d;&ae;m ge&d;oftscipe &d;&ae;s incundan Deman. 
 Hw&ae;t is elles &d;ios gewitendlice sibb  buton swelce hit sie sum sw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;re eccean sibbe? 
 Hw&ae;t m&ae;g bion dyslicre &d;onne hwa lufige hwelcre wuhte spor on &d;&ae;m duste  &amp; ne lufige &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t spor worhte? 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Dauid  &d;a he hine eallunga ge&d;iedde to &d;&ae;m ge&d;oftscipe &d;&ae;re incundan sibbe  he cy&d;de &d;&ae;t he nolde habban nane gemodsumnesse wi&d; &d;a yfelan  &d;a he cu&ae;&d;: Hu ne hatige ic &d;a ealle  Dryhten  &d;a &d;e &d;e hatiga&d;? 
 &amp; for &d;inum feondum ic aswand on minum mode  &amp; mid fulryhte hete ic hie hatode  for&d;&ae;m hie w&ae;ron eac mine find? 
 Swa mon &d;onne sceal fullfremedlice Godes fiend hatigean  &d;&ae;tte mon lufige &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie beo&d;  &amp; hatige &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie do&d;. 
 He sceal weor&d;an his life to nytte mid &d;y &d;&ae;t he n&ae;te his un&d;eawas. 
 Ac hu wene we hu micel scyld &d;&ae;t sie &d;&ae;t monn a&d;reote &d;&ae;re n&ae;tinge yfelra monna  &amp; nime sume sibbe wi&d; &d;a wierrestan  nu se witga &d;&ae;t brohte Gode to lacum &amp; to offrunga &d;&ae;t he &d;ara yfelena feondscipe ongean hine selfne aweahte for Gode? 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s &d;&ae;te Leuis kynn gefengon hiera sweord  &amp; eodon ut &d;urh &d;one here  sleande &d;a scyldgan; 
 &amp; for&d;&ae;m hit is awriten &d;&ae;t hiera honda w&ae;ren gehalgode Gode  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie ne sparodan &d;a synfullan  ac slogon. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s eac &d;&ae;tte Fines forseah his neahgebura freondscipe  &d;a he ofslog his agene geferan  &d;a he hine forl&ae;g wi&d; &d;a Madianiten  &amp; &d;a forlegisse he mid ofslog  &amp; swa mid his ierre he gestilde Godes ierre. 
 &amp; eft cw&ae;&d; Crist &d;urh hine selfne: Ne wene ge no &d;&ae;t ic to &d;&ae;m come on eor&d;an &d;&ae;t ic sibbe sende on eor&d;an  ac sweord. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne we us unw&ae;rlice ge&d;ieda&d; to yfelra monna freondscipe  &d;onne gebinde we us to hiera scyldum. 
 Be &d;ys ilcan w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte Gesapha&d;  se &d;e &ae;r on eallum d&ae;dum his lifes w&ae;s to herigenne  fullneah mid eall forwear&d; for Achabes freondscipe. 
 He w&ae;s geleahtrad from Gode  &d;urh &d;one witgan him w&ae;s to gecweden: &d;u fultemodes &d;&ae;m arleasum  &amp; &d;u gemengdest &d;inne freondscipe wi&d; &d;one &d;e hatode God  &amp; mid &d;&ae;m &d;u geearnode Godes irre  &d;&ae;r &d;a godan weorc &ae;r n&ae;ren on &d;e mette; 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;s &d;&ae;t &d;u adydes &d;a bearwas of Iudea londe. 
 Be &d;&ae;m we magon gehieran &d;&ae;tte sua micle sua we us swi&d;ur ge&d;ieda&d; &amp; gemodsumia&d; to &d;&ae;ra yfelena freondscipe  &d;&ae;tte we swa micle fier beo&d; &d;&ae;m hiehstan ryhte a&d;iedde. 
 Eac sint to monigenne &d;a gesibsuman &d;&ae;t hie him ne ondr&ae;den &d;&ae;t hie &d;as l&ae;nan sibbe ongean hie selfe gedrefen mid &d;&ae;re &d;reaunga  &d;onne hit tocym&d; &d;&ae;t hie hit sprecan sculon. 
 Ond eft hie sint to manianne &d;&ae;t hie &d;eah &d;a sibbe anwealge oninnan him gehealden  &d;a &d;e hie utane mid &d;&ae;re &d;rafunga gedrefa&d;. 
 &AE;g&d;er &d;ara Dauid s&ae;gde &d;&ae;t he swi&d;e w&ae;rlice beheolde  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Ic lufode &d;a &d;e sibbe hatodon  &amp; &d;onne ic him cidde  &d;onne oncu&d;on hie me butan scylde. 
 Hie oncu&d;on hiene for &d;&ae;re cease  &amp; he w&ae;s &d;eah hiora freond; 
 Ne a&d;reat hine no &d;&ae;t he &d;a dysegan ne t&ae;lde  &amp; &d;eah &d;e hie hine t&ae;ldon  he hie lufode. 
 Be &d;ys ilcan cw&ae;&d; eft Paulus: Ic wolde  gif hit swa beon meahte  &d;&ae;t ge wi&d; &ae;lcne monn h&ae;fden sibbe eowres gewealdes. 
 For&d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d;: Gif hit swa beon meahte  &amp; eac he cw&ae;&d;: Iowres gewealdes  for&d;&ae;m he wisse &d;&ae;t hit bi&d; swi&d;e unie&d;e &ae;g&d;er to donne  ge wi&d; &d;one to cidanne &d;e yfel de&d;  ge eac sibbe wi&d; to habbenne. 
 Ac us is swi&d;e micel &d;earf  &d;eah &d;eos hwilendlice sibb for ure cease gedrefed weor&d;e on &d;&ae;ra yfelena monna mode  &d;&ae;t hie &d;eah on ussum eallunga gehealden sie. 
 For&d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d; bi &d;&ae;re sibbe: Iowres gewealdes  for&d;&ae;m sio sib mid ryhte beon sceal &ae;g&d;er ge on &d;&ae;s cidendan monnes mode ge on &d;&ae;s ge&d;afiendan. 
 Gif hio &d;onne of o&d;res gewite  on &d;&ae;s o&d;res hio &d;urhwunige. 
 Be &d;&ae;m se ilca Paulus on o&d;re stowe monode his gingran  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Swa hwa swa urum wordum &amp; gewritum hieran nylle  do hit mon us to witanne  &amp; nabbe ge nanne gemanan wi&d; hine  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte hine gesceamige. 
 &amp; eft &ae;fter &d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d;: Ne scule ge wi&d; hine geb&ae;ran swa swa wi&d; feond  ac ge him sculon cidan swa swa bre&d;er. 
 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Forl&ae;ta&d; &d;a uterran sibbe  &amp; habba&d; &d;a innerran f&ae;ste  &d;&ae;tte eower unsibb geea&d;mede &d;&ae;s synnigan mod  swa &d;eah &d;&ae;t sio sib of eowre heortan ne gewite  &d;&ae;ah hiere mon ne recce. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a wrohtgeornan  on o&d;re &d;a gesibsuman. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to monigenne &d;a &d;e wrohte sawa&d;  on o&d;re &d;a gesibsuman. 
 &D;a wrohtgeornan sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen hw&ae;s folgeras hie sindon. 
 Be &d;&ae;m aworpnan engle is awriten on &d;&ae;m godspelle &d;&ae;t he sewe &d;&ae;t weod on &d;a godan &ae;ceras. 
 For&d;y w&ae;s bi him gecweden: Sum mon &d;is dyde &d;e ure feond w&ae;s. 
 Be &d;&ae;s ilcan feondes limum is &d;us gecweden &d;urh Salomon: Aworpen man bi&d; a unnyt  &amp; g&ae;&d; mid wo mu&d;e  &amp; bicne&d; mid &d;&ae;m eagum  &amp; trit mid &d;&ae;m fet  &amp; spric&d; mid &d;&ae;m fingre  &amp; on wore heortan bi&d; yfel donde  &amp; on &ae;lce tid sawe&d; wrohte. 
 Her we magon gehieran  &d;a he be &d;&ae;m wrohtgeornan secgean wolde  &d;&ae;t he hine nemde se aworpna; 
 For&d;on  gif he &ae;r on &d;&ae;s ofermodan engles wisan innan his ge&d;ance of Godes gesieh&d;e ne afeolle  &d;onne ne become he no utane to &d;&ae;m s&ae;de &d;&ae;re wrohte. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is ryhtlice awriten &d;&ae;t he bicne mid &d;&ae;m eagum  &amp; sprece mid &d;&ae;m fingrum  &amp; trit mid &d;&ae;m fet; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e innor bi&d; se hierde  &d;&ae;t is se willa  se hielt &d;a leomu utan. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne mon &d;a f&ae;str&ae;dnesse his modes innan forlist  &d;onne bi&d; he hwilum swi&d;e ungest&ae;&d;&d;iglice astyred utane on his limum  &amp; geky&d;&d; on &d;&ae;re styringe &d;ara telgena utane &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r ne bi&d; nan f&ae;stnung on &d;&ae;m wyrtruman innan. 
 Ac gehiren &d;a wrohtsaweras hw&ae;t awriten is on &d;&ae;m godspelle  hit is awriten: Eadige beo&d; &d;a gesibsuman  for&d;on hie beo&d; Godes bearn genemde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m worde we magon ge&d;encean  nu &d;a sint Godes bearn genemned &d;e sibbe wyrca&d;  &d;&ae;tte &d;a sindon butan tweon diofles bearn  &d;e hie toweorpan willa&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;lc &d;ara &d;e hine mid unryhte ascadan wille from &d;&ae;re ge&d;w&ae;rnesse  he wile forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;re lufan grennisse  &amp; forsearian on &d;&ae;re unge&d;w&ae;rnesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;eah he hwelcne w&ae;stm for&d;brenge godes weorces  gif he ne bi&d; of godum willan &amp; of untwiefaldre lufan ongunnen  ne bi&d; he nawuht. 
 Ge&d;encen be &d;issum &d;a wrohtsaweras hu monigfaldlice hie gesyngia&d;  &d;onne hie &d;&ae;t an yfel &d;urhtio&d;  &amp; mid &d;&ae;m anum yfele atera&d; of &d;&ae;re menniscan heortan ealle &d;a godan cr&ae;ftas. 
 Mid &d;am anum yfele hie gefremma&d; unrim o&d;erra yfela  for&d;am &d;a &d;e &d;a worhte sawa&d;  hie adw&ae;sca&d; &d;a sibbe  &d;e modor is ealra godra cr&ae;fta. 
 For&d;on&d;e nan cr&ae;ft nis Gode deorwyr&d;ra &d;onne sio lufu  ne eft &d;&ae;m deofle nan cr&ae;ft leoft&ae;lra &d;onne hie mon slite. 
 Swa hwa &d;onne swa &d;a wrohte bi&d; sawende  &amp; mid &d;y &d;a sibbe ofslih&d; on his geferan  he bi&d; hiewcu&d;lice &d;eow &d;&ae;m Godes feonde  &d;e simle wi&d;britt &d;&ae;m untruman mode &d;&ae;re sibbe &d;e he self forlet  &amp; hine mid &d;&ae;m forworhte  o&d; he ofdune afeoll  &amp; nu giet wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he us &d;one weg fordikige  &d;&ae;t we ne m&ae;gen astigan on &d;one weg &amp; on &d;a are &d;e he of afeoll. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e &d;a sibbe sawa&d;  &d;&ae;t hie swa micel weorc to recceleaslice &amp; to unw&ae;rlice ne don  &amp; huru &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r hie nyton hw&ae;&d;er sio sibb betre betwux gef&ae;stnod bi&d;  &d;e ne bi&d;  for&d;&ae;m swa swi&d;e swa hit dere&d; &d;&ae;tte &ae;nig wana sie &d;&ae;re sibbe betwux &d;&ae;m goodum  swa swi&d;e hit eac dere&d; &d;&ae;t hio ne sie gewanod betwux &d;&ae;m yfelum. 
 For&d;&ae;m  gif &d;a &d;weoran &amp; &d;a unryhtwisan hiera yfel mid sibbe gef&ae;stniga&d;  &amp; tosomne gemenga&d;  &d;onne bi&d; geiced hiera m&ae;gen  &amp; hiora yfelum weorcum gefultumod  for&d;on swa micle swa hie gemodsumeran bio&d; betwux him  swa hie beo&d; bealdran &d;a godan to swenceanne. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte sio godcunde stemn cw&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m eadgan Iobe ymb &d;a bodan &d;&ae;s idlan f&ae;tes  &d;&ae;t is se awirgda Antexrist  hio cw&ae;&d;: His fl&ae;sces lima clifa&d; &ae;lc on o&d;rum. 
 &amp; eft hio dyde sciella to bisene his heor&d;cneohtum  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: &ae;lces fisces sciell bi&d; to o&d;erre gefeged  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r ne m&ae;g nan &ae;&d;m ut betwuxn. 
 Swa eac &d;a his folgeras  swa hie unwi&d;erweardran &amp; gemodran beo&d;  swa hie swi&d;ur hleca&d; tosomne  &amp; eac f&ae;stor tosomne beo&d; gefegde to godra monna hien&d;e. 
 Swa eac se se &d;e &d;a unryhtwisan tosomne sibba&d;  he sele&d; &d;&ae;re unryhtwisnesse fultom &amp; m&ae;gen  for&d;&ae;m hie magon &d;a godan swa micle swi&d;ur geswencean swa hie hiora anmodlicor ehta&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; se &ae;&d;ela lareow sanctus Paulus  &d;a he geseah &d;&ae;t folc Phariseo &amp; Saducia anmodlice his ehtan  he tiolode hie betwux him to toscadanne  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t do ge  bro&d;ur  do&d; esnlice. 
 Hu  ne eom ic eower gefera  &amp; eom Fariscisc swa same swa ge? 
 Ond for&d;&ae;m min monn eft &d;e ic bodige ymb &d;one tohopan deadra monna &ae;restes. 
 For&d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d; &d;a word  for&d;&ae;m &d;a Saducie antsacodon &d;&ae;re &ae;riste &ae;fter dea&d;e  &amp; &d;a Farisseos geliefdon &d;&ae;re &ae;riste  swa swa &d;a halgan gewritu bodia&d;. 
 Swa he tosced &d;ara ehtera anmodnesse &d;e hine &ae;r woldon fordon  &amp; Paulus com gesund &d;onon. 
 Eac sint to manianne &d;a &d;e on &d;am beo&d; abisgode &d;&ae;t hie sibbe tiliga&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &ae;rest tilgen to ky&d;anne &d;&ae;m ungesceadwisum modum hu sio lufu beon scyle &d;&ae;re inweardlican sibbe  &d;yl&ae;s him &ae;fter firste sio uterre sib derige; 
 For&d;on  &d;onne &d;onne hie ge&d;enca&d; &d;a ryhtan lufe  &d;&ae;t hie eac ge&d;encen &d;&ae;t hie ne weor&d;en beswicene mid &d;&ae;re uterran lufe  &amp; &d;onne hie ongita&d; &d;a godcundan sibbe  &d;&ae;tte sio eor&d;lice sib hi ne geteo to wirsan. 
 Ond eft &d;onne sume yfele menn swa gerade beo&d; &d;&ae;t hie ne magon godum monnum derian  &d;eah hie willen  &d;onne is betere &d;eah &d;&ae;t mon eor&d;lice sibbe betwux &d;&ae;m f&ae;stnige  o&d;&d;&ae;t hie m&ae;gen ongietan &d;a uplican sibbe; 
 &D;&ae;tte hie &d;urh &d;a menniscan sibbe m&ae;gen astigan to &d;&ae;re godcundan sibbe  &d;eah hio him &d;onne giet feorr sie  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t yfel hiera unryhtwisnesse hie h&ae;f&d; &d;onne giet ahierde  &d;&ae;tte hie &d;onne gemonn&d;w&ae;rige sio lufu &amp; sio geferr&ae;den hiora niehstena  &amp; hie to beteran gebrenge. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e &d;a halgan &ae; ryhtlice ongietan ne cunnon; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hie ryhtlice ongieta&d;  &amp; &d;eah for ea&d;modnesse swugia&d; &d;&ae;t hi hi ne bodigea&d;. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;a halgan &ae; ryhtlice ongietan ne cunnon; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;e hie ryhtlice ongietan cunnon  &amp; &d;eah for ea&d;modnesse swigia&d; &d;&ae;t hie hie ne bodia&d;. 
 &D;a sint to maniene &d;e &d;a &ae; ryhtlice ne ongieta&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte hie &d;one halwendan drync &d;&ae;s &ae;&d;elan wines ne gehwyrfen him selfum to attre  &amp; isen &d;&ae;t hie menn mid lacnian sculdon  &d;&ae;t hie mid &d;&ae;m hie selfe to feore ne gewundigen  &d;yl&ae;s hie mid &d;y tole &d;&ae;t hale lic gewierden &d;e hie sceoldon mid &d;&ae;t unhale aweg aceorfan. 
 Eac hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen &d;&ae;t &d;a halgan gewritu sint us to leohtfatum gesald  &d;&ae;t we m&ae;gen geseon hw&ae;t we don scylen on &d;isse niht  &d;&ae;t is &d;is andwearde lif  swa swa &d;&ae;t leohtf&ae;t lieht on nieht urum eagum  &d;&ae;tte &d;a gewritu on d&ae;g liehten urum mode. 
 Ac &d;onne hwa ne cann &d;a ryhtlice ongietan  &d;onne bi&d; him &d;&ae;t leoht a&d;iestrod. 
 Ne gehwyrfde hine n&ae;fre &d;&ae;t unryhtwise inge&d;onc to &d;&ae;m won andgiete  gif he &ae;r n&ae;re on ofermettum a&d;unden. 
 Ac &d;onne hie wena&d; &d;&ae;t hie wisran sien selfe &d;onne o&d;re  &d;onne forhyggea&d; hie &d;&ae;t hie folgien o&d;rum monnum &ae;fter bettran andgiete  &amp; wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie gegitsien &amp; gelicetten &ae;t &d;&ae;m ungetydum folce wisdomes naman. 
 Higia&d; &d;onne ealle m&ae;gene &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t gedwellen &d;&ae;t o&d;re menn ryhtlice &amp; gesceadwislice ongieten habba&d;  &amp; hira agen unryht willa&d; mid &d;y getrymman. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s swi&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh Amos &d;one witgan  he cw&ae;&d;: Hie sindon &d;a Galatiscan wif &d;e bearneacene w&ae;ron  &amp; woldon mid &d;y geryman hira landgem&ae;ru. 
 &D;&ae;t folc w&ae;s gehaten Gala&d; on Ebrisc  &d;&ae;t is on Englisc gewitnesse heap  for&d;&ae;m eal sio gesomnung &d;&ae;re halgan ciricean &d;urh ondetnesse hielt &d;a gewitnesse &d;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse. 
 &D;y is swi&d;e ryhte getacnod &d;urh Galates naman sio halige gesomnung  for&d;&ae;m&d;e ealle &d;a geleaffullan bodia&d; be Gode &d;&ae;t so&d; is. 
 &D;onne getacnia&d; &d;a geeacniendan wif &d;a saule &d;e &d;a gebodu angieta&d;  &amp; hie mid godcundlicre lufan underfo&d;: gif &d;&ae;t underfangne andgit to ryhtre tide bi&d; for&d;broht  &d;onne bi&d; hit mid &d;y &d;urhtogenan weorce gedon  swelce hit sie geboren. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his mearce br&ae;de  &d;&ae;t mon his hlisan &amp; his naman m&ae;rsige. 
 Ac &d;onne mon sni&d; &d;a bearneacnan wif on Gala&d; hira mearce mid to rymanne  &d;onne &d;a gedwolmenn mid wore lare ofslea&d; &d;&ae;t mod geleaffullra monna  &d;onne &d;onne hit fur&d;um ryht andgiet underfangen h&ae;f&d;  &amp; him hw&ae;thwugu sio so&d;f&ae;s&d;nes on geeacnod bi&d;  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e hit fullboren sie  &amp; willa&d; mid &d;y gedon &d;&ae;t hie mon hlige wisdomes  mid &d;y &d;e hie ofsni&d;en mid &d;y seaxe hefiglices gedwolan &d;a unborenan bearn  &d;e &d;onne fur&d;um beo&d; mid wordum geeacnode on geleaffullra mode; 
 Ac hie wilnia&d; mid &d;y &d;&ae;t hie mon herige  &amp; cwe&d;e &d;&ae;t hie sin wise lareowas. 
 Ac gif we wilnigen &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;s wos geswicen  &d;onne sculon we hie ealra &d;inga &ae;rest &amp; geornost l&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hie ne wilnigen leasgielpes  for&d;&ae;m  gif se wyrttruma &d;&ae;re upahafenisse &ae;rest wyr&d; forcorfen  &d;onne bi&d; hit sona swutol &d;&ae;t &d;a twigu forsearia&d; &d;&ae;re unryhtan lare. 
 Eac hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;tte hie &d;urh hiera gedwolan &amp; &d;urh hiera unge&d;w&ae;rnesse &d;a Godes &ae;  &d;e us forbiet diofulum to offrianne  &d;&ae;t hie &d;a ilcan &ae; ne gehwierfen to diofulgielde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m Dryhten siofigende cw&ae;&d; &d;urh Ossei &d;one witgan  he cw&ae;&d;: Ic him sealde hw&ae;te &amp; win &amp; oele &amp; gold &amp; siolfor; 
 Ic him sealde genog  &amp; &d;&ae;t hie worhton to diofulgieldum Bale hiera gode. 
 Ac &d;onne we underfo&d; &d;one hw&ae;te &ae;t Gode  &d;onne we ongieta&d; inweardlice &d;a &ae;  &amp; onwreo&d; &d;a dieglan cwidas  swelce we nimen &d;one cl&ae;nan hw&ae;te  &amp; weorpen &d;&ae;t ceaf onweg. 
 &amp; &d;onne us sel&d; God his win  &d;onne he us oferdrenc&d; mid &d;&ae;re lare dioplices andgites. 
 &amp; &d;onne he us sel&d; his ele  &d;onne he us his bebodu openlicor gecy&d;  &amp; mid &d;&ae;m ure lif li&d;elice &amp; get&ae;slice fere&d;. 
 &amp; &d;onne he us sele&d; micel siolfor  &d;onne he us sel&d; micle getyngnesse &amp; wlitige spr&ae;ce ymb so&d;f&ae;s&d;nesse to cy&d;anne. 
 &D;onne he us gewelega&d; mid golde  &d;onne he ure heortan onlieht &amp; gebierht mid &d;&ae;m sciman healices angietes. 
 &D;is is eall ryhtwisra monna offrung Gode  ac hit brienga&d; eal &d;a gedwolmen Bale  mid &d;&ae;m&d;e hie hiora hieremonna mod gedwella&d;  &amp; eall hiera andgit forhwirfa&d; mid hiera wore lare. 
 &D;onne hie do&d; &d;one hw&ae;te &amp; &d;&ae;t win &amp; &d;one ele &amp; &d;&ae;t siolfor to diofulgieldum  &d;onne hie &d;a gesibsumnesse &amp; gesceadwisnesse to gedwolan &amp; to unge&d;w&ae;rnesse gehwyrfa&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen  &d;onne hie mid forhwirfede mode &d;&ae;re sibbe bebod gehwierfa&d; to unge&d;w&ae;rnesse  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne hie selfe ofslea&d; from lifes wordum mid ryhtum Godes dome. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;a word &d;&ae;re halgan &ae; ryhtlice ongietan cunnon  &amp; hie swa&d;eah ea&d;modlice nylla&d; l&ae;ran  hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie hie selfe ongieten on &d;&ae;m halgum gewritum  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e hie o&d;re l&ae;ren  &d;yl&ae;s hie eahtigen o&d;erra monna d&ae;da  &amp; forgieten hie selfe  &amp; &d;onne hie eal &d;a halgan gewritu ryhtlice ongiten h&ae;bben  &d;&ae;t hie ne forgiten hw&ae;t bi &d;&ae;m upah&ae;fenum gecweden is  hit is gecweden: Dysig bi&d; se l&ae;ce &amp; untyd &d;e wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he o&d;erne mon gelacnige  &amp; nat &d;&ae;t he self bi&d; gewundad. 
 For&d;&ae;m sint to monigenne &d;a &d;e ea&d;modlice nylla&d; l&ae;ran Godes word  &d;&ae;tte &d;onne &d;onne hie &d;a untruman lacnian willa&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie &ae;r gesceawigen &d;&ae;t ater hiera agenra mettrymnessa on him selfum  &d;yl&ae;s hie selfe acwelan  &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r hie &d;a o&d;re lacnia&d;. 
 Ac hie man sceal manian &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte hie selfe ne geun&d;w&ae;rigen &d;&ae;m wordum &d;e hie l&ae;ra&d; mid &d;y &d;&ae;t hie o&d;er don  o&d;er hie l&ae;ra&d;. 
 Ac gehieren hw&ae;t awriten is on &d;&ae;m &ae;rendgewrite sancte Petres  hit is awriten: Swa hwa swa sprece  sprece he Godes worde  swelce &d;a word no his ne sien  ac Godes. 
 Gif hit &d;onne Godes word bio&d;  n&ae;s his  forhwy sceal hwa &d;onne bion ah&ae;fen on &d;&ae;m  swelce hit his agenu word sien? 
 Ac hie scoldon gehieran &d;one cuide &d;e sanctus Paulus cw&ae;&d; to Corintheum  he cw&ae;&d;: Sua sua of Gode beforan Gode we spreca&d; on Criste. 
 Se &d;onne spric&d; of Gode beforan Gode  se &d;e ongiet &d;&ae;t he &d;a word &d;&ae;re lare from Gode onfeng  &amp; &d;urh &d;a wilna&d; Gode to liciganne  nalles mannum. 
 Hie sculon gehieran &d;one cuide &d;e awriten is on Salomonnes bocum  hit is awriten &d;&ae;tte God anscunige &ae;lcne ofermodne man. 
 Se &d;onne &d;e mid Godes wordum his agenne gielp sec&d;  he wile reafian &d;one &d;e hie him sealde his anwaldes; 
 &amp; ne ondr&ae;t him no  &d;eah &d;e he do God behindan hine  &d;eah &d;e him God geafe &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;r mon here&d;. 
 Eac hie sculon gehieran hw&ae;t to &d;&ae;m lareowum gecweden is &d;urh Salomon  hit is gecweden: Drinc &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter of &d;inum agenum mere  &amp; &d;&ae;tte of &d;inum agnum pytte aflowe  &amp; l&ae;t &d;ine willas iernan wide  &amp; tod&ae;l hie  l&ae;d hie gind &d;in lond  &amp; gegier &d;&ae;t hie iernen bi herestr&ae;tum  &amp; hafa hie &d;eah &d;e anum  &d;yl&ae;s el&d;iodige hie d&ae;len wi&d; &d;e. 
 &D;onne drinc&d; se lareow &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter of his agnum mere  &d;onne he gehwirf&d; &ae;res&d; to his agnum inge&d;once to hladanne &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter  &d;&ae;t is to wyrceanne &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he l&ae;r&d;. 
 &D;onne he drinc&d; of &d;&ae;m wielme his agnes pyttes  &d;onne he bi&d; self ge&d;w&ae;ned &amp; wel gedrenced mid his agnum wordum. 
 Swi&d;e wel w&ae;s &d;ios spr&ae;c mid &d;y geieced &d;e Salomon cw&ae;&d;: L&ae;t for&d; &d;ine willas  &amp; tod&ae;l &d;in w&ae;tru &ae;fter herestr&ae;tum. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte se lareow &ae;rest sceal self drincan of &d;&ae;m wille his agenre lare  &amp; si&d;&d;an geotan mid his lare &d;&ae;t ilce w&ae;ter on his hieremonna mod. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his w&ae;tru utl&ae;te  &d;&ae;t se lareow mid &d;y cr&ae;fte his lareowdomes utane on o&d;re menn giote  o&d;&d;&ae;t hie innan gel&ae;rede weor&d;en. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his w&ae;tru tod&ae;le &ae;fter cyninga herestr&ae;tum  &d;&ae;t mon &d;a godcundan spr&ae;ce &d;&ae;re menigo &d;&ae;s folces tod&ae;le gemetlice &ae;lcum be his andefne. 
 Ac for&d;on&d;e oft sio wilnung &d;&ae;s idlan gielpes gegrip&d; &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;s lareowes  &d;onne he ongiet &d;&ae;t &d;a Godes word manegum menn licia&d; &d;e &d;urh his mu&d; beo&d; gesprecen  for&d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecweden &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t we &ae;r s&ae;don &d;urh Salomon &d;one snotran  he cw&ae;&d;: &d;eah &d;u &d;in w&ae;tru tod&ae;le  hafa hie &d;eah &d;e self  &amp; ne sele el&d;iodigum hira nawuht. 
 He m&ae;nde &d;a awiergedan g&ae;stas. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m spr&ae;c Dauid swi&d;e cu&d;lice on psalmum  swa he hit oft acunnad h&ae;fde  he cw&ae;&d;: El&d;iodige arison wi&d; me  &amp; wunnon wi&d; me  &amp; swi&d;e stronge w&ae;ron &d;a &d;e min ehton. 
 We cw&ae;don &ae;r &d;&ae;t Salomon cw&ae;de &d;&ae;t mon sceolde his w&ae;tru tod&ae;lan  &amp; &d;eah him self eall habban. 
 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Eow is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t ge swa &ae;tfeolen ut &d;&ae;re lare  swa swa ge eow innan ne ge&d;ieden to &d;&ae;m awiergedum g&ae;stum &d;urh upahafenesse eowres modes  &d;yl&ae;s ge &d;urh &d;a &d;enunga &d;ara Godes worda to eow forl&ae;ten eowre fiend  &d;yl&ae;s eow &d;onon awuht gem&ae;nes weor&d;e. 
 Ac &d;onne we do&d; &ae;g&d;er  ge we &d;a w&ae;tru tod&ae;la&d; &ae;fter kyninga herestr&ae;tum  ge eac us selfe habba&d;  &d;onne &d;onne we swi&d;e wide uttogeota&d; &d;a lare  &amp; sua&d;eah &d;urh &d;a ne wilnia&d; woruldgielpes. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisa sint to manianne &d;a &d;e medomlice cunnon l&ae;ran  &amp; &d;eah for miclum ege &amp; for micelre ea&d;modnesse forwandia&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;onne giet to &d;&ae;m gewintrede ne beo&d; ne ge&d;iegene  &amp; &d;eah for hr&ae;dhydignesse bio&d; to gegripene. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to maniane &d;a &d;e medomlice l&ae;ran magon  &amp; &d;eah for micelre ea&d;modnesse him ondr&ae;da&d;; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;a &d;e unmedome bio&d; to &d;&ae;re lare o&d;&d;e for giogu&d;e o&d;&d;e for unwisdome  &amp; &d;eah for hira fortruwodnesse &amp; for hira hr&ae;dwilnesse beo&d; to gescofene. 
 &D;a &d;onne sint to manigenne &d;e nyttweor&d;lice l&ae;ran meahton  &amp; &d;eah for ungemetlicere ea&d;modnesse hit onscunia&d;  hi sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie be &d;&ae;m l&ae;ssan &d;ingum ongieten hu sui&d;e hie gesyngia&d; on &d;&ae;m maran. 
 Hw&ae;t  hie witon  gif hiera niehstan friend weor&d;a&d; w&ae;dlan  &amp; hie feoh habba&d;  &amp; his &d;onne him oftio&d;  &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; &d;onne fultemend to hiera w&ae;dle. 
 Hwy ne magon hie &d;onne ge&d;encean  gif hie on &d;&ae;m gesyngia&d;  hu micle swi&d;ur hie gesyngia&d;  &d;onne hie oftio&d; &d;&ae;re lare &d;&ae;m synfullum bro&d;rum  swelce hie gehyden lifes l&ae;cedom  &amp; his forwirnen &d;&ae;m cwelendum monnum? 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Salomon: Hu nytt bi&d; se forholena cr&ae;ft o&d;&d;e &d;&ae;t forhydde gold? 
 O&d;&d;e gif hwelc folc bi&d; mid hungre geswenced  &amp; hwa his hw&ae;te &amp; o&d;hielt  hu ne wilt he &d;onne hiera dea&d;es? 
 Be &d;issum magon ongietan &d;a lareowas hwelces wites hi wyr&d;e bio&d;  &d;onne hie l&ae;ta&d; &d;a sawla acwellan for hungre hira worda  &amp; hie nylla&d; hie fedan mid &d;&ae;m hlafe &d;&ae;re giefe &d;e hie onfengon. 
 Bi &d;&ae;m w&ae;s swi&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh Salomon: Se &d;e his hw&ae;te hytt  hine wierg&d; &d;&ae;t folc. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his hw&ae;te ahyde  &d;&ae;t se lareow gehyde &d;a word &d;&ae;re halegan lare. 
 For&d;&ae;m he for &d;&ae;re anre scylde &d;&ae;re swigan bi&d; awierged &amp; fordemed from &d;&ae;m folce  for&d;&ae;m he manigne gel&ae;ran meahte  gif he wolde. 
 Hw&ae;t we magon ge&d;encean  gif hwelc god l&ae;ce bi&d; &d;e wel cann wunda sni&d;an  &amp; &d;onne gesih&d; &d;&ae;t his hwam &d;earf bi&d;  &amp; &d;onne for his sl&ae;w&d;e agiemeleasa&d; &amp; forwirn&d; &d;&ae;t he his helpe  &d;onne wille we cwe&d;an &d;&ae;t he sie genog ryhtlice his bro&d;or dea&d;es scyldig for his agenre sl&ae;w&d;e. 
 Nu &d;onne  nu &d;a lichomlican l&ae;cas &d;us scyldige gerehte sint  nu is to ongietanne &ae;t hu micelre scylde &d;a beo&d; befangne &d;a &d;e ongieta&d; &d;a wunda on &d;&ae;m modum  &amp; agiemeleasia&d; &d;&ae;t hi hi lacnigen  &amp; mid hiera wordum sni&d;en. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s swi&d;e wel gecweden &d;urh Ieremias &d;one witgan  he cw&ae;&d;: Awierged bi&d; se mann se &d;e wirn&d; his sweorde blodes. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mann forwierne his sweorde blodes  &d;&ae;t hwa forwirne his lare &d;&ae;t he mid &d;&ae;re ne ofslea &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sces lustas. 
 Eft cw&ae;&d; Moyses be &d;&ae;m ilcan: Min sweord itt fl&ae;sc. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a &d;e oninnan him gediglia&d; &amp; gehyda&d; &d;a godcundan lare &d;one egeslican Godes cwide &d;e to him gecweden is  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t se ege &d;one o&d;erne ege utadrife  &d;&ae;t is &d;onne se cwide hu mon &d;&ae;t feoh bef&ae;ste &d;&ae;m ciepemen &d;e he scolde for&d;sellan to w&ae;stme  &amp; &d;a for&d;y&d;e he forwandode &d;&ae;t he swa ne dyde  &d;a ageaf he hit to un&d;ances  &amp; his eac h&ae;fde micelne dem. 
 Eac hi sculon gehiran &d;&ae;tte sanctus Paulus geliefde &d;&ae;t he swa micele unscyldigra w&ae;re his niehstena blodes swa he l&ae;s wandade &d;&ae;t he hira un&d;eawas ofsloge. 
 Hi magon gehieran be &d;&ae;m cuide &d;e he cw&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t ge sint ealle mine gewietan &d;&ae;t ic eom cl&ae;ne &amp; unscildig nu giet to d&ae;g eowres &ae;lces blodes  for&d;&ae;m ic n&ae;fre ne forwandode &d;&ae;t ic eow ne gecy&d;de eall Godes ge&d;eaht. 
 Eac hi sculon gehieran hu sanctus Iohannes w&ae;s gemanod mid &d;&ae;s engles stemne  &d;a &d;a he cw&ae;&d; to him: Se &d;e gehire &d;&ae;t hine mon clipige  clipie he eac o&d;erne  &amp; cwe&d;e  cum. 
 &D;&ae;t is  se &d;e ongiete &d;&ae;t he sie gecieged mid godcundre stemne  &d;&ae;tte he eac cigende &amp; l&ae;rende o&d;re &d;ider tio &amp; la&d;ige &d;ider he getogen bi&d;  &d;yl&ae;s he finde &d;a duru betynede ongean hine  &d;onne he cume  gif he cume idelhende to  &amp; &d;a mid him ne brenge  &d;e he &d;ider la&d;ian scolde. 
 Hie scoldon gehieran hu Essaias se witga hreowsigende hine selfne t&ae;lde  &d;a he w&ae;s on&ae;led mid &d;y upcundan leohte  he cw&ae;&d;: Waa me &d;&ae;s ic swigode. 
 Eac hie sculon gehieran &d;&ae;tte &d;urh Salomon is gehaten &d;&ae;m monnum &d;e lustlice &amp; unslawlice l&ae;ra&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne cunnon  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t him scyle hiera wisdom bion geieced &amp; gemanigfal&d;od. 
 Salomon cu&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;s monnes sawl &d;e wel spric&d; hio bi&d; am&ae;st  ond swa hwa swa o&d;erne drenc&d;  he wir&d; self oferdruncen. 
 Swa eac se &d;e ut wel l&ae;r&d; mid his wordum  he onfeh&d; innan &d;&ae;s innge&d;onces f&ae;tnesse  &d;&ae;t is wisdom. 
 Swa eac se &d;e ne wirn&d; &d;&ae;s wines his lare &d;a mod mid to oferdrencanne &d;e hine gehieran willa&d;  he bi&d; eac oferdrenced &amp; wel afed mid &d;&ae;m drence mislicra &amp; monigfaldra giefa. 
 Hw&ae;t we hirdon &d;&ae;tte Dauid brohte Gode to lacum &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he &d;a lare ne h&ae;l &d;e him God geaf. 
 &D;&ae;t he cy&d;de  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Dryhten  &d;u wast &d;&ae;t ic ne wyrne minra welera  &amp; &d;ine ryhtwisnesse ic ne diegle on minre heortan; 
 &D;ine h&ae;lo &amp; &d;ine ryhtwisnesse ic secgge. 
 Gehiera&d; hw&ae;t on Cantica Canticorum is awriten &d;&ae;t se brydguma scolde sprecan to &d;&ae;re bryde  he cw&ae;&d;: Hlyst hider  &d;u &d;e eardas&d; on freondes orcgearde  &amp; gedoo &d;&ae;t ic m&ae;ge gehiran &d;ine stemne. 
 &D;&ae;t is sio halige gesomnung Godes folces  &d;&ae;t earda&d; on &ae;ppeltunum  &d;onne hie wel bega&d; hira plantan &amp; hiera impan  o&d; hie fulweaxne beo&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t bi&d; &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his stemne gehiere  &d;onne &d;a gecorenan menn giornfulle bio&d; his worda to gehlystanne. 
 &amp; &d;onne wilna&d; se brydguma  &d;&ae;t is Crist  &d;&ae;t he gehire &d;a stemne &d;&ae;re bryde  &d;&ae;t is Cristenra monna gesomnung  &d;onne he &d;urh gesceadwisra &amp; him gecorenra monna mod him to clipa&d;  &amp; hie l&ae;r&d; &d;urh hiora mu&d;. 
 Eac hie sculon gehieran hw&ae;t Moyses dyde  &d;a he ongeat &d;&ae;t God w&ae;s &d;&ae;m folce ierre  he bebead &d;&ae;t menn namen hiora sweord Godes andan mid to wrecanne  &amp; cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t &d;a scolden bion synderlice Godes &d;egnas  &d;a &d;e unwandiende &d;ara scyldegena gyltas ofslogen. 
 He cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e Godes &d;egn sie  ga hider to me  &amp; do his sweord to his hype  &amp; ga&d; from geate to geate &d;urh midde &d;a ceastre  &amp; ofslea &ae;lc mon his bro&d;ur &amp; his freond &amp; his nihstan. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon his sweord doo ofer his hype  &d;&ae;t mon &d;a geornfulnesse his lare l&ae;te fur&d;ur &d;onne his fl&ae;sces lustas  &amp; &d;&ae;s gieme &d;&ae;t he unaliefede lustas &amp; lara atemige &amp; oferwinne  &d;onne he wilna&d; &d;&ae;t he haligdom l&ae;re. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon ierne from geate to o&d;rum  &d;&ae;t he ierne &d;reatigende from &d;ara un&d;eawa &ae;lcum to o&d;rum  &d;e dea&d; m&ae;ge ingan on &d;&ae;s monnes mod. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon ierne &d;urh midde &d;a ceastre  &d;&ae;tte mon sua emn sie betweox cristenum folce on &d;&ae;re &d;reaunga hiera scylda &d;&ae;t he nau&d;er ne nanum men ne olicce  ne he nanes monnes oleccunga ne recce. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s swi&d;e ryhtlice gecweden &d;&ae;t mon scolde ofslean his bro&d;ur &amp; his freond &amp; his niehstan. 
 &D;onne mon ofslih&d; his bro&d;ur &amp; his friond &amp; his niehstan  &d;onne he for nanre sibbe ne wanda&d; &d;&ae;t he &d;a gyltas ne wrece on scyldegum monnum. 
 Nu se is &d;onne gehaten Godes &d;egn se &d;e mid &d;&ae;m andan on&ae;led bi&d; godcundre lufan un&d;eawas to ofsleanne  hu  ne wi&d;s&ae;c&d; se &d;onne eallunga Godes &d;egn to bionne  se &d;e wi&d;s&ae;c&d; &d;&ae;t he ne &d;reage swa he swi&d;us&d; m&ae;ge woruldmonna un&d;eawas? 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manianne &d;a &d;e nabba&d; naw&d;er ne ildo ne wisdom to &d;on &d;&ae;t hie m&ae;gen o&d;&d;e cunnen l&ae;ran  &amp; hi &d;eah forhradia&d; &d;&ae;t hie hit ongienna&d;  &d;yl&ae;s hie himselfum fordikigen &d;one weg &d;&ae;re bote  &d;e him on fierste becuman meahte  &d;onne hi him to tio&d; &d;a byr&d;enne swa micelre &d;enunge swa hr&ae;dlice. 
 Ac &d;onne hie him &ae;r tide to tio&d; &d;&ae;t hi ne magon ne ne cunnon  &d;onne is him to ondr&ae;danne &d;&ae;t him weor&d;e to lore &d;&ae;t hie to ryhtre tide gefolgian meahton  &d;&ae;t is se wisdom  &d;e hie &ae;r tide wilnia&d; &amp; eowia&d;  ac he him wyr&d; &d;onne swi&d;e ryhtlice to lore. 
 Hw&ae;t hie magon ge&d;encean &d;&ae;t fugla briddas  gif hie &ae;r wilnia&d; to fleoganne  &ae;r hira fe&d;ra fulweaxene sin  &d;&ae;tte sio wilnung hie geni&d;ra&d; &d;e hi &ae;r upahef&d;  o&d; hie forweor&d;a&d;. 
 Eac hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen  gif mon on niwne weall unadrugodne &amp; unasti&d;odne micelne hrof &amp; hefigne onsett  &d;onne ne timbre&d; he no healle ac hryre. 
 Eac hi sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hi ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte &d;a wif &d;e &d;a geeacnodan bearn cenna&d; &d;e &d;onne git fulborene ne bio&d;  ne fylla&d; hie no mid &d;&ae;m hus ac byrgenna. 
 For &d;issum &d;ingum w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte Crist self  &d;e swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice meahte getrymian &d;one &d;e he wolde  sealde bisene &d;&ae;m lareowum to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t &d;a unl&ae;redan ne scoldon l&ae;ran: si&d;&d;an he his cnihtas gel&ae;red h&ae;fde &d;one cr&ae;ft &d;&ae;s lareowdomes  he cw&ae;&d; swa&d;eah: Sitta&d; eow nu giet innan ceastre  o&d;&d;&ae;t ge weor&d;en fullgearowode mid &d;&ae;m g&ae;s&d;lican cr&ae;fte. 
 &D;onne we sitta&d; innan ceastre  &d;onne we us betyna&d; binnan &d;&ae;m locum ures modes  &d;yl&ae;s we for dolspr&ae;ce to widgangule weor&d;en. 
 Ac eft &d;onne we fullgearowode weor&d;a&d; mid &d;&ae;m godcundan cr&ae;fte  &d;onne bio we of &d;&ae;re ceastre ut af&ae;rene  &d;&ae;t is of urum agnum inge&d;once  o&d;re men to l&ae;ranne. 
 Be &d;ys ilcan cw&ae;&d; Salomon to iongum monnum: &d;u gionga  bio &d;e uni&d;e to clipianne &amp; to l&ae;ranne  ge fur&d;um &d;ina agna spr&ae;ca  &amp; &d;eah &d;e mon tuwa frigne  gebid &d;u mid &d;&ae;re andsware  o&d; &d;u wite &d;&ae;t &d;in spr&ae;c h&ae;bbe &ae;g&d;er ge ord ge ende. 
 For &d;issum ilcan &d;ingum w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte ure Aliesend  &d;eah he on hefenum sie Scieppend &amp; engla lareow  nolde he &d;eah on eor&d;an bion monna lareow  &ae;r he w&ae;s &d;ritiges geara eald  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wolde &d;&ae;m fortruwodum monnum andrysno halwendes eges on gebrengean; 
 &D;eah &d;e he self gegyltan ne meahte  nolde he &d;eah &ae;r bodian &d;a giefe &d;&ae;s fulfremedan lifes  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e he self w&ae;re fulfremedre ielde. 
 Hit is awriten on &d;&ae;m godspelle &d;&ae;tte ure H&ae;lend  &d;a he w&ae;s twelfwintre  wurde be&ae;ftan his meder &amp; his m&ae;gum innan &d;&ae;re ceastre Hierusalem. 
 Ac eft  &d;a his m&ae;gas hine sohton  &d;a fundon hie hiene tomiddes &d;ara wietena &d;e &d;&ae;r wisoste w&ae;ron in Hierusalem  hlystende hiora worda  &amp; frinende hiora lara. 
 &D;onne is us &d;&ae;t swi&d;e wocorlice to ge&d;enceanne &d;&ae;tte ure H&ae;lend  &d;a &d;a he twelfwintre w&ae;s  &d;a w&ae;s he gemet sittende tomiddes &d;ara lareowa frignende  nalles l&ae;rende; 
 For&d;&ae;m he us wolde &d;&ae;t to bisene don &d;&ae;tte &d;a unl&ae;redan ne dorsten l&ae;ran  nu he &d;onne wolde cniht bion  &amp; wolde &d;&ae;t hiene mon l&ae;rde  se ilca se &d;e &d;a &ae;r l&ae;rde &d;e hine &d;a l&ae;rdon mid &d;&ae;m cr&ae;fte &d;&ae;s godcundan anwaldes. 
 Ond eft Paulus cw&ae;&d; to his cnihte: Bebiod &d;is &amp; l&ae;re  &amp; ne forsio nan mon &d;ine giogu&d;e. 
 We sculon wietan &d;&ae;tte oft bi&d; on halgum gewrietum genemned midfeorwe to giugu&d;hade. 
 &D;&ae;t we magon sweotolor ongietan  gif we Salomones cuida sumne herongemong eowia&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Bli&d;sa  cniht  on &d;inum giogu&d;hade. 
 Gif he hit &d;onne ne tiohchode eall to anum  &d;onne ne nemde he &d;one cniht &ae;g&d;er ge cniht ge giong man. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e woroldare wilnia&d;  &amp; hie &d;onne orsorglice habba&d;; 
 &amp; on o&d;re &d;a &d;e woroldare wilnia&d;  &amp; &d;onne hie gewilnode habba&d;  hie &d;onne mid micelre earfo&d;nesse &amp; mid micle broce on wunia&d;. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e eall orsorglice begita&d; &d;isse worulde  &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie wilnia&d;; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;isses andweardan middangeardes wilna &amp; welena wilnia&d;  &amp; swa&d;eah mid sumum wi&d;erweardum brocum hiora him bi&d; f&ae;rwirned. 
 &D;a &d;onne sint to manienne &d;e simle habba&d; &d;isse worulde &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hie ne agiemeleasien  &d;onne hi hit eall h&ae;bben  &d;&ae;t hie ne secen &d;one &d;e him to eallum gefultema&d;  &d;yl&ae;s hie lufigen &d;as el&d;iodignesse ofer hiora &ae;genne e&d;el  &amp; hiora mod eal ahon on &d;&ae;t &d;e him her gel&ae;ned bi&d;  &amp; &d;yl&ae;s hie gedwelle sio gehydnes &amp; &d;a get&ae;su &d;e hie on &d;&ae;m wege habba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie forgieten hwider hie scylen  &amp; &d;yl&ae;s hie for &d;&ae;m f&ae;geran monan &d;e hi on niht gesio&d; forhycgen &d;&ae;s d&ae;ges bierhto &amp; &d;&ae;re sunnan. 
 Eac hi sint to monienne &d;&ae;tte hie no ne geliefen &d;&ae;tte &d;a willan &amp; &d;a get&ae;su &d;e him on &d;isse worulde becuma&d;  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t sien &d;a lean &d;e him God getiohchod h&ae;f&d;  ac bi&d; &d;issa ierma&d; frofor  &amp; &d;a lean bio&d; on &d;&ae;m ecean life &d;&ae;s &d;e we to gode do&d;. 
 For&d;y we sculon ure mod getrymman wi&d; &d;isses middangeardes oliecunga  &d;yl&ae;s we hie mid ealle mode lufigen  &amp; us mid ealle hiere under&d;ieden. 
 Ac se se &d;e &d;as orsorgnesse &d;e he her h&ae;f&d; ne forswi&d; mid &d;&ae;re gesceadwisnesse his inge&d;onces &amp; mid &d;&ae;re lufan &d;&ae;s beteran lifes  &d;onne gehwierf&d; he &d;a olecunga &d;isse gewitendan worulde him to ecum dea&d;e. 
 For &d;issum &d;ingum w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte Ezechiel se witga &d;reade Israhela folc  &amp; cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hie wolden weor&d;an forlorene &amp; oferwunnene mid orsorgnesse  swa swa Idumeas w&ae;ron  for&d;&ae;m hi to swi&d;e bli&d;sodon on &d;isses middangeardes orsorgnesse. 
 Ac Dryhten hie &d;reade &d;urh &d;one witgan  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Hie dydon min land him selfum to ierfelonde mid gefean &amp; mid ealre heortan &amp; mid ealle mode. 
 Be &d;&ae;m wordum we m&ae;gon gehieran &d;&ae;t hie w&ae;ron swi&d;e sui&d;lice get&ae;lde  n&ae;s no for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie f&ae;gnodan  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie mid ealre heortan &amp; mid ealle mode f&ae;gnodan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Salomon: Giongra monna dolscipe hi ofslih&d;  &amp; dysigra monna orsorgness hi forde&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus: Sien &d;a h&ae;bbendan swelce hie nowiht h&ae;bben  &amp; &d;a &d;e &d;isses middangeardes notiga&d; swelce hi his no ne notigen. 
 &D;&ae;tte we swa lufigen &d;isne uterran &amp; &d;isne eor&d;lican fultum &d;&ae;tte we for&d;&ae;m from &d;&ae;re wilnunga &amp; from &d;&ae;re geornfulnesse &d;&ae;re godcundan lufan ure mod ne awenden  &d;yl&ae;s us weor&d;e to wope &amp; to el&d;iodignesse &d;&ae;s ecean lifes &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t us on &d;isse el&d;iodignesse to fultume &amp; to are gel&ae;ned is; 
 &D;&ae;tte we ne f&ae;gnigen  swelce we ges&ae;lige sien for &d;issum gewitendan &d;ingum  &d;onne &d;onne we betweox &d;&ae;m ongieten hu earme we bio&d; &d;ara ecena &d;inga. 
 Be &d;issum ilcan cw&ae;&d; Salomon on Cantica Canticorum &d;&ae;re bec be &d;&ae;re halgan gesomnunge  he cw&ae;&d;: Dryhtnes winestre hand is under minum heafde  &amp; his swi&d;re hand me beclip&d;. 
 Sio winestre hand Godes he cw&ae;&d; w&ae;re under his heafde. 
 &D;&ae;t tacna&d; orsorgnesse &d;isses andweardan lifes. 
 &D;a hand &d;onne ge&d;ryc&d; sio incunde lufu &d;&ae;s uplican lifes. 
 Sio swi&d;re hand hine &d;onne beclip&d;  &d;onne &d;onne he hine gehielt on &d;&ae;m willan &d;&ae;t he mid ealre estfulnesse lufa&d; &d;&ae;t ece lif. 
 Eft w&ae;s gecueden &d;urh Salomon &d;one snottran &d;&ae;tte on his swi&d;ran handa w&ae;re lang lif  &amp; on his winestran w&ae;re wela &amp; wyr&d;mynt. 
 &D;a he l&ae;rde hu we &ae;g&d;er lufian sceolden  &d;a he m&ae;t &d;one welan &amp; &d;one wyr&d;mynd to &d;&ae;re winestran handa. 
 Eft be &d;&ae;m ilcan cw&ae;&d; se psalmsceop: Geh&ae;le me &d;in sio swi&d;re. 
 Ne cw&ae;&d; he no &d;in sio winestre hond  ac &d;in sio swi&d;re. 
 Mid &d;&ae;m he gecy&d;de &d;&ae;t he ne m&ae;nde &d;is andwearde lif  ac &d;&ae;s ecean lifes h&ae;lo he sohte. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan is eft awriten on Exodo  &d;&ae;t is Moyses boc  hit is awriten: &d;in swi&d;re hand  Dryhten  gebr&ae;c &d;ine feond. 
 &D;a &d;onne &d;e Godes fiond bio&d;  &d;eah hi on &d;&ae;re winstran handa bion ge&d;igene  hi beo&d; mid &d;&ae;re swi&d;ran tobrocene  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte oft &d;is andwearde lif upahefe&d; &d;a yfelan  ac se tocyme &d;&ae;re ecan eadignesse hie geni&d;ra&d;. 
 &D;y sint to manienne &d;a &d;e on &d;isse worulde orsorglice libba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ongieten &d;&ae;tte sio orsorgnes &d;isses andweardan lifes hwilum bi&d; to &d;&ae;m gel&ae;ned &d;&ae;t hie sien &d;urh &d;a to beteran life getogene  hwilum to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie sien &d;y swi&d;ur on ecnesse gesciende. 
 Forhwam w&ae;s elles Canonea land Israhela folce gehaten  buton for&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;&ae;t ungetyde folc nolde geliefan &d;eah him mon feorr land on fierste gehete  gif him sona ne sealde sum on neaweste se him &d;&ae;t mare gehett? 
 Ond eac for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte hie &d;y f&ae;s&d;licor &amp; &d;y untweogendlicor gelifden &d;ara ecena &d;inga  swa hwanne swa him &d;a gehete  &d;yl&ae;s hi mid &d;&ae;m gehatum &amp; mid &d;&ae;m tohopan anum hi spone to &d;&ae;re giefe  ac eac mid &d;&ae;re giefe he hi teah on &d;one tohopan. 
 &D;&ae;t eac gecy&d;de se psalmsceop swi&d;e openlice  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: He him sealde ricu o&d;erra kynrena  &amp; manigra folca gestreones hie wieoldon  to &d;on &d;&ae;t hi his ryhtwisnesse geheolden  &amp; his &ae; sohten. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;&ae;t mennisce mod Godes gl&ae;dmodnesse mid godum weorcum ne geandswora&d;  &d;onne bi&d; he swi&d;e ryhtlice mid &d;&ae;m gehined &d;e mon wen&d; &d;&ae;t he mid gearod sie. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s eft gecweden &d;urh &d;one salmsceop: &d;u hie geni&d;rades  &d;a hi hi selfe upahofon. 
 Swa  &d;onne &d;onne unnyttan men &d;a godcundan gife nylla&d; leanian mid ryhtum weorcum  ac willa&d; hi selfe her mid ealle fordon mid &d;&ae;re fortruwunga &d;&ae;s to flowendan welan &amp; orsorgnesse  &amp; &d;onon &d;e hi utan bio&d; ah&ae;fene  &d;anon hie bio&d; innan afeallene. 
 Be &d;ys ilcan w&ae;s eac gecweden be &d;&ae;m welegan &d;e ges&ae;d is &d;&ae;tte on helle &d;rowude  hit w&ae;s gecweden: &d;u onfenge &d;in god eal her on worulde. 
 For&d;&ae;m anfeh&d; se yfla auht goodes on &d;isse worulde &d;&ae;t he eft &d;y maran yfles on &d;&ae;m toweardan life  gif he her nolde for &d;&ae;m goode to Gode gecierran. 
 Angean &d;&ae;t sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;ises middangeardes wilna &amp; weolena wilnia&d;  &amp; him swa&d;eah sum wi&d;erweardnes his forwiern&d;  &amp; hi geswenc&d; on &d;isse worulde  &d;a sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ge&d;encen mid hu micelre giefe ofer him waca&d; se Scippend &amp; se Stihtere ealra gesceafta  &d;onne he hi nyle l&ae;tan to hiera agnum wilnungum; 
 Swa swa se l&ae;ce  &d;onne he &d;&ae;m siocan ne truwa&d;  &amp; wen&d; &d;&ae;t his gehelpan ne m&ae;ge  &d;onne alief&d; he him eal &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hine lys&d; to donne &amp; to &d;ycganne  ac &d;&ae;s &d;e he wen&d; &d;&ae;t he gehelpan m&ae;ge  &d;&ae;m he forwiern&d; swi&d;e feola &d;&ae;s &d;e he wilna&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t we eac wierna&d; urum cildum urra peninga mid to plegianne  &d;&ae;m ilcum &d;e we eft tiochia&d; urne eard &amp; urne e&d;el &amp; ure ierfe eall &ae;tsomne to te forl&ae;tanne  &amp; hie tiochia&d; us to ierfeweardum to habbanne. 
 Ac nimen him nu be &d;isse bisene gefean &amp; tohopan &d;&ae;re ecan ierfeweardnesse  &d;a &d;e sio wi&d;erweardnes &d;isses andweardan lifes geea&d;met: ac gif hi God n&ae;fde on ecnesse getiochod to geh&ae;lanne  &d;onne ne gebridlode he hi no mid swa swi&d;licre &d;reaunga his lare. 
 Eac sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;issa hwilendlicra &d;inga wilnia&d;  &amp; him &d;eah sum broc &amp; sumu wi&d;erweardnes hiera forwiern&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie geornfullice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte oft ryhtwise menn mid &d;ys hwilendlican anwealde weor&d;a&d; upah&ae;fene  o&d; hie &d;urh &d;one anwald weor&d;a&d; mid synnum gefangne  sua sua mid sume grine  swa swa we &ae;r herbiufan s&ae;don on &d;isse ilcan bec bi Dauide &d;&ae;m Godes dirlinge &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re ryhtwisra &d;a &d;a he &d;eng w&ae;s &d;onne he w&ae;re si&d;&d;an he kyning w&ae;s. 
 &D;a &d;a he &d;egn w&ae;s  he mette his feond  &amp; &d;eah for Godes ege &amp; for ryhtwisnesse lufum he hine ne dorste ofslean. 
 Ac eft si&d;&d;an he kyning w&ae;s  for lare &amp; for tiehtinge his agenes firenlustes he ofslog &amp; besirede his getreowne &d;egn. 
 Hwa m&ae;g &d;onne &ae;hta o&d;&d;e anwaldes o&d;&d;e weor&d;scipes wilnian butan plio  nu se swelc plioh &d;&ae;ron gefor  se &d;e his no ne wilnode? 
 Hwa m&ae;g &d;onne for &d;yllecum bion gehealden butan miclum gesuince &amp; miclum plio  nu se on &d;&ae;m rice on swelce synne befioll  se &d;e God self to &d;&ae;m rice geceas? 
 Eac hie sint to manigenne &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen hu hit awriten is be Salamonne  hu he &ae;fter swa miclum wisdome afioll  emne o&d;&d;&ae;t he dioflum ongan gieldan. 
 Nis hit no ges&ae;d &d;&ae;t he &ae;nig wuht wi&d;erweardes on &d;ys middangearde h&ae;fde  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&t;e he afeol; 
 Ac si&d;&d;an him se wisdom to forl&ae;ten w&ae;s eallunga he forget hine selfne &amp; &d;a lare &amp; &d;one &d;iodscipe &d;e he geliornode  swa &d;&ae;t he his nan geswinc habban nolde ne l&ae;sse ne mare. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manianne &d;a &d;e beo&d; gebundne mid synr&ae;denne  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e freo bio&d; &d;ara benda. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e mid synnr&ae;denne bio&d; gebundene  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e &d;ara benda bio&d; frio. 
 &D;a sint to manigenne &d;e mid &d;&ae;m gebundene bio&d;  &d;onne &d;onne hie betwuh him &d;encea&d; hu hiera &ae;g&d;er o&d;res willan don scyle  &d;&ae;t hira swa tilige &ae;g&d;er o&d;rum to licianne on hiera gesinscipe  &d;&ae;t hi ne mislicien hiera Scippende; 
 &amp; &d;&ae;t hie swa wyrcen &d;isses middangeardes weorc &d;&ae;t hie ne forl&ae;ten to wilnianne &d;ara &d;e Godes sien  &amp; swa gefeon &d;issa andweardena goda &d;&ae;t hi him eac geornlice ondr&ae;den &d;a ecan yflu  &amp; swa eac &d;ara yfela &d;isse worulde hiofen &d;&ae;t hi huru hiora tohopan anwealgne gef&ae;stnigen to &d;&ae;m ecum godum; 
 &amp; &d;onne hie ongieten hu gewitendlic &d;is andwearde bi&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie her do&d;  &amp; hu &d;urhwunienede &d;&ae;t bi&d; &d;&ae;t hi wilnia&d;  &d;&ae;tte &d;onne naw&d;er ne nan yfel &d;isses middangeardes hiora mod ne gebrece ne nan god hie ne beswice  ac se gefea &d;ara hefonlicena goda hi gehierde wi&d; &d;&ae;m brocum; 
 &amp; eft se wena &d;ara toweardena yfela on &d;&ae;m toweardan dome hie geegesige on &d;&ae;re orsorgnesse; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t mod &d;ara cristenra gesamhiwena  &d;&ae;tte bi&d; &ae;g&d;er ge trum ge untrum &amp; ne m&ae;g fullice forsion &d;as hwilendlican &d;ing  he m&ae;g &d;eah hine formengan to &d;&ae;m ecum mid his willan  &d;eah he &d;onne giet on &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sces lustfulnesse licge  mid &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t he hine getrymige &amp; gefylle mid &d;&ae;m uplican tohopan. 
 Ond &d;eah he h&ae;bbe hw&ae;t eor&d;lices &amp; mennisclices him on gewunan on &d;ys wege se weg is &d;is andwearde lif ne forl&ae;te he &d;eah &d;one tohopan &d;&ae;t he becume to Gode for his godan willan  &amp; swa&d;eah ne fulga he eallunga &d;&ae;s lichoman wilnunga  &d;yl&ae;s he eallunga afealle &d;onon &d;e he f&ae;s&d;licost tohopian scolde. 
 Ymb &d;&ae;t reahte Paulus swi&d;e wel mid feaum wordum on his &ae;rendgewrite to Corinctheum  he cu&ae;&d;: &d;a &d;e wif h&ae;bben  sien &d;a swelce hie nan h&ae;bben  &amp; &d;a &d;e wepen  sien &d;a swelce hi no ne wepen  &amp; &d;a &d;e f&ae;gnigen  sien &d;a swelce hi no ne f&ae;gnigen. 
 Se &d;onne h&ae;f&d; wif swelce he nan n&ae;bbe  se &d;e hit h&ae;f&d; for licumlicre frofre  &amp; &d;eah for &d;&ae;m bryce &amp; for &d;&ae;re lufe hine ne awent from bettrum weorcum. 
 Se h&ae;f&d; eac wif swelce he nan n&ae;bbe  se &d;e ongiet &d;&ae;tte eal &d;as andweardan &d;ing bio&d; gewitendlicu  &amp; &d;eah for nied&d;earfe h&ae;f&d; giemenne his fl&ae;sces  &amp; hw&ae;&d;re mid micelre wilnunga his g&ae;stes giern&d; &d;&ae;s ecan gefean. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon wepe  &amp; ne wepe  &d;&ae;t mon &d;a ierm&d;o &d;isses middangeardes wepe  &amp; swa&d;eah wite &d;&ae;t he sceal bion afrefred  &amp; blissian on &d;&ae;m ecum gefean. 
 &amp; eft is &d;&ae;t mon blissige &amp; ne blissige &d;&ae;t mon ahebbe his mod of &d;issum eor&d;lican to &d;&ae;m hefonlican  &amp; &d;eah ne forl&ae;te &d;&ae;t he him ne ondr&ae;de &d;&ae;t he afealle of &d;&ae;m uplican to &d;&ae;m ni&d;erlican. 
 Ymb &d;&ae;t swi&d;e wel &d;&ae;rryhte &ae;fter rehte sanctus Paulus  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: &d;yses middangeardes ansien oferg&ae;&d;. 
 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Ne sculon ge no eallunga to swi&d;e lufian &d;isne middangeard  for&d;am  &d;eah ge hine lufigen  he eow ne m&ae;g ealneg standan; 
 On idelnisse ge f&ae;stnia&d; eower mod on him  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he eow flih&d;  &d;eah ge hine lufigen swelce he wunigende sie. 
 To manigenne sint &d;a gesomhiwan  &d;eah hira hw&ae;&d;rum hw&ae;thwugu hwilum mislicige on o&d;rum  &d;&ae;t hie &d;&ae;t ge&d;yldelice forberen; 
 &amp; gebidde hira &ae;g&d;er for o&d;er &d;&ae;t hie m&ae;gen &d;urh &d;&ae;t weor&d;an geh&ae;lede  for&d;&ae;m hit awriten is: Bera&d; eowre byr&d;enna gem&ae;nelice betwux iow  &d;onne gefylle ge Godes &ae;. 
 Sio lufu &d;onne is Godes &ae;: sio &ae; &amp; sio lufu us brienga&d; monig god from Criste  &amp; ure yfelu ge&d;yldelice forbier&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne we onhyriga&d; Criste  &amp; eac &d;a onhyringe gefylla&d;  &d;onne we lustlice sella&d; o&d;rum &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t us God sel&d;  &amp; ge&d;yldelice forbera&d; hiora yfelu. 
 &D;a gesinhiwan mon sceal manian  &amp; eac gehwelcne mon  &d;&ae;t hie no l&ae;s ne ne ge&d;encen hw&ae;t o&d;re men him forbera&d; &amp; ge&d;afia&d;  &d;onne hie ge&d;encea&d; hw&ae;t hi o&d;rum monnum forbera&d;; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e he m&ae;g micle &d;y ie&d; adreogan &d;a tionan &d;e him o&d;re men do&d;  gif he wile gemunan &d;a &d;e he o&d;rum monnum de&d;. 
 Eac sint to manigenne &d;a gesinhiwan &d;&ae;t hi gemunen &d;&ae;t hie for nanum o&d;rum &d;ingum ne bio&d; gesomnode  buton for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie sculon bearna strienan. 
 For&d;&ae;m hi sculon ge&d;encean  gif hie to oftr&ae;dlice &amp; to ungemetlice hie gemenga&d; on &d;&ae;m h&ae;mede  &d;&ae;t hie ne bio&d; no on ryhtum gesinscipe  gif hie &d;&ae;t on gewunan habba&d;  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hie gewemma&d; &d;one aliefedan gesinscipe mid &d;&ae;re unliefedan gemengnesse  him is micel nied&d;earf &d;&ae;t hie mid oftr&ae;dlicum gebedum &d;a scylde adiligien. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s &d;&ae;t se getyda l&ae;ce &d;&ae;s hefonlican l&ae;cedomes  &d;&ae;t w&ae;s sanctus Paulus  &ae;g&d;er ge &d;a halan l&ae;rde ge &d;am unhalum l&ae;cedom eowde  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: God bi&d; men &d;&ae;t he sie butan wife. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d;: God bi&d; mannum &d;&ae;t &ae;lc h&ae;bbe his agen wif  &amp; &ae;lc wif hire ceorl  &d;yl&ae;s hi on unryht h&ae;men. 
 &AE;g&d;er he dyde  ge he egesode &d;a &d;e on unryht h&ae;mdon  ge he liefde &d;&ae;m &d;e hit forberan ne meahton  for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte &d;a &d;e gestondan ne meahton  gif hi afeallan scolden  &d;&ae;t hi afeollen on &d;&ae;t hnesce bedd &d;&ae;s gesinscipes  n&ae;s on &d;a heardan eor&d;an &d;&ae;s unryhth&ae;mdes. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m untrumum: Agife se wer his wife hire ryht on hira gesinscipe  &amp; swa same &d;&ae;t wif &d;&ae;m were. 
 Ac &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e he hwelcehwugu gerisenlice leafe dyde &d;&ae;m gesinhiwon hira willan to fremmanne  he cw&ae;&d;: Ne cwe&d;o ic no &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t ic &ae;r cw&ae;&d; bebeodende  ac l&ae;rende &amp; ge&d;afigende. 
 &D;a he spr&ae;c gelicost &d;&ae;m &d;e hit hwelchwugu syn w&ae;re  &d;a he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he hit forgiefan wolde &amp; ge&d;afian. 
 For&d;&ae;m bi&d; sio scyld &d;y hra&d;or geh&ae;led  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hio ne bi&d; unliefedo  ac &d;eah hio aliefedu sie  ne sceal hi mon to ungemetlice began. 
 &D;&ae;t us getacnode Loth swi&d;e wel on him selfum  &d;a he fleah &d;a biernendan ceastre Sodoman  &amp; com to Segor  &d;a ne dorste he nawuht hr&ae;dlice ut of &d;&ae;re ceastre faran up on &d;a muntas. 
 Mid&d;&ae;m&d;e he fleah &d;a birnendan Sodoman  he getacnode &d;&ae;t we sculon fleon &d;one unliefedan bryne ures lichoman. 
 Sio heanes &d;onne &d;ara munta getacna&d; &d;a cl&ae;nnesse &d;&ae;re forh&ae;fdnesse. 
 &D;a &d;onne bio&d; swelce hi eardigen upp on &d;&ae;m munte &d;a &d;e bio&d; gesponnene to gesinscipe  &amp; &d;eah ne bio&d; na gemengde buton &d;onne hi wilnia&d; bearn to gestrienanne. 
 &D;onne hie stonda&d; up on &d;&ae;m munte  &d;onne &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc nauht elles ne sec&d; to &d;&ae;m o&d;rum buton tudor. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t mon stonde on &d;&ae;m munte &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t fl&ae;sc ne sie fl&ae;sclice to &d;&ae;m o&d;rum gef&ae;s&d;nod. 
 Ac monige bio&d; &d;ara &d;e hie gehealda&d; wi&d; unryhth&ae;med  &amp; swa&d;eah his agenra ryhthiwena ne bryc&d; swa swa he mid ryhte sceolde. 
 Loth for ut of Sodoman to Segor  &amp; &d;eah ne com he nauht hra&d;e onuppan &d;&ae;m muntum. 
 Swa  &d;onne &d;onne mon forl&ae;t &d;&ae;t wyrreste lif  &amp; ne m&ae;g &d;eah &d;onne git cuman to &d;&ae;m betstan  ne &d;a forh&ae;fdnesse gehealdan &d;&ae;s hean gesinscipes  &d;onne bi&d; &d;&ae;t swa swa Segor stod on midwege betweox &d;&ae;m muntum &amp; &d;&ae;m merscum &d;e Sodoma on w&ae;s. 
 Sio Segor geh&ae;lde Loth fleondne. 
 Swa de&d; sio Segor &d;&ae;s medemestan lifes: &d;a &d;e hire to befleo&d; hio geh&ae;l&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne &d;a gesinhiwan hi gemenga&d; &d;urh ungemetlice unforh&ae;fdnesse  &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r hi &d;one fiell fleo&d; &d;&ae;re synne  &d;onne magon hie &d;eah weor&d;an geh&ae;lede sui&d;e ie&d;elice &d;urh forgiefnesse &amp; &d;urh gebedu  swa swa Loth funde &d;a lytlan ceastre  &amp; hine &d;&ae;ron wi&d; &d;&ae;t fyr gescilde. 
 &D;&ae;t lif &d;ara gesinhiwena  &d;eah hit ful wundorlic ne sie on m&ae;genum weoruldwilnungum to wi&d;stondanne  hit m&ae;g &d;eah bion orsorglic &ae;lcra wita. 
 For&d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Loth to &d;&ae;m engle: Her is an lytele burg swi&d;e neah  &d;&ae;r ic m&ae;g min feorh on generian. 
 Hio is an lytel  &amp; &d;eah ic m&ae;g &d;&ae;ron libban. 
 He cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hio w&ae;re swi&d;e neah  &amp; &d;eah genog f&ae;st on his h&ae;lo. 
 Swa is &d;&ae;t lif &d;ara gesinhiwena. 
 Nis hit naht feor ascaden from &d;isse worulde  ne eac noht fremde &d;&ae;re ecan h&ae;lo  for&d;&ae;m for &d;&ae;re d&ae;de &d;e hie do&d; betwuh him hi beo&d; gefri&d;ode mid oftr&ae;dlicum gebedum betwuh him  swelce hie sien on sumere lytelre byrig belocene. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s swi&d;e ryhte gecweden &d;urh &d;one engel to Lothe: &d;inre bene ic wille nu onfon  &amp; for &d;inre bede ic ne toweorpe &d;a burg &d;e &d;u foresprics&d;. 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;t lif &d;ara gesinhiwena. 
 Ne bi&d; hit no fordemed beforan Gode gif &d;&ae;r gebedo &ae;fter fylgea&d;. 
 Ymb &d;a illcan gebedo sanctus Paulus manode  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Ne fornime incer no&d;er o&d;er ofer will butan ge&d;afunge  &d;&ae;m timum &d;e he hine wille gebiddan  ac ge&ae;mtigea&d; inc to gebedum. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e ne beo&d; gebundne mid &d;&ae;m gesinscipe  &d;a sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie swa micle ryhtlecor &d;a hefonlican bebodo healden swa hie orsorgran bio&d; &d;isses middangeardes ymbhogena  for&d;&ae;m hie nan gespann &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sclican gesinscipes ne gebiege&d; on &d;isse worulde  ne se aliefeda gesinscipe hi ne gehefega&d;. 
 &D;onne is him micel &d;earf &d;&ae;tte sio unliefde byr&d;en &d;issa eor&d;licena sorga hi ne ge&d;rysce  &d;&ae;tte hie swa micle gearran finde se ytemesta d&ae;g  &d;onne he cume  swa hi her &ae;mtegran bio&d;; 
 &amp; &d;onne hi ge&ae;metgade bio&d; &d;&ae;t hie magon bet don &d;onne o&d;re menn  &amp; hit swa&d;eah agiemeleasia&d;  &d;&ae;t hie &d;onne &d;urh &d;&ae;t ne geearnigen wyrse wite &d;onne o&d;re menn. 
 Ac hi scoldon gehiran hw&ae;t Paulus cw&ae;&d;  &d;a &d;a he sume men manode to &d;&ae;re giefe Godes &d;iowdomes; 
 Ne cw&ae;&d; he &d;eah no &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he cw&ae;&d; for&d;&ae;m&d;e he gesinscipe t&ae;lde  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wolde &d;a sorga aweg adrifan &d;isses middangeardes of his hieremonna mode &d;a &d;e bio&d; aweaxene of &d;&ae;m gesinscipe; 
 He cw&ae;&d;: &d;is ic cwe&d;e for eowerre &d;earfe  &d;yl&ae;s ic eow mid &ae;nige grine gefoo. 
 Ic eow secgge hw&ae;t eow arwyr&d;licost is to beganne  &amp; hu ge fullecost magon Gode &d;iowian &d;&ae;t eow l&ae;st &d;inga mier&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m of &d;&ae;m gesinscipe weaxa&d; eor&d;lice ymbhogan &amp; sorga  for&d;&ae;m se &ae;&d;ela &d;ioda lareow his hieremen to betran life spon  &d;yl&ae;s hi mid eor&d;licre sorge wurden gebundne; 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne se Godes &d;iow on &d;&ae;t gemearr &d;&ae;re woruldsorga befeh&d;  &d;eah he &d;onne h&ae;bbe beflogen &d;one gesinscipe  &d;onne n&ae;f&d; he no beflogen &d;a byr&d;enne. 
 Eac sint to manienne &d;a Godes &d;iowas &d;&ae;t hie ne wenen &d;&ae;t hie butan &d;&ae;m demme stranges domes hi gemengan m&ae;gen wi&d; &d;a &ae;mtegan wifmen  &d;a Paulus &d;&ae;t yfel &d;&ae;re forlegnesse swa manegum awiergdum leahtrum loh. 
 He gecy&d;de hwelc sio scyld bi&d;  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Naw&d;er ne &d;a wohh&ae;mendan  ne &d;a &d;e diofulgieldum &d;iowia&d;  ne &d;a unf&ae;s&d;radan  &d;e ne magon hira unryhth&ae;mdes geswican  ne &d;a &d;iofas  ne &d;a gietseras  ne &d;a druncenwillnan  ne &d;a wiergendan  ne &d;a reaferas Godes rice ne gesitta&d;. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;m wohh&ae;merum deme&d; Dryhten. 
 For&d;&ae;m hi sint to manigenne  gif hie &d;a halwendan forh&ae;fdnesse gehabban ne m&ae;gen  &amp; &d;a scuras &d;&ae;re costunga adreogan ne m&ae;gen  &d;&ae;t hie wilnigen &d;&ae;re hy&d;e &d;&ae;s gesinscipes; 
 For&d;&ae;m hit is awriten &d;&ae;t hit sie betere &d;&ae;t mon gehiewige &d;onne he birne  for&d;&ae;m butan synne he m&ae;g gehiwian  gif he hit &ae;r ne forhet. 
 Ac se &d;e mare god gehet &d;onne he &ae;r dyde  he gede&d; mid &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t l&ae;sse god unaliefed &d;&ae;t he &ae;r dyde. 
 Hit is awrieten on &d;&ae;m godspelle &d;&ae;t nan mon ne scyle don his hond to &d;&ae;re sylg  &amp; hawian underb&ae;c. 
 Ne &d;on ma se &d;e gehat geh&ae;t  ne wene he &d;&ae;t he sie a &d;y near hefonrice  gif he hine from went &d;&ae;m gehatum. 
 For&d;&ae;m se &d;e hine selfne maran godes beh&ae;t  &amp; &d;onne forl&ae;t &d;a maran god  &amp; went hine to &d;&ae;m l&ae;ssum  &d;onne bi&d; hit swutol &d;&ae;t he bi&d; fromlociende oferswi&d;ed. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e gefandod habba&d; &d;ara fl&ae;sclicra synna  on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;s noht ne cunnon. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e ongieta&d; &amp; witon hiera lichoman synna  on o&d;re &d;a &d;a &d;e hie nyton. 
 &D;a sint to manienne &d;e hiera lichoman synna onfunden habba&d;  &d;&ae;t hie huru &ae;fter &d;&ae;m scipgebroce him &d;a s&ae; ondr&ae;den &amp; &d;&ae;t forlor hira frecennesse  &d;onne hie hit oncnawen  &d;&ae;t hi hit onscunigen; 
 &D;&ae;tte &d;a &d;a &d;e mildheortlice bio&d; gehealdne &ae;fter hiora &d;urhtogenum synnum  &d;&ae;tte hi eft unw&ae;rlice to ne gecierren  &amp; &d;onne swelten. 
 For&d;&ae;m is gecweden to &d;&ae;re syngiendan sawle  &d;e n&ae;fre hire synna geswican nyle: &d;u h&ae;fst forlegisse andwlitan  for&d;&ae;m &d;e no ne sceama&d;. 
 &D;eah hie sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie geornlice giemen  &d;eah hi &d;&ae;t god hira gecynde gehal nolden gehealdan  &d;&ae;t hi hit huru tobrocen gebeten. 
 Him is &d;earf &d;&ae;t hie ge&d;encen hu micel menigu &d;&ae;ra getreowfulra bi&d;  &d;e &ae;g&d;er ge hi selfe cl&ae;ne gehealda&d;  ge eac o&d;re of hira gedwolan ahwierfa&d;. 
 Ac hw&ae;t cwe&d;a&d; hi &d;onne  &d;onne &d;a o&d;re stonda&d; on anwalgre h&ae;lo  &amp; hie nylla&d; &ae;fter yfelre d&ae;de gecierran? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t cwe&d;a&d; hi  &d;onne &d;a o&d;re brienga&d; &ae;g&d;er ge hie selfe ge eac o&d;re mid hiora bisenum to hefonrice; 
 Ond hie  &d;onne him God &d;one first alef&d;  &amp; him hira yffel forbier&d;  nylla&d; fur&d;um hie selfe briengan? 
 Ac hie sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie gemunen hw&ae;t hi godes &ae;r forleton &d;&ae;s &d;e hi don meahton  &d;&ae;t hi huru &d;onne forbugen &d;&ae;t andwearde yfel. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Dryhten to &d;&ae;m gewundedum modum &d;urh Ezechiel &d;one witgan  swelce he to Iudeum spr&ae;ce  &amp; he &d;ara gedonena scylda eft gemyndgade  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wolde &d;&ae;t hi sceamode &d;&ae;t hie eft on &d;&ae;re o&d;erre worulde w&ae;ren uncl&ae;ne  he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t hi hi forl&ae;gen on Egiptum on hira giogu&d;e: hi w&ae;ron &d;&ae;r forlegene  &amp; &d;&ae;r w&ae;ron gehnescode hiera breost  &amp; forbrocene &d;a dela hiora m&ae;gdenhades. 
 On Egiptum beo&d; hira breost gehnescod  &d;onne hi &d;a scandlican lustas &d;isses middangeardes mid hira modes willan underhniga&d;. 
 Ond eft on Egiptum bio&d; forbrocene &d;a w&ae;stmas &d;&ae;ra dela  &d;onne &d;&ae;t gecyndelice gewitt &ae;rest sume hwile bi&d; on him selfun anwalg untosliten  o&d;&d;&ae;t hit bi&d; gewemmed mid&d;&ae;m&d;e hit cnyssa&d; on unryhta wilnunga  &amp; hit totera&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m sint to manienne &d;a &d;e hiera synna onfunden habba&d;  &d;&ae;tte hie mid wacore mode ongieten &ae;fter hira misd&ae;dum mid hu miclum godum willan Dryhten tobr&ae;t &d;one greadan his mildheortnesse ongen &d;a &d;e to him gecierra&d;. 
 Swa swa he &d;urh Ieremias &d;one witgan cw&ae;&d;  he cw&ae;&d;: Gif hwelc wif forl&ae;t hiere ceorl  &amp; nim&d; hire o&d;erne  wenestu recce he hire &ae;fre ma  o&d;&d;e m&ae;g hio &ae;fre eft cuman to him swa cl&ae;nu swa hio &ae;r w&ae;s? 
 Hw&ae;t &d;u &d;onne eart forlegen wi&d; manigne copenere  &amp; swa&d;eah ic cwe&d;e: Gecier eft to me  cw&ae;&d; Dryhten. 
 He gereahte &d;one ryhtestan dom be &d;&ae;m forlegenan &amp; &d;&ae;m aworpnan wife  &amp; swa&d;eah us gecy&d;de  gif we &ae;fter &d;&ae;m hryre urra scylda to him gecierdon  &d;&ae;t us w&ae;re gearo his miltsung  n&ae;s &d;&ae;t ryht. 
 Of &d;issum wordum we magon oncnawan  nu he us spara&d; mid swa micelre mildheortnesse  &d;onne we gesynngia&d;  &amp; &d;onne giet nylla&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;re scylde to him gecierran  &d;&ae;t we &d;onne eft mid micle dysige syngia&d;  nu sio Godes miltsung is swa micul ofer &d;a dysegan  &d;&ae;t hiene na ne a&d;riet &d;&ae;t he hi to him ne la&d;ige  &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e hie gesyngod habba&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;re miltsunga &ae;fter &d;&ae;re la&d;unga is swi&d;e wel ges&ae;d &d;urh Essaias &d;one witgan; 
 Hit is gecweden to &d;&ae;m wi&d;erweardan men: &d;in eagan weor&d;a&d; gesionde &d;inne bebiodend  &amp; &d;in earan gehira&d; under b&ae;c. 
 Eall moncynn w&ae;s to Gode gewend  &d;a &d;a hi &ae;rest gesceapene w&ae;ron on neorxna wonge; 
 &amp; he &d;a hie manode andwearde  &amp; him forgeaf &d;&ae;t hie moston stondan on frioum anwalde  &amp; him get&ae;hte hw&ae;t hi on &d;&ae;m don sceolden  hw&ae;t ne scolden. 
 &D;a giet stodon men to him gewende. 
 Ac &d;a hie wendon hiera b&ae;c to him  &d;a hi ofermodgiende his gebod forhogdon. 
 &amp; &d;eah  &d;eah hi hine oferhogden   ne forhogde he hi no ne ne forlet: &d;&ae;t he gecy&d;de  &d;a &d;a he him sealde &ae;  &amp; hi mid &d;&ae;re ham gela&d;ode  &amp; oft sende his englas us ham to spananne to him  &amp; on &d;issum deadlican fl&ae;sce he hine selfne &ae;teowde. 
 &D;a he &d;is eal dyde  &d;a he stod &ae;fter us gewend  &amp; clipode &ae;fter us  &d;eah we from him gewende w&ae;ren; 
 &amp; &d;eah he oferhogod w&ae;re  he us eft la&d;ude to his hyldo. 
 Ac swa swa we nu &d;is reahton be eallum monnum  swa hit m&ae;g &ae;ghwelc mon be him anum ge&d;encean  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;ghwelc mon &d;e his bebod &amp; his forbod ongiet  he bi&d; swelce he beforan him stonde  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e he gesyngige. 
 &D;onne giet he stent beforan him  &d;onne he hine ne forhyge&d;  ac for his ege forbier&d; &d;&ae;t he ne synga&d;. 
 Ac &d;onne he forl&ae;t his godnesse &amp; his unscea&d;fulnesse  &amp; gecist unryhtwisnesse  &amp; &d;a gefreme&d;  &d;onne went he his hrycg to him. 
 Ac &d;eah &d;onne giet him fylg&d; God  &amp; him &ae;fter cliopa&d;  &d;onne he hine mona&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;re gedonan scylde  &amp; hine sp&ae;n&d; &d;&ae;t he to him gecierre. 
 &D;a scylda he nyle gesion  &amp; &d;one fromweardan he ciege&d;  &amp; &d;one greadan his arf&ae;stnesse &amp; his frofre he gebr&ae;t ongean &d;a &d;e to him gecierra&d;. 
 &D;onne we gehira&d; under b&ae;c &d;&ae;s maniendes stemne  &d;onne we to him gecierra&d;  &d;onne &d;onne he us ciege&d; huru &ae;fter urum scyldum  &d;onne he us &ae;fter cliopa&d;  &d;eah we &ae;r nolden &ae;fter his lare. 
 Hit is cyn &d;&ae;t we ure scomigen  &d;onne he us &ae;fter cliopa&d;  gif we us nylla&d; ondr&ae;dan his ryhtwisnesse  for&d;&ae;m we hine mid swa micle maran unryhte &amp; dysige oferhycgea&d; swa he l&ae;s forhoga&d; &d;&ae;t he us &d;onne giet to him spane  si&d;&d;an we hiene oferhycggea&d;. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manigenne &d;a &d;e &d;onne giet ungefandod habba&d; fl&ae;sclicra scylda  &d;&ae;tte hie swa micle swi&d;or &d;one spild &d;&ae;s hryres him ondr&ae;den &d;onne &d;a o&d;re swa hi ufor stonda&d; &d;onne &d;a o&d;re. 
 Hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi witen swa swa hie on hira stede gestonda&d; swa him mare gescot &amp; ma flana hiera feonda to cym&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m he ongit swa micle swi&d;ur him on feohtan swa he hine selfne untrumran gefred on his lichoman. 
 Ac gif he &d;onne &d;&ae;m wi&d;stent  &d;onne ongit he swa micle maran sige on him selfum swa he unie&d; wi&d;stod. 
 Ac hie sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie unablinnendlice &d;ara leana wilnigen  &amp; lustlice &d;&ae;t geswinc &d;&ae;ra costunga &d;e hi &d;rowia&d; hi forsion &amp; ge&d;olien  &amp; buton tweon hi geliefen &d;ara leana; for&d;&ae;m  gif hie ge&d;encea&d; &d;ara ges&ae;l&d;a &d;e him ungeendode &ae;fter &d;&ae;m geswincum becuman sculon  &d;onne &d;ynca&d; him &d;y leohtran &d;a geswinc &d;e ofergan sculon. 
 Hi sculon gehieran hw&ae;t &d;urh Essaias &d;one witgan gecweden is  he cw&ae;&d;: &d;is cwi&d; Dryhten: &d;a afyrdan  &d;a &d;e behealda&d; minne r&ae;sted&ae;g  &amp; geceosa&d; &d;&ae;t ic wille  &amp; minne freondscipe geheal&d;a&d;  ic him selle on minum huse  &amp; binnan minum wealle  wic &amp; beteran noman &d;onne o&d;rum minum sunum o&d;&d;e dohtrum. 
 Hw&ae;t elles getacnia&d; &d;a afyrdan buton &d;a &d;a &d;e of&d;rysca&d; &d;a styringe &d;&ae;s fl&ae;sclican lustes  &amp; of him selfum aceorfa&d; unryhtlico weorc? 
 &D;&ae;m monnum is gecy&d;ed hwelce stowe hi moton habban beforan urum f&ae;der  swa swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don  &d;&ae;t hie sceolden habban ece eardungstowe on &d;&ae;s f&ae;der huse fur&d;or &d;onne his &ae;gnu bearn. 
 Hi sculon gehieran hw&ae;t &d;urh sanctus Iohannes gecweden is  he cw&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t sindan &d;a &d;a &d;e mid wifum ne beo&d; besmitene  &amp; hira m&ae;ge&d;had habba&d; gehealdenne; 
 &D;a folgia&d; &d;&ae;m lambe  swa hw&ae;r swa hit f&ae;r&d;. 
 &D;a singa&d; &d;one sang &d;e nan mon elles singan ne m&ae;g  buton &d;&ae;t hundteontig &amp; feowertig &amp; feower &d;usendo. 
 &D;&ae;m is sundorlic sang to singanne mid &d;&ae;m lambe on ecnesse beforan eallum geleaffullum  &amp; to blissianne for hira fl&ae;sces cl&ae;nnesse  &d;&ae;tte &d;a o&d;re gecorenan &d;one song gehiran m&ae;gen  &d;eah &d;e hine swa singan ne m&ae;gen  &amp; for &d;&ae;m lufum &d;e hi to him habba&d;  &amp; for &d;&ae;m weor&d;scipe &d;e hi gesio&d; &d;&ae;t hie habba&d; hi f&ae;gnigen  &amp; emnswi&d;e him blissigen  &d;eah hie &d;a geearnunga n&ae;bben &d;&ae;t hi &d;one weor&d;scipe habban m&ae;gen. 
 Gehieren eac &d;a &d;e ungefandod habba&d; &d;ara fl&ae;sclicana scylda hw&ae;t sio so&d;f&ae;s&d;nes &d;urh hie selfe cw&ae;&d; bi &d;&ae;re cl&ae;nnesse  he cw&ae;&d;: Ne underfo&d; no ealle men &d;as lare.

 Eac sint to manienne &d;a &d;e ungefandod habba&d; &d;&ae;s lichoman scylda &d;&ae;t hie witen &d;&ae;t se m&ae;g&d;had is hirra &d;onne se gesinscipe  &amp; swa&d;eah hi sint to l&ae;ranne &d;&ae;t hi hi ne ahebben ofer &d;a o&d;re;

 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten on &d;&ae;m feower &amp; hundnigontigo&d;an psalme  hit is gecweden: Wuton cuman &ae;r his dome andettende.

 We habba&d; geascod from urum &ae;restan m&ae;ge Adame &d;&ae;t us is from him gecynde &d;&ae;t we &ae;lc yfel on &d;rio wisan &d;urhtion: &d;urh gespan  &amp; &d;urh lustfulnesse  &amp; &d;urh ge&d;afunga.
