 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten &d;&ae;t se hund wille etan &d;&ae;t he &ae;r aspaw  &amp; sio sugu hi wille sylian on hire sole &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e hio a&d;w&ae;gen bi&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t  se hund wile aspiwan &d;one mete &d;e hine hefega&d; on his breostum  &amp; &d;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t he for hefignesse aspaw  &d;onne he hit eft frit  &d;onne gehefega&d; hine &d;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t hine &ae;r gelihte . 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e &d;a gedonan yfelu hreowsia&d;  &d;onne hi &d;&ae;t yfel mid ondetnesse him of aweorpa&d; &d;&ae;tte hira modes inna&d; yfele &amp; hefiglice mid gefylled w&ae;s  &amp; &d;onne eft fo&d; to &d;&ae;m ilcan &amp; f&ae;ta&d; in &ae;fter &d;&ae;re ondetnesse &d;&ae;t ilce yfel &d;&ae;t hi &ae;r mid &d;&ae;re ondetnesse &amp; hreowsunga utawurpun. 
 Swa &d;et swin  &d;eah hit a&d;w&ae;gen sie  gif hit eft fil&d; on &d;&ae;t sol  &d;onne bi&d; hit fulre &d;onne hit &ae;r w&ae;s  &amp; ne forstent &d;&ae;t &d;weal nauht  &d;eah hit &ae;r a&d;w&ae;gen w&ae;re; 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;m &d;e his gedonan synna wepe&d;  &amp; hi swa&d;eah ne forl&ae;t: hefigran scylde &amp; hefigran witum he hine under&d;iet  gif he hit ne forl&ae;t. 
 For&d;&ae;m he forhogde &d;a forgifnesse &d;e he mid &d;&ae;re hreowsunga begiten h&ae;fde  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wealwode on &d;&ae;m gedrofum w&ae;tere; 
 &amp; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he &ae;r mid &d;&ae;re hreowsunga gecl&ae;nsode he beforan Godes eagum eft afylde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is eft awriten on Salomonnes bocum  hit is awriten: Ne eftga &d;u &d;in word on &d;inum gebede. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;onne &d;&ae;t mon eftgige his word on his gebede  &d;&ae;t mon &ae;fter his hreowsunga gewyrce &d;&ae;t he eft scyle hreowsian. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is eac gecweden &d;urh Essaias &d;one witgan  he cw&ae;&d;: A&d;wea&d; iow  &d;&ae;t ge sin cl&ae;ne. 
 Hw&ae;t  se &d;onne ne rec&d; hw&ae;&d;er he cl&ae;ne sie  &d;e ne sie  se &d;e &ae;fter &d;&ae;re hreowsunga hine ryhtlice &amp; cl&ae;nlice nyle gehealdan: ealne weg hi hi &d;wea&d;  &amp; ne beo&d; hie n&ae;fre cl&ae;ne  &d;eah hi ealneg wepen; 
 Ealneg hi wepa&d;  &amp; &ae;fter &d;&ae;m wope hi gewyrcea&d; &d;&ae;t hi moton eft wepan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is gecweden &d;urh sumne wisne mon: Gif hwa on hand nim&d; hw&ae;t uncl&ae;nes  &amp; hine &ae;fter &d;&ae;m a&d;wih&d;  &amp; &d;onne eft feh&d; on &d;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t he &ae;r feng  hw&ae;t forstent him &d;onne &d;&ae;t &ae;rre &d;weal? 
 Se bi&d; a&d;w&ae;gen of uncl&ae;nnesse  se &d;e a&d;wih&d; mid hreowsunga his uncl&ae;nnesse. 
 Se &d;onne gehrin&d; eft &d;&ae;re uncl&ae;nnesse &d;e synga&d; &ae;fter his hreowsunga. 
 Ac &d;a sint to manienne &d;e &d;a gedonan scylda hreowsia&d;  &amp; hi &d;eah ne forl&ae;ta&d;  &d;&ae;t hi ongieten &d;&ae;t hie beo&d; beforan &d;&ae;s dieglan Deman eagum gelice &d;&ae;m monnum &d;e swi&d;e ea&d;modlice onginna&d; beforon ricum monnum  &amp; him swi&d;e olecca&d; &d;a hwile &d;e hi him beforan beo&d;  &amp; eft  &d;onne hi him be&ae;ftan beo&d;  &d;onne do&d; hi him to demme &amp; to fiondscipe &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hi magon. 
 Hw&ae;t is &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t mon hreowsige his synna  buton &d;&ae;t mon eowa&d; Gode his ea&d;modnesse &amp; his treowa &amp; his hiersumnesse? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t is &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t mon &ae;fter his hreowsunga syngige  buton &d;&ae;t  &d;&ae;t he de&d; feondscipe &amp; ofermetto &amp; unhiersumnesse &d;&ae;m ilcan Gode &d;e he &ae;r olehte? 
 Swa swa Iacobus s&ae;de se apostol  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Swa hwa swa wille bion &d;isse weorlde freond to ungemetlice  he bi&d; gehaten Godes feond. 
 &D;a &d;onne sint to manienne &d;e &d;a gedonan scylda wepa&d;  &amp; hi swa&d;eah ne forl&ae;ta&d;  &d;&ae;tte hi ongiten &d;&ae;tte oft bi&d; swi&d;e idel &amp; unnyt &d;ara yfelena manna hreowsung  &d;onne hi &ae;fter &d;&ae;m ne tilia&d; nau&d;er ne god to donne ne yfel to forl&ae;tanne. 
 Swa bi&d; eac swi&d;e oft synleas yfel ge&d;oht &d;&ae;m godum  &d;onne hi hit mid weorcum ne &d;orhtio&d;. 
 Swa wundorlice hit tod&ae;l&d; &amp; gemetga&d; se godcunda wisdom be hira &ae;g&d;eres geearnungum  swa &d;&ae;tte &d;a yflan betwix eallum hira yflum &d;e hi fullice gefremma&d; hi fortruwia&d;  &amp; hi on ofermetto ahebba&d; for &d;&ae;m lytlan gode &d;e hi ge&d;encea&d;  &amp; no ne anginna&d; to wyrceanne. 
 Ond eft  &d;a godan  &d;onne hi beo&d; onstyrede mid &d;&ae;m yflum ge&d;ohtum &d;e hi n&ae;fre nylla&d; &d;urhtion  &d;onne beo&d; hi geea&d;medde  &amp; forsio&d; hi selfe for &d;&ae;m lytlan yfele  &amp; ne forleosa&d; nauht &d;urh &d;&ae;t hira ryhtwisnesse  ac hi hi geieca&d; mid &d;&ae;re ea&d;modnesse. 
 Hw&ae;t  Balam cw&ae;&d;  &d;a he geseah &d;a wicstowa &d;ara ryhtwisena Israhela: Geweor&d;e min lif swelce &d;issa ryhtwisena  &amp; geweor&d;e min ende swelce hira. 
 Ac eft  &d;a sio anbryrdnes hine alet  &d;a funde he swi&d;e yfel ge&d;eaht &amp; searwa ymb hira lif: for&d;&ae;m hine gehran sio gitsung  he forget &d;one freondscipe wi&d; Israhele. 
 Hw&ae;t  sanctus Paulus cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he gesawe o&d;erne gewunan &amp; o&d;erne willan on his limum  &amp; se w&ae;re feohtende wi&d; &d;&ae;m willan his modes  &amp; hine geh&ae;ftne l&ae;dde on synne gewunan. 
 Sio  he cw&ae;&d;  w&ae;re on his limum. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s sanctus Paulus gecostod mid his modes untrumnesse &d;&ae;t he ongeate his synna  &amp; for&d;&ae;m w&ae;re &d;y strangra on godum weorcum. 
 Forhwy bi&d; se synfulla onbryrd mid &d;&ae;re hreowsunga  &amp; ne bi&d; no &d;y ryhtwisra; 
 O&d;&d;e forhwy bi&d; se ryhtwisa gecostod mid yfle ge&d;ohte  &amp; ne bi&d; &d;eah gewemmed mid &d;&ae;re scylde; 
 Buton for&d;y&d;e &d;&ae;m synfullan nauht ne helpa&d; his godan ge&d;ohtas   for&d;&ae;m&d;e he n&ae;f&d; gearone willan untweogendne to &d;&ae;m weorce  ne eft &d;&ae;m ryhtwisan ne deria&d; his yflan ge&d;ohtas  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he n&ae;f&d; gearone willan &d;&ae;t woh to fulfremmanne? 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e hira synna forl&ae;ta&d;  &amp; hi &d;eah ne beta&d; ne ne hreowsia&d;  &d;&ae;t hi ne wenen  &d;eah hi hira synna forl&ae;ten  &d;&ae;t hi God him forl&ae;te  gif hi hi mid nanum &d;ingum ne beta&d; ne ne hreowsia&d;. 
 Swa se writere  gif he ne dilega&d; &d;&ae;t he &ae;r wrat  &d;eah he n&ae;fre ma nauht ne write  &d;&ae;t bi&d; &d;eah undilegod &d;&ae;t he &ae;r wrat. 
 &amp; swa eac se &d;e o&d;rum bismer cwi&d;  o&d;&d;e de&d;  &d;eah he geswice  &amp; hit n&ae;fre eft ne do  &d;eah hit bi&d; gedon &d;&ae;t he dyde  &amp; un&d;ingad  gif he hit ne bet. 
 Ac he sceal &d;a ofermodlican word mid ea&d;modlicum wordum gemetgian  gif he wi&d; &d;one o&d;erne ge&d;ingian wile. 
 Wenstu  gif hwa o&d;rum hw&ae;t gieldan sceal  hw&ae;&d;er he hine mid &d;y gehealdan m&ae;ge &d;&ae;t he him nauht mare on ne nime  ne &d;&ae;t ne gielde &d;&ae;t he &ae;r nam? 
 Swa us bi&d; &ae;t Gode  &d;onne we wi&d; hine gesyngia&d;: &d;eah we n&ae;bre eft swa ne don  gif we &d;&ae;t gedone mid nanum &d;ingum ne beta&d; ne ne hreowsia&d;  ne bio we no &d;&ae;s sicore  gif us &d;&ae;t ne mislica&d; &d;&ae;t us &ae;r licode  &d;onne ne bi&d; hit no us f&ae;rgiefen  &d;eah we nu nauht yfeles ne don on &d;isse worulde. 
 Ne sculon we &d;eah for&d;y bion to orsorge  gif we nauht to gode ne do&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e swi&d;e fela unalefedes we oft ge&d;encea&d;. 
 Hu m&ae;g se &d;onne bion orsorg se &d;e him self wat &d;&ae;t he gesynga&d;? 
 Hwelce i&d;nesse h&ae;f&d; God &ae;t urum witum  o&d;&d;e hwelcne weor&d;scipe h&ae;f&d; he &ae;t urre &d;rowunga  butan &d;&ae;t he wile geh&ae;lan &d;a wunde urra scylda mid strangum l&ae;cedome  gif he ne m&ae;g mid li&d;um  &d;&ae;tte us biterige sio hreowsung  swa swa us &ae;r swetedon &d;a synna? 
 &amp; swa swa we sigon &ae;r on &d;&ae;t unaliefede  o&d;&d;&ae;t we afeollon  swa we sculon nu forberan &d;&ae;t aliefede  o&d;&d;&ae;t we arisen; 
 &D;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte w&ae;s abisegad mid unryhtre blisse si eft abisegad on halwyndre &amp; on ryhtlicre hreowsunga  swa &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte sio upah&ae;fenes &amp; &d;a ofermetto gewundedon eft geh&ae;le sio ea&d;modnes &amp; sio forsewennes his selfes. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Dauid on &d;&ae;m feower &amp; hundsiofantigo&d;an psalme: Ic cw&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m unryhtwisum  ne do ge unryhtwislice  &amp; cw&ae;&d; to &d;&ae;m &d;e &d;&ae;r syngedon  ne hebbe ge to up eowre hornas. 
 &D;onne ahebba&d; &d;a synfullan swi&d;e up hira hornas  &d;onne hi hi n&ae;fre nylla&d; geea&d;medan to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hie ongieten hira unryhtwisnesse  &amp; &d;a hreowsian. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s eft gecweden on &d;&ae;m fiftego&d;an psalme: &d;a gedrefedan heortan &amp; &d;a geea&d;meddan ne forsih&d; hi n&ae;fre Dryhten. 
 Swa hwa &d;onne swa his synna hreowsa&d;  &amp; hi swa&d;eah ne forl&ae;t  se gedref&d; his heortan  &amp; &d;eah oferhyg&d; &d;&ae;t he hi geea&d;mede. 
 Se &d;onne  se &d;e his synna forl&ae;t  &amp; hi swa&d;eah ne hreowsa&d;  se hine ea&d;med  &amp; nyle &d;eah his mod gedrefan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus on his &ae;rendgewrite to Corinctheum  he cw&ae;&d;: Ge w&ae;ron &ae;r on yflum weorcum  ac ge sint nu gecl&ae;nsode &amp; gehalgode. 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;ghwelc man bi&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;re hreowsunga his synna cl&ae;nra &d;onne he &ae;r w&ae;s  &ae;r he gesyngade. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; sanctus Petrus  &d;a he geseah manige men ormode for hira &ae;rron yflun  he cw&ae;&d;: Hreowsia&d; &amp; weor&d;a&d; gefulwade eower &ae;lc. 
 &AE;rest he l&ae;rde &d;&ae;t hi hreowsodon  &amp; si&d;&d;an &d;&ae;t hi wurden gefullwode  swelce he cw&ae;de: Hreowsia&d; &ae;rest on eowrum mode  &amp; si&d;&d;an &ae;fter fierste a&d;wea&d; eow  &amp; gecl&ae;nsia&d; mid eowrum tearum. 
 Hu m&ae;g se bion orsorg &d;&ae;re wrace his scylda  se &d;e nu agiemeleasa&d; &d;&ae;t he hreowsige his synna? 
 Hu m&ae;g he hira bion orsorg  nu se hiehsta hierde &d;&ae;re halgan ciricean cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;tte sio hreowsung scolde bion &ae;r &d;&ae;m fulwihte? 
 Se fullwuht &d;one mon gecl&ae;nsa&d; from his synnum  &amp; ealra &d;inga swi&d;os&d; &d;a synna adw&ae;sc&d;. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e &d;a unaliefedan &d;ing  &d;a &d;e hi do&d;  heriga&d;; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;e hi t&ae;la&d;  &amp; swa&d;eah do&d;. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e &d;&ae;t unliefde heriga&d;  &amp; eac do&d;; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;e hit lea&d;  &amp; swa&d;eah do&d;. 
 &D;a sint to manienne  &d;a &d;e &ae;g&d;er ge hit do&d; ge hit heriga&d;  &d;&ae;t hi ongieten &d;&ae;t hi oft swi&d;or gensyngia&d; mid &d;&ae;m wordum &d;onne hi don mid &d;&ae;m d&ae;dum; 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;onne hi yfel do&d;  &d;onne do&d; hi &d;&ae;t him anum  ac &d;onne hi hit heria&d;  &d;onne l&ae;ra&d; hi hit &ae;lcne &d;ara &d;e hit gehier&d; herian. 
 For&d;y hi sint to manienne  &d;onne hi licetta&d; &d;&ae;t hi willen astyfecian &d;&ae;t yfel on him selfum  &d;&ae;t hi hit &d;onne ne dyrren s&ae;wan on o&d;rum monnum; 
 Ac &d;&ae;t him &d;ynce genog on &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi hit selfe dydon. 
 Ond eft hi sint to manienne  &d;eah hi him nyllen &d;&ae;t ondr&ae;dan &d;&ae;t hi yfele sien  &d;&ae;t hi huru scamige &d;&ae;t men witen hwelce hi sin. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft &d;&ae;t yfel &d;&ae;t forholen bi&d;  hit bi&d; fleonde  for&d;&ae;m  &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod sceama&d; &d;&ae;t hit mon wite  &d;onne m&ae;g hit ea&d;e ges&ae;lan &ae;t sumum cierre &d;&ae;t hine eac scamige &d;&ae;t he hit wyrce. 
 Hw&ae;t  &ae;lc unryhtwis mon  swa he scamleaslicor his yfel cy&d;  swa he freolicor hit &d;urhtieh&d;  &amp; hit him aliefedlicre &d;ync&d;. 
 Swa hit him &d;onne aliefedlicre &d;ync&d;  swa he &d;&ae;r diopor on gedyf&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten on Essaies bocum: Hi l&ae;rdon hira synna swa swa Sodome dydon  &amp; hi hi nanwuht ne h&ae;lon. 
 Gif Sodome hira synne h&ae;len  &d;onne ne syngodon hi na butan ege  ac hi forleton eallinga &d;one bridels &d;&ae;s eges  &d;a hi ne scrifon hw&ae;&d;er hit w&ae;re &d;e d&ae;g &d;e niht  &d;onne &d;onne hi syngodon. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is eft awriten on Genesis &d;&ae;tte swi&d;e w&ae;re gemanigfal&d;od Sodomwara hream &amp; Gomorwara. 
 Se cliopa&d;  se &d;e dearninga synga&d;; 
 Ac se hrem&d;  se &d;e openlice &amp; orsorglice synga&d;. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e hira synna onscunia&d;  &amp; swa&d;eah ne forl&ae;ta&d;  &d;&ae;t hi fore&d;onclice ongieten hu hi hi willen beladian on &d;&ae;m miclan dome  &d;onne hi hi nylla&d; her beladian mid&d;&ae;m&d;&ae;t hi him selfum demen  &amp; hiora agna scylda on him selfum wrecen. 
 Hw&ae;t bio&d; hi elles buton liceteras  &d;onne hi t&ae;la&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hi nylla&d; forl&ae;tan? 
 Ac hie sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi ongieten &d;&ae;t hit bi&d; se degla Godes dom &d;&ae;t hi eft &d;y mare wite h&ae;bben &d;e hi gere witon &d;&ae;t hi on &d;weorh do&d;  &amp; &d;eah nylla&d; geswican  ne nanwuht ymb &d;&ae;t swincan &d;&ae;t hi hit m&ae;gen forl&ae;tan. 
 Swa hi hit &d;onne swutolor witon  swa hi swi&d;ur forweor&d;a&d;  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi onfengon &d;&ae;t leoht &d;&ae;s ondgietes  &amp; &d;eah noldon forl&ae;tan &d;a &d;istro &d;&ae;s won weorces  ac &d;&ae;t andgiet &d;&ae;t him God sende to fultome hi agimeleasedon. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce andgit bi&d; eft on gewitnesse hira yfela &ae;t &d;&ae;m dome  &amp; geiec&d; hira witu &d;&ae;tte him &ae;r w&ae;s onsended mid to dielgianne hira synna. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi her syngia&d;  &amp; hit him no ne hreow&d;  hi gehrin&d; her sumu wracu &ae;r &d;&ae;m ecum witum &d;&ae;t hi ne sien freo ne orsorge on &d;&ae;m anbide &d;&ae;s maran wites. 
 Ac swa micle hi onfo&d; &d;&ae;r mare wite swa hi her gearor witon &d;&ae;t hi untela do&d;  &amp; hit &d;eah nylla&d; forl&ae;tan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Crist on his godspelle: Se &d;egn  se &d;e wat his hlafordes willan  &amp; &d;onne nyle wyrcean &ae;fter his hlafordes willan  he bi&d; manigra wita wyr&d;e. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan cw&ae;&d; eac se salmscop on &d;&ae;m feower &amp; fiftiogo&d;an psalme  he cw&ae;&d;: Hi sculon gan libbende on helle. 
 &D;a &d;e libbende bio&d;  hi witon &amp; ongieta&d; hw&ae;t ymb hi gedon bi&d;; &d;a deadan ne magon nanwuht witan. 
 &D;a bio&d; genemde deade  &amp; &d;a stiga&d; on helle  &d;a &d;e nyton hwonne hi untela do&d;; 
 Ac &d;a &d;e hit witon  &amp; swa&d;eah do&d;  &d;a ga&d; libbende &amp; witende on helle. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice bio&d; oferswi&d;de mid sumre unryhtgewilnunge; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e longe &ae;r ymb&d;eahtigea&d;  &amp; hit &d;onne on las&d; &d;urhtio&d;. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e mid f&ae;rlice luste bio&d; oferswi&d;de  on o&d;re &d;a &d;e lange ymb&d;encea&d; &amp; &d;eahtia&d;  &amp; swa weor&d;a&d; beswicene. 
 &D;a &d;onne sint to manienne &d;e mid f&ae;rlice luste bio&d; beswicene  &d;&ae;t hi ongieten &d;&ae;t hi &ae;lce d&ae;ge beo&d; on &d;&ae;m gefeohte &d;isses andweardan lifes. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte ne m&ae;g gesion &d;a flane &ae;r hit sie gewundad  hit be&d;earf &d;&ae;t hit h&ae;bbe simle on honda &d;one scield Godes eges  &amp; him symle ondr&ae;de &d;a diglan gescotu &d;&ae;s sweocolan feondes  &amp; hine w&ae;rlice healde on &d;&ae;re byrg his modes wi&d; nihtlicum gefeohtum  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi willa&d; simle on &d;istrum feohtan. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte n&ae;f&d; singale sorge hit self to behealdanne  &d;onne bi&d; hit on sume healfe open to wundianne; 
 For&d;&ae;m se lytega feond swa micle ie&d;elicor &d;&ae;t mod gewunda&d; swa he hit ongiet nacodre &d;&ae;re byrnan w&ae;rscipes. 
 For&d;y sint &d;a to manienne &d;a &d;e mid hr&ae;dlice luste bio&d; oferswi&d;de  &d;&ae;t hie to georne ne giemen &d;issa eor&d;licena ymbhogena  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi ne magon ongietan mid hu manugum un&d;eawum hi beo&d; gewundode  &d;a hwile &d;e hi to ungemetlice smeaga&d; ymb &d;as eor&d;lecan &d;ing. 
 Be &d;&ae;m s&ae;de Salomon &d;&ae;t se mon sceolde cwe&d;an  se &d;e w&ae;s sl&ae;pende gewundad: Hi me wundedon  &amp; ic hit ne gefredde; 
 Hi me drogon  &amp; ic hit nyste; 
 &amp; sona swa ic anwoc  swa wilnode ic eft wines. 
 Swa bi&d; &d;&ae;t mod sl&ae;pende gewundad swa hit ne gefret  &d;onne hit bi&d; to gimeleas his agenra &d;earfa. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t mod &d;&ae;tte bi&d; mid un&d;eawum oferdrenced  hit ne m&ae;g ongietan &d;a toweardan yfelo  ne fur&d;um &d;a nat &d;e hit de&d;. 
 Hit mon dr&ae;g&d; swa hit ne gefret  &d;onne &d;onne hit iern&d; on &d;a unaliefedan un&d;eawas  &amp; hit swa&d;eah ne onw&ae;cne&d; to &d;on &d;&ae;t hit eft on ierne mid hreowsunga. 
 Ac hit wilna&d; &d;&ae;t hit to &d;on onw&ae;cne &d;&ae;t hit m&ae;ge eft weor&d;an oferdruncen; 
 For&d;&ae;m  &d;eah &d;&ae;t mod sl&ae;pe godra weorca  hit waca&d; hw&ae;&d;&d;re on &d;&ae;m ymbhogum &d;isse worlde  &amp; wilna&d; &d;&ae;t hit sie oferdruncen his agnes willan. 
 Swa hit gebyre&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t mod sl&ae;p&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e hit wacian sceolde  &amp; waca&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e hit slapan scolde. 
 Be &d;&ae;s modes sl&ae;pe w&ae;s &ae;r awriten on &d;&ae;re ilcan Salomonnes bec  hit w&ae;s awriten &d;&ae;t hit w&ae;re swelce se stiora slepe on midre s&ae;  &amp; forlure &d;&ae;t stiorro&d;ur. 
 &D;&ae;m stiorere bi&d; gelicost se mon &d;e ongemong &d;isses middangeardes costungum &amp; ongemong &d;&ae;m y&d;um un&d;eawa hine agimeleasa&d;. 
 Se de&d; swa se stiora &d;e &d;&ae;t stiorro&d;or forlies&d;  se &d;e forl&ae;t &d;one ymbhogan &amp; &d;a geornfulnesse &d;e he mid stioran scolde &d;&ae;re sawle &amp; &d;&ae;m lichoman. 
 Se bi&d; swi&d;e onlic &d;&ae;m stioran &d;e his stiorro&d;or forliest on s&ae;  se &d;e forl&ae;t &d;one fore&d;onc his gesceadwisnesse ongemong &d;&ae;m bisegum &d;isses middangeardes. 
 Ac gif se stiora his stiorro&d;or gehilt  &d;onne cym&d; he orsorglice to lande  hwilum &d;eah ongean wind &amp; ongean &d;a y&d;a  hwilum mid &ae;g&d;rum. 
 Swa de&d; &d;&ae;t mod  &d;onne hit wacorlice stiere&d; &d;&ae;re sawle: sume un&d;eawas hit ofertrit  sume hit &ae;r gesih&d;  &amp; utan becier&d;; 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hit &d;a gedonan un&d;eawas swincende gebete  &amp; &d;a ungedonan fore&d;oncelice becierre  swa se stiora de&d;: sume &d;a y&d;a he becer&d; mid &d;y scipe  sume hit oferstig&d;. 
 Ymb &d;&ae;t is eft gecweden on &d;&ae;m Salomones bocum &d;e we hata&d; Cantica Canticorum be &d;&ae;m strengestan cempum &d;&ae;s uplican e&d;les  hit is gecweden: H&ae;bbe eower &ae;lc his sweord be his &d;eo for nihtlecum ege. 
 &D;onne mon h&ae;f&d; his sweord be his &d;io  &d;onne mon teme&d; his unaliefde lustas mid &d;&ae;m wordum &d;&ae;re halgan lare. 
 &amp; sio niht getacna&d; &d;a &d;istro &d;&ae;re blindnesse urre tidernesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e nan mon ne m&ae;g on niht gesion hu neah him hwelc frecenes sie  him is &d;earf &d;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe his sweord be his hype. 
 Swa sculon &d;a halgan weras simle stondan gearuwe to gefohte wi&d; &d;&ae;m lytegan fiende  for&d;&ae;m hi him ondr&ae;da&d; &d;a frecenesse &d;e hi ne gesio&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is eft gecweden on &d;&ae;re Salomones bec &d;e we hata&d; Cantica Canticorum  hit is gecweden: &d;in nosu is swelce se torr on Libano. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t we oft gestinca&d; mid urum nosum &d;&ae;t we mid urum eagum gesion ne magon. 
 Mid &d;&ae;m nosum we tosceada&d; &amp; tocnawa&d; gode stencas &amp; yfele. 
 Hw&ae;t is elles getacnod &d;urh &d;a nosu buton se fore&d;onc &amp; sio gesceadwisnes &d;ara godena manna? 
 Hw&ae;t elles getacna&d; se hea torr on Libano buton &d;one hean fore&d;onc &amp; &d;a gesceadwisnesse &d;ara godena monna  &d;a sculon ongietan &d;a costunga &amp; &d;&ae;t gefeoht  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e hit cume  &d;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen &d;y f&ae;stor gestondan  &d;onne hit cume? 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;lc here h&ae;f&d; &d;y l&ae;ssan cr&ae;ft &d;onne he cym&d;  gif hine mon &ae;r wat  &ae;r he cume; 
 For&d;&ae;m he gesih&d; &d;a gearwe &d;e he wende &d;&ae;t he sceolde ungearwe findan. 
 Him w&ae;re &d;onne ie&d;re &d;&ae;t he hira &ae;r gearra wende &d;onne he hira ungearra wende  &amp; hi &d;onne gearuwe mette. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e &ae;r &d;encea&d; to syngianne  &amp; ymb&d;eahtia&d;  &ae;r hi hit &d;urhtion  &d;&ae;t hi ongiten mid fore&d;onclicre gesceadwisnesse &d;&ae;t hi on&ae;la&d; &d;earlran dom wi&d; him mid &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi her ymb &d;&ae;t yfel &d;eahtia&d;  &ae;r hi hit don  &amp; hi beo&d; mid swa micle strengran cwide &d;&ae;s domes gesl&ae;gene swa hi beo&d; f&ae;stor gebundne mid &d;&ae;m bende &d;&ae;s yflan ge&d;eahtes. 
 Micle hr&ae;dlicor hi w&ae;ren a&d;w&ae;gene &d;&ae;ra scylda mid &d;&ae;re hreowsunga  gif hi f&ae;rlecor syngoden unbe&d;ohte. 
 Ac hi beo&d; &d;&ae;s &d;e lator &d;e hi oftor ymb&d;eahtia&d;; 
 For&d;&ae;m  gif &d;&ae;t mod eallunga &ae;r ne forsawe &d;a ecan edlean  &d;onne ne gesirede hit no &d;&ae;t hit &d;urhtuge swelce synne. 
 Swa micel toscead is betwuh &d;&ae;re be&d;ohtan synne  &d;e mon longe ymbsire&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;re &d;e mon f&ae;rlice &d;urhtieh&d;; 
 Swa &d;&ae;tte se se &d;e &d;a synne gesire&d;  &ae;g&d;er ge gesynga&d;  ge eac sy&d;&d;an hwilum on ormodnesse gewit. 
 For&d;&ae;m ne t&ae;lde Dryhten &d;a twa scylda gelice. 
 &D;&ae;t he cy&d;de  &d;a he cw&ae;&d; &d;urh Ieremias &d;one witgan: Healda&d; eow &d;&ae;t ge ne on&ae;len min ierre mid eowrum searwum  &d;&ae;t ge hit ne m&ae;gen eft adw&ae;scan. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ilcan he cw&ae;&d; eft ierrenga &d;urh &d;one ilcan witgan  he cw&ae;&d;: Ic write on eow &ae;fter eowrum ge&d;eahte. 
 &D;y ne wric&d; Dryhten no gelice &d;a gesiredan synne &amp; &d;a f&ae;rlice &d;urhtogenan  for&d;&ae;m sio gesirede syn bi&d; ungelic eallum o&d;rum synnum. 
 Ac sio &d;e hr&ae;dlice &d;urhtogen bi&d;  sio bi&d; hwilum for giemeleste  hwilum for untrymnesse modes o&d;&d;e lichoman. 
 Sio &d;onne &d;e longe gesired bi&d;  sio cym&d; symle of yflum inge&d;once. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecweden swi&d;e ryhte &d;urh &d;one psalmscop on &d;&ae;re heringe &d;&ae;s eadgan weres  &amp; on &d;&ae;m forman psalme  hit is gecweden &d;&ae;t he no ne s&ae;te on &d;&ae;m wolberendan setle. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s &d;is gecweden &d;e hit is swi&d;e gewunelic &d;&ae;tte domeras &amp; rice menn on setelum sitten. 
 Se &d;onne sit on woles setle  se &d;e yfel wyrc&d; mid ge&d;eahte. 
 &amp; se sit eac on wolberendum setle  se &d;e gesceadwislice tocnawan con god &amp; yfel  &amp; &d;eah geleorna&d; &d;&ae;t he de&d; &d;&ae;t yfel. 
 Se sit  swelce he sitte on &d;&ae;m stole &d;&ae;s forhwierfdan gemotes  se &d;e hine upahefe&d; on &d;a ofermetto swelcre unryhtwisnesse &d;&ae;tte he fullfremme hwelc yfel huru &d;urh ge&d;eaht. 
 For&d;&ae;m swa micle swa se bi&d; beforan &d;e on &d;&ae;m stole sitt &d;&ae;m o&d;rum &d;e &d;&ae;r ymb stonda&d;  sw&ae; bi&d; sio syn &d;e longe &ae;r ge&d;oht bi&d;  &amp; &d;onne &d;urhtogen  ofer &d;a &d;e f&ae;rlice ge&d;oht bi&d;  &amp; &d;onne &d;urhtogen. 
 For&d;&ae;m sint to manianne &d;a &d;e lange ymbsieria&d; &d;&ae;t hi ongieten hu micel wite hi sculun habban beforan &d;&ae;m o&d;rum  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi nu nylla&d; bion &d;ara synnfullena geferan  ac willa&d; bion hira ealdormenn. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monienne &d;a &d;e oftr&ae;dlice lytla scylda wyrcea&d;; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hi gehealda&d; wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda  &amp; &d;eah hwiltidum afella&d; on hefegum scyldum. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e oftr&ae;dlice syngia&d;  &amp; &d;eah lytlum scyldum; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hie wi&d; &d;a l&ae;ssan scylda bewarenia&d;  &amp; &d;eah hwilum afealla&d; on micla scylda. 
 Hi sint to manienne  &d;onne hi oft syngia&d;  &d;eah hi lytlum syngien  &d;&ae;t hie ma &d;encen hu manega synna hi fremma&d; &d;onne hi &d;encen hu micle hi hie gefremmen; 
 &amp; gif hi oferhycgen &d;&ae;t hi him ondr&ae;den hiora lytlan synna  &d;onne &d;onne hi hi gesio&d;  ondr&ae;den hi him huru  &d;onne hi hi hrima&d;. 
 Swi&d;e lytle beo&d; &d;a dropan &d;&ae;s smalan renes  ac hi wyrcea&d; &d;eah swi&d;e micel flod &amp; swi&d;e strongne stream  &d;onne hi gegaddrode beo&d;  for&d;on&d;e hira bi&d; swi&d;e fela. 
 Swi&d;e lytlum sicera&d; &d;&ae;t w&ae;ter &amp; swi&d;e degellice on &d;&ae;t hlece scip  &amp; &d;eah hit wilna&d; &d;&ae;s ilcan &d;e sio hlude y&d; de&d; on &d;&ae;re hreon s&ae;  buton hit mon &ae;r utaweorpe. 
 Swi&d;e lytle bio&d; &d;a wunda on &d;&ae;m hreofan lice  &amp; &d;eah  gif sio hreofl hit eal oferg&ae;&d;  hio gede&d; &d;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t sio micle wund gede&d; on &d;&ae;m breostum. 
 Be &d;&ae;m is awriten on Salomonnes bocum &d;&ae;tte se  se &d;e nylle onscunian his lytlan scylda  &d;&ae;t he wille gelisian to maran. 
 &amp; gif he agiemeleasa&d; &d;&ae;t he &d;a lytlan hreowsige  &amp; hwilum forcierre  he wile afeallan on &d;a miclan  &d;eah hit late sie. 
 Ac hi sint to manienne  &d;onne hi oft syngia&d; lytlum  &d;&ae;t hie geornlice ongieten &d;&ae;t mon oft wyrs gesynga&d; on &d;&ae;m lytlum synnum &d;onne on &d;&ae;m miclum  for&d;&ae;m hi mon ongin&d; swa micle &ae;r betan swa hie mon &ae;r ongiet; 
 Ac &d;a lytlan mon ne gelef&d; to nanre synne  ac nim&d; hi to gewunan  &amp; hi &d;onne &d;y earfo&d;licor gebet. 
 &D;onon cym&d; oft &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t mod him &ae;rest na ne ondr&ae;t &d;a lytlan scylda  ne  &d;onne on last  &d;a miclan. 
 Ac hit gewuna&d; to &d;&ae;m synnum o&d; hit becym&d; to sumum ealdordome &d;ara scylda  &amp; &d;onne swa micle l&ae;s onscuna&d; &d;a miclan swa hit &ae;r orsorglicor gewunode to &d;&ae;m lytlum  &amp; him &d;a l&ae;s ondred. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e hi gehealda&d; wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda  &amp; hwilum &d;eah gedufa&d; on &d;&ae;m miclum  hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi geornlice hi selfe ongieten  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hiora mod bi&d; swi&d;e oft upah&ae;fen  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi hi habba&d; swa w&ae;rlice gehealden wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda. 
 Ac him is &d;earf &d;&ae;t hi for &d;&ae;re orsorgnesse ne &d;urhtion hefigran scylda  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hi for hira upah&ae;fennesse ne befeallen on &d;one pytt ofermetta  &d;yl&ae;s hi forswelge sio swelgend &d;&ae;re upah&ae;fenesse. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft  &d;onne hi oferswi&d;a&d; utane &d;a lytlan scylda  hi a&d;inda&d; innane on idlum gilpe. 
 &amp; &d;onne &d;&ae;t mod bi&d; innan oferswi&d;ed mid &d;&ae;m ofermettum  hi toflowa&d; swi&d;e hr&ae;&d;e ut  &amp; &ae;tiewa&d; on openum yfle. 
 For&d;&ae;m sint to manienne &d;a &d;e hi wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda gehealda&d;  ond &d;eah hwilum gedufa&d; on &d;&ae;m miclum  hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi hi behealden &d;&ae;t hi innan ne afeallen &d;onon &d;e hi wena&d; &d;&ae;t hi utan stonden  &d;yl&ae;s sio upah&ae;fenes for &d;&ae;re lytlan ryhtwisnesse him weor&d;e to wege micelre scylde &ae;fter &d;&ae;s &d;earlwisan Deman dome &amp; edleane. 
 Ac &d;onne hi wena&d; &d;&ae;t hi of hira &ae;gnum m&ae;gene hi h&ae;bben gehealden wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda  &d;onne weor&d;a&d; hi swi&d;e ryhtlice forl&ae;tene from Gode  o&d;&d;&ae;t hi afealla&d; on maran scylda; 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi ongiten feallende &d;&ae;t hie &ae;r hiora agnes &d;onces ne stodon  &d;&ae;tte &d;&ae;t mod  &d;e &ae;r w&ae;s upah&ae;fen for lytlum gode  si &d;onne gebiged to miclum yfele. 
 Ac hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hie ongieten &d;&ae;t hie oft gesyngia&d; giet wyrs on &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi hi warenia&d; wi&d; &d;a lytlan scylda &d;onne hi don on miclum scyldum; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e hi licetta&d; hie unscyldge  &d;onne hi hi w&ae;renia&d; wi&d; &d;a lytlan. 
 Ac hi hi ne ladia&d; nowiht  &d;onne hi wyrca&d; &d;a miclan &amp; &d;a openan. 
 &D;&ae;t is open yfel beforan Gode &d;&ae;t mon &d;a miclan do  ac &d;&ae;t is licettung haligdomes for monnum &d;&ae;t mon &d;a lytlan forga  &amp; &d;a miclan do. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecweden on &d;&ae;m godspelle to Fariseum &d;&ae;t hi wi&d;bleowen &d;&ae;re fleogan  &amp; forswulgun &d;one olfend. 
 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: &d;a lytlan yflu ge fleo&d;  &amp; &d;a miclan ge freta&d;. 
 &D;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t ilce &d;&ae;t eft w&ae;s get&ae;led &d;urh &d;one mu&d; &d;&ae;re So&d;f&ae;stnesse  &d;&ae;t is Crist  he cw&ae;&d;: Ge tiogo&d;ia&d; eowre mintan &amp; eowerne dile &amp; eowerne kymen  &amp; l&ae;ta&d; untiogo&d;ad &d;&ae;tte diorwyr&d;re is eowra o&d;ra &ae;hta  &amp; &d;a bebodu &d;e giet maran sint on &d;&ae;re &ae;we ge no ne healda&d;: &d;&ae;t is ryht dom &amp; mildheortnes &amp; treowa. 
 Nis us nawht recceleaslice to gehiranne &d;&ae;tte he nemde &d;a undiorestan wyrta &d;e on wyrttunum weaxe  &amp; &d;eah swi&d;e welstincenda. 
 &D;urh &d;one stenc sint getacnode &d;a liceteras  &d;e willa&d; habban &d;one hlisan haligdomes  &amp; don &d;eah lytel godes; 
 &amp; &d;eah hi for micel god ne don  hi wilnia&d; &d;&ae;t hi micel &d;yncen  &amp; hi mon widherge. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e nanwuht godes ne onginna&d;; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e hit onginna&d;  &amp; wel ne geendia&d;. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e nan god ne onginna&d;; 
 On o&d;re &d;a &d;e hit onginna&d;  &amp; no ne geendia&d;. 
 &D;a &d;onne &d;e nan god ne onginna&d;  ne sint hi no to l&ae;renne hw&ae;t hi don scylen  &ae;r him si belagen &d;&ae;t hi &d;onne do&d;; 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e hi nylla&d; underfon &d;&ae;t uncu&d;e &d;&ae;t hi gehira&d;  buton hi &ae;r ongieten hu frecenlic &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hi cunnon; 
 For&d;&ae;m nan mon ne bitt o&d;erne &d;&ae;t he hine r&ae;re  gif he self nat &d;&ae;t he afeallen bi&d;; 
 Ne eac se  se his wunde sar ne gefret ne wilna&d; he nanes l&ae;ces. 
 For&d;y him is &ae;rest to cy&d;anne hu idel &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hi lufia&d; &amp; hu unnytt  &amp; si&d;&d;an him is to reccanne hu nyttwyr&d;e &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hi forl&ae;ten habba&d;. 
 &AE;rest hi sculon ongietan &d;&ae;t hi fleon &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hi lufia&d;. 
 &D;onne magon hi si&d; ie&d;elice ongietan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t is to lufianne &d;&ae;t hi &ae;r flugon. 
 Micle &d;y bet hi underfo&d; &d;&ae;t uncu&d;e  gif hi on &d;&ae;m cu&d;an gewislice ongieta&d; hw&ae;t &d;&ae;ron t&ae;lwyr&d;es bi&d;. 
 &D;onne hi leornia&d; mid fulre estfulnesse &d;a so&d;an god to secanne  &d;onne hi mid fulle gesceade ongieta&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t w&ae;s leas &amp; idelnes &d;&ae;t hi &ae;r heoldon. 
 Ac gehiren hi &d;&ae;t &d;as andweardan god bio&d; from &ae;lcre lustfulnesse swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice gewitende  &amp; swa&d;eah sio scyld &d;e hi &d;urh &d;a lustfullnesse &d;urhtio&d; ungewitendlice bi&d; &d;urhwuniende mid wr&ae;ce; 
 &amp; nu &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie lyst hi sculon nedenga forl&ae;tan  &amp; &d;eah &d;&ae;t hi nu nedenga forl&ae;ta&d; him bi&d; eft to wite gehealden. 
 Oft &d;eah weor&d;a&d; men swi&d;e halwendlice af&ae;rde mid &d;&ae;m ilcan &d;ingum &d;e hi &ae;r unnytlice lufedon: &d;onne &d;&ae;t gesl&ae;gene mod gesih&d; swa healicne dem his agnes hryres  &amp; ongit hine selfne on swelcre frecennesse &amp; on swelcne spild forl&ae;d  &d;onne wi&d;trem&d; he  &amp; onhupa&d;  &amp; ondr&ae;t him &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he &ae;r lufode. 
 Leorna&d; &d;onne to lufianne &d;&ae;t he &ae;r forhogde. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecweden to Ieremie &d;&ae;m witgan  &d;a he w&ae;s onsended to l&ae;ranne  hit w&ae;s gecweden: Ic h&ae;bbe &d;e nu tod&ae;g gesetne ofer rice &amp; ofer &d;ioda &d;&ae;t &d;u hi toluce &amp; toweorpe &amp; forspilde &amp; tostence &amp; getimbrie &amp; geplantige. 
 For&d;&ae;m  buton he &d;&ae;t woh &ae;r towurpe ne meahte he noht nytwyr&d;lice &d;&ae;t ryht getimbrian; 
 For&d;&ae;m  buton he of his hieremonna mode &d;a &d;ornas &d;&ae;re idlan lufan &ae;r up atuge  unnyt he plantode on hi &d;a word &d;&ae;re halgan lare. 
 For&d;&ae;m w&ae;s eac &d;&ae;tte sanctus Petrus &ae;rest towearp &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he eft timbrede. 
 &D;&ae;t w&ae;s &d;a &d;a he Iudeas nolde nan wuht l&ae;ran hw&ae;t hi don scolden  ac him cidde  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi &ae;r dydon  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: &d;one Nazareniscan H&ae;lend &d;&ae;t w&ae;s afandon wer betwux eow on m&ae;genum &amp; tacnum &amp; foretacnum  &d;a worhte Dryhten &d;urh hine ongemang eow  &d;one ge beswicon &d;urh unryhtwisra monna honda  &amp; ofslogon &amp; ahengon &d;urh eower ge&d;eaht  swa swa hit God &ae;t fruman wisse  &amp; &d;eah ge&d;afode; 
 Se ilca God hine eft aweahte to onliesanne &d;a geh&ae;ftan on helle. 
 For&d;&ae;m him &ae;twat Petrus &d;a d&ae;de &d;e he walde  si&d;&d;an hi ongeaten hiora w&ae;lhreownesse  &d;&ae;t hi w&ae;ren gedrefde &amp; geea&d;medde  &amp; &d;&ae;s &d;e nytweor&d;licor gehierden &d;a halgan lare  &d;e hi &ae;r wilnodon &d;&ae;t hi gehiran mosten. 
 &D;a andwyrdon hin &d;a Iudeas  &amp; cw&ae;don: Hw&ae;t magon we his nu don  bro&d;ur Petrus? 
 Petrus andswarode  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Do&d; &ae;rest hreowsunga  &amp; weor&d;a&d; si&d;&d;an gefullwade. 
 &D;a edniwunge &amp; &d;a lare hi swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice forsawen  &d;&ae;r hi &ae;r ne ongeten &d;one hryre &amp; &d;a toworpennesse hira w&ae;lhreownesse &d;urh his &d;reaunga. 
 Gelicost &d;&ae;m &d;e sancte Paule w&ae;s  &d;a him &d;&ae;t leoht com of hefonum  &amp; hine gebregde: n&ae;s him no &d;a giet to gecweden hw&ae;t he mid ryhte &d;onon for&d; don scolde  ac him w&ae;s ges&ae;d hw&ae;t he &ae;r to unryhte dyde . 
 Ac &d;a he swa gebreged on eor&d;an feoll  &amp; ascode  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t eart &d;u  Dryhten? 
 &D;a w&ae;s him swi&d;e hra&d;e geandwyrd: Ic eom se Nazarenisca H&ae;lend  &d;e &d;u ehtst. 
 &amp; &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Dryhten  hw&ae;t h&ae;tst &d;u me ge don? 
 &D;a ondwyrde him Dryhten: Aris  &amp; gong to geonre byrig; 
 &D;e mon s&ae;g&d; &d;ara hw&ae;t &d;u don scealt. 
 Loca nu  hu Dryhten w&ae;s sprecende of hefonum to his ehtere  &amp; hine &d;reade for his &ae;rgedonan weorcum. 
 &AE;r&d;&ae;m&d;e he him s&ae;de hu he hine for&d; healdan sceolde  &d;a w&ae;s gehroren sio upah&ae;fenes Paules &amp; eal &d;a weorc &d;e he &d;urh &d;a worhte. 
 &amp; sona &ae;fter &d;&ae;m hryre &d;&ae;re upah&ae;fennesse he ongan timbrian ea&d;modnesse. 
 &D;a &d;a he wilnode lare &ae;t Gode  &d;a gefeoll se egeslica ehtere to &d;on &d;&ae;t he swa micle stranglicor arise swa he hefiglicor afeoll. 
 Swa sint to teweorpanne &ae;rest &d;a &d;e nan god &ae;r ne dydon &d;urh &d;reaunge of &d;&ae;re heardnesse hiora yfelnesse  to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t hi sien eft on firste ar&ae;rde &amp; gestonden on ryhtum weorce; 
 For&d;&ae;m we ceorfa&d; heah treowu on holte &d;&ae;t we hi eft up ar&ae;ren on &d;&ae;m botle  &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r we timbran willen  &d;eah we hi forhr&ae;dlice to &d;&ae;m weorce don ne m&ae;gen for grennesse  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e hi adrugien. 
 Ac swa swa hi swi&d;ur adrygde bio&d; on eor&d;an swa hi mon m&ae;g orsorglicor up fegean. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e n&ae;bre nylla&d; fulfremman &d;&ae;t god &d;&ae;t hi onginna&d;  &d;&ae;t hi ongieten mid w&ae;rlice ymbe&d;once &d;&ae;tte  &d;onne &d;onne hi forl&ae;ta&d; hiora willes &amp; hiora gewealdes &d;a god &d;e hi getiohchod &ae;fdon to donne  &d;&ae;t hi &d;onne mid &d;y dilgia&d; &d;a &d;e hi &ae;r ongunnon; 
 For&d;&ae;m  gif &d;&ae;t ne wex&d; &d;&ae;t hie tiohhia&d; to donne  &d;onne wana&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hi &ae;r dydon. 
 Ac &ae;lces mannes mod on &d;ys middangearde h&ae;f&d; scipes &d;eaw. 
 &D;&ae;t scip wile hwilum stigan ongean &d;one stream  ac hit ne m&ae;g  buton &d;a rowend hit teon  ac hit sceal fleotan mid &d;y streame: ne m&ae;g hit no stille gestondan  buton hit ankor geh&ae;bbe  o&d;&d;e mon mid ro&d;rum ongean tio; 
 Elles hit gelent mid &d;y streame. 
 Swa de&d; sio forl&ae;tnes &d;&ae;s godan weorces. 
 Hio win&d; wi&d; &d;a god &d;e mon &ae;r gedon h&ae;f&d;  buton mon simle swincende &amp; wyrcende sie god weorc o&d; ende. 
 Be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gecweden &d;urh Salomon &d;one snotran  he cw&ae;&d;: Se &d;e his willum for his sl&ae;w&d;e forl&ae;tt his godan weorc  he bi&d; gelicost &d;&ae;m men &d;e his towirp&d;.

 For&d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t he for&d;y ne funde his weorc fulfremed beforan Gode  &d;a &d;e he &ae;r worhte  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he &d;a ne worhte  &d;a &d;e he &d;a wyrcean sceolde. 
 Swa eac  gif we ne gebeta&d; &d;&ae;t on us deadb&ae;res is &d;urh synna  &d;onne acwil&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;tte on us &ae;r lifde &d;urh god weorc. 
 Eac hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi geornlice ge&d;encen &d;&ae;tte hit bi&d; wyrse &d;&ae;t mon a onginne faran on so&d;f&ae;stnesse weg  gif mon eft wile ongeancierran  &amp; &d;&ae;t ilce on faran.

 Ac hi scoldon gehiran &d;one cwide &d;e awriten is on &d;&ae;m &ae;rendgewrite sancte Petres; 
 Hit is awriten &d;&ae;t him w&ae;re betere &d;&ae;t hi no so&d;f&ae;stnesse weg ne ongeaten  &d;onne hi underb&ae;c gecerden  si&d;&d;an hi hine ongeaten. 
 Eac hi sculon gehiran &d;one cwide &d;e be him awriten is on &d;&ae;m bocum &d;e hatton Apocalipsin  hit is awriten &d;&ae;t se engel cw&ae;de be &d;&ae;m biscepe to sancte Iohanne: Eala  w&ae;re he au&d;er  o&d;&d;e hat  o&d;&d;e ceald. 
 Ac for&d;on&d;e he is wlaco  &amp; nis nau&d;er  ne hat  ne ceald  &d;eah ic hine supe  ic hine wille eft ut aspiwan of minum mu&d;e. 
 Se &d;onne bi&d; wearm  nalles wlaco  &d;e god geornlice ongin&d;  &amp; eac geenda&d;. 
 Ac se bi&d; ceald &d;e nan god ne ongin&d;. 
 Ac swa swa &d;&ae;t cealde &ae;rest ongin&d; wlacian  &ae;r hit fulwearm weor&d;e  swa eac &d;&ae;t wearme wlaca&d;  &ae;r hit eallunga acealdige. 
 Swa eac se &d;e forl&ae;t &d;one cele ungetreownesse. 
 &amp; wyr&d; wlacra treowa  &amp; nyle &d;onne &d;&ae;t wl&ae;ce oferwinnan  &amp; wearmian o&d; he wealle. 
 Butan tweon  se &d;e to lange &amp; to f&ae;ste wuna&d; on &d;&ae;m wlacum treowum  he geortreow&d; &d;&ae;t he &ae;fre m&ae;ge on welme weor&d;an  o&d;&d;&ae;t he mid ealle acola&d;; 
 &amp; &d;eah he &ae;r truwige  &d;onne he ceald bi&d;  &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge wearm weor&d;an  he geortriew&d;  &d;onne he wlacu bi&d;  gif he to longe on &d;&ae;m stent. 
 Swa eac se &d;e nu giet on synnum is  n&ae;f&d; he no forl&ae;ten &d;one truwan &amp; &d;one tohopan his gehwearfnesse; 
 Ac se  se &d;e &ae;fter his gehwerfnesse to lange wl&ae;c bi&d;  &d;onne lytla&d; him se tohopa &d;e he h&ae;fde  &d;a he synful w&ae;s. 
 For&d;&ae;m wilna&d; God to &ae;lcum men &d;&ae;t he sie o&d;&d;e wearm o&d;&d;e ceald  &d;yl&ae;s he for wl&ae;cnesse sie ut aspiwen. 
 For&d;&ae;m se cealda &d;enc&d; to wearmianne  &amp; se wearma wel&d; on godum cr&ae;ftum  &d;yl&ae;s he sie wealg for wl&ae;cnesse  &amp; for&d;&ae;m weor&d;e ut aspiwen. 
 For&d;&ae;m &ae;lc w&ae;ter bi&d; &d;y unwerodre to drincanne  &ae;fter&d;&ae;m&d;e hit wearm bi&d;  gif hit eft acola&d;  &d;onne hit &ae;r w&ae;re  &ae;r hit mon o ongunne wleccan. 
 &D;&ae;tte on o&d;re wisan sint to monianne &d;a &d;e diegellice yfel do&d;  &amp; god openlice; 
 &amp; on o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e willa&d; helan &d;&ae;t hi to gode do&d;  &amp; of sumum &d;ingum openlice cy&d;a&d; &d;&ae;t hie willa&d; &d;&ae;t men wenen &d;&ae;t hi yfle beon. 
 On o&d;re wisan sint to manienne &d;a &d;e yfel degellice do&d;  &amp; god openlice; 
 On o&d;re wisan &d;a &d;e &d;a god hela&d; &d;e hi do&d;  &amp; ne recca&d; hw&ae;t him mon ymbe r&ae;swe. 
 &D;a &d;onne sint to manienne &d;a &d;e yfel degellice do&d;  &amp; god openlice  &d;&ae;t hi ge&d;encen hu hr&ae;dlice se eor&d;lica hlisa oferg&ae;&d;  &amp; hu unanwendendlice se godcunda &d;urhwuna&d;. 
 Hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi on &d;ara &d;inga ende hiora modes eagan af&ae;stnien  &amp; gesion &d;&ae;tte &d;is mennisce lof swi&d;e hr&ae;dlice gewit  &amp; se uplica Dema &amp; se eca &d;a deglan scylda ealla wat  &amp; simle bi&d; gearo to &d;&ae;m edleanum. 
 Ac &d;a dieglan yfel habba&d; ecne gewutan on &d;&ae;m godcundan Deman. 
 Ac &d;a god &d;e hi openlice do&d; beforan monnum beo&d; fulneah swelce hi sien butan gewitnesse  for&d;&ae;m hi n&ae;bba&d; ece gewitnesse. 
 Ac hi habba&d; ece gewitnesse &d;ara yfela &d;e hi diegellice do&d;  &d;onne hi heola&d; from monnum &d;&ae;t hi secggan scoldon  &amp; secga&d; &d;&ae;t hi heolan scoldon. 
 Be swelcum monnum cw&ae;&d; Dryhten &d;&ae;t hi w&ae;ren gelicost deadra manna byrgennum  &d;a bio&d; utan oft swi&d;e wlitige geworhte  &amp; bio&d; innan swi&d;e fule gefylde. 
 Swa bio&d; &d;a &d;e hira god eowia&d; beforum monnum  &amp; hira yfel hela&d; oninnan him selfum: hi licetta&d;  &amp; woldon lician for manna eagum utane buton godum weorcum innane. 
 Ac hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi ne forsion &d;a god &d;e hi do&d;  ac wenen him maran mede to &d;onne hi wena&d;. 
 To swi&d;e hi hi forsio&d;  gif hi him maran mede to ne wena&d; &d;onne eor&d;lices lofes  &amp; him &d;&ae;r genog &d;ync&d;. 
 Hi sella&d; wi&d; to lytlum weor&d;e &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hi meahton hefonrice mid gebycggan: sella&d; wi&d; manna lofe. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Dryhten on his godspelle &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t w&ae;re hira med. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi &d;&ae;t god openlice do&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t yfel diegellice  hi tacnia&d; mid &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t men scylen onscunian &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hie degellice do&d;  &amp; lufian &d;&ae;t hi openlice do&d;: for &d;&ae;re bisene hi libba&d; &d;eah o&d;rum monnum  &amp; cwela&d; him selfum. 
 Ongean &d;&ae;t sint to manienne &d;a &d;e god diegellice do&d;  &amp; swa&d;eah on sumum weorcum gelicceta&d; &d;&ae;t hi openlice yfel don  &amp; ne recca&d; hw&ae;t men be him sprecen  hi sint to manienne &d;&ae;t hi mid &d;&ae;re licettunge o&d;rum monnum yfle bisene ne astellen  &d;eah hi self teladon &d;&ae;t hi mid &d;&ae;re licettunga o&d;re men ne dwellen ne him ne derigen  &d;yl&ae;s hit sie ongieten &d;&ae;t hie lufigen hi selfe swi&d;ur &d;onne hiora niehstan  swelce hi hie selfe drencen mid wine  &amp; &d;&ae;m o&d;rum sellen attor. 
 Ac &d;onne hi &d;a yflan bisne openlice do&d;  &amp; &d;&ae;t god degellice  &d;onne ne helpa&d; hi mid o&d;rum &d;ara nauht hira niehstum  mid o&d;rum hi him deria&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m swa hwa swa hil&d; his godan weorc  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wile fleon idel gielp  &d;onne ne l&ae;t he nanne o&d;erne &ae;fter him on &d;a godan weorc  &d;onne he nyle &d;a bisne o&d;rum eowian &d;e he mid ryhte eowian sceal. 
 He de&d; swelce he plantige treowu  &amp; ceorfe of &d;a wyrtruman. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; Crist on his godspelle: Do&d; eower godan weorc beforan mannum  &d;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen weor&d;ian eowerne F&ae;der &d;e on hefonum is. 
 Ac swa&d;eah is awriten on &d;&ae;m ilcan bocum ungelic cwide &d;issum  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t he cw&ae;&d;: Behealda&d; eow &d;&ae;t ge ne don eowre ryhtwisnesse beforan monnum  &d;yl&ae;s hi eow herien. 
 Ac hw&ae;t wile &d;&ae;t nu beon weorca &d;&ae;t us on o&d;erre stowe forbiet &d;&ae;t we hit beforan mannum don  on o&d;erre l&ae;r&d; buton &d;&ae;t we hit for&d;&ae;m helen  &d;&ae;t us mon ne herige  &amp; for&d;y yppen &d;&ae;t mon God herige  &amp; o&d;re men &d;a ilcan bisne underfon? 
 Ac &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r us God forbead &d;&ae;t we ure ryhtwisnesse beforan monnum dyden  he us gecy&d;de forhwy he hit forbead  &d;a he cw&ae;&d; &d;yl&ae;s hi eow herigen. 
 Ond eft &d;a he us het &d;&ae;t we hit beforan monnum dyden  &d;a cw&ae;&d; he sona &d;&ae;r&ae;fter  to &d;on &d;&ae;t hi weor&d;igen eowerne F&ae;der &d;e on hefonum is.

 For &d;&ae;m &d;ingum bi&d; &ae;lc god weorc god  sie swa open swa degle  sw&ae;&d;er hit sie. 
 &D;onne se mon no his &ae;genne gielp mid ne sec&d;  ac &d;&ae;s uplican F&ae;der  &d;eah he hit openlice do  he hit gediegle&d; mid &d;y &d;&ae;t he h&ae;f&d; &d;&ae;s gewitnesse &d;e he &d;&ae;r cweman &d;enc&d; &d;&ae;t he hit for Gode dyde  n&ae;s for gielpe. 
 Ac se &d;onne se hit degellice de&d;  &amp; &d;eah wolde &d;&ae;t he wurde arasod  &amp; si&d;&d;an for&d;y hered  &d;eah hit &d;onne nan mon nyte  swa&d;eah hit bi&d; beforan monnum gedon  emne swelce hit sie on ealra &d;ara gewitnesse gedon &d;e he on his mode wilnode &d;&ae;t hit hereden. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit is betere  swa swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don  &d;&ae;tte &ae;lc mon adryge of o&d;erra monna mode &d;one wenan be him &ae;lces yfeles  swa swa he butan synne fyrmest m&ae;ge  for&d;&ae;m  gif he swa ne de&d;  &d;onne scenc&d; he &d;a scylde mid &d;&ae;re bisene &ae;lcum &d;ara &d;e him &ae;nges yfles to wen&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit gebyre&d; oft  &d;onne hwa ne rec&d; hu micles yfeles him mon to wene  &d;eah he self nan yfel ne do  &d;&ae;t he &d;eah gesynga&d; &d;urh &d;a &d;e be him bisnia&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; sanctus Paulus to his giongrum  &d;a &d;a he sumun liefde to &d;icgganne &d;&ae;tte he nolde &d;&ae;t hi ealle &d;igden  &d;yl&ae;s &d;a untruman be him bisneden  &amp; &d;urh &d;&ae;t wurden astyrede mid &d;&ae;ra costunga hwelcre &d;e hi eft wi&d;stondan ne meahton; 
 For&d;&ae;m he cw&ae;&d;: Locia&d; nu &d;&ae;t &d;ios eowru leaf ne weor&d;e o&d;rum monnum to biswice. 
 Ond eft he cw&ae;&d; be &d;&ae;m ilcan: &d;onne forwyr&d; &d;in bro&d;ur for &d;inum &d;ingum  for &d;one &ae;r Crist ge&d;rowade. 
 Swa &d;onne ge gesyngia&d; wi&d; eowre bro&d;er  &amp; ofslea&d; hira untruman gewit  &d;onne gesyngige ge wi&d; God. 
 &D;&ae;t ilce m&ae;nde Moyses  &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Ne cwe&d;e ge nan la&d; &d;&ae;m deafan.

 Se &d;onne cwi&d; yfel &d;&ae;m deafan  se &d;one &ae;fweardan t&ae;l&d;  gif he hine unscyldigne wat. 
 &amp; se screnc&d; &d;one blindan  &d;e &d;one ungesceadwisan mir&d; mid &d;y &d;e he his god degellice de&d;  &amp; &d;eah licet swelce he yfel do. 
 Ymbe &d;&ae;t  hu mon monige scyndan scyle to &d;&ae;m &d;&ae;tte his godan d&ae;da ne weor&d;en to yflum d&ae;dum. 
 &D;is sint nu &d;a lara &d;e &d;&ae;s modes hierdas &amp; &d;&ae;re sawle sceolon ealle men l&ae;ran &d;&ae;t hi ealneg h&ae;bben &d;a sealfe gearuwe &d;e to &d;&ae;re wunde belimpe &d;e hi &d;onne gesion. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit bi&d; swi&d;e geswincful &d;&ae;t mon &ae;lcne mon scyle on sundrum l&ae;ran  hit is &d;eah earfo&d;re ealle &ae;tsomne to l&ae;ranne  for&d;&ae;m&d;e he sceal gemetgian swa cr&ae;ftelice his stemne &d;&ae;tte he &ae;ghwelcum men finde &d;one l&ae;cedom &d;e him to gebyrge  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;a mettrymnessa ne beo&d; ealra manna gelica. 
 &amp; huru &d;&ae;t he self do swa swa he o&d;re l&ae;r&d;  for&d;on &d;&ae;t he m&ae;ge self gan orsorglice betwuxn o&d;erra monna un&d;eawas  swa swa scearp sweord &d;a wunde tosceat on tu  &amp; g&ae;&d; gehalre ecgge for&d;. 
 Ond &d;&ae;t he huru swa egesige &d;a ofermodan  &d;&ae;t he &d;a ea&d;modan mid &d;y to swi&d;e ne f&ae;re; 
 Ond swa l&ae;re &d;a o&d;re ea&d;metta  swa he &d;one ege to swi&d;e &d;&ae;m o&d;rum ne geiece; 
 &D;&ae;t he swa frefre &d;a ea&d;modan  swa &d;a ofermodan ne weor&d;en unmidlode; 
 Ond swa l&ae;re &d;a slawan geornfulnesse godes weorces  swa he &d;a geornfullan to ungemetlice ne geswence; 
 Ond swa tilige hira geswinc to gemetgianne  swa he &d;a idlan ne gedo orsorge  &d;&ae;t hi for&d;y ne aslawien; 
 Ond &d;&ae;t he swa stiere &d;&ae;m unge&d;yldegum irsunga  swa he &d;one hnescan &d;afettere on recceleste ne gebrenge;

 Swelce he openlice cw&ae;de: Ic wende &d;&ae;t ic w&ae;re swi&d;e strong on manegum cr&ae;ftum  ac ic ongeat swi&d;e hra&d;e  si&d;&d;an &d;u me forlete  hu untrum ic w&ae;s. 
 &amp; eft he cw&ae;&d; on &d;&ae;m eahta &amp; hund&ae;lleftiogo&d;an psalme  he cw&ae;&d;: Ic swor swa swa ic getiohhod h&ae;fde &d;&ae;t ic wolde gehealdan &d;ine domas &amp; &d;ine ryhtwisnesse  Dryhten. 
 Ac he ongeat swi&d;e hra&d;e  &d;a he gemette &d;a gedrefednesse  &d;&ae;t hit n&ae;s on his agnum onwalde &d;&ae;t he meahte gehealdan &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he &ae;r gehet &amp; swor. 
 &amp; &d;a wende he hine sona to his gebede  &amp; sohte him &d;&ae;r fultum to  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic eom gehened &ae;ghwonane &amp; on &ae;ghwam  Dryhten; 
 Ac gecwuca me &ae;fter &d;inum wordum  Dryhten. 
 Swa oft sio godcunde gemetgung  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e hio &d;&ae;m men selle cr&ae;ftas &amp; m&ae;gen  hio him geeowa&d; his untrymnesse  &amp; his unmehta hine gemyndga&d;  &d;yl&ae;s he hine upahebbe for his cr&ae;ftum. 
 For&d;&ae;m eac w&ae;s gecweden to Ezechiele &d;&ae;m witgan &d;&ae;t he w&ae;re monnes sunu  &ae;r&d;&ae;m&d;e him w&ae;ren geeowad &d;a hefonlican &d;ing. 
 Swelce hine God openlice manode  &amp; him to cw&ae;de: Ne beo &d;u to upah&ae;fen on &d;inum mode for &d;&ae;m &d;ingum &d;e &d;u gesihst  ac ge&d;enc w&ae;rlice hw&ae;t &d;u eart; 
 &amp; &d;eah &d;u &d;&ae;t hehste &d;urhfare  ne forgiet &d;u &d;eah &d;&ae;t &d;u man eart  ac ge&d;enc &d;one bridel &d;inre mettrymnesse swi&d;e geornlice on &d;e selfum  &d;eah &d;u sie up ofer &d;ine m&ae;&d; ah&ae;fen. 
 For&d;&ae;m is micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t we ures modes eagan gecerren to &d;&ae;re sceawunga urre untrymnesse. 
 &D;onne us fullicost olecca&d; &d;a cr&ae;ftas &amp; &d;a m&ae;genu  &d;onne is us micel &d;earf &d;&ae;t we ea&d;modlice ofdune anluten mid urum mode  &amp; halwendlice ge&d;encen &d;a god &d;e we forgiemeleasodon  n&ae;s &d;a we dydon; 
 &D;&ae;tte ure mod &d;y f&ae;stre &amp; &d;y strengre beforan Gode sie on &d;&ae;m cr&ae;ftum for &d;&ae;re ea&d;modnesse &d;e we hit mid gewundia&d;  &d;onne we gemuna&d; ure giemeleste. 
 For&d;&ae;m oft se &ae;lmiehtiga God forlet &d;&ae;t mod his gecorenra gesyngian on sumum lytlum &d;ingum  &d;eah hi on manegum sien fullfremede  &d;&ae;t hi him ondr&ae;den  &amp; murkien for hira unfullfremednesse  &d;eah hi beorhte scinen on sumum wunderlicun cr&ae;ftum; 
 &D;&ae;t hi hi for &d;&ae;m miclum &d;ingum ne m&ae;gen to upahebban  &d;a hwile &d;e hi ne magon gebetan &d;&ae;t lytle; 
 &D;yl&ae;s hi dyrren ofermodgian for &d;&ae;m &ae;&d;elestum weorcum  &d;a hwile &d;e hi ne magon oferswi&d;an &d;a ytemestan yfelu. 
 Loca nu  &d;u goda wer Iohannes  hu f&ae;gerne &amp; hu wlitigne monnan ic h&ae;bbe at&ae;fred  swa unwlitig writere swa swa ic eom. 
 &D;&ae;r ic h&ae;bbe get&ae;ht hwelc hierde bion sceal. 
 To &d;&ae;m ic w&ae;s gened mid &d;inre t&ae;lnesse  &d;&ae;t ic nu h&ae;bbe manege men gel&ae;d to &d;&ae;m st&ae;&d;e fullfremednesse on &d;&ae;m scipe mines modes  &amp; nu giet hwearfige me self on &d;&ae;m y&d;um minra scylda. 
 Ac ic &d;e bidde &d;&ae;t &d;u me on &d;&ae;m scipgebroce &d;isses andweardan lifes sum bred ger&ae;ce &d;inra gebeda  &d;&ae;t ic m&ae;ge on sittan o&d; ic to londe cume  &amp; ar&ae;r me mid &d;&ae;re honda &d;inra geearnunga  for&d;&ae;m&d;e me h&ae;f&d; gehefegad sio byr&d;en minra agenra scylda.
